NTD_1.1.1^1	tattvam jñāyate anena iti tattva jñānam śāstram tasmāt pramāṇa ādi padārtha tattva avagama avāntara vyāpārāt niḥśreyasasya adhigamaḥ prāptiḥ bhavati iti śāstra niḥśreyasayoḥ hetu hetumat bhāva pratipādana artham sūtram evam ca sati pramāṇa ādi padārtha śāstrayoḥ jñāpyajñāpaka bhāvaḥ pramāṇa ādi padārtha tattva jñānayoḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāva lakṣaṇaḥ ca saṃbandhaḥ sūcitaḥ bhavati viṣa ghna mantra vat sva rūpeṇa avivakṣita arthasya śāstrasya niḥśreyasa hetu tva anabhyupagamāt atha pramiti sādhanāni pratyakṣa ādīni pramāṇāni yat viṣayam mithyājñānam saṃsāram tanoti yat viṣayam ca samyak jñānam tat nivartayati tat mumukṣuṇā prakarṣeṇa jñeyam ātma ādi dvādaśavidham prameyam anavadhāraṇa ātmakaḥ pratyayaḥ saṃśayaḥ yad artha adhyavasāyāt puruṣaḥ pravartate tat prayojanam vādi prativādinoḥ buddhi sāmya viṣayaḥ arthaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ pramāṇa mūla abhyupagama vyavasthā siddhāntaḥ para artha anumāna mūla vākya eka deśāḥ pratijña ādayaḥ avayavāḥ 
NTD_1.1.1^2	 sāmānyatas avagate viśeṣataḥ ca anavagate viśeṣa avadhāraṇa artham kāraṇa upapatya ūhaḥ pravartate sa tarkaḥ vicāra pūrvaka anyatara pakṣa avadhāraṇam nirṇayaḥ nānā pravaktṛkaḥ vicāra vastu viṣayaḥ vākya sandarbha viśeṣaḥ tattva jñāna phalakaḥ vādaḥ saḥ eva chala jāti nigraha sthāna sādhana upālambhaḥ jalpaḥ sa pratipakṣa sthāpanā hīnaḥ vitaṇḍā anyatama liṅga dharma anuvidhānena pravartamānāḥ ahetavaḥ santaḥ hetu vat ābhāsamānāḥ hetvābhāsāḥ sāmānya śabdasya aneka artha tve satya vivakṣita artha adhyapāropeṇa vacana vighātaḥ yaḥ kriyate tad chalam sādharmya vaidharmyayoḥ anyatareṇa pratīpam avasthānam jātiḥ vipratipattiḥ apratipattiḥ ca nigraha sthānam iti padārthānām vyutpattiḥ yadi api saṃśaya ādīnām padārthānām pramāṇa prameyayoḥ eva yathāsaṃbhavam antarbhāvaḥ tathā api ātma viṣaya manana jñāna janana samartha padārtha anumāna apara paryāyasya parīkṣā vidheḥ tad mūla tvāt tena tena ākāreṇa te jñātāḥ vidyā prasthānasya bhedakāḥ iti teṣām pṛthak vacanam 
NTD_1.1.2^1	 duḥkha janma pravṛtti doṣa miththā jñānānām uttarottara apāye tad anantarā pāyāt apavargaḥ duḥkha janma pravṛtti doṣa mithyā jñānānam uttarottara apāye tad anantara abhāvāt tattva jñānāt mithyājñāna nivṛttau tad mūlānām doṣāṇām nivṛttiḥ tad nivṛttau tad mūlāyāḥ pravṛtteḥ nivṛttiḥ pravṛtti nivṛttī nikāya viśiṣṭa pūrva pūrva indriya śarīra vedanā ādi saṃbandha lakṣaṇasya janmanaḥ nivṛttiḥ tad nivṛttau= anāgata sakala duḥkha nivṛttiḥ ayam punar anāgata duḥkha nivṛtti lakṣaṇaḥ mokṣaḥ tattva jñāna anantaram eva mithyājñāna ādi nivṛtti krameṇa bhavati 
NTD_1.1.2^2	 utpanna tattva jñānasya prāpta para niḥśreyasasya muneḥ avasthāna saṃbhavāt śāstra sampradāya avicchedaḥ tattva jñānasya niḥśreyasa hetu tvam ca aniṣiddham iti tad anupapattyā prathama sūtre pratipādita saṃbandha vighātaḥ anena parihriyate iti tattva parīkṣaṇam asya arthaḥ uttarottara apāyaḥ iti pāṭhā apekṣayā anādi bhava parampara upātta anantā niyata vipāka samaya prācīna karma vināśaḥ prasaṃkhyāna paripākāt tad upayogi bahuvidha śarīra nirmāṇa dvāreṇa iti veditavyam na tattva jñāna mātrāt upabhogāt prakṣayaḥ iti asmin pakṣe āgama anumāna lakṣaṇasya pramāṇa dvitayasya vidyamāna tvāt 
NTD_1.1.3	 pratyakṣa anumāna upamāna śabdāḥ pramāṇāni pramiti sādhanam pramāṇam iti pramāṇa sāmānya lakṣaṇa sūcana dvāreṇa pratyakṣa ādīnām vibhāga uddeśa artham sūtram vibhāgaḥ ca niyama arthaḥ niyamaḥ ca nyūna adhika nivṛti arthaḥ akṣam akṣam prati vartate iti pratyakṣam anu paścāt mānam anumānam upamīyate yena tad upamānam āptasya para prayojana artham yat vacanam sa śabdaḥ ebhiḥ eva caturbhiḥ pramāṇaiḥ deva manuṣya tiraścām vyavahārāḥ pravartante na atas anyathā iti vibhāgasya viśeṣāt deśa rūpa tvāt na śāstra pravṛtteḥ traividhya virodhaḥ 
NTD_1.1.4^1	 indriya artha sannikarṣa utpannam jñānam avyapadeśyam avyabhicāri vyavasāya ātmakam pratyakṣam indriya artha sannikarṣa utpannam api jñānam avyabhicāri yatas bhavati tat pratyakṣam iti phala viśeṣaṇa pakṣam āsthāya lakṣaṇam na kāraṇa pakṣam tasya viśeṣaṇavat tva anupapatteḥ sannikarṣaḥ punar ṣoḍhā saṃyogaḥ saṃyukta samavāyaḥ saṃyukta samaveta samavāyaḥ samavāyaḥ samaveta samavāyaḥ viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvaḥ ca iti tat punar pratyakṣam dvividham sa vikalpakam nirvikalpakam ca iti tatra vastu svarūpa mātra avabhāsakam nirvikalpakam yathā prathama akṣa sannipāta jam jñānam viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāva avagāhi jñānam sa vikalpakam yathā gauḥ śuklaḥ parispandate viṣāṇi iti 
NTD_1.1.4^2	 nanu tarhi avyapadeśyam vyavasāya ātmakam iti pada dvayam kim artham vipratipatti nirāsa artham tathā hi nāma ādi rahitam avikalpakam na asti iti yat matam tad nirāsa artham avyapadeśyam iti vyapadeśyam viśeṣaṇam upalakṣaṇam vā jāti ādi yat ca avyapadeśyam avikalpakam jñānam tat api pratyakṣam iti tathā vyavasāyaḥ viniścayaḥ vikalpaḥ iti anarthāntaram tad ātmakam jñānam sa vikalpakam tat api pratyakṣam vividha kalpanā yogena viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāva avagāhi jñāna tvāt śabda adhyāsa kṣaṇika tva pakṣa pratikṣepeṇa ubhayoḥ nirvikalpaka sa vikalpaka jñānayoḥ avyabhicāri tve sati indriya artha sannikarṣa utpanna tvāt pratyakṣa tvam yuktam eva viparyaya saṃśaya jñānayoḥ indriya artha sannikarṣa avyabhicāri pada dvayāt eva yathāsaṃkhyam nirāsaḥ draṣṭavyaḥ 
NTD_1.1.5^1	 atha tad pūrvakam trividham anumānam pūrvavat śeṣavat sāmānyatas dṛṣṭam ca tad pūrvakam iti atra tad śabdena liṅga liṅginoḥ sa bandha darśanam dvitīya liṅga darśanam saṃbandha smaraṇam ca abhisaṃbadhyate tathā ca sati liṅga liṅgi saṃbandha darśana dvitīya liṅga darśana saṃbandha smaraṇa pūrvakam tṛtīya liṅga darśanam śeṣa artha paricchitti phalakam anumānam iti uktam bhavati tat idam anumānam deśa kāla nara avasthā bhedena anekam api anena rūpeṇa trividham pūrvavat śeṣavat sāmānyatas dṛṣṭam ca iti tatra pūrvam kāraṇam vidyate yasya tat pūrvavat iti kāraṇena kārya anumānam yathā megha unnatyā bhaviṣyati vṛṣṭiḥ iti 
NTD_1.1.5^2	 kāryam kāraṇasya upayukta tvāt tat vidyate yasya cheṣa vat iti kāryāt kāraṇa anumānam yathā nadīpūreṇa vṛṣṭiḥ iti sāmānyatas dṛṣṭam iti akārya kāraṇa anumānam yathā balākayā salila anumānam iti athavā pūrvavat śeṣavat sāmānyatas dṛṣṭam ca iti kevala anvayī kevala vyatirekī anvaya vyatirekī ca iti lakṣaṇataḥ hetu traya pratipādana artham tatra avidyamāna vipakṣaḥ pakṣa sa pakṣayoḥ eva yathānyāyam vartamānaḥ hetuḥ kevala anvayī yathā vivāda āspadībhūtāni adṛṣṭa ādīni kasyacid pratyakṣāṇi prameya tvāt kara tala vat iti avidyamānasapakṣaḥ vipakṣāt vyāvṛttaḥ pakṣaḥ eva vyāptyā vartamānaḥ hetuḥ kevala vyatirekī 
NTD_1.1.5^3	 yathā sarvam kāryam sarva vid kartṛ pūrvakam kādācid ka tvāt yat sarva vid kartṛ pūrvakam na bhavati tat kādācid kam api na bhavati yathā ākāśam iti pakṣa dharma tayā yuktaḥ sa pakṣe sākalyena eka deśena vā vartamānaḥ vipakṣāt atīva vyāvṛttaḥ hetuḥ anvaya vyatirekī yathā anityaḥ śabdaḥ kṛtaka tvāt ghaṭa vat iti pūrvavat iti anvayinaḥ grahaṇam anvayasya pūrvam gṛhyamāṇa tvena pūrva śabda abhidheya tvāt śeṣavat iti vyatirekiṇaḥ grahaṇam anvayasya pūrvam gṛhīta tvena śiṣṭasya vyatirekasya śeṣa śabda abhidheya tvāt 
NTD_1.1.5^4	 sāmānyatas dṛṣṭam iti anvaya vyatirekiṇaḥ grahaṇam pakṣe sāmānyena anvayasya sa pakṣe dṛṣṭa tvāt adṛṣṭa tvāt ca vipakṣe tat evam avadhāraṇa ākāra praśleṣābhyām hetu traya para tvena pada trayam yojanīyam saṃbandha smaraṇam iti atra saṃbandhaḥ avinābhāvaḥ vivakṣitaḥ sa punar liṅga liṅginoḥ anaupādhikaḥ sa deṣaḥ bhūyas darśana saṃskāra sadhrī cīnena saṃbandha grāhiṇā pramāṇena yatra yena jñātaḥ tatra tasya anumānam liṅgam iti boddhavyam traikālya grahaṇāt na kevalam lakṣaṇataḥ kim tarhi viṣaya bhedāt api anumānam pratyakṣa bhinnam tri kāla viṣaya tvāt vartamāna eka viṣayam pratyakṣam tri kāla viṣayam anumānam iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_1.1.6	 prasiddha sādharmyāt sādhya sādhanam upamānam prasiddham sādharmyam yasya yena vā saḥ ayam prasiddha sādharmyaḥ gavayaḥ tasmāt prasiddha sādharmyāt prasiddhiḥ ca ubhayī pratyakṣa mayī anumāna mayī ca sādhyasya saṃjñā saṃjñi saṃbandhasya sādhanam pratipattiḥ yatas bhavati tad upamānam atideśa vākya smaraṇa savyapekṣam saṃjñā saṃjñi saṃbandha pramiti phalakam pratyakṣa janita dharmi jñānam upamānam iti tātparya arthaḥ 
NTD_1.1.7–1.1.8	 āpta upadeśaḥ śabdaḥ āptasya yathāvat dṛṣṭa arthasya tathā eva upadeṣṭuḥ para prayojana vat vacanam upadeśaḥ śabda lakṣaṇam pramāṇam iti sūtra arthaḥ sa dvividhaḥ dṛṣṭa adṛṣṭa artha tvāt dṛṣṭaḥ arthaḥ yena yasya vā saḥ ayam dṛṣṭa arthaḥ adaṣṭaḥ anumitaḥ yena yasya vā saḥ ayam adṛṣṭa arthaḥ dṛṣṭa adṛṣṭa artha tvābhyām sa ca ayam āgamaḥ dvividhaḥ yathā kārīrī nirvapet vṛṣṭi kāmaḥ yathā vā agnihotram juhuyāt svarga kāmaḥ iti nanu kimartham dvaividhya kathanam ucyate dṛṣṭa artha sādhāraṇyāt adṛṣṭa arthasya api prāmāṇyam anumātum śakyam iti kathana artham 
NTD_1.1.9–1.1.10^1	 atha prameyam ātma śarīra indriya artha buddhi manaḥ pravṛtti doṣa pretya bhāva phala duḥkha apavargāḥ tu prameyam yat viṣayam mithyājñānam saṃsāram tanoti yat viṣayam ca samyak jñānam tat nivartayati tat idam mumukṣuṇā prakarṣeṇa bodhyam dvādaśavidham prameyam iti sūtra arthaḥ icchā dveṣa prayatna sukha duḥkha jñānāni ātmanaḥ liṅgam yat jātīyasya sannikarṣāt sukham ātma upalabdhavān tat jātīyam artham paśyan= ādātum icchati tad viparītam paśyan dveṣṭi tat ubhayam āptum hātum ca prayatate sukha duḥkha smṛtau ca tad sādhanam ādadānaḥ sukham upalabhe duḥkham upalabhaḥ iti sukha duḥkhe ca ete bubhutsamānaḥ khalu ayam vimṛśati vimṛśan= ca jānīte tat evam icchā ādīni jñāna antāni smṛtyā saha eka kartṛ tvena pratisandhīyamāna tvāt ātmanaḥ liṅgam bhavanti liṅgam ca ātmanaḥ lakṣaṇam iti sūtra arthaḥ nanu katham icchā ādīnām smṛtyā saha eka kartṛ tvena pratisandhānam ucyate prathamam tāvat kadalī phala jñāna samanantaram etat jātīyam mama sukha sādhana tvena daṣṭam iti smṛtiḥ paścāt idam api tathābhūtam iti parāmarśa anubhavaḥ 
NTD_1.1.10^2	 tad anantaram upādāna icchā sā iyam icchā pūrva apara pratyayābhyām smṛtyā saha eka kartṛ tvena pratisandhīyate yasya mama icchā tasya prathama anubhavaḥ yasya prathama anubhavaḥ tasya sukha sādhana tva smṛtiḥ yasya smṛtiḥ tasya parāmarśa anubhavaḥ yasya parāmarśa anubhavaḥ tasya icchā iti evam dveṣa prayatna ādiṣu api yojyam tat evam icchā ādīni jñāna antāni pūrva apara pratyayābhyām smṛtyā saha eka kartṛka tvena pratisandhīyamāna tvāt śarīra indriya vedanā vyatiriktam ātmānam anumāpayanti yajñadattasya icchā ādīni tad pūrva apara pratyayābhyām smṛtyā saha aikartṛkāṇi tābhyām tayā saha eka kartṛka tvena pratisandhīyante yathā devadattasya icchā ādīni yajñadatta pratyaya smṛti ādibhiḥ na ca tathā etāni tasmāt ukta sādhyāni 
NTD_1.1.10^3	 na ca indriyā aikyāt śarīra aikyāt vā pratisandhānam bhavati indriya antara śarīra antara anubhūteṣu api pratisandhāna adarśanāt yathā mātuluṅga phala darśanāt rasanā indriya vikāraḥ danta udaka saṃplava lakṣaṇaḥ tatra pratisandhānam tathā bālye dṛṣṭasya kumāra vṛddha avasthayoḥ pratisandhānam idam anubhūtam iti na ca tatra avasthā bhedaḥ eva na śarīra bhedaḥ iti vācyam pariṇāma bhedasya āśraya bheda hetu tvena ghaṭa paṭa ādau= iva avaśya āśrayaṇīya tvāt tad aikya pratyabhijñānasya sādṛśya vaśena punar jāta nakha keśa ādiṣu iva saṃbhavāt na ca kārya kāraṇa bhāvāt buddhitaḥ eva pratisandhānam na ātma vaśāt iti vācyam satyabhāvāt asati ca bhāvāt asti khalu upādhyāya vijñānāt śiṣya jñāna utpattiḥ na ca tatra pratisandhānam iti samanantara pratyaya tva abhāvāt iti ced samaḥ ca asau= anantara pratyayaḥ ca iti samanantara pratyayaḥ 
NTD_1.1.10^4	 yathā rasa jñānāt rasa jñānam upādhyāya jñānam punar adhipati pratyayaḥ atas ca na pratisandhānam iti mā evam upādhyāya jñānasya api samanantara pratyaya tva saṃbhavāt yathā rasa upadeśāt rasa jñāna utpattau= iti atha ekasmin santāne yaḥ sadṛśa pratyayaḥ sa samanantara pratyayaḥ na santāna antaraḥ iti ced tarhi santāna aikya kṛtaḥ ayam anusandhāna pratyayaḥ na samanantara pratyaya mātra kṛtaḥ iti sva siddhānta vyākopaḥ tathā ekasmin pradeśe avasthitasya āmalakī phalasya apanaye tad sadṛśa phala antara saṃsthāpane tat eva idam yat mayā anubhūtam āmalakī phalam iti anusandhānam dṛṣṭam na ca tatra kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ atas ca kartṛ ā aikya kṛtaḥ ayam anusandhāna pratyayaḥ na kārya kāraṇa bhāva nibandhana iti siddham deha indriya vedanā vyatiriktaḥ ātma icchā ādibhiḥ anumeyaḥ iti 
NTD_1.1.11	 ceṣṭa indriya artha āśrayaḥ śarīram asamūrta antara pratyaya yoge sati hita ahita prāpti parihāra lakṣaṇa parispanda āśrita tvāt indriya anugrāhaka tvāt artha upakāraka tvāt ca śarīram tasmāt bhidyate iti arthaḥ kim punar indriya anugrāhaka tvam artha upakāraka tvam vā śarīrasya tat ucyate sva upaghāta anupaghāta anuvidhānam svādhīna prayojana siddhiḥ ca śarīra upaghātena upahanyate tad anupaghātena sva viṣaya grahaṇa samarthāni bhavanti indriyāṇi tathā rūpa rasa ādayaḥ arthāḥ śarīram āśritya sva prayojana sukha duḥkha saṃvedana nimitta tvam bhajante na atas anyathā atas śarīra upaghāta anuvidhānam śarīrasya indriya anugrāhaka tvam rūpa ādi artha kṛta sukha duḥkha vedana nimitta tvam ca śarīrasya artha āśrita tvam na punar ceṣṭā vat indriya artha samavāyaḥ indriya ārambhaka paramāṇuṣu vyabhicārāt iti 
NTD_1.1.12	 ghrāṇa rasana cakṣuḥ tvac śrotrāṇi indriyāṇi bhūtebhyaḥ yat śarīra saṃyuktam saṃskāra doṣa vyatiriktam sākṣāt pramiti sādhanam tat indriyam iti sāmānya lakṣaṇa sūcana dvāreṇa jighrati anena ityādi samākhyā sāmarthyāt sva viṣaya grahaṇaiḥ pañca bāhya indriyāṇi lakṣyante iti sūtra arthaḥ ghrāṇa m itarasmāt bhidyate indriya tve sati rūpa ādiṣu madhye gandhasya eva vyañjaka tvāt yat tu na bhidyate na tad indriya tve sati rūpa ādiṣu madhye gandhasya eva vyañjakam yathā rasanā indriyam na tathā idam tat itarasmāt bhidyate iti tad astitve kim pramāṇam iti ced anumānam pramāṇam yathā hi gandha upalavdhiḥ karaṇa kāryā kriyā tvāt chedana kriyā vat tat ca karaṇam pārthivam rūpa ādiṣu madhye niyamena gandhasya eva vyañjaka tvāt abhibhūta candana gandha udbodhaka kastūrikā dravya vat evam indriya antareṣu api yojanīyam tad lakṣaṇam ca indriyāṇām bhautika tve saṃbhavati na ahaṅkārika tvaḥ iti jñāpana artham bhūtebhyaḥ iti padam āhaṅkārika tve tad eka kāraka tvāt iti niyata bhūta guṇa grahaṇa sāmarthyam indriyāṇām na saṃbhavati 
NTD_1.1.13–1.1.15	 pṛthivī ap tejaḥ vāyuḥ ākāśam iti bhūtāni etāni indriya kāraṇāni iti sūtra āryaḥ gandha rasa rūpa sparśa śabdāḥ pṛthivī ādi guṇāḥ tad arthaḥ teṣām indriyāṇām arthāḥ tad arthāḥ indriyaiḥ arthyamāna tvam arthānām lakṣaṇam anyat sarvam suhṛd bhāvena iti mantavtam pṛthivī ādīni tad guṇāḥ ca iti dvandvaḥ gandha ādiṣu indriya niyama jñāpana artham gandha ādi grahaṇam buddhiḥ upalabdhiḥ jñānam iti anarthāntaram buddhi ādi śabda vācya tvam buddheḥ lakṣaṇam sārvajanīna saṅketa tvāt iti buddhiḥ itarasmāt bhidyate tad vācaka tvena sarva loka praddhi buddhi ādi paryāya śabda vācya tvāt yat tu na bhidyate tat na tathā yathā manaḥ ādīni 
NTD_1.1.16	 yugapad jñāna anutpattiḥ manasaḥ liṅgam rūpa ādi grahaṇāni cakṣuḥ ādi vyatirekeṇa adhiṣṭhāyaka antara apekṣāṇi teṣu satsu api ayugapad utpadyamāna tvāt yāni yeṣu satsu api yugapad na utpadyante tāni tad vyatirekeṇa adhiṣṭhāyaka antara apekṣāṇi yathā aneka śilpa abhijña puruṣeṇa kriyamāṇāni ratha ādīni vā asi a ādiṣu karaṇeṣu satsu sati ca aneka śilpa abhijñe tasmin puruṣe krama bhāvitad hasta saṃyoga apekṣāṇi yugapad na utpadyante tathā ca etāni rūpa ādi jñānāni tasmāt tad hi atirekeṇa adhiṣṭhāyaka antara apekṣāṇi iti tathā abāhya indriya nimittāḥ smṛti ādayaḥ kriyā viśeṣāḥ kāraka antara nimittāḥ kriyā tvāt chidi kriyā vat iti manaḥ anumīyate tad liṅga tvam ca manasaḥ na lakṣaṇam iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_1.1.17	 pravṛttiḥ vāc buddhi śarīra ārambhaḥ vācā jñāna utpādana dvāreṇa buddhyā manasā śarīreṇa vā yaḥ ārambhaḥ sā pravṛttiḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ buddhi śabdena manaḥ atra vivakṣitam sā iyam pravṛttiḥ dvidhā puṇya apuṇyā ca tatra puṇyāḥ daśavidhāḥ śarīreṇa dānam paricaraṇam paritrāṇam vācā ca satyam priyam hitam mitam manasā dayā aspṛhā śraddhā ca iti sā iyam pravṛttiḥ evam lakṣamāṇā nirvedāya avakalpate iti 
NTD_1.1.18–1.1.19	 pravarttana ālakṣaṇa doṣāḥ pravartanā pravṛtti hetu tvam tat ca moha eka artha samavāyaḥ katham pravartamānaḥ khalu atra rāga dveṣābhyām pravartate tau pravartayantau yasmin= ātmāna samavetau mithyājñānena saha tam eva pravartayataḥ na amūḍham mithyājñāna rahitam atas tayoḥ pravartanā mohasya api tad eka artha samavāyaḥ tayā pravartanayā ye lakṣyante rāga dveṣa mohāḥ te doṣāḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ punar utpattiḥ pretyabhāvaḥ śarīra ādi parityāgāt anya śarīra ādi upasampattiḥ yā sā iyam ātmanaḥ utpattiḥ sā pretyabhāvaḥ saṃsāraḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ tasya saṃsārasya anādi tva jñāpana artham punar grahaṇam 
NTD_1.1.20–1.1.21	 pravṛtti doṣa janitaḥ arthaḥ phalam śarīra ādikam phalam sarvam pravṛtti janya tvāt artha grahaṇam gauṇa mukhya lakṣaṇa avadhāraṇa artham mukhyam duḥkha saṃvedanam gauṇam anyat sarvam iti doṣa grahaṇam pravṛtti janana dvāreṇa dukha duḥkha hetu tvam doṣāṇām iti sūcayitum yadi api sukha duḥkha vyatiriktam phalam na asti tathā api pravṛtti doṣa janita tva dvāreṇa vijñātam tat eva śarīra indriya ādi sannirvedāya avakalpate iti pṛthak upanyāsaḥ pravṛtteḥ dharma adharma janana dvāreṇa saṃsāra hetu tva pratiṣedha artham vā doṣa grahaṇam doṣa salila avasiktayām ātma bhūmau pravṛtti janite dharma adharma bīje sukha duḥkhe samutpādayataḥ na itaratra iti bādhanā lakṣaṇam duḥkham etat eva śarīra ādi bādhanayā duḥkhena lakṣitam anuṣaktam duḥkham viṣa sampṛktān na vat evam sati sarvam duḥkham iti bhāvanāt virajyate viraktaḥ mucyate iti 
NTD_1.1.22	 tad atyanta vimokṣaḥ apavargaḥ tena śarīra ādinā duḥkhena ātyantikaḥ viyogaḥ śarīra ādi antarasya vā punar utpāda abhāvaḥ nanu tasmin sati kim bhavati utpannaiḥ utpadyamānaiḥ aśeṣa viśeṣa guṇaiḥ viyuktaḥ ātmā sva rūpeṇa tiṣṭhati vijñānam ānandam brahma iti sāmānādhikaraṇya śruti prāmāṇyāt pūrvam anāvirbhūtasya ānandasya ātma avasthāyām āvirbhāvaḥ iti kecid tat ayuktam tad ānanda sadbhāvasya pramāṇa bādhita tvena śruti gata ānandasya ca atyantika duḥkha abhāva viṣaya tvāt dṛṣṭaḥ ca duḥkha abhāve ayam ānanda śabdaḥ bhāra ākrāntasya vāhakasya tad apāyaḥ iti kim tat bādhakam pramāṇam ānanda vat tad anubhavasya nitya tve mukta saṃsāra avasthayoḥ aviśeṣa prasaṅgaḥ na ca śarīra ādīnām pratibandhaka tvam bhoga sādhana tvāt teṣām anitya tve tu tad utpattau kāraṇa abhāvaḥ na ca ātma manaḥ saṃyogasya yoga ja dharma sāpekṣasya tu kāraṇa tvam bhavati śarīra ādi saṃbandha sāpekṣasya tasya anubhavasya darśanāt mokṣa avasthāyām tad abhāvaḥ iti tat uktam tad abhāvaḥ ca apavargaḥ iti 
NTD_1.1.23	 samāna aneka dharma upapatteḥ vipratipatteḥ upalabdhi anupalabdhi avyavasthātaḥ ca viśeṣa apekṣaḥ vimarśaḥ saṃśayaḥ samāna dharma upapatteḥ aneka dharma upapatteḥ vipratipatteḥ ca iti trividhaḥ eva saṃśayaḥ itarada viśeṣaṇāt bhava ti iti sūtra arthaḥ tatra viṣaya svarūpa anavadhāraṇa pratyayaḥ saṃśayaḥ iti sāmānya lakṣaṇam viśeṣa lakṣaṇāni trīṇi tathā hi samānaḥ sadṛśaḥ dharmaḥ yasya saḥ ayam samāna dharmā tasya upalabdheḥ tasyāḥ kim kevalāyāḥ na kim tu upalabdhi anupalabdhi avyavasthātaḥ ca iti sādhaka bādhaka pramāṇa abhāvāt ca viśeṣa apekṣāyāḥ ca gṛhyamāṇa viśeṣa smaraṇāt ca saṃśayaḥ sthāṇuḥ vā puruṣaḥ vā iti anekaḥ asādhāraṇaḥ dharmaḥ asya saḥ ayam aneka dharmā tasya upalabdheḥ ca saṃśayaḥ pūrvavat viśeṣaṇam boddhavyam udāharaṇam tu satve sati vibhāga jananāt kim dravyam guṇaḥ karma vā śabdaḥ iti vipratipatteḥ ca iti vyāhata artha pravādaḥ vipratipatti śabdasya arthaḥ vyāhata artha pravādam upalabhamānasya upalabdhi anupalabdhi avyavasthāne sati tad gata viśeṣa anusmṛtau ca satyām saṃśayaḥ bhavati kim bhautikāni indriyāṇi uta abhautikāni iti 
NTD_1.1.24–1.1.25	 yam artham adhikṛtya pravartate tat prayojanam sa sādhanau sukha duḥkha prāpti parihārau prayojanam tat adhikṛtya pravartanāt yasmāt ayam puruṣaḥ pravartamānaḥ sa sādhanau sukha duḥkha prāpti parihārau= adhikṛtya viniścitya pravartate sukha māsyāmi dukham hāsyāmi iti tasmāt tau tasya prayojanam iti sūtra arthaḥ laukika parīkṣakāṇām yasmin= arthe buddhi sāmyam sa dṛṣṭāntaḥ buddhi sāmya viṣayaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ tasmāt laukika parīksaka grahaṇena vādi prativādinaḥ vivakṣita tvam anyathā tu ākāśa paramāṇu ādeḥ adraṣṭānta tā syāt iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_1.1.26	 tantra adhikaraṇa abhyupagama saṃsthitiḥ siddhāntaḥ tantram pramāṇam adhikaraṇam yeṣām arthānām te tantra adhikaraṇāḥ teṣām abhyupagama saṃsthitiḥ itthambhāva vyavasthā siddhāntaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ ābhimānikam pramāṇa tvam adhikaraṇa tvam anyathā vastunaḥ vairūpya prasaṅgāt iti sarva tantra siddhānte tu yathāsambhavam vyavasthā yojanīyāḥ 
NTD_1.1.27	 sa caturvidhaḥ sarva tantra pratitantra adhikaraṇa abhyupagama saṃsthiti artha antara bhāvāt siddhāntaḥ caturvidhaḥ sarva tantra siddhāntaḥ prati tantra siddhāntaḥ adhikaraṇa siddhāntaḥ abhyupagama siddhāntaḥ ca iti kutas sarva tantra pratitantra adhikaraṇa abhyupagama saṃsthitīnām artha antara bhāvāt parasparam vilakṣaṇa tvāt iti sūtra artham 
NTD_1.1.28–1.1.29	 sarva tantra prasiddhaḥ arthaḥ sarva tantra siddhāntaḥ sarveṣām saṃpratipatti viṣayaḥ arthaḥ sarva tantra siddhāntaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ yathā pramāṇaiḥ prameyasya adhigamaḥ iti samāna tantra siddhaḥ paratantra asiddhaḥ pratitantra siddhāntaḥ ekasmin= tantre siddhasya tantra antareṣu asiddhasya abhyupamaḥ pratitantra siṃddhāntaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ yathā na asataḥ utpattiḥ sataḥ ātma lābhaḥ iti sāṃkhyasya 
NTD_1.1.30–1.1.31	 yat siddhau= anya prakaraṇa asiddhiḥ saḥ adhikaraṇa siddhāntaḥ yasya arthasya sādhyasya hetoḥ vā siddhi viṣaye tad anuṣaṅgiṇaḥ arthāḥ tad antarbhāveṇa gamyante saḥ a rthaḥ sākṣāt adhikriyamāṇaḥ tad anuṣaṅgiṇām ca ādhāraḥ anena rūpeṇa adhikaraṇa siddhāntaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ yathā kārya anumāne sarvajña tva ādi siddhiḥ yathā vā pratisandhāna anumānaḥ indriya nānā tva siddhiḥ iti aparīkṣita abhyupagamāt tad viśeṣa parīkṣaṇam abhyupagama siddhānta yaḥ arthaḥ sūtreṣu na upanibaddhaḥ śāstre ca abhyupagataḥ saḥ abhyupagama siddhāntaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ yathā naiyāyikānām manasaḥ indriya tvam iti 
NTD_1.1.32–1.1.33	 pratijñā hetu udāharaṇa upanaya nigamanāni avayavāḥ yasya pratijña ādibhiḥ upakṛtasya viśeṣa avasthāpanam arthaḥ tat vākyam iti sāmānya lakṣaṇa sūcana dvāreṇa avayavānām vibhāga uddeśa artham sūtram iti arthaḥ sāmya nirdeśaḥ pratijñā prajñāpanīya dharma viśiṣṭaḥ dharmaḥ sādhyaḥ tasya nirdeśaḥ parigraha vacanam pratijñā iti sūtra arthaḥ yayā anityaḥ śabdaḥ iti 
NTD_1.1.34	 udāharaṇa sādharmyāt sādhya sādhanam hetuḥ anena sūtreṇa hetu sāmānya lakṣaṇam vyatireki viśeṣa lakṣaṇam ca pratipādyete tathā hi avayava tve sati pārokṣī āpanna sādhya sādhana vacana tvam sāmānya lakṣaṇam sādhya sādhana padāt sūcitam udāharaṇena eva sa pakṣeṇa eva sādhya sādhanam yat tasmāt utthāya svarūpa sādhya sādhana vacana tvam sati vipakṣe anvaya vyatirekiṇaḥ lakṣaṇam asati vipakṣe tat eva anvayinaḥ api lakṣaṇam iti tatra udāharaṇam anityaḥ śabdaḥ utpatti dharmaka tvāt paṭa vat iti sa pakṣa vyāpakasya jātimattve satyasmad ādi bāhya indriya grāhya tvāt iti tasya sarva anitya tva vādinaḥ anityaḥ śabdaḥ prameya tvāt iti sa pakṣa vyāpakasya anvayinaḥ pratyakṣa tvāt iti anyasya 
NTD_1.1.35–1.1.36	 tathā vaidharmyāt satām vipakṣeṇa iva vaidharmyam eva yat tasmāta samutthāya svarūpa sādhyasya sādhana vacana tvam sati sa pakṣe vyatirekiṇaḥ lakṣaṇam iti sūtra arthaḥ yathā na idam nirātmakam jīvat śarīram aprāṇa ādimattva prasaṅgāt loṣṭa vat iti sādhya sādharmyāt tad dharma bhāvaḥ dṛṣṭānte udāharaṇam vyāpya vyāpaka bhāva jñāpaka dṛṣṭānta vacanam udāharaṇam iti sāmānya lakṣaṇa sūcana dvāreṇa anvayaḥ dāharaṇa sūcana artham sūtram tathā hi sādhyena eva sādharmyam eva yat tasmāt sādhana sādharmyāt prayojana ātmakāt tasya eva dharmiṇaḥ prayojyaḥ yaḥ dharmaḥ saḥ eva bhāvaḥ saḥ asya asti iti tad dharma bhāvī etat uktam bhavati sādhana dharma bhāva prayukta sādhya dharma bhāva jñāpana dṛṣṭanta vacanam anvaya udāharaṇam iti yathā yat utpatti dharmakam tat sarvam anityam yathā ghaṭaḥ iti 
NTD_1.1.37–1.1.38	 tad viparyayāt viparītam sādhya dharma abhāva prayukta sādhana dharma abhāva jñāpaka dṛṣṭānta vacanam vyatireka udāharaṇam iti anena pratipādyate iti arthaḥ yathā yat nirātmakam tat sarvam aprāṇādimat dṛṣṭam yathā loṣṭa ādiḥ iti udāharaṇa apekṣaḥ tathā iti upasaṃhāraḥ na tathā iti vā sādhyasya upanayaḥ udāharaṇa apekṣaḥ sādhyasya vyāpti hetumat tayā upasaṃhāraḥ upanayaḥ iti sāmānya lakṣaṇam tathā na tathā iti sāmānya lakṣaṇa apekṣeṇa iti arthaḥ svasya iva parasya api parāmarśa jñāna utpādana artham upanaya vacanam anyathā prathama liṅga darśana dvitīya liṅga darśana saṃbandha smṛtīnām paraspara vārtā anabhijña tvena eka kārya karaṇa tva ayogāt iti tathā ca utpatti dharmakaḥ śabdaḥ iti anvaya upanayasya udāharaṇam tathā aprāṇādimat na bhavati jīvat śarīram iti vyatirekasya iti 
NTD_1.1.39	 hetu apadeśāt pratijñāyāḥ punarvacanam nigamanam hetu apadeśāt sa hetukam pratijñāyāḥ punarvacanam nigamanam iti sūtra arthaḥ tasmāt utpatti dharmaka tvāt anityaḥ śabdaḥ iti yasya pūrvam sādhya tvam tasya eva siddha tvam idānīm iti avasthā dvayavantam etam āśritya punarvacanam boddhavyam anyathā nigamanasya avayava antara tva abhāva prasaṅga āditya bādhita viṣaya tva asat pratipakṣa tva lakṣaṇa rūpa dvaya samarthanam na syāt iti 
NTD_1.1.40–1.1.41	 avijñāyam āna tatve arthe kāraṇa upapatti tastatva jñāna artham ūhaḥ tarkaḥ avijñāyamāna tattve arthe kāraṇa upapattitaḥ sambhavati asmin= arthe pramāṇam iti saṃbhāvanā dvāreṇa tattva jñāna artham yaḥ ūhaḥ pravartate sa tarkaḥ na punar ūha mātram iti sūtra arthaḥ udāharaṇam tu yadi atra tadānīm upalabhyeta na ca upalabhyate tasmāt na astitayā bhavitavyam saḥ ayam tarkaḥ pramāṇa viṣaya vivecanāt pramāṇa anugāhakaḥ na punar svayam pramāṇam aniścāyaka tvāt na ca praṣṭavyam kim pramāṇa anugraheṇa ayam eva niścāyakaḥ kasmāt na bhavati iti sāmpratam tasya prasaṅga tayā pāratantryeṇa svayam abādhaḥ dyamāna tvayoḥ vyāpti lakṣaṇam punar prasaṅga hetuḥ sattvam tad upalabdhiḥ vā tasmāt na pramāṇam pramāṇa anugrāhakaḥ tu bhavati iti vimṛśya pakṣa pratipakṣābhyām artha avadhāraṇam nirṇayaḥ vimṛśya sandeham kṛtvā pakṣa pratipakṣābhyām yat anyatara pakṣe artha avadhāraṇam bhavati sa nirṇayaḥ iti parīkṣā viṣayasya nirṇayasya idam lakṣaṇam na punar nirṇaya mātrasya pratyakṣa ādi pramāṇa phalasya tasya nyāya pravṛtti anaṅga tvāt iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_1.2.1^1	 pramāṇa tarka sādhana upālambhaḥ siddhānta aniruddhaḥ pañca avayava upapannaḥ pakṣa pratipakṣa parigrahaḥ vādaḥ nānā pravaktṛkā vicāra viṣayā vākya saṃdṛbdhiḥ kathā iti sāmānya lakṣaṇa sūcana dvāreṇa vādasya viśeṣa lakṣaṇam anena pratipādyate tathā hi vastu viśeṣau= eka adhikaraṇau viruddhau= eka tattva anavasitau pakṣa pratipakṣau tayoḥ parigrahaḥ itthaṃbhāva niyamaḥ evaṃdharmāḥ ayam dharmaḥ na eva dharma iti sa ca ayam vādaḥ kiṃviśiṣṭaḥ pramāṇa tarka sādhana upālambhaḥ pramāṇa mūlaiḥ eva avayavaiḥ tarkeṇa ca sādhanaḥ ca upālambhaḥ ca asmin kriyate iti tathā uktaḥ ābhiprāyikam pramāṇa mūla tvam veditavyam 
NTD_1.2.1^2	 tat evaṃlakṣaṇake vāde tattva nirṇaya phalake upālambha grahaṇāt sarvam nigraha sthānam prāpnoti iti niyata nigraha sthāna svīkāra artham siddhānta aviruddhaḥ pañca avayava upapannaḥ iti pada dvayam katham siddhānta aviruddhaḥ iti apasiddhānta aviruddhaḥ iti apasiddhānta svīkāraḥ pañca grahaṇāt nyūna adhikayoḥ avayava grahaṇāt tad ābhāsānām iti etat uktam bhavati vastu viśeṣayoḥ eka adhikaraṇayoḥ viruddhayoḥ eka kāle anavasthitayoḥ parigraha vacanam vādi prativādi abhiprāya kalpita prāmāṇya yukta pramāṇa mūla avayavaiḥ tarkeṇa ca sva pakṣa sādhana yuktam tathābhūtaiḥ ava yavaiḥ tarkeṇa nyūna adhika apa siddhānta avayava ābhāsa vilakṣaṇaiḥ pratipakṣa sādhana dūṣaṇa upetam kathā sāmānya lakṣaṇena viśeṣitam vādaḥ iti 
NTD_1.2.2–1.2.3	 yathā ukta upapannaḥ chala jāti nigraha sthāna sādhana upālambhaḥ jalpaḥ yathā ukta upapannaḥ iti artha labhya abhiprāya nigraha sthāna niyama lakṣya pada vyatiriktaḥ anya vāda lakṣaṇa upapannaḥ yaḥ sa jalpaḥ jāti nigraha sthānaiḥ api sādhanam sādhanasya upālambhaḥ ca asmin bhavati iti tathā uktaḥ saḥ ayam evaṃbhūtaḥ pakṣa pratipakṣa parigrahaḥ jalpaḥ iti sa pratipakṣa sthāpanā hīnaḥ vitaṇḍā sati prathame pakṣe dvitīya pakṣasya pratipakṣa tvam saṃbhavati iti pratipakṣa śabdena dvitīya pakṣaḥ ucyate tathā sati saḥ eva jalpaḥ yadā pratipakṣa sthāpanā hīnaḥ bhavati tadā vitaṇḍa iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_1.2.4	 savyabhicāra viruddha prakaraṇa sama sādhya sama atīta kālāḥ hetvābhāsāḥ anya liṅga dharma anuvidhānena pravartamānāḥ ahetavaḥ santaḥ hetu vat avabhāsamānāḥ hetvābhāsāḥ iti sāmānya lakṣaṇa sūcana dvāreṇa hetvābhāsānām vibhāga uddeśa artham sūtram anekadhā pravṛttaḥ api hetvābhāsa bhedaḥ savyabhicāra ādi rūpeṇa pañcadhā bhavati prastāraḥ tu vārtike 
NTD_1.2.5	 anaikāntikaḥ savya cicāraḥ ekasmin= ante niyataḥ aikāntikaḥ tad viparyayāt anaikāntikaḥ anvayena vyatirekeṇa vā yaḥ sa pakṣa vipakṣa gāmī sa savyabhicāraḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ yathā nityaḥ śabdaḥ prameya tvāt iti anvayena ubhaya pakṣa gāminā yasmāt prayeya tvasya anvayaḥ sa pakṣe gagana ādau vipakṣe ghaṭa ādau= api asti atas sa pakṣa vipakṣa gāmī anvaya tvāt sādhāraṇa anaikāntikaḥ bhavati tathā nityaḥ śabdaḥ sāmānyavat tve sati śrāvaṇa tvāt iti vyatirekeṇa ubhaya pakṣa gāminaḥ asya api vyatirekaḥ sa pakṣe ghaṭa ādau ca asti atas sa pakṣa vipakṣa vṛtti vyatireka tvāt asau= asādhāraṇā anaikāntikaḥ bhavati iti 
NTD_1.2.6	 siddhāntam abhyupetya tad virodhī viruddhaḥ savyabhicāra lakṣaṇa anākrānta tve sati abhyupagata artham viruṇaddhi viruddhyate vā yena saḥ ayam viruddhaḥ hetvābhāse iti sūtra arthaḥ yathā nityaḥ śabdaḥ utpatti dharmaka tvāt gagana vat iti atra nitaya tvasya sādhya dharmasya utpatti dharmaka tvena sādhana dharmeṇa saha vyāptau jijñāsitāyām nitya tva viparīta dharmeṇa anitya tvena vyāptasya utpatti dharmaka tvasya prathamam pratīta tvāt tena nitya tvam nitya tvena vā tat viruddham iti bhavati eva viruddhaḥ hetvābhāse iti vikāraḥ śabdaḥ vyakteḥ ātma lābhāt apaiti naśyati nāśi tvāt ca utpattimān tat nitya tva pratijñāne vyakteḥ apetasya api astitvam abhyupeyate tat idam nitya tvam utpatti dharmā viruṇaddhi iti bhāṣya gama nika avakṣiptam 
NTD_1.2.7	 yasmāt prakaraṇa cintā sa nirṇaya artham apadiṣṭaḥ prakaraṇa samaḥ yasmāt tattva anupalabdhi lakṣaṇāt viśeṣa adarśanāt arthāt prakaraṇa cintā prakriyamāṇasya arthasya cintā vimarśāt prabhṛti yāvar nniṇayam prastuta artha nirūpaṇam pravartate saḥ eva viśeṣa adarśana lakṣaṇaḥ arthaḥ yadi ekatas nirṇayāya apadiśyate tadā pratipakṣe api samāna tvāt prakaraṇa samaḥ bhavati sa pratipakṣaḥ hetuḥ prakaraṇa samaḥ iti tātparya arthaḥ yathā nityaḥ śabdaḥ anupalabhyamāna anitya dharmaka tvāt gagana vat iti atra yadā prativādī anitya tva viśeṣa anupalabdhi vat nitya tva viśeṣa anupalabdhiḥ api asti iti anityaḥ śabdaḥ anupalabhyamāna nitya dharmaka tvāt ghaṭa vat iti pratyavatiṣṭhate tadā prathamasya sādhanasya sat pratipakṣa tayā prakaraṇa sama tvam dvitīyasya tu prathama sādhana sat pratipakṣatā rūpa prakaṭana artha tvāt na idam dūṣaṇam api tu dūṣaṇa antara m ūhanīyam iti na prakaraṇa samasya udāharaṇam bhavati iti 
NTD_1.2.8–1.2.9	 sādhya aviśiṣṭaḥ sādhya tvāt sādhya samaḥ sādhyena aviśiṣṭaḥ yaḥ sādhana dharmā saḥ ayam asiddha tvāt sādhya samaḥ hetvābhāse iti yathā dravyam chāyā gatima tvāt iti kāla atyaya apadiṣṭaḥ kāla atītaḥ hetu apadeśasya sandeha viśiṣṭaḥ kālaḥ yaḥ punar pratyakṣa ādinā pramāṇena viparīta nirṇaye sati sādhya sandeha viśiṣṭam kālam atipatati saḥ ayam kālasya atyaye apadiśyamānaḥ kāla atītaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ yathā anuṣṇaḥ agniḥ avayavī kṛtaka tvāt ityādi atra hi anuṣṇa tva kṛtaka tvayoḥ vyāpti grahaṇa artham uṣṇa tvam kvacid dharmiṇi dṛṣṭam pratiṣeddhavyam anyathā anuṣṇa tvasya uṣṇa pratiṣedha ātmakasya eva apratīteḥ naca etat uṣṇa tvam tejaḥ avayavi vyatirikte dharmiṇi dṛṣṭam iṣṭam vā atas prathamam viparīta artha niścaye sati sa dviparīta artha niścayāya pravartamānam tad mūla pramāṇa apekṣam kṛtaka tva sādhanam sandigdha gharmiṇi nirdeśa lakṣaṇa hetu apadeśa kālasya atyayena apadiṣṭa tvāt kāla atītaḥ bhavati iti 
NTD_1.2.10–1.2.11	 vacana vighātaḥ artha avikalpa upapattyā cchalam artha vikalpa upapattyā ityarthasya vividhaḥ kalpaḥ vikalpaḥ tasya upapattiḥ saṃbhavaḥ tayā artha vikalpa upapattyā etat uktam bhavati sāmānya śabdasya aneka viśeṣa saṃbandhi tve sati avivakṣita artha adhyāropeṇa vacana vighātaḥ yaḥ kriyate tat chalam iti sūtra arthaḥ tat trividham vā akcchalam sāmānyacchalam upacāra= chalañca tat idam chalam deśa kāla avasthā bhedena anekadhā bhinnam api anena rūpeṇa trividham iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_1.2.12	 aviśeṣa abhihite arthe vaktuḥ abhiprāyāt artha antara kalpanā vākcchalam aviśeṣeṇa abhihite vākye pade vā vaktuḥ abhiprāyāt yad artha antaram kriyate pratiṣedha artham tad artha viṣaye tat vāc nimittam chalam vākchalam iti sūtra arthaḥ yathā navakambalaḥ ayam māṇavakaḥ iti atra nūtana kambala tvam vaktuḥ abhipretam vihāya kutas asya nava kambalāḥ iti saṃkhyā vivakṣayā pratiṣedhaḥ evam pade api boddhavyam aśvaḥ ityādau tat etat ayuktam ubhaya artha pratibhāsanam sambhavat artha parityāgena asambhavat artha kalpanāyāḥ ayogāt iti 
NTD_1.2.13	 sambhavataḥ arthasya ati sāmānya yogāt asat bhūta artha kalpanā sāmānyacchalam kenacid viśeṣaṇena viśiṣṭi tayā sambhavataḥ arthasya ati sāmānya yogāt tad viśeṣaṇa rahita vyakti vyāpi sāmānya yogāt asat bhūta artha kalpanayā avivakṣita hetu kalpanayā yaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ kriyate vākye tad sāmānya nimittam chalam sāmānya chalam iti sūtra arthaḥ aho nu khalu asau brāhmaṇaḥ catur veda abhijñaḥ iti ukte chalavādi āha na brāhmaṇa tvam catur veda abhijña tve hetuḥ vrātyena ana ekāntāt iti tat etat ayuktam avivakṣita hetuke vākye hetu ayogāt asya vākyasya brāhmaṇa praśaṃsā parasya viśiṣṭa brāhmaṇa viṣaya tāyāḥ abhipreta tvāt iti 
NTD_1.2.14	 dharma vikalpa nirdeśe artha sadbhāva pratiṣedhaḥ upacāracchalam dharmaḥ prayogaḥ tasya vikalpaḥ dvaividhyam guṇa pradhāna bhāvena nirdeśaḥ etat uktam bhavati guṇa pradhāna bhāvena loke śabda prayoge siddhe api gauṇa prayoge artha saṃbhavena yaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ tad upacāra viṣayam chalam upacāracchalam iti sūtra arthaḥ mañcāḥ krośanti iti ukte chalavādi āha na mañcāḥ krośanti kintu mañca sthāḥ puruṣāḥ iti na etat ayuktam ubhayathā api loke prayoga darśanāt iti 
NTD_1.2.15–1.2.16	 parīkṣā parvaṇaḥ sānnidhyāt tad artham ātmanaḥ sāmarthyam ālocayan sūtrakāraḥ chalam lakṣaṇa parvaṇi api parīkṣate vākchalam eva upacāra= chalam tat aviśeṣāt tasyāḥ artha antara kalpanāyāḥ aviśeṣāt tatra api artha antara kalpanam iha api artha antara kalpanam iti vāc chala upacāra= chalayoḥ nimitta bhūtasya artha antara kalpanā lakṣaṇasya arthasya ubhayatra aviśeṣāt eka tvāt vāc chalam eva upacāra= chalam na tasmāt vilakṣaṇam iti sūtra arthaḥ na tad artha antara bhātāt tasya upacāra= chala nimittasya artha sadbhāva pratiṣedhasya vāc chala nimittāt artha antara kalpanātaḥ artha antara bhāvāt dharma pratiṣedhāt dharmi pratiṣedhasya vilakṣaṇa tvāt tad aviśeṣāt iti pūrva sūtra uktam abheda sādhanam na yuktam iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_1.2.17	 aviśeṣeṇa kiñcid sādharmyāt eka chala tva prasaṅgaḥ yadi kiñcid sādharmyāt artha antara kalpanasya aviśeṣāt vāc chala upacāra= śalayoḥ eka tvena chala dvi tvam abhyanujñāyate tarhi tasmāt eva kiñcid sādharmyāt vacana vighāta ādi lakṣaṇāt kenacid nyāya vādī āha kim atra āścaryam saṃbhavati hi brāhmaṇe catur veda abhijña tvam iti atra sarvam chalam ekam prāpnototi chala dvi tvam abhyanujñātam yat tvayā tat nivartate iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_1.2.18–1.2.19	 sādharmya vaidharmyābhyām pratyavasthānam jātiḥ prayukte hetau tad ābhāse vā samīkaraṇa abhiprāyeṇa sādharmya vaidharmya mātrayoḥ anyatareṇa yat pratīpam avasthānam sā jātiḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ tat etat jāti sāmānya lakṣaṇam caturviṃśati prabheda bhinnāsu sarvāsu jātiṣu asti iti yathākathañcidūhanīyam yena kenacid sādharmyasya yena kena cit vaiṣamyasya vā sarvatra sambhāvyamāna tvāt vipratipattiḥ apratipattiḥ ca nigraha sthānam anyathā abhihitasya arthasya anyathāpratipattiḥ vipratipatiḥ sva para artha uttarā saṃvittirapratipattiḥ etat ubhayam nigraha sthānam parājaya nimitta tvāt parājaya nimittam khalu nigraha sthānam tad anayoḥ anyatarasmin paryavasyati iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_1.2.20	 tad vikalpāt jāti nigraha sthāna bahu tvam tasya sādharmya vaidharmyābhyām pratyavasthānasya vikalpāt tayoḥ vipratipatti apratipattyoḥ vikalpāt bahvyaḥ jātayaḥ bahuni nigraha sthānāni iti sūtra arthaḥ tad etat jāti nigraha sthāna vikalpānām bahūnām vivicya viśeṣa lakṣaṇa abhidhānam pañcame adhyāye bhaviṣyati iti na iha pratanyate yadi punar atra eva teṣām viśeṣa lakṣaṇam pravartate tadā śāstra pradhāna pratipādyasya ātma ādeḥ prameya jātasya uddeśa mātrāt upajātam tattva jñānam tirodhīyate atas eva ca tad vikalpāt jāti nigraha sthāna bahutvam iti sūtram api sa prayojanam tad vilamba pratipādana artha tvāt asya iti iti pramāṇa ādi padārtha sārtha nirddeśaḥ uddeśa purassaraḥ ayam samarthitaḥ saṃprati tad parīkṣā pracakṣmahe vārtika sūtra netrāḥ iti bhaṭṭa vāgīśvara viracitāyām nyāya sūtra tātparyadīpikāyām prathamaḥ adhyāyaḥ 
NTD_2.1.1	 tatra yathoddeśam yathālakṣaṇam parīkṣā iti pramāṇa lakṣaṇam eva prathamam parīkṣitum yuktam tathā api na tat prathamam parīkṣitam tasmāt avimṛśya pakṣa pratipakṣābhyām artha avadhāraṇam nirṇayaḥ iti ukta tayā samasta pramāṇa ādi padārtha sārtha parīkṣā para paryāyasya vicārasya vimarśa pūrvakatva niyamāt atas tat ullaṅghya vimarśa lakṣaṇam eva prathamam yuktam iti sūtrakāraḥ tad lakṣaṇam tāvat parīkṣate samāna aneka dharma adhyavasāyāt vā na saṃśayaḥ samāna dharma adhyavasāyāt aneka dharma adhyavasāyāt vā saṃśayaḥ na punar samāna dharma mātrāt aneka dharma mātrāt vā svādhyavasāya rahitāt kiñca anyatara dharmaḥ aneka dharmaḥ tad adhyavasāyāt na saṃśayaḥ aneka dharmasya avadhāraṇa hetu tvena tad darśanasya anyatara niścaya hetu tvāt iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.1.2–2.1.3	 vipratipatti avyavasthā adhyavasāyāt ca na vipratipatti mātrāt avyavasthā mātrāt vā saṃśayaḥ kintu vipratipattim avyavasthām ca upālabhamānasya iti sūtra arthaḥ vipratipattau ca saṃpratipatteḥ vipratipattau vipratipatti svarūpe yadi vipratipattiḥ iti anena ākāreṇa saṃpratipatteḥ sva rūpa virodhāt na vipratipattiḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.1.4–2.1.5	 avyavasthā ātmani vyavasthi tvāt ca avyavasthāyāḥ avyavasthā ātmani avyavasthā svarūpe yadi avyavasthā iti anena ākāreṇa vyavasthā syāt tarhi sva rūpa virodha at na avyavasthā syāt iti sūtra arthaḥ tathā atyanta saṃśayaḥ tad dharma sātatya upapatteḥ yadi samāna dharma ādibhyaḥ svādhyavasāya rahitebhyaḥ kāraṇebhyaḥ saṃśayaḥ syāt tadā teṣām samāna dharma ādīnām kāraṇānām sātatya upapatteḥ nityam saṃśayaḥ syāt iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.1.6^1	 tat etat sarvam saṃśaya lakṣaṇa satrū gata upapatti śabdasya upalabdhi paryāya tvam ajānānasya ca udyam iti draṣṭavyam tad paratve tu na etat dūṣaṇam iti anena abhiprāyeṇa parihāram āha yathā ukta adhyavasāyāt eva tad viśeṣa apekṣāt saṃśaye na asaṃśayaḥ atyanta saṃśayaḥ vā yadi nirviśeṣaṇam samāna dharma ādikam saṃśaya kāraṇam ucyate tatas pūrvam kāraṇāt paścāt api na kuryāt iti asaṃśayaḥ pūrvam vā kāraṇāt paścāt api kuryāt iti atyanta saṃśayaḥ na tu etat nirviśeṣaṇam saṃśaya kāraṇam api tu upalabdham sat viśeṣa smṛti ādi sahitam iti na asaṃśayaḥ na api atyanta saṃśayaḥ katham punar etat sūtra padeṣu upalabhyate viśeṣaṇa apekṣaḥ iti vacanāt sāmānyena upalabdhe viśeṣa apekṣā bhavati na punar atīva upalavdheḥ anupalabdheḥ vā atas viśeṣa apekṣaḥ iti vacanāt upapatti śabdena upalabdhiḥ sūtrakāreṇa vivakṣitā iti na kaścid virodhaḥ 
NTD_2.1.6^2–2.1.7	 yat punar anyatara dharmaḥ asādhāraṇa dharmaḥ tasya darśanāt anyatara avadhāraṇam bhavati iti etat api na asti iti asādhāraṇa dharmasya vyatireka mukhena na vyabhicāra tvena avyabhicāri viśeṣa rūpa tva abhāvāt yat ca uktam vipratipattau ca saṃpratipatteḥ avyavasthā ātmani vyavasthi tattvāt ca avyavasthāyāḥ iti tat ayuktam nimitta antarāt saṃjñā antara kāraṇena vastu tathā bhāvasya pratiṣeddhum aśakyatvāt viṣaya antara apekṣayā khalu iyam vipratipattiḥ avyavasthā ca na punar svarūpa apekṣayā saṃpratipattiḥ vyavasthā iti saṃjñā antara karaṇena viṣaya apekṣitayā aavasthitasya vipratipatti avyavasthā ātmakasya artha tathā bhāvasya pratiṣedhaḥ na yuktaḥ na ca avyavasthā pṛthak saṃśaya kāraṇam pūrvasmāt aviśeṣāt iti uktam tasmāt saṃśaya lakṣaṇam yathā uktam eva upapannam iti yatra saṃśayaḥ tatra evam uttarottara prasaṅgaḥ yatra yatra saṃśaya pūrvikā parīkṣā śāstre kathāyām vā tatra tatra pareṇa saṃśaye pratiṣiddhe api samādhāna hetubhiḥ ebhiḥ samādheyam punar ete samādhānataḥ etad lakṣaṇa niyatāḥ eva iti śiṣya śikṣā sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.1.8	 atha idānīm avasara prāptāni pramāṇāni parīkṣamāṇaḥ sāmānya lakṣaṇa pūrvaka tvāt viśeṣa lakṣaṇānām prathamam tāvat pramāṇa sāmānya lakṣaṇam parīkṣate pratyakṣa ādīnām aprāmāṇyam traikālya asiddheḥ pramiti sādhanam pramāṇam iti pramāṇa sāmānya lakṣaṇam tat idam pramiti sādhana tva lakṣaṇa prāmāṇyam pratyakṣa ādīnām na siddhyati kutas traikālya asiddheḥ tri kālasya bhāvaḥ traikālyam tatra asiddheḥ pramāṇa prameyayoḥ pūrva apara sahabhāva anupapattyā pratyakṣa ādīnām pramāṇānām pramiti sādhana tva ayogāt iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.1.9–2.1.10	 tatra jñāna prāmāṇya pakṣam avalambya prameyāt pūrvam pramāṇa siddhau doṣam āha pūrvam hi pramāṇa siddhau na indriya artha sannikarṣāt pratyakṣa upapattiḥ jñānam hi nāma pramāṇam tat yadi pūrvam prameyāt avadhāryamāṇāt arthāt ucyeta tatra pūrvam na asau prameya lakṣaṇa arthaḥ siddhaḥ iti indriya artha sannikarṣa utpannam iti pratyakṣa lakṣaṇa sūtra vyāghātaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ atha paścāt prameyāt pramāṇa siddhiḥ tatra api doṣam āha paścāt siddhau na pramāṇebhyaḥ prameya siddhiḥ prameya tvam nāma vastunaḥ sva rūpam pramāṇa saṃbandha nibandhanam tat ced pramāṇāt pūrvam siddham paścāt pramāṇa siddhiḥ tarhi pramāṇa yoga nibandhanam prameya tvam na syāt iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.1.11	 yugapad siddhau doṣam āha yugapad siddhau pratyartha niyata tvāt krama vṛtti tva abhāvaḥ buddhīnām rūpa rasa gandha sparśa ādayaḥ prameya bhūtāḥ arthāḥ yugapad kāla saṃbandhinaḥ dṛṣṭāḥ tad viṣayāṇi ca jñānāni taiḥ saha tasmin= eva kāle yadā siddhāni tadā yugapad jñānānutpattiḥ manasaḥ liṅgāma iti sūtra vyāghātaḥ cakṣuḥ ādibhiḥ krameṇa utpadyamānānām teṣām dṛṣṭa vyāghātaḥ ca iti sūtra artha jñāna prāmāṇya nirūpaṇa adhīna nirūpaṇa tvāt indriya ādi prāmāṇyānām tad prāmāṇya dūṣaṇa vaśāt eva teṣām api prāmāṇya dūṣaṇam bhavati iti na pṛthakkṛtya sūtreṇa dūṣaṇam uktam iti boddhavyam tat anena sūtra catuṣṭayena saṃkṣepa vistarābhyām pratyakṣa ādīni na eva pramāṇa tvena vyavahartavyāni kāla traye api arthāpatti pratipādaka tvāt yat evaṃvidham tat pramāṇa tvena na vyavahriyate yathā śaśa viṣāṇam tathā ca etāni tasmāt tathā iti para abhyupagata pramāṇānām paraspara virodhena yat vilayanam uktam mādhyamikena tad upanyastam veditavyam 
NTD_2.1.12	 traikālya asiddheḥ pratiṣedha anupapattiḥ pratyakṣa ādīnām aprāmāṇyam traikālya āsiddheḥ iti pramāṇa pratiṣedham kurvat mādhyamikaḥ praṣṭāyaḥ ayam khalu pratiṣedhaḥ kim pratiṣedhyāt pūrvam paścāt saha vā iti yatra yadi pūrvam tadānīm asati pratiṣedhye kim anena pratiṣiddhyeta atha paścāt pratiṣedhaḥ na tarhi pratiṣedha adhīnā pratiṣedhya siddhiḥ tad vyatirekeṇa pratiṣedhyasya prathamam eva siddha tvāt atha yugapad pratiṣedhya pratiṣedhayoḥ siddhiḥ tadā pratiṣedhyasya prāmāṇyasya sadbhāva abhyanujñānāt anarthakaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ tat evam sva vacana virodhena sva pratipādita anumānasya ātma lābha abhāvāt pratyakṣa ādīnām prāmāṇyam iti sūtra artha 
NTD_2.1.13	 sarva pramāṇa tiṣedhāt ca pratiṣedha anupapattiḥ pratyakṣa ādīni na pramāṇa tvena vyavahartavyāni ityādi pratiṣedha lakṣaṇe vākye vākya aṅga bhūtāni udāharaṇa ādīni pareṇa upādīyante na vā yadi upādīyeran tadā udāharaṇa ādi viṣayaiḥ sarvaiḥ pramāṇaiḥ vipratiṣedhāt virodhāt bādhita tvāt anupapannaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ atha na upādīyeran tadā udāharaṇa ādi rahita tvena asiddha vyāpti kalpaka tvāt anumānasya anarthakaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ abhimata artha asiddheḥ iti sūtrāthaḥ 
NTD_2.1.14	 tad prāmāṇye vā na sarva pramāṇa viprāteṣedhaḥ atha abhimata artha siddhi artham teṣām pratiṣedha vākya avayava āśritānām pramāṇānām prāmāṇyam abhyanujñāyeta tadā na sarva pramāṇa vipratiṣedhaḥ keṣāñcid tad pratiṣedha vākya avayava an āśritānām pratiṣedhaḥ tad āśrita anāñca na pratiṣedhaḥ prāmāṇya abhyanujñā iti pakṣapātaḥ mādhyanikasya syāt iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.1.15	 traikālya apratiṣedhaḥ ca śabdāt ātodya siddhi vat tad siddheḥ kāla traya artha apratipādaka tvāt iti hetoḥ asiddha todbhāvanam asya arthaḥ tathā hi pūrvam siddham ātodyam paścāt tad utthena śabdena yathā anumīyate vīṇā vādyate veṇuḥ pūryate iti yathā vā pūrvam siddhena sāvitra prakāśena paścāt avirodha utpannam vastra ādi vastu gṛhyate yathā vā saha siddhau vahniḥ saha siddhena dhūmena anumīyate tathā kvacid pūrvam siddhena pramāṇena prameyam avadhāryate kvacid paścāt siddhena kvacid yugapad siddhena iti siddham pratyakṣa ādīnām kāla traye api aniyamena artha pramiti sādhana tvam kutas pramāṇa tva sāmānyasya aneka vyakti niṣṭha tvena kadācid kasyāścid vyakte tad sādhana tva sambha vāt asādhāraṇa svarūpa yogya tā mātra vaśāt eva pācaka ādi śabda vat pramāṇa prameya śabdayoḥ lokataḥ eva akuvardavasthāyām api pravṛtti siddheḥ na indriya artha sannikarṣa utpannam iti ādi sūtra virodhaḥ tathā eva prayoga darśanāt iti 
NTD_2.1.16^1	 saṃprati prakāra antareṇa sāmaṇyam ākṣipya samādhīyate tathā hi pratyakṣa ādīnām pramāṇānām upalabdhiḥ asti vā na vā yadi na asti tadā sva upalabdhi rahitaiḥ pratyakṣa ādibhiḥ pramāṇaiḥ yathā saṃvyavahāra siddhiḥ tathā sva upalabdhi rahitaiḥ eva ghaṭa śakaṭa ādibhiḥ prameyaiḥ saṃvyavahāra siddheḥ tad siddhi sādhanānām pramāṇānām abhāva prasaṅgaḥ atha upalabdhiḥ asti tadā upalabdhi viṣaya tvāt prameya tvam upalabdhi sādhana tvāt pramāṇa tvam iti aniyata aneka rūpa saṃbandhi tvena asattva prasaṅgaḥ yat uktam tat aniyatam tat aparama artha sat yathā rajjvām āropitam sarpa tvam tathā ca pramāṇa prameya bhāvaḥ tasmāt asat iti tatra upalabdhiḥ na asti iti pakṣa svīkāra abhāvāt eva pratikṣiptiḥ 
NTD_2.1.16^2	 pakṣa antare aniyata aneka rūpa saṃbandhi tvena asattva prasaṅgaḥ iti uktam iti ced tatra āha prameyā ca tulā prāmāṇya vat guru tva parimāṇa jñāna sādhanam tulā dravyam pramāṇam suvarṇa ādīnām tulā antara paricchinna parimāṇena dravyeṇa yadā pramīyate tadā prameyam kṣaṇa bhaṅga pariṇāma nirāse sati sva rūpeṇa avasthitasya padārthasya tad tad dharma yogena tad rūpeṇa parama artha sattve sati virodha abhāvāt yathā sva prāmāṇye prameyā ca tulā tathā sarvam api pramāṇa jātam sva prāmāṇye prameyam vastu antara paricchede tu pramāṇam iti na kālpanika tvena rajjvām āropita sarpa tvat asattva prasaṅgaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.1.17	 nanu pratyakṣa ādīnām upalabdhiḥ asti iti uktam sā iyam upalabdhiḥ sa sādhanā niḥsādhanāḥ vā yadā sa sādhanā tadā pratyakṣa ādi janyā pramāṇa antara janyā vā yadā pratyakṣa ādi janyā tadā yā ekā vyaktiḥ tayā eva kim vyakti antareṇa iti tatra tayā eva vyaktyā iti pakṣaḥ sva ātmani vṛtti virodhāt eva dūṣitaḥ pakṣa antare doṣam āha pramāṇataḥ siddheḥ pramāṇānām pramāṇa antara siddhi prasaṅgaḥ pratyakṣa ādi vyatirikta pramāṇa antara svīkāra pakṣe vibhāga sūtra vyāghātaḥ anavasthā pātaḥ ca anyatama vyakti antara grahaṇa pakṣe tu anavasthā pātaḥ eva iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.1.18	 niḥsādhana pakṣe tu doṣam āha tad vinivṛtteḥ vā pramāṇa siddhi vat prameya siddhiḥ tasya pratyakṣa ādi pramāṇa viṣaya pratipatti sādhanasya nivṛtte nivartanāt pramāṇa siddhi vat prameya siddhiḥ yathā pratyakṣa ādi pramāṇa viṣayā siddhiḥ upalabdhiḥ niḥsādhanā tathā ghaṭa śakaṭa ādi prameya viṣayā siddhiḥ api niḥsādhanā bhaviṣyati iti pramāṇa mātra abhāva prasaṅgaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.1.19^1	 tat etat sūtra dvaya upaḍhaukitam pūrva pakṣam pratikṣipan artha bhedam āha na pradīpa prakāśa siddhi vat tad siddheḥ yathā dīpa prakāśaḥ pramāṇa avayavaḥ sanścakṣuḥ ādinā pratyakṣa viśeṣeṇa kadācid gṛhyate kadācid āpta upadeśena kadācid māna antareṇa na ca pratyakṣa ādi vyatirikta pramāṇa antareṇa vā pramāṇam na tayā eva vyaktyā vā tathā anyeṣām api pratyakṣa ādīnām pramāṇānām pratyakṣa ādi pramāṇa madhya vartinā vyakti antareṇa vyakti antarasya grahaṇe na vibhāga sūtra vyāghātaḥ na api anavasthāpātaḥ na ca niḥsādhanā pramāṇa upalabdhiḥ iti na ca sva jñānena eva sarvatra pramāṇānām sva kārya kāraṇa tvam cakṣuḥ ādiṣu adarśanāt 
NTD_2.1.19^2	 sva jñānena eva sva kāryam kurvatām dhūma ādīnām api cakṣuḥ ādiṣu niṣṭhālābhena anavasthāpātaḥ na ca prāmāṇya jñāna purassarā pravṛttiḥ pravartamānasya phala prāptyā paścāt prāmāṇya viniścaya saṃbhavāt abhyāsa daśa āpanneṣu tad jātīya tva liṅgena jhaṭiti prāmāṇya viniścaya vaśāt eva pravṛtti siddheḥ tad jātīya tva liṅga grāhiṇaḥ api jñānasya abhyāsa anabhyāsa daśa āpanna vijñāna varga dvaya madhya varti tvena bīja aṅkura vat uktena nyāyena kāla bhedena prāmāṇya grahaṇe sati anādi tvena anavasthā bhāvāt sarvatra saṃśayam āpādayataḥ tad hetu niścaya abhāvena tasya eva abhāva prasaṅgāt tasmāt pramāṇa sāmānyam asti iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.1.20^1	 nanu yathā pradīpa prakāśaḥ pradīpa antaram antareṇa gṛhyate tathā pramāṇāni api pramāṇa antaram antareṇa grahīṣyante iti ayam arthaḥ pūrva sūṇā atra ibhihitaḥ iti vyākhyānam kasmāt na iṣyate iti āśaṅkya āha kvacid nivṛtti darśanāt ani vṛtti darśanāt ca kvacid anekāntaḥ kvacid pradīpa antare grāhye grāhakasya pradīpasya nivṛtti darśanāt kvacid ghaṭa ādau grāhye tasya eva grāhakasya anivṛtti darśanāt pradīpa vyatirekeṇa gṛhyamāṇa pradīpa antaravāt pramāṇa vyatirekeṇa api pramāṇāni grahīṣyante pradīpa pramāṇayaḥ grāhya tva aviśeṣāt iti ayam hetuḥ anekāntaḥ kim kāraṇam pradīpa dṛṣṭāntaḥ eva grāhyaḥ na ghaṭa dṛṣṭāntaḥ iti viśeṣa hetu abhāvāt atha pradīpa dṛṣṭāntasya pramāṇa vat prakāśaka tvāt tat eva viśeṣa hetuḥ tat dṛṣṭāntaḥ iti ced tathā hi prakāśaḥ san pradīpa prakāśaka antara nirapekṣaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ sva prakāśena prakāśyaḥ na ghaṭaḥ īdṛśaḥ iti 
NTD_2.1.20^2	 tat ayuktam tasya api prakāśakasya sataḥ pradīpasya sva prakāśe cakṣuḥ ādi prakāśaka antara sāpekṣa tvāt samāna jātīya prakāśaka pradīpa antara nirapekṣa tvam iha vivakṣitam na punar prakāśa mātra nirapekṣa tvam iti ced tat api asāram vikalpa anupapatteḥ tathā hi kim atyanta sajātīya nivṛttiḥ pradīpe kathañcid samāna jātīya nivṛttiḥ vā yadi atyanta samāna jātīya nivṛttiḥ sā tarhi asti eva jñāne api ghaṭa viṣaya jñānasya ghaṭa viṣaya jñāna antaram antareṇa gṛhyamāṇa tvāt kena tarhi gṛhyate iti ced ghaṭa viṣaya jñānam ghaṭa viṣaya jñāna viṣaya jñānena iti brūmaḥ atha kathañcid samāna jātīya nivṛttiḥ iti yaḥ kalpaḥ saḥ api anumitaḥ taijasa tva ādinā kathañcid samāna jātīyena cakṣuḥ ādinā grāhya tvāt tasmāt viśeṣa hetu abhāvāt grāhya tva aviśeṣāt pradīpa vat pramāṇāni pramāṇa antara nirapekṣāṇi iti ācārya eka deśīyānām vyākhyānam api apavyākhyānam iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.1.21	 kathañcid samāna jātīyena cakṣuḥ ādinā gṛhyamāṇa pradīpa vat prāmāṇyāni api kathañcid samāna jātīyena ca pramāṇa antareṇa grahīṣyante iti asmadīya vyākhyāne viśeṣa hetu parigrahasya vidyamāna tvāt na ayam abhipreta doṣaḥ iti āha upasaṃhāra abhyanujñānāt apratiṣedhaḥ taijasa tva ādinā kathañcid samāna jātīyena cakṣuḥ ādinā pradīpaḥ gṛhyate iti viśeṣa hetu parigraheṇa sva pakṣe pradīpa dṛṣṭāntasya upasaṃhārasya abhyanujñānāt abhyupagamāt pratiṣedhaḥ na saṃbhavati iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.1.22	 atha idānīm pramāṇa viśeṣam parīkṣamāṇaḥ pratyakṣasya prādhānyena prathamam uddiṣṭa tvāt tad lakṣaṇam tāvat parīkṣyate pratyakṣa lakṣaṇa anupapattiḥ asamagra vacanāt tatra indriya artha sannikarṣa utpannam iti sūtreṇa pratyakṣa lakṣaṇam vā ucyate pratyakṣa kāraṇam vā na tāvat lakṣaṇam indriya artha sannikarṣa utpannam iti asya kāraṇa apadeśa tvāt na hi kāraṇa apadeśaḥ lakṣaṇam bhavati na khalu mṛd daṇḍa cakra sūtra ādayaḥ kāraṇam ghaṭasya iti ukte ghaṭaḥ upalakṣitaḥ bhavati tasmāt na yuktaḥ lakṣaṇa pakṣaḥ atha kāraṇam anena ucyate tat api ayuktam alakṣaṇa tvāt kāraṇa apadeśasya na hi kāraṇa apadeśaḥ lakṣaṇam bhavati iti uktam eva bhavatu kāraṇa pakṣa āśrayaṇam tathā api ayuktam asamagra vacana tvāt santi ca anyāni api kāraṇāni pratyakṣa jñānasya nahi indriya artha sannikarṣa mātrāt pratyakṣa jñānam jāyate api tu āloka ādibhiḥ api iti tasmāt pratyakṣa lakṣaṇasya vā kāraṇasya vā anupapattiḥ pratyakṣa lakṣaṇa anupapattiḥ lakṣaṇa pakṣe kāraṇa pakṣe ca ubhayatra tasya sūtrasya asamaya vacana tvāt iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.1.23	 nanu kāraṇa pakṣe asamagra vacana tvam asiddham iti ced tatra āha na ātma manasoḥ sannikarṣa abhāve pratyakṣa utpattiḥ jñānam hi nāma saṃyoga jaḥ guṇaḥ na asaṃyukte dravye saṃyoga jasya guṇasya utpattiḥ iti ātma manaḥ saṃyogaḥ kāraṇam ananyathā siddha anvaya vyatireka tvāt tathā hi śarīra saṃbandhāt ātma pradeśe manaḥ saṃyoge sati jñānam jāyate asati tu tasmin na jāyate iti tathā indriya manaḥ saṃyoga abhāve jñānam na jāyate sati tu tasmin jāyate iti tasya api anvaya vyatirekavat tvena kāraṇa tvam anyathā yugapad jñāna utpatti prasaṅgāt tasmāt ātma manaḥ indriya artha sannikaṛṣayaḥ saṃyogayoḥ abhāvena pratyakṣa jñānasya utpattiḥ iti asamagra vacana tvam tatra siddham iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.1.24	 nanu ananyathā siddhārtha anvaya tvena kāraṇa tvam kim iti ucyate yāvatā sati bhāva mātreṇa kāraṇa tvam kim iti na iṣyate iti yeṣām pakṣaḥ teṣām mate doṣam āha diś deśa kāla ākāśeṣu api evam prasaṅgaḥ diś deśa kāla ākāśa ādīnām nitya vibhu tvābhyām saṃnnidhera varjanīya tve sati bhāva mātrasya vidyamāna tvāt teṣām api kāraṇa tva prasaṅgaḥ evam bhavati iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.1.25	 yat tāvat ātma manaḥ sannikarṣasya pratyakṣa lakṣaṇam sūtre pāṭhādasamagra vacana tvam kāraṇa pakṣe abhyadhāyi tatra parihāram āha jñāna liṅga tvāt ātmanaḥ na anavarodhaḥ jñāna liṅga tvam tāvat ātmanaḥ icchā ādi sūtre jñāna padāt sthitam tena hi jñāna padena abhidhīyamānam kāryam anitya tvāt kāryatve sati vibhu dravya samavāyāt guṇataḥ ca tasya ca guṇasya kārya bhūtasya yat upādānakāraṇam saḥ ātmā tad anyasya tad upādāna kāraṇatva asambhavāt tat evam ātma āśraya tve siddhe jñāna guṇasya saṃyoga ja tvāt saṃyoga antarasya ca asaṃbhavāt ātma manaḥ saṃyogaḥ eva kāraṇa tvena arthāt siddhaḥ bhavati siddhe punar ātma manaḥ saṃyoge tasya saṃyogasya jñāna kāraṇa bhūtasya pratyakṣa lakṣaṇa sūtre anavarodhaḥ iti etat na asti jñāna liṅga tvāt ātmanaḥ lakṣaṇa sūtra sthita jñāna pada mātrāt eva sarvasya padārthasya anabhidhāne api sāmarthya labhya tvāt iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.1.26	 nanu anabhidhīyamānam api yadi kāraṇa bhūta indriya ātma mana ssaṃyoga ādi jñāna pada sāmarthyāt labhyate tasmin indriya artha sannikarṣaḥ api na abhidhātavyaḥ jñāna pada sāmarthyāt eva labhyamāna tvāt iti āśaṅkya āha pratyakṣa nimitta ayaugapadya liṅga tva ucca na manasaḥ yat punar indriya manaḥ saṃyogasya anabhidhānena asamagra vacana tvam uktam tat api na asti kutas tad ayaugapadya liṅga tvāt tasya jñānasya uyaugapadyam yugapad anutpattiḥ tat liṅgam manaḥ yugapad jñāna anutpattiḥ manasaḥ liṅgam iti vacanāt tatas ca jñāna pada svīkāra sārthyāt eva indriya manaḥ saṃyoge api kāraṇa tvena tatra tat labhyate eva iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.1.27^1	 tattvāt ca indriya artha sannikarṣasya yasmāt indriya arthayoḥ saṃnikarṣaḥ pratyakṣasya eva nimittam na anyasya ātma manaḥ sannikarṣa ādi vat atas tasya abhidhānam kartavyam etat uktam bhavati kāraṇa pakṣe tat eva kāraṇam vaktavyam yat asādhāraṇa tvena pratyakṣa jñānam akhila m itarasmāt vyavacchinatti anyathā lakṣaṇa karaṇe pravṛttasya sūtrakārasya kāraṇa mātra kathanena aprastuta abhidhāyi tva prasaṅgāt anabhidhāne ca pratyakṣasya alakṣitattva āpatteḥ na ced daśama sādhāraṇa tvam ātma manaḥ saṃyogasya indriya manaḥ saṃyogasya āloka ādeḥ anyasya vā sambhavati ekasya sādhāraṇyāt itareṣām avyāpaka tvāt tasmāt indriya arthayoḥ sannikarṣaḥ sakala pratyakṣa vyāpi tvena lakṣaṇa tvāt abhidhātavyaḥ 
NTD_2.1.27^2	 kāraṇa pakṣe api iti etena indriya artha sannikarṣa utpannam iti asya kāraṇa apadeśa tvena alakṣaṇa tvāt lakṣaṇa pakṣa āśrayaṇam ayuktam iti yat uktam tat api nirastam bhavati nanu asādhāraṇa kāraṇa kathanam yadi lakṣaṇam saṃbhavati tarhi kāraṇa pakṣa avalambanam vyartham akāraṇasya api lakṣaṇa tvena vyavasthāpyamāna tvāt evam tathā api prauḍhi vādatayā tad sūtra kāreṇa kṛtam na tu parama siddhānta tvena iti boddhavyam yat khalu kāraṇam akāraṇam vā pratyakṣasya samāna asamāna vyavacchedakam bhavati tat eva vaktavyam na anyat tathā api kāraṇa mukhena tat uktam iti etāvān eva viśeṣaḥ iti abhisandhiḥ sūtrakārasya iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.1.28^1	 pratyakṣa jñāna kāraṇeṣu madhye lakṣaṇa artham indriya artha sannikarṣasya eva grahaṇam kāryam na ātma manaḥ saṃyoga ādeḥ kutas tasya eva prādhānyāt iti āha supta vyāsakta manasām ca indriya arthayoḥ sannikarṣa nimittattvāt suptānām vyāsakta manasā añca tīvra dhvani sparśa ādinā prabodha jñāne sahasā upasthita viṣaya antara vijñāne ca indriya artha sannikarṣasya prādhāna nimitta tvāt tasya eva grahaṇam kāryam na anyasya tathā hi yathā khalu ayam ardharātre mayā utthātavyam iti saṅkalpya suptaḥ tīvra dhvani sparśa vaśāt tasmin= eva ardharātre prabudhyate tadā tasya tīvra dhvani sparśa viṣayam prabodha jñānam upajāyamānam indriya artha sannikarṣāt eva upajāyate na ātma manaḥ saṅkalpābhyām tayoḥ tadānīma sambhavāt 
NTD_2.1.28^2	 tathā ca yadi kasmiścid viṣaya antare vyāsaktaḥ prayatna preritam manaindriya arthena saṃyojya viṣaya antaram jānānaḥ stimita tā jhaṭiti upasthāpita tīvra dhvani sparśa ādi viṣaya antara viṣayam vijñānam upajāyamānam na ātma manaḥ saṅkalpa prayatnābhyām jāyate kintarhi indriya artha sannikarṣāt eva tayoḥ anyatra vyāpṛta tvāt atas pratyakṣa jñāna kāraṇeṣu madhye indriya artha sannikarṣasya eva prādhānyam na anyasya nanu ātma manaḥ saṅkalpa prayatnayoḥ abhāve manasaḥ kriyā kāraṇa abhāvāt ātma manaḥ saṃyogasya apradhāna tvena api kāraṇa bhūtasya tadānīm asaṃbhavāt supta vyāsakta manasoḥ puruṣayoḥ utpadyamānam prabodha jñānam na utpadyeta satyam eva tathā api avasarpaṇa upasarpaṇa nyāyena adṛṣṭa vaśāt utpanna kriyam manaḥ ātmanā saṃyujyate tena ca ātma manaḥ saṃyogena saha kṛtaḥ indriya artha sannikarṣaḥ prādhānyena prabodha jñānam janayati iti adoṣaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.1.29–2.1.30	 itas api prādhānyam iti āha taiḥ ca apadeśaḥ jñāna viśeṣāṇām yeṣu ayam indriya artha sannikarṣaḥ taiḥ indriḥ arthaiḥ ca apadeśaḥ jñāna viśeṣāṇām gandha vijñānam rūpa vijñānam rasa vijñānam ghrāṇa vijñānam cakṣruḥ vijñānam ityādi na punar evam anyatra ātma ādiṣu vyapedeśaḥ tasmāt asya eva prādhānyam iti sūtra arthaḥ indriya artha sannikarṣasya prādhāṇya kathanena anyasya anyasya kāraṇa tvam uktam iti manyamānaḥ codayati vyāhata tvāt ahetuḥ indriya artha sannikarṣa mātrāt eva yadā pratyakṣa jñānam jāyate tadā vyāhatam bhavati kasmāt ātma manaḥ saṃyoga ādiṣu satsu pratyakṣa jñāna utpatteḥ asaṃbhavāt tasmāt sūtra tritayena anyeṣām akāraṇa tve yaḥ hetuḥ uktaḥ na sa yuktaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.1.31	 pariharati na artha viśeṣa prābalyāt artha viśeṣaḥ tīvra dhvani sparśa ādiḥ tena prābalyam prādhānyam indriya artha sannikarṣasya tasmāt artha viśeṣa prābalyāt etat uktam bhavati na mayā ātma manaḥ saṃyoga ādeḥ pratyakṣa kāraṇa tvam pratiṣidhyate kim tarhi indriya artha sannikarṣasya anantara ukta nyāyena prādhānyāt pratyakṣa sūtre samāna asamāna jātīyasya vyavaccheda artham upādānam kṛtam iti atas vyāhata tvāt ahetuḥ iti yat uktam tat na yuktam iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.1.32	 idānīm lakṣya asambhava mukhena lakṣaṇam dūṣayitum āha pratyakṣam anumānam eka deśa grahaṇāt upalabdheḥ yat indriya artha sannikarṣāt utpadyate jñānam ayam vṛkṣaḥ iti etat kila pratyakṣam tattva numānam eva kasmāt eka deśa grahaṇāt upalabdheḥ eka deśam avayavam gṛhītvā tena tad sahacaritāni eka deśa antarāṇi anumāya paścāt pratisandhānena vṛkṣaḥ iti upalabhate yathā āsandikā eka deśam dṛṣṭvā tadā eka deśa antaram anuminoti etat uktam bhavati na tāvat avayavī nāma kaścid asti padārthaḥ tad sadbhāve pramāṇa abhāvāt api tu avayavāḥ eva parama artha santaḥ kathañcid saṅgatāḥ teṣu katipayān avayavān gṛhītvā tad sahacarita avayavān anumāya pratisandhāna jeyam vṛkṣa buddhiḥ tān eva avayava anālambamāna anumānam iti pratyakṣasya anumāne a ntarbhāvena pṛthak lakṣya asaṃbhavāt vibhāga sūtre nyūnadhika saṃkhyā vyavacchedaḥ tad lakṣaṇa kathanañcā iti dvitayam anupapannam iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.1.33	 lakṣya asaṃbhavāt pratyakṣasya yat idam anumāne antar bhāva kathanam tat na saṃbhavati iti āha na pratyakṣeṇa yāvat tāvat api upalambhāt pratyakṣam anumānam eka deśa grahuṇāt iti atra sūtre yāvat eka deśasya grahaṇam avayava antara anumāna artham aṅgīkriyate tāvat eka deśasya grahaṇam pratyakṣeṇa svīkriyate na vā yadi svīkriyate tarhi tāvataḥ pratyakṣa tvena lakṣya siddheḥ viruddhaḥ hetuḥ kim kāraṇam na pratyakṣeṇa yāvat tāvat api upalambhāt yāvantam eka deśam gṛhītvā yam eka deśam eka deśa antaram vai eka deśa tvāt pūrva upalabdha eka deśa vat iti anuminoti tā= ataḥ anumāpakasya eka deśasya pratyakṣeṇa upalambhāt atha na svīkriyate tarhi asiddhaḥ hetuḥ anumāpakasya eka deśasya agrahaṇāt āsandikā aṅge ca ukta doṣasya samāna tvāt iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.1.34	 nanu gṛhyamāṇasya anumānaḥ grahaṇam mā bhūt pratyakṣeṇa anumānena māna antareṇa vā bhavatu kaḥ doṣaḥ iti ced tatra āha na anumāna prasaṅgaḥ tad pūrvaka tvāt anyathā api ca pratyakṣasya na anumāna tva prasaṅgaḥ kutas tat pūrvaka tvātaḥ pratyakṣam pūrvam yasya tat idam tat pūrvakam tasya bhāvaḥ tad pūrvaka tvam tasmāt tad pūrvaka tvāt iti anumāna prasaṅgaḥ iti upalakṣaṇam prasaṅgaḥ iti api draṣṭavyam samāna nyāya tvāt etat uktam bhavati na tāvat anumānasya anumāna antareṇa tena eva vā anumānena tad vyāpti grahaṇam sambhavati ekatra anavasthā pātāditara tra itara itara āśraya tva prasaṅgāt atas su dūram api gatvā liṅga liṅgi saṃbandha darśanam dvitīya liṅgi darśanam ca adyāt pratyakṣate iti vaktavyam tathā ca sati tad viṣayasya pratyakṣasya lakṣya tvena siddheḥ viruddham tad avastham eva iti sūtra arthaḥ evam upamāna śabdayoḥ api tad pūrvakatva niyamaḥ boddhavyaḥ 
NTD_2.1.35^1	 tat evam para pakṣa avalambana mukhena dūṣaṇam uktam sūtrakāreṇa sāmpratam sva pakṣa siddham dūṣaṇam āha naca eka deśa upalabdhiḥ avayavi sadbhāvāt avayavinaḥ asattvam manyamānena tvayā eka deśa mātra upalabdhyā pratyakṣa buddheḥ anumāna tvam uktam natu iyam eka deśa upalabdhiḥ api tu tasya tad sahacaritasya avayavinaḥ ca upalabdhiḥ kim kāraṇam avayavi sadbhāvāt avayavinaḥ api avayava vat upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpta tvena gṛhyamāṇa viśeṣa tvāt kā punar iyam upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptiḥ mahattva aneka dravya rūpa viśeṣa samavāyāḥ na ca evam upaladhi lakṣaṇa prāpta tvena upalabhyamānasya asati bādhake nāstitvam pratipādayitum śakyam nanu vṛtti vikalpa ādi bādhakam pramāṇam asti iti ced tathā hi kim avaya vi avayaveṣu vartamānaḥ eka deśena vartate kārtsnyena vā na tāvat eka deśena vartate vartamāna eka deśa vyatirekeṇa eka deśa antara abhāvāt na ca kārtsnyena ekatra kṛtsna samāptasya anyatra vṛtti asambhavāt eka dravyasya kāraṇa vibhāga asambhavena nitya tva prasaṅgāt ca 
NTD_2.1.35^2	 na ca gati antareṇa vṛttiḥ asti atas vidyamāna vṛttika tvāt vāji viṣāṇa vat asattvam eva avayavinaḥ iti tathā viruddha dharma saṃsargaḥ ca avayavi abhyupagame durvāraḥ kim kāraṇam ekasya avayavasya rāge kampe grahaṇe āvaraṇe ca sati tad sthānasya avayavinaḥ rāga kampa grahaṇa āvaraṇa saṃbhavena avayava antara avasthitasya api tasya abhedena tathā abhāva prasaṅgāt kampa rāga grahaṇa āvaraṇa pratyayāḥ bhaveyuḥ na ca etat dṛṣṭam iṣṭam vā athavā avayavasya rāga ādayaḥ na avayavinaḥ iti ced tarhi rakta avayava sthānasya api tasya ārakta tvam pṛthak gatimat tvena yuta siddha tvena gṛhīta avayava sthānasya api agrahaṇam āvṛta avayava sthānasya anāvaraṇam iti doṣāḥ prādurbhaveyuḥ tasmāt na asti avayavī iti tat ayuktam ekasmin kṛtsna eka deśa vikalpā sambhavāt tathā hi ekam avayavinam aneka avayaveṣu vartamānam aṅgīkṛtya tvayā kṛtsna eka deśa vikalpaḥ kṛtaḥ kim eka deśena vartate kārtsnyena vā iti 
NTD_2.1.35^3	 tatra yadā eka deśena vartate tadā tasya avayavinaḥ eka deśāḥ eka deśeṣu vartante iti syāt na punar ekam anekatra iti yathā kārtsnyena iti ukte sarvatra avayaveṣu pratyekam avayavinaḥ parisamāpteḥ anekam anekatra vartate iti syāt na punar ekam anekatra iti tasmāt yat anuyoga adhikaraṇe vyāghātaḥ mā bhūt iti avayavi avayaveṣu vartate iti etāvat eva vaktavyam na anyat tatas ca avidyamāna vṛttika tvāt vāji viṣāṇavat asattvam iti riktā vācoyuktiḥ sva rūpeṇa vṛtteḥ abhyupagamāt yat punar viruddha dharma saṃsargaḥ iti dūṣaṇam uktam tatra ekāvayava rāge avayavinaḥ rāgaḥ iti etat na asti rāgasya anya dharma tvāt rāga khalu kusumbha ādi dravya saṃbandhī na avayavasya tantoḥ tad avayavinaḥ paṭasya vā paṭaḥ raktaḥ tantuḥ raktaḥ iti tu kusumbha ādi dravya vaśāt bhramaḥ na ca avayave tantau= iva tad avayavini paṭe sarvatra rāga bhrāntyā bhramitavyam kusumbha ādi dravya saṃbandhasya bhrānti hetoḥ avyāpya vṛtti tvāt tasmāt na rakta ārakta lakṣaṇa viruddha dharma saṃsargāt paṭasya pūrvarūpeṇa avasthānāt 
NTD_2.1.35^4–2.1.36	 na api avayavi kampa anabhyupagame pṛthak gatimat tvena yuta siddhi doṣaḥ kim kāraṇam yutasiddhiḥ nāma tad saṃbandhasya avidyamāna tā naca avayava avayavinoḥ pṛthak gatimat tve api avayava saṃbandhasya avayavini vidyamāna tā samasti tad saṃbandhasya eva tad utpatti rūpa tvāt jātaḥ saṃbandhaḥ ca iti ekaḥ kalpaḥ iti tasmāt na kampā kampa prasaṅgaḥ na api grahaṇa agrahaṇa virodhaḥ sambhavati gṛhīta avayava sthānasya avayavinaḥ gṛhīta tvāt na ca bahu avayava sthānasya grahaṇa vat sthaulya aupalambhena bhavitavyam iti vācyam sthaulyasya parimāṇa viśeṣa tvena sāmagryantara grāhya tvāt na hi sāmagrī antara grāhyasya tad āśrayasya dravyasya grahaṇam sambhavati iti etena āvṛtānāvṛta tva virodhaḥ api parihṛtaḥ katipaya avayava āvaraṇe api anāvṛta avayavaiḥ sārdham grahaṇāt tat evam vṛtti vikalpa ādi bādhaka viruddha dharma saṃsargayoḥ abhāvāt avayavi siddheḥ na eka deśīya grahaṇa mātreṇa pratyakṣa siddhiḥ kintu a vaya vi grahaṇāt api tad siddhiḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.1.37	 avayavi sadbhāva pratipādaka pramāṇa upanyāsāt prāk eva sūtrakāraḥ tad praveśa mārga sādhanāya tarka apara nāmānam prasaṅgam āha sarva agrahaṇam avayavi a siddheḥ pratyakṣa ādibhiḥ pramāṇam sarveṣām dravya guṇa karma sāmāni a ādīnām agrahaṇam yadi avayavī nāma na syāt padārthaḥ tadā sarveṣām dravya guṇa karma sāmānya viśeṣa abhāvānām agrahaṇam prasajyeta sarvaiḥ pratyakṣa ādibhiḥ pramāṇaiḥ yat idam grahaṇam iṣṭam paṭaḥ śuklaḥ parispandate sa ca asti tad ārambhāḥ paramāṇavaḥ vyāpṛtāḥ tatra guṇa ādayaḥ vartante sa ca anyatra asti iti tatra syāt kim kāraṇam nirāśraya tvena rūpa ādīnām anupalabdheḥ niravayava viṣayasya pratyakṣasya asambhavena tad mūlānām anumāna ādīnām asaṃbhavāt ca na ca rūpa ādi paramāṇūnām svatantrāṇām grahaṇam iti vācyam paramāṇūnām atīndriya tvena sthūla upalabhya abhāvasya agre vakṣyamāṇa tvāt atas avaśyam asti na avayavinā bhavitavyabhiti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.1.38^1	 tat evam pramāṇa anugrāhakam prasaṅgam pratipādya tad anugrāhyam pramāṇam āha dhāraṇa ākarṣaṇa upapatteḥ ca na kevalam idam ekam dravyam iti sthūla upalambha lakṣaṇa pratyakṣāt avayavi siddhiḥ kim tarhi dhāraṇa ākarṣaṇa upapatteḥ dhāraṇa ākarṣaṇa upapatti lakṣaṇa anumānāt ca iti pramāṇa dvaya samuccaya arthaḥ cakāraḥ tatra dhāraṇam nāma eka deśa sāhacarye satya vayavinaḥ deśa antara prāpti pratiṣedhaḥ ākarṣaṇañca eka deśa sāhacarye satya vayavinaḥ deśa antara prāpaṇam ete dhāraṇa ākarṣaṇe vijñāna ākāśa ādau= adarśanāt avayavinam sādhayataḥ 
NTD_2.1.38^2	 tathā hi yaḥ asau dṛśyamānaḥ ghaṭa ādiḥ arthaḥ avayavī paramāṇu sañcaya rūpeṇa vivāda adhyāsitaḥ na asau= anavayavaḥ dhāraṇā karṣaṇavat tvāt yaḥ punar niravayavaḥ na ca asau dhāraṇā karṣaṇavān yathā vijñāna ākāśa ādi na ca ghaṭādiḥ arthaḥ tasmāt na avayavi iti nanu jatu ādi dravya saṃgraha kārite dhāraṇa ākarṣaṇe na avaya vikārite iti ced tat ayuktam jatu ādi dravya saṃgraha kāritayoḥ api tayoḥ avayavini ā iva dṛṣṭa tvāt na khalu jatu saṃgṛhītāḥ tṛṇa upala kāṣṭha ādayaḥ dhāryamāṇāḥ ākṛṣyamāṇāḥ vā niravayavāḥ bhavanti atas dhāraṇā karṣaṇavat tvāt asti avayavī iti tathā idam eka dravyam iti sthūla vastu palambha aindriyakaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ 
NTD_2.1.38^3	 naca asau= upalambhaḥ paramāṇu mātra viṣayaḥ iti vaktum śakyam paramāṇūnām atīndriya tvena tad viṣaya tva abhāvāt tathā hi paramāṇavaḥ kim pratyekam dvitīya bhāvam bhajeran sañcitāḥ vā na tāvat pratyekam sthaulya anava bhāsa prasaṅgāt ata undriya tvāt ca na ca pratibhāsa dharma sthaulyam artha dharma tayā bahiṣṭvena pratibhāsamāna tvāt na api sañvitāḥ eka tva pratibhāsā bhāva prasaṅgāt na khalu bahuṣu paramāṇuṣu eka tva pratibhāsaḥ yuktaḥ anekeṣu eka pratyayasya adṛṣṭa tvāt sañcita tve api atīndriya tva apāyāt ca natu āloka manaskāra ādi artha antara ādi saṃbaddhāḥ eva paramāṇavaḥ samutpadyante 
NTD_2.1.38^4	 te sa atiśayāḥ sañcitāḥ iti ucyante na punar yatra tatra utpannāḥ atas yatra tatra utpannānām aṇūnām atīndriya tve api sa atiśayānām aindriyaka tve na kaścid virodhaḥ iti ced tat ayuktam madhya para bhāga avasthitānām api aṇūnām sa atiśaya tva aviśeṣeṇa arvāc bhāgavat aindriyaka tva prasaṅga aeka pratyaya abhāva prasaṅgāt ca tasmāt aneka tvāt tīndriya tvābhyām sa atiśayāḥ paramāṇavaḥ imām eka pratyakṣa jñānasya na viṣaya tām āsādayanti na ca ayam pratyakṣaḥ niviṣayaḥ nirālambana jñānasya agre nirākariṣyamāṇa tvāt atas yaḥ tasya pratyakṣa jñānasya viṣayaḥ saḥ asti avayavi iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.1.39	 senā vana vat grahaṇam iti ced na atīndriya tvāt aṇūnām nanu ārāda gṛhyamāṇa pṛthaktveṣu anekeṣu hasti aśva ratha ādiṣu yathā senā iti ekaḥ pratyayaḥ yathā vā nānā jātīyeṣu ārāda gṛhyamāṇa pṛthaktveṣu dhava khadira ādiṣu vanam ipi ekaḥ pratyayaḥ tathā sa atiśayeṣu paramāṇuṣu pratyekam agṛhyamāṇa pṛthak tvaṣu ekam idam dravyam iti eka tva pratyayaḥ bhaviṣyati iti ced na atīndriya tvāt pūrva ukta nyāyena sarvadā paramāṇūnām atīndriya tvena kadācid api svarūpeṇa pṛthak rūpeṇa vā yogya tva abhāvāt tasmāt senā vana vat grahaṇam iti viṣamaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.1.40^1	 atha idānīm avasara prāptam anumānam parīkṣyate rodha upaghāta sādṛśyebhyaḥ vyabhicārāt anumānam apramāṇam rudhyate anena iti rodhaḥ vāyu abhra saṃyoga ādiḥ varṣa pratibandhaḥ tasmin sati paridṛṣṭā api megha unnatiḥ na vṛṣṭim utpādayati upaghātaḥ nāma pipīlakānām nīḍa avasthitānāmaṇḍa ādīnām trāsanam sādṛśyam nāma dhūma sadṛśe bāṣpa ādau dhūma jñānam tathā hi megha unnatyā bhaviṣyati vṛṣṭiḥ iti pūrvavat tat kāraṇena kārya anumānasya udāharaṇam uktam kasmāt dṛṣṭvā api megha unnatim kvāpi pratibandhena varṣa anutpatti darśanāt tathā api pipīla kānām aṇḍa saṃcāreṇa avāntara kāryeṇa varṣa hetu bhūtaḥ saṃkṣobhaḥ anumīyate tasmāt bhūta saṃkṣobhāt bhauma enā ūṣmaṇā kvāthyamānā pipīlikā svāṇḍāni upariṣṭān nayanti 
NTD_2.1.40^2	 tat khalu śeṣavataḥ kāryāt kāraṇa anumānasya udāharaṇam tat api vyabhicarati tasmāt nīḍa upaghātāt api trastānām pipīlikā aṇḍa saṃcāra darśanāt tathā sva kāraṇāt utpannena dhūmena sva saṃyuktaḥ vahniḥ anumīyate tad khalu sāmānyatas dṛṣṭasya udāharaṇam bhavati kārya kāraṇa rūpa viśeṣasya api vivakṣita tvāt tat api vyabhicarati kvacid bahula bāṣpa dhūlī paṭala ādau dhūma buddhi saṃbhavena vahni abhāve api vahni anumāna saṃbhavāt tat etebhyaḥ hetubhyaḥ pūrvavat ādi udāharaṇeṣu vyabhicāra sambhavena lakṣya asiddheḥ anumāna lakṣaṇam asaṅgatam iti sūtra arthaḥ atra khalu sūtre bhāṣya vārttika mārga anusaraṇam yat īṣat mayā kṛtam tad anumāna lakṣaṇa parīkṣā sūtra vyākhyāna sāmañjasyāya iti mantavyam iti 
NTD_2.1.41	 tat etat pariharati na eka deśa trāsa sādṛśyebhyaḥ artha antara bhāvāt apratibaddhāyām satyām khalu megha unnatau vṛṣṭiḥ avaśyambhāvinī sā megha unnatiḥ varṣa liṅga tvena vivakṣitā na unnati mātram unnati mātram tu liṅga eka deśaḥ tathā bhūyiṣṭhānām atra sthānām pipīlikānām bhūyiṣṭheṣu sthāneṣu pravāheṇa aṇḍa sañcāraṇam varṣa hetu bhūtu saṃkṣobhasya liṅgam na aṇḍa sañcāraṇa mātram tathā sātatyam bahula tva ādi guṇa viśiṣṭam ca dhūma darśanam vahneḥ anumāpakam na dhūma vastu udgama mātram tad khalu sādṛśyāt mithyā iti kāraṇam liṅga jñāne pratipattṛ naipuṇyasya vivakṣita tvāt etat uktam bhavati eka deśa trāsa sādṛśyebhyaḥ megha unnati aṇḍa saṃcāra dhūma vastu udgama mātrebhyaḥ anumāpakānām viśiṣṭa unnati prabhṛtīnām viśiṣṭa pratipattṛ dṛṣṭānām artha antara bhāvāt vilakṣaṇa tvāt lakṣya sambhavena anumāna lakṣaṇam saṅgatam iti yat uktam tat na iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.1.42	 traikālya grahaṇāt iti anena sūtreṇa tri kāla viṣayam anumānam iti uktam tatra dūṣaṇam āha vartamāna abhāvaḥ patataḥ patita patitavya kāla upapatteḥ atra vartamāna abhāvaḥ iti viśeṣa pratiṣedhaḥ eva diś deśa niyama anapekṣa para apara vyatikara yaugapadya ayaugapadi a cira kṣi pratyayānām ananya nimitta tvena kāla svarūpa siddhi su vyaktaḥ iti manvānaḥ sūtra kāraḥ tat parīkṣām upekṣya kāla viśeṣa parīkṣām eva kṛtavān iti sūcayati tatas ca asya sūtrasya ayam arthaḥ na tāvat kriyā vyaṅgyaḥ kālaḥ tasyāḥ sādhya tvena kāla avyañjaka tvāt kim tarhi kāraka vyaṅgyaḥ tasya siddha tvena kāla vyaktim prati hetu tva saṃbhavāt evañca vartamāna kālasya asaṃbhavāt kim kāraṇam vṛntāt patataḥ phalasya patita patitavya kāla upapatteḥ patita vyapatitā sva lakṣaṇa kāraka dvaya vyajyamānayoḥ patitavya patita kālayoḥ eva upapatti sambhāvanā na ca madhye kaścid adhvā vidyate yena tena abhivyajyamānaḥ vartamānaḥ kālaḥ gṛhyate tasmāt vartamāna kāla abhāvāt tri kāla viṣayam anumānam iti ayuktam iti 
NTD_2.1.43^1	 tayoḥ api abhāvaḥ vartamāna abhāve tad apekṣa tvāt phalati patitānām gatau kāle bhavatā abhyupagatau tayoḥ api abhāvaḥ prasajyate vartamāna abhāve vartamāna kāla anabhyupagame sati kutas tad apekṣa tvāt tasya vartamāna kālasya apekṣā vidyate yayoḥ atīta anāgatayoḥ tau tad apekṣau tayoḥ bhāvaḥ tad apekṣa tvam tasmāt tad apekṣa tvāt tathā hi na tāvat adhva lakṣaṇaḥ kāraka vyaṅgyaḥ kālaḥ tasya sva rūpeṇa bheda abhāvāt kim tarhi patana kriyā vyaṅgyaḥ tasyāḥ vinaṣṭa utpanna an utpanna tva lakṣaṇa bhedasya vidyamāna tvāt tatra vidyamāna patana kriyā viśiṣṭam phalam yadā paśyati tadā patati phalam iti vartamāna kāla saṃbandhi tvena vyapadiśati kriyā āśrayam 
NTD_2.1.43^2	 yadā uparata kriyā phalam paśyati tadā apatat kriyā phalam iti atīta kāla viśiṣṭam yadā anutpanna kriyam kriyā kāraṇaka yuktam paśyati tadā patiṣyati phalam iti anāgata kāla viśiṣṭa upetā bhavati na atītāḥ na āgata kāla vyapadeśau vartamāna kāla kriyā apekṣau anyathā kasya vināśānutpatti apekṣā atīta anāgata vyapadeśau bhavataḥ kasya vā kāraṇam aphala āśrayaḥ guru tva guṇaḥ kasya vā phalabhūti saṃyogaḥ kāryaḥ tasmāt kriyā dvāreṇa vartamāna kāla apekṣa tvāt atīta anāgatayoḥ vartamāna kālaḥ sa ca tad apekṣasya api siddheḥ asti vartamāna kālaḥ iti vartamāna kāla abhāvena tri kāla viṣayasya tu anumānasya na saṃbhavaḥ iti yat uktam pūrva sūtreṇa tat ayuktam iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.1.44–2.1.45	 na atīta anāgatayoḥ itaretara apekṣā siddheḥ nanu paratva aparatvayoḥ hrasva dīrgha tvayoḥ iva atīta anāgatayoḥ api paraspara apekṣā siddhiḥ bhaviṣyati iti kṛtam vartamāna kālena tad apekṣeṇa iti ced tat naḥ itaretara apekṣā siddheḥ eva hetoḥ ubhaya asiddhi prasaṅgāt yatra itara itara apekṣa vastu dvaya siddhiḥ tatra ubhaya siddhiḥ avaśyam bhāvinī iti atīta anāgatayoḥ api asiddhi prasaṅgāt na ca paratva aparatva ādīnām api siddhiḥ paraspara apekṣā sannikṛṣṭa viprakṛṣṭa buddhi ādibhiḥ na kāraṇa janya tvena paraspara apekṣa tvāt tasmāt atīta anāgatābhyām sva siddhi artham apekṣitavyaḥ asti vartamāna kālaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ vartamāna abhāve sarva agrahaṇam pratyakṣa anupapatteḥ vartama akāla anabhyupagame pratyakṣasya vartamāna sādhāraṇasya anupapattyā tad mūlānām api māna antarāṇām anupapatteḥ sarvasya dravya guṇa karma ādi padārthasya agrahaṇāt āndhyam aśeṣasya jagataḥ prāpsyati iti atas api asti vartamānaḥ kālaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.1.46	 kriyamāṇe kṛta tā kartavyatā upapatteḥ tu ubhayathā grahaṇam ubhaya prakāreṇa grahaṇam bhavati katham atīta anāgatābhyām saṃpṛktā saṃpṛktaḥ ca iti tatra yadā pacati chinatti iti ādi kriyā santāna vyaṅgyaḥ tadā saṃpṛktaḥ kim kāraṇam kriyamāṇe kṛta tā kartavyatā upapatteḥ tu yat ca idam pacyamānam chidyamānam vā vastu tad kriyamāṇam tasmin kriyamāṇe kṛta tā kartavyatā upapatteḥ pūrva aparībhāvaḥ papatteḥ yasmāt kāścana kriyāḥ atītāḥ kāścana vartamānāḥ kāścana anāgatāḥ iti yadā punar vidyate iti kriyā mātra vyaṅgyaḥ tadā asaṃpṛktaḥ gṛhyate tatra pūrva aparībhāva anupapatteḥ iti sūtra gataḥ tu śabdaḥ kriyā mātra vyaṅgyāt kriyā santāna vyaṅgyasya vyavacchedam āha atīta anāgatābhyām asaṃpṛktaḥ śuddhaḥ vartamānaḥ kālaḥ sa tu punar aśuddhaḥ atīta anāgatābhyām saṃpṛktaḥ iti tat idam saṃpṛktā saṃpṛkta bhedena vartamāna kālasya ubhayathā grahaṇa kathanam saṃpṛkta pakṣe kāla antara abhyupagamena kāla apahnavaḥ iti pratipādanam aśakyam iti na asaṃpṛkta pakṣaḥ iti jñāna artham iti mantavyam 
NTD_2.1.47	 atha upamāna parīkṣā kim punar upamānam vākya artha smaraṇa sahakāri pratyakṣa janita dharma jñānam saṃjñā saṃjñi saṃbandha pratīti phalakam upamānam iti uktam purastāt lakṣaṇa sūtra gatasya sādharmya śabdasya dharma upalakṣaṇa tvena vyākhyānāt tatra dūṣaṇam āha atyanta prāya eka deśa sādharmyāt upamāna asiddhiḥ atyanta sādharmyāt sarvathā sādharmyāt prāyas sādharmyāt bhūyas avayava sādharmyāt eka deśa sādharmyāt eka deśa mātra sādharmyāt vā upamāna asiddhiḥ upamānasya siddhiḥ na asti iti kim kāraṇam atyanta ādi sādharmyeṣu upamāna vākya prayogasya adarśanāt na khalu yathā gauḥ ayam gauḥ iti vā yathā anaḍvān evam mahiṣaḥ iti vā yathā meruḥ tathā sarṣapaḥ iti vā prayogaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ na ca prakāra antareṇa upamānam vartate tasmāt upamāna asiddhiḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ atra api sādharmya śabdasya upalakṣaṇa tvāt akhila dharma upadeśasya aśakya tvāt alpa dharma upadeśaḥ eka dharma upadeśaḥ eka dharma upadeśe ca atiprasaṅgāt karabha ādi sārūpya vyatirekeṇa dharma mātreṇa apravartamānam api upamānam na sambhavati iti api draṣṭavyam 
NTD_2.1.48	 pariharati prasiddha sādharmyāt upamāna siddheḥ yathā ukta doṣa anupapattiḥ prakaraṇa ādi apekṣam hi vākyam arthasya pratipādakam na vākya mātram tatas ca yādṛśam sādharmyam atyantam prāyas vā alpam vā prakaraṇa apekṣeṇa vākyena prathaya siddhiḥ paścāt pratyakṣeṇa prasiddhyati tasmāt prasiddhaḥ eva sādharmyāt saṃjñā saṃjñi saṃbandha pratipatti siddhyā upamāna pramāṇa prasiddheḥ yathā ukta doṣa anupapattiḥ yathā uktasya doṣasya sādharmyasya kṛtsna prāya alpatām āśritya na upamānam pravartate iti uktasya doṣasya anupapattiḥ yathā uktasya sādharmyasya kṛtsna prāya alpatām āśritya na upamānam kutas yena kenacid sādharmyeṇa api pramāṇa dvaya siddhena saṃjñā samarthana dvāreṇa upamāna siddheḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.1.49	 karabha ādiṣu dharma mātra viṣaya upamāne api prakaraṇa ādi para upanīta prasiddha dharmi viṣayā pramāṇa siddhiḥ boddhavyā iti na tatra anupapattiḥ iti api draṣṭavyam tat evam upapannasya upamānasya anumāne antarbhāvam āha upamānam anumānam pratyakṣeṇa apratyakṣa siddheḥ yathā pratyakṣeṇa dhūmena apratyakṣasya vahneḥ siddhiḥ anumānam tathā pratyakṣeṇa go sādṛśyena gavaya sthena apratyakṣasya saṃjñā saṃjñi saṃbandhasya siddheḥ upamānam anumānam iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.1.50	 nanu yathā gauḥ tathā gavayaḥ iti idam api upamāna eka deśa tvāt upamānam tat ca para artham tena śrotuḥ eva pratipatti siddheḥ anumānantu tathā na bhavati anumānāt ātma pratipatteḥ api siddheḥ iti anayoḥ bhedam manyate siddhānta vādī tam āśaṅkya pariharati na apratyakṣe gavaye pramāṇa artham upamānasya paśyāmaḥ iti para artham upamānam iti ced na svaya madhyavasāyāt evam ukta prakāreṇa para artham upamānam iti ced manyase siddhāntavādin= tat na svaya madhyavasāyāt tasmāt yathā gauḥ tathā gavayaḥ iti vākyāt śrotuḥ iva uccarituḥ api adhyavasāyaḥ bhavati tasmāt upamāna eka deśasya atideśa vākyasya para artha tvāt upamānasya anumānāt bhedaḥ na asti iti kim tarhi pratyakṣeṇa apratyakṣa siddheḥ iti pūrva uktena nyāyena anumānāt upamānasya abhedaḥ eva iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.1.51^1	 tam imam anumāna antarbhāva pakṣam tad sāmagrī tvena dūṣayati tathā iti upasaṃhārāt upamāna siddheḥ na aviśeṣaḥ tathā iti sādṛśya abhidhānam upasaṃhāraḥ atra sthitasya anyatra ati deśaḥ tasmāt tathā iti upasaṃhārāt etat uktam bhavati yathā gauḥ tathā gavayaḥ iti vākyāt go sādṛśya viśiṣṭam kiñcid vastu prathamam avagamya paścāt tad anveṣaṇa artham aṭavī maṭan kadācid tādṛśam piṇḍam pratyakṣeṇa pratipadyate smaḥ iti vā atideśa vākyāt anubhūta artham anantaram ca vākya artha sahakāriṇā tena pratyakṣeṇa gavayanāmā ayam iti saṃjñā saṃjñi saṃbandham pratipadyate 
NTD_2.1.51^2	 tat īdṛśam upamānam liṅga liṅgi saṃbandha darśana dvitīya liṅgi darśana vyāpti smaraṇa pūrvakam tṛtīya liṅga darśana rūpāt anumānāt atyantam bhinnam iti anena kāraṇena tathā iti upasaṃhārāt upamāna siddheḥ na aviśeṣaḥ anumāna īpa mānayoḥ aviśeṣaḥ na asti kiṃtu viśeṣaḥ eva iti na ca vākya artha mātrāt saṃjñā saṃjñi saṃbandha pratipatti siddhiḥ saṃjñinaḥ gavayasya apratīteḥ na ca gavaya śabda mātrāt saṃjñinaḥ gavayasya pratītiḥ tad ānīma gṛhīta saṃbandha tvāt gavaya śabdasya vākyena ca saṃbandha grahaṇe tu itaretara āśraya tva prasaṅgāt
