NTD_2.1.51^3	 na ca yaḥ hi yatra prayujyate saḥ asati bādhake tasya vācakaḥ yathā go śabdaḥ go tve prayuktaḥ ca ayam gavaya śabdaḥ gavayatve atas vācaka tvam anumātum śakyam saṃbandha grahaṇāt prāk saṃjñini gavayatve prayukte ayam gavaya śabdaḥ iti viniścaya abhāvena atra prayukta tvāt iti hetoḥ asiddha tvāt vākyena saṃjñi samarpaṇe ca itaretara āśraya tva prasaṅgāt saṃjñi samarpaṇe sati tatra prayukta tvena tad vācaka tva siddhiḥ anumānāt tad siddhau ca tad pada sahitāt vākyāt saṃjñi samarpaṇam iti na ca gavaya pada vyatiriktāt vākyāt pratīyamānam sādṛśyam eva saṃjñi gavaya śabdasya aneka artha tva prasaṅgāt ajāti śabda tva prasaṅgāt ca tasmāt na ati deśa vākyāt saṃjñā saṃjñi saṃbandha pratipattiḥ na api sādṛśya pratyakṣa mātrāt saṃjñā saṃjñi saṃbandhāt pratipattiḥ iti vācyam aśrutā atideśa vākyasya sādṛśya pratyakṣe api saṃjñā saṃjñi saṃbandha pratipatteḥ abhāvāt tasmāt āgamāt āhita saṃskāra smṛti apekṣam pratyakṣa janita dharma jñānam saṃjñā saṃjñi saṃbandha pratipattim kurvat itara pramāṇa vilakṣaṇa tvāt vilakṣaṇa pramāṇa janaka tvāt ca upamānam pṛthak pramāṇam iti siddham 
NTD_2.1.52	 atha idānīm avasara prāptam śabda lakṣaṇam parīkṣamāṇaḥ sūtrakāraḥ pramāṇa bhāvaḥ asya na parīkṣaṇīyaḥ śabda ātmanā vā vivakṣā sūcanena vā vaktṛ abhiprāya jñāpanena vā anumāna ātmanā vā paramparayā spaṣṭa pratipatti sādhana tvena vā sarva vādi sammata tayā prasiddha tvena śiṣyaiḥ eva svayam avagantum śakya tvāt iti pramāṇa abhāva parīkṣām upekṣya anantara prakaraṇa saṅga tām anumāna antargatim eva parīkṣate śabhaḥ anumānam arthasya anupalabdheḥ anumeya tvāt śabdaḥ anumānam apṛthak pramāṇam kasmāt arthasya pratyakṣeṇa anupalabdheḥ hetoḥ anumeya tvāt yatra pratyakṣeṇa anupalabdhaḥ arthaḥ paścāt mitena liṅge na anumīyate tatra anumāna tvam dṛṣṭam yathā dhūmāt agni jñāne tathā ca śabde tasmāt pratyakṣeṇa anupalabhyamāna artha viṣaya tvāt anumānam śabdaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.1.53	 itas ca anumānam śabdaḥ upalabdheḥ advi pravṛtti tvāt yayoḥ pramāṇayoḥ bhedaḥ kārya bhūta upalabdhiḥ dvi pravṛttiḥ prakāra dvayavatī dṛṣṭā yathā pratyakṣa anumānayoḥ na tathā śabda anumānayoḥ kārya bhūta upalabdhiḥ prakāra dvayavatī eka ākāra sāmagrī janya tvena eka prakāra tvāt tasmāt śabda anumānayoḥ upalabdheḥ advi pravṛtti tvāt anumānam śabdaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.1.54	 saṃbandhāt ca yayoḥ saṃbaddhayoḥ arthayoḥ saṃbandha prasiddhiḥ tayoḥ ekatareṇa jñānena anyatarasya jñānam anumānam dṛṣṭam yathā dhūma agnyoḥ tathā saṃbaddhayoḥ śabda arthayoḥ saṃbandha prasiddhau śabda upalabdheḥ artha jñānam anumānam eva kasmāt saṃbandhāt dhuma agnyoḥ iva śabda arthayoḥ api sambandhasya vidyamāna tvāt nanu anena krameṇa śabdasya anumāna tve katham apratipādaka vākya śravaṇa samanantaram pratipādyasya puruṣasya vākya artha rūpe saṃsarga viśeṣe pratipatteḥ upapattiḥ ucyate nadyāḥ tīre phalāni santi ityādi pratipādaka vākya avayava bhūtaiḥ padaiḥ smāritāḥ padārthāḥ guṇa pradhāna bhāvena avasthitāḥ paraspara saṃsargavantaḥ ākāṅkṣa ādimattve sati padaiḥ smārita tvāt vyutpitsoḥ bālasya pramāṇa antara avagata gām abhyāja iti ādi padasmārita padārtha vat tāni dharmāṇi sva smārita padārtha saṃsargavanti ākāṅkṣa ādimattve sati padārtha tvāt tādṛśa gām abhyājā iti ādi pada āvalī vat tat evam padārthānām padānām vā liṅga tayā vākya artha pratipatti hetu tvāt na tatas artha antaram śabdaḥ iti 
NTD_2.1.55^1	 tat etat pariharati āpta upadeśa sāmarthyāt śabdāt artha saṃpratyayaḥ śabdāt eva artha saṃpratyayaḥ na arthāt tad smāritāt kiṃbhūtāt śabdāt āpta upadaśa sāmarthyāt āptaḥ prāptaḥ upadeśaḥ sāmarthyam abhidhā vyāpāraḥ yena saḥ ayam āpta upadeśa sāmarthyaḥ tasmāt āpta upadeśa sāmarthyāt etat uktam bhavati na tāvat vāṣpa avayava bhūtaiḥ padaiḥ smāritāḥ padārthāḥ pada vyatirekeṇa kevalam liṅga tayā vākya artha rūpa saṃsarga avabodham utpādayanti svarūpataḥ sannidhi yogya tve sati api pada upasthāpita eka prayojana svīkāra abhāve sati paraspara ākāṅkṣa abhāvena saṃsarga asaṃbhavāt na ca prakāra antara upajanitā kāṅkṣā padārthānām vākya artha rūpa saṃsarga hetuḥ bhavitum arhati tathā sati raktaḥ paṭaḥ bhavati iti vākyasya eka deśaḥ paṭaḥ bhavati iti ayam kevalam paṭaḥ bhavati iti vākya padam kañcid guṇam ākṣipya nirvṛṇuyāt na paṭaḥ iti etat apekṣeta 
NTD_2.1.55^2	 tathā bhavati iti etat api kāraka mātra apekṣayā nirākāḍkṣaḥ sannirvṛṇuḥ ayāt na raktam paṭam vā apekṣeta bhavatu kaḥ doṣaḥ iti ced sarvatra vākye padārthānām yathāyogya kriyā guṇa dravya apekṣayā nirākāṅkṣa tvena tad abhidhāyinām padānām pratyekam avākya tvena ekasmin vākye aneka vākya tva prasaṅgāt pada samūhaḥ vākyam iti etat na syāt na ca etat dṛṣṭam iṣṭam vā kasmāt eka prayojana pratipādana paraiḥ padaiḥ smāritānām padārthānām tat para tvam antareṇa paryavasāna tvam eva akāṅkṣa iti yuktam utpaśyāmaḥ tatas ca pada vyatirekeṇa padasmāritānām padārthānām vākya artha avabodhaka tvam liṅga tayā na saṃbhavati iti ākāṅkṣa ādimattve satī iti viśeṣaṇasya asiddha tvāt iti siddham na padasmāritāt padārthāt saṃsarga siddhiḥ iti nanu mā bhūt padārtha liṅgakaḥ vākya artha pratyayaḥ tathā api tad smaraṇā avāntara vyāpāra vat aliṅgakaḥ bhaviṣyati iti uktam iti ced mā evam 
NTD_2.1.55^3	 padāni sva smārita padārtha saṃsargavanti ākāṅkṣa ādimattve sati padatvāditi atra pada viśeṣaṇībhūta padārtha saṃsargasya padaiḥ sārdham anumiteḥ prāc saṃbandha abhāvena anumāna pravṛtteḥ aśakya tvāt yatra dharmiṇaḥ sisādhayiṣita dharmasya ca tathā ardha padaiḥ sārdham padārtha saṃsargasya padānām tat jñāna janaka tvam antareṇa anyatas prāc siddhaḥ saṃbandhaḥ asti yena anumānam pravartate anumānena ca tad siddhau= itaretara āśraya tvam pada liṅgaka anumānāt padānām padārtha jñāna janaka lakṣaṇa saṃbandha siddhiḥ saṃbandha siddhau ca tat jñāna jananāya paścāt pada liṅgakam anumānam pravartate iti tasmāt na padam tad arthaḥ vā vākya artha bodhe liṅgam avyāpta tvāt anala anumāne rāsabha ādi vat tat evam anena sūtreṇa abhidhāna vyāpāra sahitāt śabdāt eva vyāpti ādi rahitāt vākya artha buddhiḥ upajāyate iti pratipādayan sūtra kāraḥ pratyakṣeṇa anupalabhyamāna artha viṣaya tvāt upalabdhiḥ ca paraspara saṃbandhaḥ pūrvam eva prasiddhaḥ 
NTD_2.1.55^4	 tatra tat jñāna jananāya anumānam pravartate yathā parvata analayoḥ kim kāraṇam anala jñāna janaka tva vyatirekeṇa parvata anala saṃbandhasya saṃyogasya pūrvam eva siddha tvāt cakāra dvaividhya rahita tvāt iti dūṣaṇa dvitayam parihṛtavān iti mantavyam śabda anumāna sāmagryoḥ prakāra bheda kathanena anayoḥ pūrva pakṣa hetvoḥ dūṣaṇa tvena anaikāntika asiddha tvayoḥ pratīyamāna tvāt iti athavā āpta upadeśa sāmarthyāt śabdāt arthe saṃpratyayaḥ iti āptasya yathā dṛṣṭa arthasya tathā eva upadeṣṭuḥ puruṣasya eva upadeśaḥ iti sāmarthyam āpta praṇīta tvāt tasmāt āpta praṇīta tvāt śabda arthe saṃpratyayaḥ śabdāt asmaryamāṇe samyak pratyayaḥ pramāṇa tā jñānam sambhavati iti na ca evam anumāne āpta prāmāṇyāt prāmāṇya jñānam atas na anumānam śabdaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.1.56	 yat punar sambandhāt ca iti anena sūtreṇa gamaka aṅgasya saṃbanvasya vidyamāna tvāt anumānam śabdaḥ iti uktam tatra dūṣaṇam āha na upalabdheḥ atīndriya tvāt sa khalu śabda artha saṃbandhaḥ prāpti lakṣaṇaḥ vā pratyāyya pratyāyaka rūpaḥ vā yadi prāpti lakṣaṇaḥ tarhi tasya pratyakṣeṇa upalabdhiḥ anumānena vā tatra tāvat pratyakṣeṇa na upalabdhiḥ kasmāt atīndriya tvāt paramāṇu ādi śabdasya atīndriyeṇa anupalabhyamāna tvena apratyakṣa tvāt yatra saṃbandhasya pratyakṣeṇa upalabdhiḥ tatra saṃbandhinoḥ dvayoḥ pratyakṣa tvam dṛṣṭam yathā ghaṭa paṭayoḥ na ca tathā sambandhinoḥ dvayoḥ api pratyakṣa tvam sambhavati paramāṇu ādi śabdasya pratyakṣa tvāt tad arthasya paramāṇu ādeḥ atīndriya tvāt iti yadi api sattā guṇa śabdānām tad artha anāñca śravaṇa indriya pratyakṣa tvam tathā api tatra saṃbandha pratipatteḥ abhāvāt na tad saṃbandhasya pratyakṣa tvam iti na pratyakṣeṇa upalabdhiḥ prāpti lakṣaṇa sambandhasya iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.1.57	 atha anumānena upalabdhiḥ iti dvitīyaḥ tatra āha pūraṇa pradāha pāṭana anupalabdheḥ ca saṃbandha abhāvaḥ anumānena pratipattau śabda deśam arthaḥ prāptaḥ iti vā anumeyaḥ artha deśam śabdaḥ prāptaḥ iti vā na tāvat śabda deśam arthaḥ prāptaḥ iti anumeyaḥ kasmāt mukhe sthāna karaṇa uccāraṇīyaḥ śabdaḥ iti anna agni asi śabda uccāraṇe tad āśrayasya mukhasya tad artha prāpti kāryāṇām pūraṇa pradāha pāṭanānām saṃbhavena upalabdhi prasaṅgāt na ca upalabdhiḥ asti iti tasmāt na śabda deśam arthaḥ prāptaḥ iti na dvitīyaḥ kalpaḥ śabda hetu bhūtayoḥ artha deśe sambhavasya cakāreṇa sūcita tvāt na ca ubhayam ubhayatra prāptam ubhaya pratiṣedhāt ekaḥ vitatya avasthitaḥ śabdaḥ iti ced na śrotra viṣaya saṃskāra pakṣe dvayoḥ abhivyañjaka niyama asaṃbhavena sarva śabdānām sarva puruṣāṇāñca yugapad upalabdhi prasaṅgāt tasmāt na anumeyaḥ śabda arthayoḥ prāpti lakṣaṇaḥ sambandhaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.1.58	 śabda artha vyavasthānāt apratiṣedhaḥ bhavatu nāma prāpti lakṣaṇasya śabda artha sambandhasya pratiṣedhaḥ pramāṇa abhāvāt tathā api vācya vācaka lakṣaṇasya svābhāvikasya sambandhasya apratiṣedhaḥ kasmāt śavda artha vyavasthānāt go śabdāt sāsna ādimān ā iva arthaḥ pratīyate aśva śabdāt kesara ādi mān ā iva ityādi yat idam pratyaya vyavasthānam tena anumimīmahe asti śabda arthayoḥ sambandhaḥ vyavasthā kāraṇam iti tathā hi śabdasya vācyena arthena sambandhaḥ tad prayaya niyama hetu tvāt yaḥ yat pratyaya niyama hetuḥ sa tad sambaddhaḥ yathā pradīpaḥ iti sa ca sambandhaḥ svābhāvikaḥ asvābhāvika tve avyavasthā pātena sambandha grahaṇa anupapatteḥ tasmāt asti śabda arthayoḥ sambandhaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.1.59	 pariharati na sāmayika tvāt śabda artha saṃpratyayasya yat uktam pratyaya vyavasthānāt asti śabda arthayoḥ sambandhaḥ iti tat na sāmayika tvāt samaya kārita tvāt śabda artha saṃpratyayasya pratyaya vyavasthānakasya kaḥ punar samayaḥ asya śabdasya idam artha jātam abhidheyam iti abhidhāna abhidheyayoḥ sarga ādau= īśvareṇa kṛtaḥ tasmin= upayukte jñāte śabda artha pratyayasya vyavasthā bhavati go śabdāt sāsna ādimān ā iva arthaḥ abhidhīyate aśva śabdāt kesara ādimān eva iti sa ca ayam samayaḥ svābhāvika sambandha vādinā api avaśya abhyanujñeyaḥ anyathā agṛhīta saṅgatibhiḥ api śabdaiḥ artha pratyaya prasaṅgāt tasmāt śabda artha pratyaya vyavasthānasya samaya kārita tvena anyathā siddha tvāt na tena svābhāvika sambandha anumānam iti pratyutā asti pramāṇam vivāda adhyāsitaḥ śabda artha sambandhaḥ sa aṅketikaḥ śabda artha sambandha tvāt devadatta ādi śabda arthavat tasmāt na asti svābhāvikaḥ śabda arthayoḥ sambandhaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.1.60^1	 nanu asvābhāvika tve yaiḥ ayam sarga ādau samayaḥ kriyate śabdaiḥ teṣām api atas a nyaiḥ teṣām api atas anyaiḥ teṣām api atas anyaiḥ iti anavasthā pātena asya samaya karaṇam aghaṭamānam eva syāt iti avaśyam samaya kāribhiḥ kaiścid śabdaiḥ svābhāvika sambandha śālibhiḥ bhavitavyam iti atas āha prayujyamāna grahaṇāt ca samaya upayogaḥ asya śabdasya idam abhidheyam iti niyamaḥ samayaḥ tasya upayogaḥ parijñānam tat dvedhā parameśvarāt grahaṇam prayujyamānānām śabdānām grahaṇāt ca 
NTD_2.1.60^2	 tatra ye sarga ādi bhuvaḥ prajāpatayaḥ devāḥ jñāna vairāgya aiśvarya śālinaḥ teṣām asya śabdasya idam artha jātam abhidheyam abhidhāyakaḥ ca ayam śabdaḥ iti ayam pratyayaḥ amīṣām bhavati saṅkalpa mayāt śabda rahitāt parameśvara anugrahāt parijñānam tatas paścāttanānām asmad ādīnām tad vyavahāra paramparāsu prayujyamānānām grahaṇāt ca iti ca arthaḥ na ca asmad ādīnām tatra saṅketa smṛti apekṣā āpta paramparā prayoga balāt eva tad vyatirekeṇa api tad prakṛta pravṛtti nivṛtyāḥ vyavahāra upapatteḥ ataeva ca vyākaraṇasya api sāphalyam ye śabdāḥ yatra arthe vācaka tvena parameśvareṇa saṅketitāḥ te tatra sādhavaḥ na itaratra iti tad niyoga jñāpana artha tvāt 
NTD_2.1.61	 itas ca sāmayikaḥ śabda arthayoḥ sambandhaḥ jāti viśeṣe ca aniyamāt yasmāt āri a mleccha ādi jāti viśeṣe niyamena śabda prayogaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ tasmāt na svābhāvikaḥ śabda arthayoḥ sambandhaḥ na hi svābhāvika sambandhānām pradīpa ādīnām niyamena jāti viśeṣe prakāśaka tvam dṛṣṭam kvacid jāti viśeṣe pradīpaḥ prakāśayati rūpam kvacid anyam iti śabde punar aniyamaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ tathā hi yava śabdāt dīrghaśūka padārtham āryāḥ jānate priyaṅgum mlecchāḥ tathā anyatra api na ca sarve śabdāḥ sarva arthaiḥ svabhāvataḥ sambaddhāḥ daṣṭāḥ vyañjaka niyamān niyamyante iti vācyam vyañjakeṣu api aniyamasya jāti viśeṣaḥ eva yava śabda ādau dṛṣṭa tvāt na hi sarvatra dṛṣṭānām go śabda ādīnām jāti viśeṣe niyata vyañjaka vyaṅgya tvam dṛṣṭam tasmāt na asti śabda arthayoḥ svābhāvikaḥ sambandhaḥ tad abhāvāt tad sambandha balena gamaka aṅga tvāt anumānam śabdaḥ iti yat uktam tat na bhavati tasmāt na anumānam śabdaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.1.62^1	 nanu bhavatu nāma śabda mātrasya prāmāṇyam anumānāt bhedaḥ ca tathā api prathama sūtra upātta niḥśreyasa padarya ālocanayā hi sūcita prāmāṇyasya aniyamena prāmāṇyam siddhyati tad prāmāṇya siddhimūlaḥ ca sakalaḥ ayam śāstra artha sāram vyavahāraḥ iti tad artham prakaraṇam idam ārabhyate iti atas idam ucyate tad aprāmāṇyam anṛta vyāghāta punarukti doṣebhyaḥ putra kāma iṣṭi havana abhyāseṣu tasya vedasya aprāmāṇyam tat aprāmāṇyam kutas anṛta vyāghāta punarukti doṣebhyaḥ doṣa śabdaḥ pratyekam abhisambat dhyate anṛta doṣāt putra kāma iṣṭau vyāghāta doṣāt havane punarukti doṣāt abhyāse iti tathā hi putra kāmaḥ putra kāma iṣṭyā yajeta iti putra janma sādhana tvena putra kāma iṣṭiḥ vihitā na ca asyām iṣṭau saṃsthitāyām api putra janma dṛśyate adarśana at na iṣṭiḥ putra janana kāraṇam iti tasyāḥ tad kāraṇa pratipādana param vākyam anṛta tvāt apramāṇam iti niścīyate ghaṭa kāmaḥ paṭaiḥ dhaṭam kuryāt iti asādhana apadeśa vākya vat 
NTD_2.1.62^2	 tathā agnihotram juhuyāt iti upapatti vākya vihitasya agnihotrasya sāyam prātar agnihotram juhuyāt iti kāla sambandham vidhāya prātar kāle viśeṣam vidhatte udite hotavyam anudite hotavyam samaya adhyuṣite hotavyam iti vākya trayeṇa tat evaṃvidhasya punar svayam eva pratiṣedham āha aśyāvaḥ vā asya āhutim abhyavaharati yaḥ udite juhoti śabalaḥ vā asya āhutim abhyavaharati yaḥ anudite juhoti śyāva śabalau vā asya āhutim abhyavaharataḥ yaḥ samaya adhyuṣite juhoti evam ca prātar kāla sambandham vidhāya tasya udita ādi viśeṣa traya sahitasya vākyasya aśeṣatas pratiṣedhāt udita ādi homa pratiṣedha vākyasya udaya anantara kāla vyatirekeṇa madhyāhna sāyāhna vācaka tva pakṣe homa mātra pratiṣedhāt ca paraspara vyāghātena apramāṇa tvam asti na asti ca iti vākya vat yathā tris prathamām anvāha tris uttamām iti prathama uttamayoḥ sāmidhenyoḥ abhyāse codyamāne punarukti doṣaḥ bhavati punaruktañca pramatta vākya vat apramāṇam tatas ca eka deśa vibhāvita nyāyena vākya antarāṇām api anṛta tva ādi doṣa niścayena sandehena vā apramāṇa tvam iti spaṣṭam iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.1.63	 tatra anṛta doṣe parihāraḥ na karma kartṛ sādhana vaiguṇyāt na putrakāma iṣṭi vākyanām anṛta doṣaḥ kasmāt karma kartṛ sādhana vaiguṇyāt karmaṇaḥ saṃprayogasya kartuḥ mātā pitroḥ sādhanasya iṣṭeḥ vaiguṇyena viguṇa tayā putra janma abhāvasya anyathā siddha tvāt tathā hi na tauvat iṣṭiḥ kevalā putra janmanaḥ kāraṇam api tu iṣṭyā kāraṇa bhūtayā saṃprayujyamānau pitarau putram janayate iti na saṃprayoga ādi kāraṇa antara rahitā sā tatra puruṣāyi tattva ādi saṃprayoga doṣāt mātā pitroḥ yoni bīje jayoḥ vyāpada upahata tva lakṣaṇa doṣāt ṛttvikmantra haviḥ homa ādi vaiguṇyāt api putra janma ādi vākyasya āpādayati iti anṛta tva ādi hetoḥ asiddha tā iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.1.64	 nanu putra janma abhāvaḥ karma kartṛ sādhana vaiguṇyāt āhosvidanṛ tattvāt iti sandehaḥ iti atas āha guṇa yoge phala niṣpatti darśanāt na anṛta tvāt putra janma abhāvaḥ kim tarhi karma kartṛ sādhana vaiguṇyāt eva kutas teṣām karma kartṛ sādhanānām guṇa yoge phala niṣpattiḥ putra janma sambhavaḥ dṛśyate yatas kvacid guṇa yoge agi phala niṣpattiḥ na dṛśyate anyatra tu mleccha ādau dṛśyate iti ced na kāraṇa tve sati eva prabala karma pratibandhena tad ānīm asattve api kāla antare phala utpatti sambhavāt atas eva ākṛta iṣṭeḥ mleccha ādeḥ putra janma sambhavaḥ bhava antara saṃbhūtam tadīyam putrūkā meṣṭi sadbhāvam sūcayati tatas ca anṛta tva doṣāt putra kāma iṣṭi vākyasya asādhana uddaśa vākya vat aprāmāṇyam ayuktam iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.1.65	 idānīm vyāghāta doṣa parihāram āha abhyupetya kāla bhede doṣa vacanāt na tāvat vihitasya viśeṣa traya sahitasya prātaḥkālasya aviśeṣatas pratiṣedhāt kāla mātra pratiṣedha mukhena udita anudita ādi vākyena homa mātra pratiṣedhāt vā havane vyāghāta doṣaḥ saṃbhavati kasmāt ādhāna samaye vihita madhye kañcana kāla homa adhikaraṇa tvena abhyupetya tasya kālasya paścāt bhede bhaṅge sati tasya doṣa vacanāt nindā vacanāt yaḥ sva abhyupetam kālam bhinatti tasya āhutayaḥ deva sāra meya bhakṣyāḥ bhavanti na homāḥ apūrva sādhanāḥ iti na ca etāvatā havana mātrasya prātar kāla sambandha mātrasya vā pratiṣedhaḥ sambhavati tasya anīdṛśa puruṣa viṣaye sa avakāśa tvāt iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.1.66	 yaḥ punar sāmidheni abhyāse punarukta doṣaḥ sa na asti iti āha anuvāda upapatteḥ ca caḥ hetu arthaḥ yasmāt ekādaśasāmidhenīnām madhye prathama uttamayoḥ tris abhyāsena pañcadaśa tvam sāmidhenīnām siddhyati idam aham bhrātṛvyam pañcadaśa āreṇa vāc vajreṇa vā iti mantra varṇa avagata sāmidhenī pañcadaśa tva saṃpatti artha tvāt anuvādasya tad upapatteḥ na anarthakaḥ abhyāsaḥ evam punarukti doṣaḥ api na saṃbhavati iti prāmāṇyam siddhyati tatas ca anṛta vyāghāta punarukti doṣa yukta vāc ca tritaya dṛṣṭānta avaṣṭambhena vākya antarāṇām api aprāmāṇyam anumīyate iti yat uktam tat asaṃbaddham iti sūtra catuṣṭaya tātparya arthaḥ 
NTD_2.1.67–2.1.68	 na ca pratiṣedha hetu uddhāra mātrāt eva vedānām prāmāṇyam siddhyati iti tad prāmāṇya hetūn upapādayan prathamam tāvat sambhāvanā hetum āha vidhi artha vāda anuvāda vacana viniyogāt vidhiḥ anuvādaḥ artha vādaḥ iti anena artha vibhāgavat tvena vacanasya vedasya viniyogāt tathābhūta artha vibhāgavat mad u ādi vākya vat veda prāmāṇyam saṃbhāvyate iti sūtra arthaḥ tatra vidheḥ lakṣaṇam āha vidhiḥ vidhāyakaḥ yat vākyam vidhāyakam ajñātaḥ kam kartṛ apa īkṣita upāya tā jñāpana dvāreṇa puruṣasya pravartanam karoti sa vidhiḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ yathā agnihotram juhuyāt svarga kāmaḥ iti 
NTD_2.1.69	 arthavāda lakṣaṇam āha stutiḥ nindā parakṛtiḥ purākalpaḥ iti artha vādaḥ vidhi pratiṣedhayoḥ pravṛtti nivṛtti artham yat prāśastya vacanam saḥ artha vādaḥ yathā sarva jitā viśvedevāḥ sarvam ajayan= ityādi yathā vā saḥ arodīt yat rodot iti evamādi atra sphuṭatara prāśastya aprāśastya pratītyabhāvāt para kṛti purā kalpayoḥ bhedena upanyāsaḥ udāharaṇantu hutvā meva agre abhidhārayanti atha pṛṣat ājyam iti tasmāt vā etena purā brāhmaṇāḥ bahiṣpavamāna stonāḥ sāma stoma maḥ tauṣan iti evamādi ca 
NTD_2.1.70–2.1.71	 vidhi vihitasya anuvacanam anuvādaḥ prayojana antara śeṣa tayā vidhi vihitasya arthasya vidhāyakasya vā śabdasya yat anuvacanam paścāt bhāṣaṇam saḥ anuvādaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ udāharaṇam darśa pūrṇamāsābhyām iṣṭvā somena yajeta iti ayaḥ aśvamedhena yajate ityādi na anuvāda punaruktayoḥ viśeṣaḥ śabda abhyāsa upapatteḥ pratīta artha śabda abhyāsasya ubhayatra upapadyamāna tvāt anuvādasya punar uktāt viśeṣaḥ na asti iti vyarthaḥ anuvādaḥ punarukta vat iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.1.72	 śīghratara gamana upadeśa vat abhyāsa an na aviśeṣaḥ yathā śīghram āgamyatām iti uktvā śīghrataram gamyatām iti ukte tarapā kriyā atiśayasya śīghra śabdāt pratītasya pratīteḥ na punar ukta doṣaḥ tathā śīghram śīghram gamyatām iti asya sātatya avadhāraṇa ādi atiśayasya pratīteḥ na dvitīya śīghra śabda vaiyarthyam evam anuvāde api prayojana antarasya pūrvam apratītasya pratīteḥ na punar uktāt prayojana antara rahitāt aviśeṣaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.1.73^1	 tat evam veda prāmāṇya sambhāvanā hetum abhidhāya idānīm sākṣāt prāmāṇyam āha mantra āyurveda prāmāṇya vat ca tad prāmāṇyam āpta prāmāṇyāt tasya vadasya prāmāṇyam tat prāmāṇyam kutas āpta prāmāṇyāt āptasya yathāvat dṛṣṭa arthasya tathā eva upadeṣṭuḥ prāmāṇyāt pramāṇa bhūta tvāt mantra āyurveda prāmāṇya vat mantrasya viṣa nirharaṇa ādi hetoḥ āyurvedasya vārogya kāmaḥ pathyam aśnīyāt iti evamādeḥ prāmāṇyam vat ca śabdaḥ prāmāṇya saṃbhāvanā hetu anukarṣaṇa arthaḥ etat uktam bhavati pramāṇam vedāḥ āpta praṇīta tvāt mantra āyurveda vat mantra āyurveda vākyeṣu tad pratipādita artha avisaṃvādi tvena tad pramāṇe tu āpta tva niścayāt yathā prāmāṇyam siddham ta mā vedeṣu āpta praṇīta tva niścayāt prāmāṇyam siddham iti nanu yathāvat dṛṣṭasya tathā eva upadeṣdṛ tvam āpta tvam iti uktam na ca etat mantra āyurveda vākyeṣu saṃbhavati tad pratipāditānām auṣadhānām tad saṃyoga anantaram mantra akṣarā vāpa udvāpa bhedānām ca anantānām aniyata ādi gdeśa kāla varti tvena tad anvaya vyatirekayoḥ asmad ādi vat aśakya grahaṇa tvāt 
NTD_2.1.73^2	 tatas ca āpta praṇīta tvam mantra āyurveda vākyānām veda vākyānām iva siddham iti katham tat dṛṣṭāntena prāmāṇya niścayaḥ mā evam sarveṣām api veda tad anuyāyinām śabdānām sarvajña pūrvaka tvena āpta praṇīta tva niścayāt tathā hi vivāda adhyāsitāni sarvajña kartṛkāṇi samagra lokayātrā nirvoḍha tve sati alaukikā artha abhidhāyaka tvāt yat asarvajña kartṛkam tad ukta sādhanam na bhavati yathā ca iti avandana ādi vākyam na ca tathā etāni tasmāt sarvajña kartṛkāṇi iti tat evam sarvajña pūrvaka tve siddhe tasya āśraya doṣa ādi asambhavena āpta tva niścayāt tad praṇītānām prāmāṇyam upapannam 
NTD_2.1.73^3	 āpta praṇīta laukika vākya vat na ca buddha ādīnām sarvajña tva sambhavaḥ tad sadbhāve pramāṇa abhāvāt tad āgama āśrayaṇe anyonya āśraya tvāt kṣiti ādi kartṛkatva anabhyupagamāt ca tatas ca tanu bhuvana ādi kārya viśeṣa anumita sarvajña tvena parama āptena bhagavatā bhargeṇa vedāḥ eva praṇītā na āgama antarāṇi tad tad kartṛ viśeṣa smṛti upagṛhītattvāt teṣām iti siddham āpta ukta tvena veda prāmāṇyam iti iti bhaṭṭa vāc īśvara viracitāyām nyāya sūtra tātparyadīpikāyām dvitīya adhyāyasya prathama āhnikam samāptam 
NTD_2.2.1	 atha idānīm catvāri eva pramāṇāni iti vibhāga uddeśaḥ na yuktaḥ iti āha na catuṣṭvam aitihya arthāpatti sambhava abhāva prāmāṇyāt iti ha ūcuḥ iti anirdiṣṭa pravaktṛkam pravāda pāramparyam aitihyam yathā vaṭe vaṭe yakṣaḥ prativasati iti arthāt anupapadyamānāt artha antarasya āpatti kalpanam arthāpattiḥ yathā asatsu megheṣu vṛṣṭiḥ na bhavati iti ukte satsu bhavati iti gamyate sambhavaḥ nāma avinābhāva vartinoḥ dvayoḥ ekatarasya grahaṇāditarasya sattā grahaṇam yathā droṇasya grahaṇāt āḍhakasya sat tā iti abhāvaḥ api māna virodhī yathā abhūtam varṣaṇa karma bhūtasya vāyu abhra saṃyogasya tat evam eteṣām api prāmāṇyāt prāmāṇyasya sambhavāt na catuṣṭvam eva pramāṇānām iti saṃkhyā aniyamaḥ siddhyati iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.2.2^1	 yadi api aitihi ādīni pramāṇāni tathā api pramāṇa catuṣṭayam na upapadyate iti yaḥ ayam pratiṣedhaḥ sa na pratiṣedhaḥ kasmāt  śabdaḥ aitihya anartha antara bhāvāt anumāne arthāpatti sambhava abhāva anartha antara bhāvāt ca apratiṣedhaḥ tathā hi aiti ha ūcuḥ vṛddhāḥ iti nirdiṣṭa pravaktṛkam pravāda pāramparyam aitihyam āpta upadeśaḥ śabdaḥ iti śabda lakṣaṇam na ativartate iti śabda pramāṇe tasya anartha antara bhāvaḥ atha anirdiṣṭa pravaktṛkam aitihyam tat apramāṇam eva aniścita mūla tvāt tathā asatsu megheṣu vṛṣṭiḥ na bhavati iti ukte satsu bhavati iti jñānam arthāpattiḥ satsu eva megheṣu vṛṣṭiḥ na bhavati iti anena arthena vinā arthe satsu vṛṣṭi abhāvasya anupapadyamāna tvena tasya tasya gamaka tvāt sā ca iyam arthāpattiḥ 
NTD_2.2.2^2	 anumānena na artha antara bhūtāḥ kasmāt asati kāraṇe kārya abhāvasya sati bhāva tvena vyāpta tvāt evam avinābhā vinoḥ dvayoḥ ekasya grahaṇāditarasya grahaṇa sambhavaḥ anumānam eva dhūma ādi vat avinā abhāva balena eva gamaka tvāt tathā varṣa karma abhāvaḥ jñāyamānaḥ vāyu abhra saṃyogasya gamakaḥ abhavat na abhāvatayā pramāṇam kim tarhi dhūma ādi valliṅga tayā kim kāraṇam vidhāraka vāyu saṃyoga ādi pratibandhaka abhāva viśiṣṭasya varṣa karma hetu tva niścayena varṣa karma abhāvena vāyu abhra saṃyoga ādi pratibandhasya vyāpta tvāt tasmāt abhāvaḥ api anumānāt na arthantara bhūtaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.2.3–2.2.4	 tat evam aitihya ādīnām prāmāṇyam abhyupetya pramāṇeṣu antarbhāvaḥ kathitaḥ tatra artha āpatteḥ pramāṇa bhāvam asahamānaḥ pūrvapakṣayati arthāpattiḥ apramāṇam anaikāntika tvāt asatsu megheṣu vṛṣṭiḥ na bhavati iti ukte satsu bhavati iti jñānam arthāpattiḥ satsu api ekadā na bhavati iti apramāṇam anaikāntika tvāt kim tarhi satsu eva bhavati iti bhavanasya meghavyāptiḥ tatas ca na anaikāntika tvam aniyatattvam arthāpatteḥ anartha āpattau= artha apatti abhimānāt kasmāt anartha āpattau satsu megheṣu vṛṣṭiḥ na bhavati eva iti evaṃrūpāyām arthāpatti abhimānāt samyak arthāpatti bhramāt na artha āpatteḥ aprāmāṇyam iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.2.5	 atha satsu eva bhavati iti ukta viṣaya vyatirekeṇa arthāpatteḥ viṣaya antaram satsu bhavati eva iti evaṃrūpam kalpayitvā anaikāntika tvam ucyate tarhi tad pratiṣedhe api samānam iti āha pratiṣedha aprāmāṇyam ca anaikāntika tvāt arthāpattiḥ apramāṇam anaikāntika tvāt iti yaḥ ayam pratiṣedhaḥ tasya aprāmāṇyam abhilaṣita artha asādhaka tvam kutas anaikāntika tvāt aniyata tvāt arthāpatti sattvasya apratiṣedhāt iti yathā arthāpatteḥ sva viṣaya vyatirekeṇa viṣaya antaram kalpayitvā tvayā aprāmāṇyam ucyate tathā tad pratiṣedha vyāpi tat prāmāṇya lakṣaṇa sva viṣaya vyatirekeṇa viṣaya antara sattām kalpayitvā tad apratiṣedhena aprāmāṇyam mayā api vaktum śakyam eva iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.2.6	 atha sva viṣaya vyatirekeṇa viṣaya antara kalpanama yuktam atiprasaṅgāt iti yadi pratiṣedhasya sva viṣaye prāmāṇyam abhyupagamyate tarhi tad artha āpattau= api samānam iti āha tad prāmāṇye vā na artha apatti aprāmāṇyam tasya pratiṣedhasya sva viṣaye arthāpatti prāmāṇya pratiṣedhe prāmāṇye na arthāpatti aprāmāṇyam artha āpatteḥ api sva viṣaye satsu eva megheṣu vṛṣṭiḥ bhavati iti evam rūpeṇa aprāmāṇyam sā ca iyam apramāṇam anaikāntika tvāt aniyata tvāt iti katham aniya tattvam satsu api megheṣu kadācid vṛṣṭiḥ na bhavati iti atas ca apramāṇa tvāt arthāpatteḥ pramāṇeṣu antar bhava kathanam ayuktam iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.2.7^1	 pariharati na anaikāntika tvam arthāpatteḥ anartha āpattau= artha āpatti abhimāṇāt asatsu megheṣu vṛṣṭiḥ na bhavati iti ukte satsu bhavati eva iti na iyam arthāpattiḥ kim tarhi prāmāṇyam eva atas ca arthāpatteḥ pramāṇa tvāt antarbhāva kathanam eva yuktam iti etena sataḥ gṛha abhāva darśanena bahis bhāva kathanam iti etat api parāḥ tam sataḥ gṛha abhāva darśanena liṅgena bahirbhāva anumānāt tathā hi yatra khalu san= ekatra na asti tadā anyatra asti iti sva śarīraḥ eva vyāpti grahaḥ sukaraḥ na ca asya sadbhāvena gṛha abhāvaḥ śakyaḥ apahnotum yena asau= asiddhaḥ hetuḥ syāt na api gṛha abhāvena sattva apahnavaḥ yena anupapadyamānam sattvam ātmānam na bahis avasthāpayet iti gṛha abhāvena sattvam viruddhayate iti ced na vikalpa anupapatteḥ 
NTD_2.2.7^2	 sattva mātram vā gṛha abhāvena viruddhyate gṛhe sattvam vā na tāvat sattva mātram yatra kvacana sattvena gṛhe asattvasya asamāna viṣaya virodha abhāvāt deśa sāmānyena gṛha viśeṣa ākṣepaḥ api pākṣikaḥ iti samāna viṣaya tayā virodhaḥ iti ced na pramāṇa niścitasya sāṃśayikena pratikṣepa ayogāt na api pramāṇa viniścitaḥ eva gṛha abhāvaḥ gṛhe sattvam pratikṣipan sattva mātram pratikṣeptum sāṃśayika tvam vā tasya netum arhati asamāna viṣaya tvena sattva mātra pratikṣepasya tat sāṃśayika tvasya vā āpādanatva ayogāt na api sattva asattva grāhakayoḥ pramāṇayoḥ avirodha āpādaka tvena viṣaya vyavasthāpana sambhavaḥ avacchinna anavacchinna viṣayayoḥ pramāṇayoḥ asamāna viṣaya tvena virodha abhāvāt tasmāt sataḥ gṛha abhāvena liṅgena bahis bhāvam anumīyate iti sūtra tātparya arthaḥ 
NTD_2.2.8	 abhāvaḥ tarhi pramāṇam iti āha na abhāvaḥ pramāṇam prameya asiddheḥ atra abhāva śabdena tat jñānam vivakṣitam abhāvasya svarūpeṇa pramāṇa tva asambhavāt tatas ca na abhāva jñānam pramāṇam viṣayasya prameyasya abhāvasya asiddheḥ na asti iti vyāhāra vyavahārayoḥ vastu mātra viṣaya tvena kālpanika tvena vā upapadyamāna tvena abhāvasya abhāvaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.2.9^1	 pariharati lakṣiteṣu alakṣaṇa lakṣita tvāt alakṣitānām tat prameya siddhiḥ alakṣitāni vāsāṃsi ānayā iti ukte kenacid lakṣaṇena lakṣiteṣu keṣucid vāsassu anupādeyeṣu dṛṣṭa lakṣaṇaḥ puruṣaḥ upādeyānām alakṣitānām vāsasām tad lakṣaṇa abhāvam paśyan tena tāni eva vāsāṃsi pṛthakkṛtya upādatte na lakṣitāni atas ca lakṣaṇa abhāva jñānam tad abhāva viṣayam tad upādāne pramāṇam bhavati iti na abhā= asya prameya asiddhiḥ vāsaḥ mātra viṣayam lakṣaṇa abhāva jñānam na tad vyatirikta abhāva viṣayam iti ced kim idam vāsaḥ mātram nāma kim vāsāṃsi āhosvit anyat ca 
NTD_2.2.9^2	 na tāvat pūrvaḥ kalpaḥ lakṣiteṣu api vāsassu vāsaḥ rūpasya vidyamāna tvena lakṣaṇa abhāva prasaṅgāt na api dvitīyaḥ kalpaḥ anyat abhāvaḥ iti saṃjñā mātra bhedāt na ca dṛśye pratiyogini vastu mātra upalabhyaḥ bhāva vyavahāra hetuḥ iti yuktam tadānīm dṛśyamānasya api pratiyoginaḥ dṛśya tva anapāyena tatra api tad vyavahāra prasaṅgāt na ca kālpanika tvam abhāva vyavahārasya kalpanāyāḥ api samyak jñāna mūla tvāt tasmāt asti vastu antaram abhāvaḥ iti tad jñānasya upādāna ādi viṣaye pramāṇa tvam sambhavati iti tasya antar bhāva kathanam eva yuktam iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.2.10–2.2.11	 pradhvaṃsa abhāvaḥ iti manvānaḥ codayati asati arthe na abhāvaḥ iti ced yatra yasya abhāvaḥ tatra tasya abhāvena bhavitavyam na ca ālakṣiteṣu vāsassu lakṣaṇāni santi yena tatra teṣāma bhāvaḥ upapadyate tasmāt alakṣiteṣu vāsassu lakṣaṇa ātmake asati na tad abhāvaḥ śakyaḥ pratipādayitum iti sūtra arthaḥ pariharati na anya lakṣaṇa upapatteḥ na pradhvaṃsa abhāvaḥ eva abhāvaḥ kintu itaretarābhāvaḥ api tatas ca anya lakṣaṇa upapatteḥ anyeṣu vāsassu eva lakṣaṇānām upapatteḥ anyatra alakṣiteṣu vāsassa teṣām lakṣitānām itaretara abhāvasya upapatteḥ vidyamāna tvena pradhvaṃsa abhāva mātra avalambanena yat coditam tat na asti iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.2.12–2.2.13	 dūṣayati tad siddheḥ alakṣiteṣu ahetuḥ teṣām lakṣaṇānām siddheḥ lakṣiteṣu iva ālakṣiteṣu api vidyamāna tvāt tatra teṣām abhāvaḥ na asti bhāva abhāvayoḥ virodhāt iti na abhāva jñānam alakṣita upādāne hetuḥ na pramāṇam iti sūtra arthaḥ māna tvāt bhāva abhāvayoḥ bhinna adhikaraṇa tvena virodha abhāvāt yat uktam bhāva abhāvayoḥ virodha āditya abhiprāya antara kalpanam tat na iti sūtra arthaḥ pariharati na lakṣaṇa avasthita apekṣa siddheḥ na mayā sarvatra lakṣaṇānām abhāvaḥ pratipādyate kim tarhi lakṣaṇena saha yāni avasthitāni vāsāṃsi tāni apekṣya tatra teṣām abhāvaḥ atas lakṣaṇa avasthita apekṣayā teṣām siddheḥ vidya lakṣiteṣu eva lakṣaṇānām bhāvam asiddhāntinā kathitam iti adhyāropyaḥ 
NTD_2.2.14	 na kevalam itaretara abhāva balena lakṣaṇānām alakṣiteṣu abhāva sambhavaḥ kim tarhi prāc abhāva balena api iti āha prāk utpatteḥ abhāva upapatteḥ ca yathā utpatteḥ paścāt pradhvaṃsanena abhāvaḥ yathā ca itaratra vidyamānasya itaratra abhāvaḥ tathā utpatteḥ prāk pūrvasmin kāle abhāva upapatteḥ api lakṣaṇānām abhāva upapatteḥ ca alakṣiteṣu vāsassu lakṣaṇa abhāvaḥ asti iti sarvam avadātam iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.2.15	 tat evam śabda parīkṣā prastutya tad prāmāṇya purassaram vibhāga uddeśaḥ parīkṣitaḥ samprati śabda parīkṣā śeṣam vartayiṣyan saṃśaya kāraṇam āha vimarśa hertu anuyoge ca vipratipatteḥ saṃśayaḥ vyāhata artha pravādaḥ vipratipattiḥ tasmāt saṃśayaḥ bhavati tathā hi eke tāvat bruvate nityaḥ śabdaḥ abhivyakta dharmā iti apare bruvate anityaḥ śabdaḥ utpatti dharmā iti tat evam vyāhata artha pravāda viṣayam śabdam upalabhamānasya kim atra tattvam iti saṃśayaḥ bhavati iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.2.16^1	 tatra anityaḥ śabdaḥ iti etat tattvam kutas  ādimattvāt aindriyaka tvāt kṛtaka vat upacārāt ca ādiḥ yoniḥ kāraṇam tat yasya asti saḥ ādimān tasya bhāvaḥ tattvam tasmāt ādimattvāt etat uktam bhavati anityaḥ śabdaḥ kāraṇavat tvāt yat yat kāraṇa vat tat tat anityam dṛṣṭam yathā ghaṭaḥ tathā ca ayam śabdaḥ tasmāt anityaḥ iti yuktam kim punar idam anitya tvam nāma pradhvaṃsa abhāva upalakṣitā sattā yasmāt pradhvaṃsa abhāva upalakṣita vastu sattā saṃbandhi padārthaḥ anityaḥ iti vyapadiśyate tasmāt sā eva anitya tā iti kim punar śabdasya kāraṇam saṃyogaḥ vibhāgaḥ ca nanu saṃyoga vibhāgau na śabdasya utpādakau api tu abhivyañjakau= iti ādimat tvam asiddham iti ced atas āha aindriyaka tvāt iti indriya pratyāsattigrāhya aindriyakaḥ tasya bhāvaḥ aindriyaka tvam atra śabda nitya tva vādinaḥ trayaḥ pakṣāḥ sambhavanti sarve anāśrita āśritāḥ vyāpinaḥ vyoma vat nityāḥ iti ekaḥ ākāśa āśritāḥ vyāpinaḥ nityāḥ iti aparaḥ gandha ādi saha vṛttayaḥ bherī ādi dravyeṣu sanniviṣṭāḥ sthāyinaḥ iti anyaḥ 
NTD_2.2.16^2	 yadi punar saṃyoga vibhāgau śabdasya abhivyañjakau syātām tadā samāna deśa samāna indriya grāhyāṇām śabdānām pratiniyata vyañjaka vyaṅgya tva abhāvena śrotra saṃskāra pakṣe sarveṣām śabdānām grahaṇam viṣaya saṃskāra pakṣe sarvaiḥ ekasya grahaṇam iti doṣau syātām na api bherī śaṅkha patra sthāne abhivyaktasya śabdasya niṣkriyasya śabdasya śrotra deśa pratyāsattiḥ sambhavati na ca ahaṅkārika tayā śrotra indriyasya tatra vṛttiḥ sambhavati indriyāṇām bhautika tvena āhaṅkārika tva pratiṣedhāt 
NTD_2.2.16^3	 na ca abhighāta preritena vāyunā stimita vāyu apanaya paramparāyām satyām śrotra deśa avasthitānām śabdānām tad pratyāsattiḥ sambhavati iti vācyam vyañjaka niyama abhāvena yugapad upalabdhi prasaṅgāt na ca etat dṛṣṭam iṣṭam vā tasmāt abhivyakti pakṣe śabdasya indriya pratyāsatti grāhya tvam aindriyaka tvam na syāt asti ca idam aindriyaka tvam atas avagacchāmaḥ saṃyoga vibhāgau śabdasya utpādakau= iti tad utpannaḥ śabdaḥ sarva dikkāni sārvadikāni śabda antarāṇi vīcī taraṅga nyāyena ārabhante tatra yaḥ śrotra deśe samutpannaḥ śabdaḥ sa tena gṛhyate iti aindriyaka tvena ādima tvam śabdasya siddham iti 
NTD_2.2.16^4	 nanu mā bhūt asiddha tvam ādimattvasya hetoḥ tathā api saḥ eva ayam gakāraḥ ityādi pratyabhijñāyā abādhita viṣama tvāt kāla atyaya apadiṣṭa tvam asti eva atas āha kṛtaka vat upacārāt ca atra kṛtaka vat upacāraḥ iti anena śabda bheda pratyayam upalakṣayati yasmāt tīvram tīvrataram tīvratamam mandam mandataram mandatamam iti kṛtakam upacaryate sukha duḥkha vartī vat prāyas a yam gakāraḥ manda mandaḥ ayam gakāraḥ anunāsikaḥ ayam gakāraḥ iti nāri śārikā prabhedeṣu bheda prathā puṃsām sabhā tasmāt bhinnāḥ eva gakārāḥ tad tad kāraṇaiḥ samutpadyante 
NTD_2.2.16^5	 teṣu pratyabhijñā gatvā ādi sāmānya nibandhanā sādṛśya nibandhanā vā bhavati iti na ādimattvasya hetoḥ kāla atyaya apadiṣṭa tvam āpādayitum śaknoti iti na ca ayam bheda pratyayaḥ aupādhikaḥ iti vastum śakyam vikalpa anupapatteḥ tathā hi aupādhika tvam ānubhāvika tvam vā syāt upapatti gocaraḥ vā na tāvadānubhāvikam nara ādi upādhi bhedam aviduṣaḥ api kāṇḍa paṭa ādi āvṛte nara ādau jāyamāna tvāt na api upapatti gocaraḥ pramāṇa abhāvāt na hi śabda samavāyinaḥ bheda pratyayasya aupādhika tve kiñcana pramāṇam asti mukhasya iva maṇi kṛpāṇa darpaṇa ādareṣu bhinna parimāṇa tayā pratīyamānasya ekatvena ca iyam pratyabhijñā pramāṇam anyathā api upapadyamāna tvāt 
NTD_2.2.16^6	 na tāvat dhvani dharmāḥ tālu ādi saṃyoga vibhāga dharmaḥ tīvra manda tva ādayaḥ śabde samāropyante iti vācyam teṣām agrahaṇena āropa asambhavāt na ca dhvanīnām tālu ādi saṃyoga vibhāgānām vā dharmāḥ śrotreṇa gṛhyante tad anya dharma vat na ca tadānīm smṛtyā vā pramāṇa antareṇa vā upanīyante aśakya tvāt tasmāt na samāropaḥ iti maṇḍūka vasā akta akṣāṇām anavagatā bhūta uragāṇām api vaṃśeṣu uraga samāropa vat atra api samāropaḥ iti ced na tatra aropya āropa viṣaya grahaṇa purassara tva sambhavāt vaṃśānām tāvat asti bhūyas sārūpyam urageṇa tena gṛhītāḥ śaknuvanti smārayitum uragam 
NTD_2.2.16^7	 na ca vaṃśa ākāra grahaṇam viśeṣa darśanam asti iti vācyam maṇḍūka vasā añjanena vihita tvāt na ca agṛhīta sarpasya bhavati iti śakyam vaktum asmin janmani janma antare sarpa grahaṇa sambhavāt dhvani dharmāḥ tu tīvra manda anunāsika tva ādiḥ asmin= iva janmani janma antare api aśakya grahaḥ tasmāt varṇaḥ tīvra manda manda anunāsika tva ādiḥ pratīyamānaḥ varṇa dharmaḥ iti na bheda pratyayasya aupādhika tvam upapattyā siddhyati na pratyabhijñāyai abādhita viṣaya tvāt kāla atyaya apadiṣṭa tvam anitya tva hetoḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.2.17	 śabda anitya tva sādhanāya hetu tritayam uktam pūrva sūtreṇa iti matvā vyabhicāram āha na ghaṭa abhāva sāmānya nitya tvāt nityeṣu api anitya vat upacārāt ca kāraṇavataḥ khalu ghaṭa abhāvasya pradhvaṃsa abhāvasya ekasya ca sāmānyasya ghaṭasya pradeśa kaṃbalasya pradeśāḥ itivat ātmanaḥ pradeśe ākāśasya pradeśaḥ iti kṛta vat upacaryamāṇasya ātma ākāśa ādeḥ nitya tva darśanena vyabhicārāt ādimattva ādibhyaḥ hetubhyaḥ śabdasya anitya tvam siddhyati iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.2.18–2.2.20^1	 pariharati tattva bhākta tvāt na tattvasya vighātāt santāna anumāna viśeṣaṇāt kāraṇa dravyasya pradeśa śabdena abhidhānāt avyabhicāraḥ iti vākya śeṣaḥ nitya tvam iti atra pradhvaṃsa abhāva anupalakṣita vastu sattā tattvam na ca asau pradhvaṃsa abhāve sambhavati abhāvasya sva rūpa asattvena sattā saṃbandhi tva abhāvāt bhāktam tu nitya tvam asya bhavati iti nitya vat nityaḥ iti upacārāt yatra yathā jātīyakaḥ śabdaḥ tathā jātīyakam kiñcid nityam dṛṣṭam iti na ādimattvasya vyabhicāraḥ tattva bhāktayoḥ pāramārthikā pāramārthikayoḥ nānātvasya bhedasya vibhāgāt vibhakta tvāt iti na api aindriyaka tvasya nitya sāmānye samīkṣaṇāt vyabhicāraḥ kim kāraṇam tena śabda anitya tva sādhanāt kim tarhi tena kriyate santāna anumāna viśeṣaḥ yasmāt idam aindriyaka tvam anitya tvasya santāna pratītyā śrotra deśa samutpannasya śabdasya sambhavati na abhi vyaktasya nityasya abhivyañjaka niyama abhāvāt 
NTD_2.2.18–2.2.20^2	 tasmāt santāna anumāna viśeṣaṇāt hetoḥ aindriyaka tvasya apṛthak hetuka tvāt avyabhicāraḥ na ca api nityeṣu ātma ākāśa ādiṣu kṛtaka vat pradeśa vyapadeśa darśanena kṛtaka vat upacāra ādityasya vyabhicāraḥ kasmāt kāraṇa dravyasya pradeśa śabdena abhidhānāt yatra pradeśa śabdena vyabhicāraḥ kalaśa śakala kuliśa ādiṣu tatra pradeśa śabdena tad kāraṇam abhidhīyate na ca īdṛśaḥ pradeśaḥ ātma ākāśa ādiṣu samasti teṣām nitya tvena kāraṇa abhāvāt yadi api pradeśa vat dravya sāmānyam syāt vyāpya vṛtti saṃyoga ādhārasya vidyamāna tvena bhāktaḥ tathā api anitya vat mukhasya pradeśa vyapadeśa abhāvāt na kṛtaka vat upacārāt upacāra ādityasya vyabhicāraḥ arthaḥ tasmāt kāraṇa dravyasya pradeśa śabdena abhidhānena nityeṣu kṛtaka vat upacārasya apāramārthika tvāt na ca kṛtaka vat upacārāt iti svarūpeṇa anitya tve hetuḥ kim tarhi śabda bheda pratyayasya pratijñā pratyanīkasya upalakṣakaḥ tasmāt yathā ukta vyākhyāne vyabhicāraḥ trayāṇām hetūnām iti sūtra tritaya arthaḥ 
NTD_2.2.21	 itas api anityaḥ śabdaḥ iti āha prāc uccāraṇa ādi anupalabdheḥ āvaraṇa ādi anupalabdheḥ ca uccāraṇāt prāk na asti śabdaḥ kasmāt anupalabdheḥ tadānīm anupalabhyamāna tvāt nanu sataḥ api anupalabdhiḥ āvaraṇa ādinā sambhavati iti ced na iti a ahaa āvaraṇa anupalabdheḥ ca iti pramāṇena anupalabhyamāna tvena asattvāt iti tat ayam arthaḥ uccāraṇa anantaram upalabhyamānaḥ śabdaḥ sva upalambha kālāt prāk na asti āvaraṇa ādi anupalabdhi kāraṇa abhāve sati tadānīm na upalabhyate tad sva upalambha kālāt prāk na asti yathā sukham tathā śabdaḥ tasmāt sva upalambha kālāt prāk na asti anena eva nyāyena sva upalambha kālāt ūrdhvam api na asti śabdasya anitya tvam siddham iti 
NTD_2.2.22	 tat etat jātyā dūṣayati tad anupalabdheḥ anupalambhāt āvaraṇa upapattiḥ tasyāḥ āvaraṇa anupalabdheḥ upalabdhiḥ asti na vā yadi asti tadānīm upalabbhi tva hāniḥ upalabdhi anupalabdhyoḥ virodhāt atha na asti tarhi anupalambhāt āvaraṇa anupalabdheḥ asattvena āvaraṇa upalabdhau satyām āvaraṇa upapatiḥ āvaraṇa sadbhāvaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.2.23	 atha etad pakṣa ukta doṣa apajihīrṣayā anupalabhyamānā api āvaraṇa anupalabdhiḥ asti iti ibhyupagamyate tarhi anupalabhyamānam api āvaraṇam asti iti na āvaraṇa anupapattiḥ iti āha anupalambhāt api anupalabdhi sadbhāva anna āvaraṇa anupapattiḥ anuḥ iti anupalambhāt anupalambhāt hetoḥ yathā āvaraṇa anupalabghi sadbhāvaḥ tadā tasmāt eva anupalambhāt nimittāt āvaraṇa anupapattiḥ api na asti iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.2.24	 tat etat nirākaroti anupalambha ātmaka tvāt anupalabdheḥ ahetuḥ āvaraṇa anupalabdheḥ upalabdhi virodhi tvena anupalambhāt asattvena āvaraṇa upalabdhiḥ iti yaḥ hetuḥ āvaraṇa sadbhāve yaḥ vā āvaraṇa anupalabdheḥ anupalambhe api sambhavat anupalambhā viśeṣāt āvaraṇa upapattiḥ iti sa na hetuḥ tasmāt anupalambha ātmaka tvāt anupalabdheḥ āvaraṇa anupalabdheḥ anupalambha ātmaka tvena niṣedha viṣaya pramāṇena upalabdhau virodha abhāvena āvaraṇa upapatteḥ sattvena vidhi viṣaya pramāṇena āvaraṇa upalabdheḥ asattvena āvaraṇa anupapatteḥ tasmāt āvaraṇa anupalabdhi vat tad āvaraṇa siddhiḥ iti ajñātvedam ucyate iti sūtrāthaḥ 
NTD_2.2.25–2.2.26	 tat evam sva pakṣa sādhanam uktvā para pakṣa sādhanam dūṣayitum upanyasyati asparśa tvāt nityaḥ śabdaḥ asparśa tvāt ākāśa vaditi sūtra arthaḥ dūṣayati na karma anitya tvāt na hi yaḥ yaḥ sparśaḥ sa sarvaḥ nityaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ iti yaḥ vā nityaḥ na bhavati sa sparśaḥ api na bhavati iti vā vyāptiḥ asti anityena karmaṇā bhavataḥ vyabhicāra siddheḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.2.27–2.2.29	 na api samavyāptikam anayoḥ iti āha na aṇoḥ nitya tvāt ardha sparśavataḥ paramāṇoḥ nitya tvāt kṛtaka tva anitya tva vadarspa nitya tvayoḥ nasam avyāptiḥ asti iti sūtra arthaḥ saṃpradānam tarhi śabda sthāyi tve hetuḥ iti āha saṃpradānāt saṃpradīyamānam ghaṭa ādi vyavasthitam dṛṣṭam tathā śabdaḥ iti sthāyi tva siddhiḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ dūṣayati tad antarāla anupalabdheḥ ahetuḥ saṃpradīyamāna ghaṭa ādi vastu yatas apaiti yasmai ca dīyate tayoḥ antarāle samupalabhyate na tathā śabdaḥ upalabhyate tasmāt saṃpradīyamāna tvam sthāyi tve na hetuḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.2.30	 nanu mā bhūt pratyakṣeṇa antarāle śabdasya upalabdhiḥ tadā hi anumānena upalabdhiḥ asti kim anumānam adhyāpanam yat adhyāpyate dātrā saṃprati prāpyate tad antarāle avasthitam dṛṣṭam yathā ghaṭa ādi tathā ca śabdaḥ iti atas āha adhyāpanāt apratiṣedhaḥ nṛtta adhyāpana vat antarāle anavasthitasya api śabdasya adhyāpanāt antarālāva sthāne śabdasya anadhyāpanam hetuḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.2.31–2.2.32	 ayam tarhi hetuḥ avasthānaḥ iti āha abhyāsāt yat abhyasyamānam tat avasthitam dṛṣṭam yathā pañca kṛtvas paśyati daśa kṛtvas paśyati iti daśa tvena abhyasya māna rūpam tathā daśa kṛtvas adhīyate pañca kṛtvas adhīyate iti abhyasyate śabdaḥ tasmāt sthāyi iti sūtra arthaḥ dūṣayati na anyatve api abhyāsasya upacārāt dvis nṛtyatu bhavān tris nṛtyatu bhavān dvis anṛtyat tris anṛtyat dvis agnihotram jahoti dvis bhuṅkte ityādiṣu nartana ādi kriyāṇām anavasthāyi tve api abhyāsa upacārāt abhyāsaḥ śabdasya sthāyi tve na hetuḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.2.33–2.2.34	 atra samyak uttaram apaśyaṃchabda nitya tva vādī chalena pratyavatiṣṭhate anyat anyasmāt ananya tvāt ananyat iti anya tā bhāvaḥ anyat nāma vastu svarūpāt anyat anan yat vā yadi ananyat tarhi ananya tvāt anya ta abhāvaḥ atha anyat tathā api anya tā bhāvaḥ anyasmāt ananya tvāt avyatirikta tvāt iti sūtra arthaḥ anya parihāra sūtram atadbhāve na asti ananya tā tayoḥ itaretara apekṣa tva siddheḥ tad abhāve tasya anyasya abhāve na asti ananya tā kasmāt tayoḥ itaretara apekṣa tva siddheḥ tayoḥ anyā ananyayoḥ madhye ananya tvasya tvayā abhyupagatasya anya apekṣa tva siddheḥ anya pratiṣedha ātmakasya ananyasya anādi abhyupagame śakti abhyupagama tvena ananya vastu siddheḥ anya bhāvaḥ iti yat uktam pūrva sūtre tat na asti iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.2.35–2.2.36	 idam tarhi hetuḥ iti āha vināśa kāraṇa anupalabdheḥ yadi anityaḥ syāt chavdaḥ tadānīm ghaṭa ādiṣu iva vināśa kāraṇam api upalabhyeta tasmāt vināśa kāraṇa anupalabdheḥ na ayam anityaḥ śabdaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ tat etat sāmya āpādanena dūṣayati aśravaṇa kāraṇa anupalabdheḥ satata śravaṇa prasaṅgaḥ yadi nityaḥ śabdaḥ tadānīm sarvadā śrūyeta tasmāt aśravaṇa kāraṇa anupalavdheḥ avidyamānasya śabdasya kadācid aśravaṇa kāraṇam abhivyañjaka abhāva ādinā upapadyate tasmin niyama niṣedhena tasya eva abhivyañjakasya pratiṣiddha tvāt kasmāt anitya pakṣe vināśa kāraṇa anupalabdheḥ avināśa vat nitya pakṣe api aśravaṇa kāraṇa anupalabdhaḥ satata śravaṇa prasaṅgaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.2.37	 nanu abhihanyamāneṣu ghaṇṭā ādi dravyeṣu tāratara tāratam ādi śruti bheda bhinnāḥ śabdāḥ śanaiśśanais śrūyante śruti vināśa kāraṇa anupalabdhiḥ ca na asti iti āha upalabhyamāne ca anupalabdheḥ asadbhāvāt anapadeśaḥ śabda santāna upapādana samaye kārya kāraṇa ubhaya virodhi tva kathana anumānāt upalabhyamāne śabdasya vināśa kāraṇe tad upalabdheḥ asadbhāvāt vināśa kāraṇa anupalabdhiḥ iti ayam anapadeśaḥ ahetuḥ asiddha tvāt iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.2.38^1	 nanu abhihanyamāneṣu ghaṇṭā ādi dravyeṣu tārataratama ādi śruti bheda bhinnāḥ śabdāḥ śanais śanais śrūyante na ca anitya tva pakṣe tādṛśa śruti bheda ghaṇṭā ādi dravya saṃsthaḥ tasmāt aupādhika bheda bhinnāḥ śabdāḥ tad abhighāta janita saṃskāreṇa tādṛśena vyajyante iti ced mā evam abhivyakti pakṣe śrutiḥ bhedasya asambhavāt tathā hi na tāvat avasthitena saṃskāreṇa śruti bhedaḥ tasya eka rūpa tvāt na api santāna vartinā ekena eva saṃskāreṇa abhivyañjaka niyata śravaṇa kāraṇa anupalabdheḥ avidyamānasya śabdasya kadācid aśravaṇa kāraṇam abhivyañjaka abhāva ādinā upapadyate 
NTD_2.2.38^2	 tasmin niyama niṣedhena tasya evabhivyañjakasya pratiṣiddha tvāt sarva śabda upalabdhi prasaṅgāt na api aupādhika tvam pūrvam eva pratiṣiddha tvāt santāna vartinā ghaṇṭā ādi dravya saṃsthitena saṃskāreṇa samutpadyante iti vaktum yuktam nanu tādṛśasya śruti bheda hetoḥ saṃskārasya anupalabdheḥ asattvam iti uktam iti ced atra āha pāṇi nimitta praśleṣāt chavda abhāve na anupalabdhiḥ pāṇeḥ hastasya nimitta kāraṇa bhūtasya ghaṇṭā ādeḥ praśleṣāt prakṛṣṭa saṃbandhāt tāratama bheda bhinna śabda anupapattau satyām tad bheda hetoḥ kintarhi upalabdhiḥ eva vyatireka anuvidhāyi tvena prasiddha tvāt iti 
NTD_2.2.39	 siṃha avalokana nyāyena pūrva ukta hetum dūṣayati vināśa kāraṇa anupalabdheḥ ca avasthāne tad nitya tva prasaṅgaḥ pratyakṣeṇa śabda vināśa kāraṇasya anupalabdheḥ avasthāna abhyupagame tad nitya tva prasaṅgaḥ tasya śabda śravaṇasya pratyakṣeṇa anupalabhyamānaḥ vināśa kāraṇasya anitya tvena abhimatasya api nitya tva prasaṅgaḥ viśeṣa abhāvāt iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.2.40	 pratighāti dravya saṃśleṣāt śabda abhāvaḥ iti uktam tad saṃśleṣa samāna adhikaraṇasya sambhavati na vā na vyadhikaraṇasya atiprasaṅgāt tasmāt kampa samāna āśrayaḥ śabdaḥ na ākāśa āśrayaḥ iti atas āha asparśa tvāt apratiṣedhaḥ na ākāśa āśrayaḥ iti yaḥ ayam pratiṣedhaḥ sa na pratiṣedhaḥ kasmāt asparśa tvāt āśrayasya sparśavat dravya āśraya tve śrotra indriyasya na ahaṅkārite nyatra pravṛtti abhāvena agrahaṇa prasaṅgāt eka āśraya tve tatratya sparśa dravyasya api dravya tvāt santāna vṛttyā śrotra deśam āha tasya graha araṃbhavati iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.2.41	 gandha rasa rūpa sparśa śabda samudāye vīṇā dravyam tatra sthitaḥ eva śabdaḥ abhivyajyate iti yaiḥ ucyate tān nirācikīrṣuḥ āha vibhakti antara utpatteḥ ca samāse gāndhāra dhaivata madhyama ādi bhedena vibhāga tāratamya ādi śruti bhedena vi vibhakti antaram tasya upapattiḥ tasyāḥ vibhakti antara upapatteḥ samāse gandha ādi samudāye saṃniviṣṭaḥ śabdaḥ na abhivyajyate kasmāt vibhakti antara upapatteḥ na hi gandha rasa rūpa sparśa śabdānām samāse abhivyajyamānānām vibhakti antara upapattiḥ asti teṣām aikarūpyeṇa abhivyajyamāna tvāt tasmāt na gandha ādi saha vṛttiḥ śabdaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.2.42	 tat evam gandha ādi saha vṛttiḥ śabdaḥ iti sāṃkhya pakṣam dūṣayitvā tasya eva avasthitaḥ varṇa ātmakaḥ śabdaḥ abhivyajyate iti abhiprāya antaram dūṣayiṣyan saṃśayam āha vikāra ādeśa upadeśāt saṃśayaḥ vikāraḥ ca ādeśaḥ ca vikāra ādeśau tayoḥ upadeśaḥ tasmāt vikāra ādeśa upadeśāt dadhi atra iti atra kecid ikāraḥ yakāram āpadyate iti vikāram upadiśanti kecid ikārasya prayoge saṃhitā viṣaye yakārasya prayogam ādeśam upadiśanti tat evam vyākhyāti na vipratipattiḥ kim atra tattvam iti samīpa sthasya saṃśayaḥ bhavati iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.2.43	 tatra ādeśa pakṣaḥ eva tattvam na vikāra pakṣaḥ iti āha prakṛti vivṛddhau vikāra vivṛddheḥ prakṛti anuvidhānam vikāreṣu dṛṣṭam nārikela bījāt nārikela pādapaḥ nyagrodha bījāt nyagrodha pādapaḥ iti na ca iha tathā dīrgha ādi kārāt dīrghaḥ yakāraḥ hrasvāt hrasvaḥ iti prakṛti anuvidha anuvidhānam asti tasmāt prakṛti vṛddhau vikāra vṛddheḥ prakṛti anuvidhānāt vikāra pakṣaḥ na upapadyate iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.2.44	 tat etat sūtram yathā śruta artha bhrāntyā dūṣayati nyūna samādhika upalabdheḥ vikārāṇām hetuḥ nyūnaḥ ca samaḥ ca adhikaḥ ca nyūna sama adhikāḥ nyūna samādhika upalavdheḥ vikārāṇām madhye prakṛteḥ nyūnasya adhikasya samasya ca vikārasya mahat tūla piṇḍa nyagrodha bīja paramāṇu dvaya ārabdha tantu nyagrodha pāda pad vi aṇukeṣu upalabdheḥ na prakṛti vṛddhau vikāra vṛddhiḥ vikāra sadbhāve hetuḥ vyabhicārāt tatas ca vivṛddha īrikāra prakṛtikasya yakārasya vivṛddhi yogyasya tathā attva adarśanena vikāra pakṣaḥ na upapadyate iti yat uktam pūrva sūtreṇa tad asaṃbaddham iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.2.45	 tat etat dūṣayati na atulya prakṛtīnām vikāra vikalpāt atulyāḥ ca tāḥ prakṛtayaḥ ca atulya prakṛtayaḥ tāsām atulya prakṛtīnām vikāra vikalpāt vikāra vaiṣamya darśanāt etat uktam bhavati na tāvat prakṛteḥ nyūnaḥ samaḥ vā vikāraḥ sambhavati mahat tūla piṇḍānām raṇḍa ākara tala karkaśa vimardanena vināśe sati aṇubhiḥ eva alpa parimāṇaiḥ utpadyamāna tvāt tantūnām na api dvi aṇukasya paramāṇu parimāṇam tena prakṛti sāmyam mahatva abhāve api paramāṇu parimāṇa atirikta parimāṇa tva sambhavāt tasmāt nyagrodha vat prakṛteḥ adhikaḥ eva sarvatra vikāraḥ iti na anaikāntika tvam prakṛti vivṛddhau vikāra vivṛddheḥ iti asya sambhavati na api tatra prakṛti vivṛddhau vikāra vṛddhiḥ vivakṣitā kim tarhi prakṛti anuvidhānam vikārasya tat ca atulya prakṛti vikāreṣu api draṣṭavyam iti na anaikāntika tvam prakṛti anuvidhānasya saṃbhavati iti dīrghekāra vikārasya prakṛti anuvidhāna niyamāt dīrgha tva prāptiḥ vikara pakṣe tad avasthā eva iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.2.46	 tat etat ākṣipati dravya vikāra vaiṣamya vat varṇa vikāra vikalpaḥ dravya ātmanā nyagrodha bīja ādi prakṛtīnām tulya tve api yathā tad vikārāṇām vaiṣamyam na tathā varṇaḥ ca vikāraḥ ca varṇa vikārau tayoḥ vikalpaḥ vaicitryam vikāra ātmanā yakārasya ekatve api prakṛteḥ iva ṛṇasya nānātvam varṇa vikārayoḥ vikalpaḥ vaiṣamyam sambhavati iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.2.47	 tat etat na iti āha na vikāra dharma anupapatteḥ vikāra dharmaḥ jātimat dravya anupapattiḥ tasya anupapatteḥ yat khalu vikriyate tasya pūrva vyūha parityāgena vyūha antara prāptau jātimat dravya anuvṛttiḥ dṛṣṭā yathā kuṇḍala tvam hitvā rucaka tvam āpadyamānasya suvarṇasya suvarṇa tva jātīya anuvṛttiḥ na ca iha tathā itvam hitvā yatvam āpadyamānasya jātimat avayava anuvṛttiḥ asti tasmāt vikāra dharma anupapatteḥ dravya vikāra vaiṣamya vat varṇa vikārayoḥ vaiṣamyam na sambhavati dravya ātmanā nyagrodha bījānām ekatve api tad vikāra vaiṣamye nyagrodha tvāt i avāntara prakṛti bheda prayojaka tvena vikāra mātrasya tatra aprayojaka tvāt iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.2.48–2.2.49	 itas api na varṇa vikāraḥ iti āha vikāra prāptānām apunar āpatteḥ ye kṣīra ādayaḥ vikāra prāptāḥ dadhi bhāvam āpannāḥ teṣām apunar āpatteḥ punar kṣīra tva prāpti abhāva ādi kārasya saṃhitāyām yakāra tvam prāpya punar asaṃhitāyāmi tvam āpadyamānasya na yakāraḥ vikāraḥ bhavitum arhati punar āpatti abhāvasya vikāra niyatasya atra avidyamāna tvāt iti sūtra arthaḥ apunarāvṛttiḥ vikāre na hetuḥ vyabhicārāt iti āha suvarṇa ādīnām punar āpatteḥ ahetuḥ suvarṇa ādīnām dravyāṇām rucaka tva ādi rūpam hitvā kuṇḍala ādi rūpam prāptānām punā rucaka tva prāpti darśanāt apunarāvṛttiḥ iti ayam abhipreta artha sādhane na hetuḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.2.50	 tat etat dūṣayati na tad vikārāṇām suvarṇa bhāva avyatirekāt te ca te vikārāḥ ca tad vikārāḥ teṣām tad vikārāṇām yaiḥ rucaka tvam hitvā kuṇḍala tvam prāpya punā rucaka tvam āpadyante teṣām vikārāṇām suvarṇa bhāva avyatirekāt na api vikārāḥ rucaka tva ādi rūpeṇa kuṇḍala tvam bhajante kim tarhi rucaka tvam apahāya suvarṇa tvam prāpya tena eva ākāreṇa tatas ca rucakasya sataḥ kuṇḍala tvam prāptasya punā rucaka tva prāptyā vikāra prāptasya punarāvṛttiḥ suvarṇa ādiṣu sambhavati iti etat na vaktum śakyate teṣām tad prakṛti tva asambhavāt iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.2.51	 yadi savarṇa tva avyatirekāt tad vikāreṣu api punar āpatti abhāvaḥ tarhi varṇa tva avyatirekāt varṇa vikāreṣu api punar āpatti abhāvaḥ iti āha varṇa tva avyatirekāt varṇa vikārāṇām apratiṣedhaḥ varṇa vikāraṇām apīka araya kāra ādīnām varṇa tva avyatirekeṇa eva varṇa tvasya tad prakṛti tvena yakāra prāptasya īkārasya punar āpatti asambhavāt tad sambhavena varṇa vikāraḥ na sambhavati iti yaḥ ayam pratiṣedhaḥ sa pratiṣedhaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.2.52	 asya uttaram sāmānyavataḥ dharma yogaḥ na punar sāmānyasya sāmānyavataḥ padārthasya mṛd suvarṇa ādiṣu vikāra prakṛti tva darśanena atra api varṇa tva sāmānya yuktasya prakṛti bhāvena bhavitavyam na ca ikāraya kāra vyatirekeṇa varga tva sāmānya yuktam padārtha antaram asti iti teṣām eva prakṛti vikāra bhāvena punar āpatti sambhavaḥ yad avasthaḥ eva iti etat sūtra stha eka deśasya apratiṣedhaḥ iti asya āvṛttyā sva buddhyā vā svayam ūhanīyam yaḥ tu rucaka tva ādīnām kuṇḍala tva ādi prakṛti tva asambhavena punar āpatti asambhave api suvarṇa tva sāmānya yuktasya avayava kuṇḍala tvam prāptasya punar sva rūpa prāpti sambhavena punar āpatti sambhavāt tat punar āpatteḥ vyabhicāram manyate tasya api na vikāra dharma anupapatteḥ iti etat sūtra pratipādita anvaya grahaṇam eva parihāraḥ veditavyaḥ 
NTD_2.2.53	 itas api na varṇa vikāraḥ iti āha nitya tve avikārāt anitya tve ca anavasthānāt varṇānām nitya tve vikāra ādikāraya kārayoḥ anupajana apāya dharmaka tvena tathā eva avasthita tva at na ekasya anyaḥ vikāraḥ sambhavati anitya tve varṇānām anavasthānāda aśutara vināśi tvena ekasya vināśe sati dvitīyasya utpādāt kaḥ kasya vikāraḥ syāt iti ubhayathā api na vikāra pakṣaḥ sambhavati iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.2.54–2.2.55	 atra samyak uttaram apaśyan sā vikalpa samāsādharmya samābhyām jātibhyām nitya anitya pakṣayoḥ yathāsaṃkhyam sūtra dvayena pratiṣedham āha nityānām atīndriya tvāt tad dharma vikalpāt ca varṇa vikārāṇām apratiṣedhaḥ anavasyāyi tve varṇa upalabdhi vat tad vikāra upapattiḥ nityānām ākāśa paramāṇu ādīnām atīndriya tvāt indriya pratyāsatti grāhya tva abhāvāt tad dharma vikalpāt ca tasya atīndriyasya dharmasya vikalpāt keṣucid nityeṣu sāmānya ādiṣu bhāvāt varṇa vikārāṇām apratiṣedhaḥ yathā nitya tve sati api keṣāñcid atīndriya tvam keṣāñcid aindriyaka tvam tathā nitya tve sati api varṇānām vikāri tvam ākāśa ādīnām avikāri tvam iti varṇa vikārāṇām apratiṣedhaḥ iti tathā anavasthāyi tve api ca varṇānām yathā upalabdhiḥ sambhavati tathā anavasthāyi tve api teṣām vikāra upapattiḥ api sambhavati iti sūtra dvitaya arthaḥ 
NTD_2.2.56	 anayoḥ uttaram vikāra dharma tve nitya tva abhāvāt kāla antare vikāra upapatteḥ ca apratiṣedhaḥ aindriyaka tva an aindriyaka tvayoḥ nitya tva anitya tvābhyām saha vyāpti abhāvāt tatra dharma vikalpaḥ sambhavati vikāra dharmasya anitya tvena saha vyāpta tvena tad dharma tve nitya tva abhāvāt na atra dharma vikalpaḥ sambhavati iti na vikalpa samājāti utthānam na api anavasthāyi tvam varṇa upalabdhi vat tad vikāra upapattiḥ kasmāt kāla antare vikāra upapatteḥ dvi tri kṣaṇa avasthāna mātreṇa api varṇa upalabdhiḥ sambhavati na cira kāla bhāvinā vikāreṇa sādharmya samā bhavati saṃhitā saṃhita avasthā svarūpa upalabdhi lakṣaṇaṣṭka vyatirekeṇa vikāra anupapatteḥ tasmāt na sādharmya samāyāḥ jāteḥ upapattiḥ iti ādeśa pakṣasya apratiṣedhaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.2.57–2.2.58	 hetu antaram āha prakṛti aniyamāt varṇa vikārāṇām yatra prakṛti vikāra bhāvaḥ tatra prakṛti niyamaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ yathā kṣīra jātīyāt dadhi jātīya utpattiḥ na punar dadhi jātīyāt kṣīra jātīya utpattiḥ iti niyamaḥ api asti vidhyati ityādiṣu yakāra ādi kāra utpatteḥ tasmāt prakṛti a niyamāt varṇa vikārāṇām prakṛti vikāra bhāvaḥ varṇānām na sambhavati iti sūtra arthaḥ atra pūrva pakṣa vādī vāc chalena pratyavatiṣṭhate aniyame niyama anna aniyamaḥ ayam prakṛti aniyamaḥ sva ātmani niyataḥ na vā yadi niyata starhi aniyame niyatanvāt niyata tva hāniḥ tayoḥ paraspara virodhāt na ced niyataḥ aniyata tva svarūpa hāniḥ niyata ātmani avasthitaḥ syāt iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.2.59	 atha uttaram niyama aniyama virodhāt aniyame niyamāt ca apratiṣedhaḥ niyama aniyamayoḥ sva viṣaye virodhaḥ na sva ātmani tasmin svena eva ākāreṇa niyata tvāt tasmāt niyama aniyamayoḥ sva viṣaye virodhāt aniyame sva ātmani niyamāt ca apratiṣedhaḥ na aniyata tva hāniḥ aniyamasya sva ātmani niyata tvena niyama śabda abhidheya tve api arthasya tathā eva avasthānāt iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.2.60	 nanu yadi ādeśa pakṣaḥ eva śreyān na vikāra pakṣaḥ tarhi katham śābdikānām vikāra vyapadeśaḥ sambhavati iti atas āha guṇa antara āpatti upamarda hrāsa vṛddhi leśa śleṣebhyaḥ tad vikāra upapatteḥ varṇa vikārāḥ guṇa antara āpattiḥ udāttasya anudātte iti evamādiḥ upamardaḥ nāma rūpa nivṛttau rūpa antarasya utpattiḥ yathā bruvaḥ vaciḥ iti hrāsaḥ dīrghasya hrasvaḥ vṛddhiḥ hrasvasya dīrghaḥ leśaḥ iti asteḥ akāra lope sakāra mātrasya avasthānam śleṣaḥ āgamaḥ prakṛteḥ pratyayasya vā etebhyaḥ tad vikāra upapatteḥ varṇa vikārāḥ taiḥ vyapadiśyante iti tat uktam bhavati ekasya aprayoge anyasya prayogaḥ vikāraḥ yadi varṇeṣu api prakṛti vikāra bhāvaḥ syāt tadānīm prakṛti niyamena bhavitavyam na ca atra prakṛtiḥ asti guṇa antara upamarda ādi bhedena tatra tatra vyākhyāyante iti 
NTD_2.2.61^1	 tat evam varṇānām aniyata tvam agandha ādi saha vṛtti tvam avikāri tvam ca pratipādya avarṇa ātmakasya sphoṭasya varṇaiḥ abhivyajyamānasya nitya tvena pada nitya tvam saṃpadyate iti yaḥ manyate tad mata nirākaraṇa artham na varṇa vyatiriktaḥ sphoṭaḥ nāma kaścid padārthaḥ vidyate iti āha te vibhakti antāḥ padam vibhaktiḥ vyākaraṇa prasiddhā suraptiṅlakṣaṇā ataeva varṇāḥ vibhakti antāḥ padam na tad vyatiriktaḥ sphoṭa ātmā kaścid asti tad sadbhāve pramāṇa abhāvāt na tāvat idam ekam padam iti pada ekatva avabhāsaḥ pramāṇam teṣu eva bahuṣu varṇeṣu eka smṛti samārūḍha tayā vā eka artha siddhi hetu tayā vā upapadyamāna tvena anyathā siddha tvāt na ca evam anyonya āśraya tva manaṛte rthe pada avadhāraṇāt saṃbandha agrahaṇena artha avagamaḥ na ca artha avagamam antareṇa pada avadhāraṇam 
NTD_2.2.61^2	 pada avadhāraṇam antareṇa na saṃbandha grahaṇam iti eka smṛti samārabdha tayā ekīkṛtānām artha pratyayam antareṇa api sva artha saṃketa grahaṇasya sukara tvāt na api artha pratyayāni atha anupapattyā sphoṭa kalpanā varṇānām pratyekam artha pratyaya an udbhāvāt na tu nirbhāgasya ekasya padasphoṭasya krama bhāvibhiḥ varṇaiḥ sphuṭa asphuṭa pratibhāsaḥ janyate iti vaktum śakyam prathama varṇa vibhāsena agṛhīta aṃśasya eva avidyamāna tvena sphuṭa asphuṭa tva sambhavāt na ca tat eva agṛhītam gṛhotañca iti sambhavati kiñca artha pratyayā anyathā anupapattyā sphoṭa kalpanāyāḥ sphuṭam itaretara āśraya tvam artha pratyayāt sphoṭa avagamaḥ sphoṭa avagamāt artha pratyayaḥ iti tasmāt dṛṣṭebhyaḥ eva varṇebhyaḥ dṛṣṭa prakāra anupātibhyaḥ artha pratyayaḥ pratipadyamānaḥ dṛṣṭa caram sphoṭa ātmānam kalpayitvā tad nitya tvena śabda nitya tvam sambhāvayati iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.2.62	 tat evam pada svarūpam nirūpayitvā tasya ayam arthaḥ iti niścetum saṃśayam āha vyakti ākṛti jāti sannidhau= upacārāt saṃśayaḥ sannidhiḥ avinābhāvaḥ upacāraḥ prayogaḥ tasmāt avinā abhāvena vartamānāsu vyakti ākṛti viṣayam yoga śabdaḥ prayujyate tasmāt kim jātiḥ padārthaḥ uta vyakti ratha ākṛtiḥ āhosvit sarve iti saṃśayaḥ bhavati prayogasya samāna tvāt iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.2.63	 tatra padārtha vādī āha yā śabda samūha tyāga parigraha saṃkhyā vṛddhi apacaya varṇa samāsa anubandhānām vyaktau= upacārāt vyaktiḥ yā śabda= chalena saṃbhinnasya prayogaḥ yā gauḥ tiṣṭhati iti samūhaḥ saṃbhūya avasthānam gavām iti tyāgaḥ parasmai pradānam vaidyāya gām dadāti iti parigrahaḥ svena abhisaṃbandhaḥ kauṇḍinyasya gauḥ iti syaṃkhyā parigaṇanam daśa gāvaḥ viṃśatiḥ gāvaḥ iti vṛddhiḥ avayava upacayaḥ avardhata gauḥ iti apacayaḥ kārśyam kṣīṇāḥ gauḥ iti varṇaḥ śvaitya ādiḥ śuklāḥ gauḥ kṛṣṇā gauḥ iti samāsaḥ sukha ādi saṃbandhaḥ go sukham go hitam iti anubandhaḥ sarūpa prajanana santānaḥ gaurgām janayati iti evam eteṣām śabdānām vyaktau= upacārāt vyaktau= eva prayoga darśanāt vyaktiḥ eva padārthaḥ na jāti ākṛtī yā gauḥ tiṣṭhati ityādi sthāna ādi viśeṣaṇā sambhavāt iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.2.64	 tat evam vyakti abhidhāna niyama vādinam dūṣayati na tad anavasthānāt na vyaktiḥ padārthaḥ kasmāt tasyāḥ vyakteḥ anavasthāna āditya nitya tva aneka tvaiḥ anavadhāraṇīya tvena vyakti padārtha pakṣe saṃbandha grahaṇasya aśakya karaṇa tvāt na ca jāteḥ aśabda artha tve api upādhi tvena saṃbandhasya śakya karaṇa tā iti vācyam apratīyamānāyāḥ tasyāḥ upādhi tva ayogāt na ca māna antareṇa asyāḥ pratipattiḥ sambhavati iti tad śabdāt pratītau na vyakti mātram padārthaḥ kim tarhi jāti vyaktī iti niyamaḥ na syāt iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.2.65	 yadi na vyaktiḥ padārthaḥ kathantarhi yā gauḥ tiṣṭhati ityādi prayogaḥ vyaktau= iti atas āha sahacaraṇa sthāna tādarthya vṛtta māna dhāraṇa sāmīpya yoga sādhana ādhipatyebhyaḥ brāhmaṇa mañca kaṭa rāja saktu candana gaṅgā śāṭaka anna puruṣeṣu atad bhāve api tad upacāraḥ sahacaraṇam sāhacaryam sthānam avasthitiḥ tādarthyam tad artha tvam vṛttam tadvat ācaraṇam mānam parimāṇam dhāraṇam smṛtiḥ sāmīpyam abhyarṇanā yogaḥ sambandhaḥ sādhana tva karaṇa tvam ādhipatyam prādhānyam tat etebhyaḥ nimittebhyom brāhmaṇa ādiṣu paryanteṣu atad bhāve api tadvat upacāraḥ atad śabdasya tad śabdena prayogaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ yathā yaṣṭikām praveśaya mañcāḥ krośanti kaṭam karoti yamaḥ rājā āḍhakam saktuḥ tulā candanam gaṃgāyām ghoṣaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ śāṭakaḥ annam prāṇāḥ nṛpaḥ ayam puruṣaḥ iti tathā atra api jāti sāhacaryāt vyakteḥ jāti śabdasya vyaktau= upacāreṇa api prayogaḥ sambhavati tathā śabda ādi prayoga sāmarthyāt vyakteḥ eva padārtha tvam sambhavati iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.2.66	 yadi jātyā vinā vyakteḥ aniyata tvena aśakya saṃketa tvāt na vyakti mātram padārthaḥ iti jātiḥ api abhidheyā tarhi sā api jātiḥ ākṛtyā vinā na niyamyate iti ākṛtiḥ eva padārthaḥ iti āha ākṛtiḥ tad apekṣa tvāt sattva vyavasthāna siddheḥ ākṛtiḥ padārthaḥ kasmāt tad apekṣa tvāt sattva vyavasthāna siddheḥ vyavatiṣṭhate anena iti vyavasthānam sattvasya vyavasthānam sattva vyavasthānam tasya siddhiḥ sattva vyavasthāna siddhiḥ tasyāḥ sattva vyavasthāna siddheḥ gauḥ aśvaḥ puruṣaḥ hastī iti sattva vyavasthānam yena sāmānyena siddhyati iti tasya asiddhiḥ tad apekṣā ākṛti apekṣā yasmāt sāmānyasya api siddhiḥ abhivyaktiḥ ākṛti apekṣā tasmāt sā eva ākṛtiḥ padārthaḥ sāmānyasya vyaktiḥ vyavasthāpanasya tad apekṣa tvāt iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.2.67	 atra ākṛteḥ api kevalāyāḥ vyakti vat ānanti avyabhicārābhyām aśakya saṃketa tvena padārtha tva avadhāraṇam na jātyā vinā siddhyati iti parihāraḥ na tad anavasthānāt iti anena sūtreṇa spaṣṭaḥ iti manvānaḥ sūtrakāraḥ tad artham sūtra antaram akṛtvā eva yayā pada padārthayoḥ śakya saṃketa tvam siddhyati iti sā eva jātiḥ padārthaḥ iti āha vyakti ākṛti yukte api aprasaṅgāt prokṣaṇa ādīnām mṛd gavake jātiḥ vyakti ākṛtiḥ ākṛtiḥ vā padārthaḥ syāt tadā tayoḥ ubhayoḥ api mṛdgavake vidyamāna tvena prokṣaṇa ādi kriyā saṃskārāḥ prasajyeran tat na prasajyate tatra jāteḥ abhāvāt prasajyate tu parama arthe gavi tasmāt prokṣaṇa ādi kriyā saṃskāra anvaya vyatireka anuvidhāyi tvāt śakya saṃketa tvāt ca sā eva jātiḥ padārthaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.2.68	 tat etat dūṣayati na ākṛti vyayati apekṣa tvāt jāti abhivyakteḥ na jāti mātram padārthaḥ kasmāt jāti abhivyakteḥ ākṛti vyakti apekṣa tvāt yadi api prokṣaṇa bandha ādi kriyā saṃskārān arha tvena gāḥ prokṣaya gāḥ vadhāna ityādi prayogeṣu go śabdāt na go tva mātram śuddham pratīyate vyakti ākṛti anapekṣam eva tatas ca jāti abhidhāna pakṣe śakya saṃketa tve api na tāvat mātram padārthaḥ iti vivektum śakyam ākṛti vyaktyoḥ api tasmāt eva śabdāt pratīteḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.2.69^1	 tat evam anyatama abhidhānam nirākṛtya niyama abhidhānam siddhāntam āha vyakti ākṛti jātayaḥ tu padārthaḥ arthyante iti arthāḥ padārthāḥ tisraḥ api vyakti ākṛti jātayaḥ padena smaryamāṇa tvāt padārthāḥ na punar āsām anyatamā sarvāsām eva padena smaryamaṇa tvasya samāna tvāt tathā hi go śabda uccāraṇa samanantaram vidita saṅgataiḥ ekadā eva vyakti ākṛti jāti nirbhāsaḥ pratyayaḥ udayam āsādayati na ca gaṅgāyām ghoṣaḥ iti vat gauḥ vāhīkaḥ itivat vā gaṅgā tva go tva avagama uttara kālam vākya artha anvaya anupapattyā tad avinā bhāvena lakṣyamāṇam tīram guṇa yogena avagamyamānaḥ vāhīkaḥ iva jāti avagama uttara kālam tad anvayonupapattyā vyakti ākṛtyoḥ avagamaḥ iti vaktum śakyam eka prakṛti bhāsa gocara tvena tathā abhāva asambhavāt na ca padbha patra śata vyatibhedaḥ iva śīghra tayā sanna prakṛṣṭa pratibhāsa bhedaḥ na lakṣyate iti vācyam asati bādhake balīyasi pratibhāsa bhedāḥ 
NTD_2.2.69^2	 vanyathā karaṇa yogāt kiñca rūpi śūnya avagatiḥ rūpam dravyasya jātiḥ tena rūpyamāṇa tvāt na ca rūpyate tad anavagame rūpyasya avagamaḥ iti jāti upalambhaḥ dravya upalambha eka deśaḥ dravya upalambhanam antareṇa kevalaḥ sambhavati tasmāt eka upalambha gocara tvam na jātimataḥ lakṣya lakṣaṇa bhāvaḥ na ca vācyam eka upalambha gocara tve api jāti vyaktyoḥ jātiḥ eva vācyā na vyaktiḥ eka vācya tve api ubhaya upapattau ubhaya viṣaya tva kalpanā anupapattiḥ iti kārya vyaṅgyam hi sāmarthya kārakāṇām kāryañca anubhavaḥ sa ca ekaḥ eva iti na śakti bheda kalpanā na api puruṣa saṃketa adhīna pravṛttīnām padānām tad vyatirekeṇa sāmarthyam nāma kiñcid asti pramāṇa gocaram yat ekam anekam vā syāt tasmāt eka pratipatti gocara tvāt vyakti ākṛti jātayaḥ tisraḥ api padārthāḥ sūtra gatāt tu śabdāt tisṛṇām eka pratipatti gocara tve pradhāna bhāvam kvacid kasyāñcid eva boddhavyam iti sūtra tātparya arthaḥ 
NTD_2.2.70–2.2.71	 tatra vyakti lakṣaṇam āha vyakti guṇa viśeṣa āśrayaḥ mūrtiḥ mūrchitaḥ paraspara avayava saṃyuktaḥ ca yaḥ sā vyakti rathavā guṇāḥ ca te viśeṣāḥ ca iti guṇa viśeṣāḥ ākṛti vyatiriktā rūpa ādayaḥ guṇebhyaḥ vā viśeṣāḥ guṇa viśeṣāḥ utkṣepaṇa ādayaḥ teṣām āśrayaḥ dravyam mūrtyante kenacid prakāreṇa saṃbadhyante iti mūrti śabdena viśeṣa samavāya abhāvāḥ evañca jāti ākṛti vyatiriktasya sarvasya api padārtha sāmarthyasya vyaktiḥ anena sūtreṇa pratipāditā bhavati vyākhyānataḥ viśeṣa pratipattiḥ nahi sandehāt alakṣaṇam iti sūtra tātparya arthaḥ ākṛteḥ lakṣaṇam āha ākṛtiḥ jāti liṅga ākhyā jāti liṅgāni ca jāti liṅge te ākhyāyete yayā sā jāti liṅga ākhyā ākṛtiḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_2.2.72	 jāteḥ lakṣaṇam āha samāna prasava ātmikā jātiḥ paraspara vyāvṛtteṣu gavā ādiṣu anaupādhika anuvṛtta buddheḥ prasūtikā sā jātiḥ iti evañca pācaka ādiṣu anuvṛtta buddhi janaka tvāt na jāteḥ asadbhāvaḥ abādhitasya anuvṛtta pratyayasya ananya nimitta tvāt na ca vṛtta vikalpa ādi bādhakam pramāṇam tasya avayavi samarthana samaye nirākṛta tvāt na ca anya vyāvṛtti rūpa sāmānyam tasya sva lakṣaṇāt bheda abheda nānātva ekatva tucchādi vikalpa anupapatteḥ tasmāt asti vastu satī jātiḥ samāna prasava ātmikā iti sūtra arthaḥ saṅgrahaślokaḥ iti iha sandeha vicāra pūrvakam pramāṇa sāmānya viśeṣa lakṣaṇam saṃkhyānam eṣām kṣaṇika tvam akṣare padam padārthena samam samīkṣitam iti nyāya sūtra artha tātparyadīpikāyām dvitīya adhyāyasya dvitīyam āhnikam 
NTD_3.1.1	 atha idānīm avasara prāptam prameyam parīkṣamāṇaḥ tad ātmā ādi iti prathamam ātmānam parīkṣitum saṃśayam āha vyapadeśasya ubhayatha asiddheḥ saṃśayaḥ kriyā karaṇayoḥ kartrā sambandhasya abhidhānam vyapadeśaḥ sa ca ubhayathā dṛṣṭaḥ eka deśena samudāyasya stambhaiḥ prāsādaḥ dhriyate mūlaiḥ vṛkṣaḥ tiṣṭhati iti anyena ca anyasya yathā paraśunā vṛścati pradīpena paśyati iti tathā atra api vyapadeśaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ cakṣuṣā paśyati manasā vijānāti iti sa ca ayam vyapadeśaḥ kim eka deśena cakṣuṣā śarīra indriya buddhi saṃghātasya mūlaiḥ vṛkṣaḥ tiṣṭhati iti vat āhosvit anyena cakṣuṣā anyasya ātmanaḥ vyapadeśaḥ paraśunā vṛścati iti saṃśayaḥ bhavati iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.1.2	 atra anyena anyasya vyapadeśaḥ iti etat tattvam iti āha darśana sparśanābhyām ekārtha grahaṇāt dṛśyate anena iti darśanam cakṣuḥ spṛśyate anena iti sparśanam tvac indriyam ābhyām darśana sparśanābhyām arthasya grahaṇam artha grahaṇam tasmāt ekārtha grahaṇāt darśana sparśanābhyām ekasya puruṣasya eka artha viṣayau pratyayau bhavataḥ iti pratisandhānena dṛṣṭaḥ yam aham adrākṣam cakṣuṣā tam aham spṛśāmi yam ca āspārkṣam sparśanena tam paśyāmi iti na ca etad pratisandhānam indriyāṇām kartṛ tve sambhavati indriya antareṇa dṛṣṭasya indriya antareṇa pratisandhāna abhāvāt na api saṃghātena tasya api nānātvena anya tvāt vyāvṛtteḥ na ca manasā tasya api karaṇa tvena kartṛ antara sāpekṣa tvāt darśana sparśana pratyayayoḥ yaḥ ekaḥ pratisandhātā śarīra indriya buddhi vedanā vyatiriktaḥ saḥ ātmā asti iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.1.3	 tat etat na iti āha na viṣaya vyavasthānāt na deha ādi saṃghātāt anyaḥ cetanaḥ kasmāt viṣaya vyavasthānāt viṣaya vyavasthānena indriyāṇām acetana tvāt sati cakṣuṣi rūpa grahaṇam bhavati na asati tathā eva ghrāṇa ādiṣu api tatas ca indriya bhāva abhāvayoḥ viṣaya grahaṇasya tathā abhāvāt indriyāṇām eva rūpa ādi viṣaya grahaṇāni na tad vyatiriktasya ātmanaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.1.4	 dūṣayati tad vyavasthānāt eva ātma sadbhāvāt apratiṣedhaḥ teṣām indriyāṇām vyavasthānāt svam svam viṣayam prati vyavasthita tvāt avyavasthita viṣayeṇa jñātrā bhavitavyam anyathā avyavasthita viṣaya pratisandhāna anupapatteḥ na api vyavasthita viṣaya tvena indriya caitanya sambhavaḥ teṣām cetanā upakāraka tve api vyavasthita viṣayasya upapatteḥ atas ca indriya vyavasthānāt eva deha ādi saṃghāta vyatiriktasya ātmanaḥ sadbhāvāt na viṣaya vyavasthānāt iti pūrva sūtreṇa yaḥ ayam tasya pratiṣedhaḥ sa na pratiṣedhaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.1.5	 yadi deha ādi saṃghāta mātraḥ eva ātmā na tad vyatiriktaḥ kaścid tadānīm kṛta nāśa akṛta āgama lakṣaṇa aniṣṭa prasaṅgaḥ iti āha śarīra dāhe pātaka abhāvāt śarīra grahaṇena śarīra indriya buddhi vedanā saṃghātaḥ prāṇi bhūtaḥ gṛhyate tathābhūtam saṃghāta antaram avadhīt tasya dāhe sati anyaḥ saṃghātaḥ utpadyate phala bhoga samaye tatas ca yena hiṃsā kṛtā na tasya phala bhogaḥ yasya phala bhogaḥ na tena hiṃsā kṛtā iti kṛta nāśa akṛta āgamau syātām iti pātaka abhāvaḥ na ca yat śarīra citta santāna prabhavam karma tad śarīra citta santāna prabhavam phalam iti kārya kāraṇa bhāvāt kartṛ tva bhoktṛ tva vyavahāraḥ iti vācyam kārya kāraṇa bhāve api santāna antara vat anyatva anupagamāt uktam ca na kārya kāraṇam āvaḥ pratisandhāna ādi kārya niyāmakaḥ vyabhicārāt iti icchan sūtre tasmāt avyakta ātma vādinaḥ kṛta nāśa akṛta āgama aniṣṭa prasaṅgaḥ durvāraḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.1.6	 deha atikti lakṣaṇāṇe api aniṣṭa prasaṅgaḥ iti āha tad abhāvaḥ sa ātmaka pradāhe api tad nitya tvāt yasya api pātaka kārasya śarīram dahyate tasya api tad abhāvaḥ tayoḥ hiṃsā phalayoḥ abhāvaḥ kasmāt tad nitya tvāt tasya ātmanaḥ nitya tvena avikāri tvāt na hiṃsā na api phala bhogaḥ nitya tvena avikāri tvena phala bhoga lakṣaṇa vikāra asambhavāt sambhave vā nitya tva abhāva prasaṅgāt iti kṛta nāśa akṛta āgamau samānau anupapanne ca hiṃsā tad phala bhoktṛ tve iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.1.7^1	 tat etat dūṣayati na kārya āśraya kartṛ vadhāt kāryam sukha pratisaṃvedanam tasya āśrayaḥ adhiṣṭhānam iti kārya āśraya śabdena śarīram ucyate kartṛ śabdena api viṣaya upalabdhi kāraṇāni indriyāṇi kathyante teṣām vadhaḥ kārya śraya kartṛ vadhaḥ tasmāt kārya āśraya kartṛ vadhāt na nityasya ātmanaḥ vadhaḥ hiṃsā kim tarhi anucchitti dharmakasya yat upabhoga adhiṣṭhānam śarīram tad mayāni ca viṣaya upalabdhi sādhanāni indriyāṇi teṣām vadhaḥ hiṃsā iti upacaryate gati antara abhāvāt 
NTD_3.1.7^2	 yasya ca pratikṣaṇam vināśinaḥ saṃskārāḥ tasya api vināśa rūpāṇām bhāvānām vināśasya hetuka tayā vilakṣaṇa utpādaḥ eva kāraṇa vyāpāra janyaḥ iti saḥ eva hantrā kriyamāṇa padārthasya hiṃsā iti upacaritavyam tathā sati yasya mate hantuḥ phala bhoga sambhavaḥ saḥ eva upacāra svīkartavyaḥ sa ca nitya ātma vādi kāryāśraya kartṛ vadhaḥ iti sā eva hiṃsā na ca nityasya avikāri tvena phala bhoga asambhavaḥ kṣaṇa bhaṅga pariṇāma nirāse sati nityasya api sahakāri samavadhāna vaśāt dharma antara āvirbhāva tirobhāvayoḥ sambhavāt tasmāt deha ādi vyatirikta ātma vādi pakṣe api kṛta nāśa akṛta āgamau anupapanne ca hiṃsā tad phala bhoktṛ tve iti yat uktam pūrva sūtreṇa tat ayukta bhiti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.1.8	 yaḥ tu ekasmiñt śarīre cakṣuḥ dvi tvam abhyupagamya viṣaya pratyabhijñānena api ātma sattvam manyate tat matam upanyasyati savya dṛṣṭasya itareṇa pratyabhijñānāt savyena cakṣuṣā dṛṣṭam itareṇa api cakṣuṣā dṛṣṭvā pratyabhijānāti yam aham adrākṣam tam paśyāmi iti vā apratisandhānam pratyabhijñānam tasya smṛti pūrvaka tvāt pūrva apara pratyaya anatham ekam kartṛvam sādhayati iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.1.9	 na ekasminnāsa asthi vyavahite dvi tva abhimānāt ekam idam cakṣuḥ dvi adhiṣṭhānam madhye nāsikā vyavahitam tasmin= ekasminnāsa asthi vyavahite dvau= etau gṛhyamāṇa adhiṣṭhāna bhedau= anumīyamānau dvi tva abhimānam prayojayataḥ yathā ekasya madhya vyavahitasya dīrgha dravyasya antau= iti na punar paramārthataḥ dve cakṣuṣī pramāṇa virodhāt iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.1.10	 bheda vādi āha eka vināśe dvitīya avināśa at na eka tvam ekasmin= udvṛtte upahate vā cakṣuṣi dvitīyam avatiṣṭhate iti viṣaya grahaṇam anena anumīyate yadi punar ekam eva cakṣuḥ syat tadā ānīm eka upaghāte tasya upahata tvāt dvitīyena viṣayaḥ na gṛhyeta gṛhyate ca viṣayaḥ antareṇa tasmāt viṣaya grahaṇāt ekasya vināśe dvitīya vināśaḥ na asti iti dve cakṣuṣi iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.1.11	 pariharati tat etat cakṣuḥ eka tvena ākṣipati avayava vināśe api avaya vyupalabdheḥ ahetuḥ eka vināśe dvitīya avināśāt iti ayam cakṣuḥ dvi tve na hetuḥ avayava vināśe api avaya vyupalabdheḥ katipaya avayava vināśe api pariśiṣṭaiḥ avayavaiḥ avasthita saṃyoga janitaiḥ ārabdhasya vṛkṣasya upalabdhiḥ iti saḥ evam cakṣuṣaḥ katipaya avayava vināśe vyavasthitaiḥ eva avayavaiḥ ārabdhasya avayavi antarasya cakṣuṣaḥ a dhiṣṭhāna antara āśrayasya sambhavena viṣaya grahaṇa upapattyā prācīnasya dvitīyasya cakṣuṣaḥ avasthāne pramāṇa abhāvāt na api eka adhiṣṭhāna vināśe cakṣuṣaḥ vināśaḥ sambhavati tasya adhiṣṭhāna antara āśraya tvena api vyavasthāna sambhavāt api ca cakṣuḥ dvi tvena paramāṇu parimāṇānām yugapad u bhaya adhiṣṭhāna asambhavena vikala avikala locanayoḥ tulya upalambhaḥ syāt na api ekatve cakṣuṣaḥ nāsau= aṃśena avapīḍitena aṅgulyā avapīḍita locana vat bhinna avabhāsitā āgantuka avapīḍanasya śrama hetu tvena svābhāvikasya nāsā = aṃśāvapīḍanasya tad hetukatva anupapatteḥ tasmāt ekam eva cakṣuḥ ekasmin dehaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.1.12	 ye tu avayava vināśe api avaya vyupalabdheḥ iti yathāśrutam sūtram varṇayanti teṣām dūṣaṇam āha dṛṣṭānta virodhāt apratiṣedhaḥ na khalu kāraṇa dravya vibhāge kārya dravyam avatiṣṭhate iti pramāṇam asti dṛṣṭānta abhāvāt tasmāt dṛṣṭānta virodhāt yathāśrutam pūrva sūtram cakṣuḥ dvi tvasya apratiṣedhakam iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.1.13–3.1.14	 tat evam ātmani pratyakṣam pramāṇayitvā anumānam pramāṇayati indriya antara vikārāt kasyacid āhṛtasya gṛhīta sāhacarye rūpe gandhe vā gṛhyamāṇe tad sāhacaryāt rasa anubhava janita saṃskāra udbodha krameṇa tad rasa smṛtiḥ upajāyate smṛtyā ca rasa tṛṣṇayā danta udaka saṃplava lakṣaṇaḥ rasanā indriya vikāraḥ janyate sā iyam rasanā indriya vikāra kāriṇī smṛtiḥ pūrva apara jñānayoḥ eka kartṛ tve sambhavati na anyathā iti tasmāt ātmā anumīyate iti sūtra arthaḥ etat ākṣipati smṛteḥ smartavya viṣaya tvāt smṛtiḥ ātmānam kāraṇa tvena vā gamayet tad viṣaya tvena vā na tāvat kāraṇa tvena tasyāḥ saṃskāra kāraṇa tvāt na ca viṣaya tvena tasyāḥ smartavya viṣaya tvāt na prakāra antareṇa tasmāt na tayā anumīyate iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.1.15–3.1.16	 samādhatte tad ātma guṇa tva sadbhāvāt apratiṣedhaḥ tasyāḥ smṛteḥ ātma guṇa tvena sadbhāvāt apratiṣedhaḥ ātmanaḥ yadi api tad viṣaya tvena na ātmānam gamayati smṛtiḥ tasyāḥ smartavya rasa ādi viṣaya tvāt tathā api kāraṇa tvena gamayet nanu uktam saṃskāraḥ kāraṇam iti tat na upādāna kāraṇa tva abhyupagamāt na saṃskāraḥ upādānakāraṇam tasya guṇa tvena tathā abhāva anupapatteḥ na śarīram upādānam bhūta caitanya pratiṣedhāt na api indriyam upādānam teṣām api bhautika tvāt na ca virodhaḥ bhāva rūpa kārya tvāt tasmāt ādhāra tvena yat upādānakāraṇam saḥ ātmā tayā kārya bhūtayā anumīyate aiva iti sūtra arthaḥ ca ādeyati na ātma pratipatti hetūnām manasi sambhavāt yaḥ ete ātmanaḥ śarīra ādibhyaḥ vyatituḥ eka pratipatti hetavaḥ upadiṣṭāḥ eteṣām manasi sambhavāt te ete manasi sambhavanti manasaḥ sarva viṣaya tvena pratisandhāna ādi hetu tva sambhavāt evam ca na manasaḥ vyatirekaḥ ātmanaḥ siddhyati iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.1.17	 pariharati jñātuḥ jñāna sādhana upapatteḥ saṃjñā bheda mātram yathā jñātāram abhyupagacchatā jñāna sādhanam cakṣuḥ ādi abhyupagamyate tathā manasaḥ jñātṛ tve jñapti sādhanena kāraṇa antareṇa bhavitavyam akāraṇikāyāḥ kriyāyāḥ adarśanāt na ca manasaḥ grahaṇe kāraṇa antara abhāvaḥ iti vācyam yugapad jñāna anutpattyā liṅga ādi śāna sahitasya kāraṇa tvena kevalasya manasaḥ viṣaya tva abhyupagamāt evam ātma jñāne api kevalasya kartṛ tvāt bhoktṛ tva ādi dharma sahitasya karma tva at na ekasya jñātṛ jñeya bhāvaḥ evam ca ātmani ātma saṃjñā na mṛṣyate manasi ca manaḥ saṃjñā na mṛṣyate iti saṃjñā bheda mātra tvena artha bheda abhāvāt manaḥ vyatirikta ātma siddhiḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.1.18	 tat evam uktena pratibandhena ātmanaḥ śarīra ādi vyatirekaḥ utpatti prabhṛti yāvat pramāṇam bālya kaumāra yauvana ādi avasthā bhedena śarīra bheda vyavasthānam ca sādhitam saṃprati deha vināśāt ūrdhvam avyavasthānena aneka śarīra yogaḥ asya asti vā nava iti vicārayitum nitya anitya tva saṃśayam āha ubhayathā dṛṣṭa tvāt saṃśayaḥ vidyamānam ubhayathā dṛṣṭam nityam anityañca ātmā ca pramāṇataḥ upalabdheḥ vidyamānaḥ sa ca vidyamāna tvāt ghaṭa vat anityaḥ syāt āhosvit ākāśa vat nityaḥ syāt iti saṃśayaḥ bhavati iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.1.19	 tatra deha vināśāt ūrdhvam api vyavasthānena nityaḥ iti āha pūrva abhyasta smṛti anubandha āt ta jātasya harṣa bhaya śoka saṃpratipatteḥ jāta mātraḥ khalu ayam kumārakaḥ viṣaya avagamā samartheṣu indriyeṣu harṣa bhaya śokān smita calita rudita anumeyān pratipadyamānaḥ pramāṇena lakṣitaḥ tathā hi smita ādi hetu tvena harṣa ādīnām yauvana ādi avasthāsu darśanāt tathā harṣa ādi hetu tvena pūrva abhyasta smṛti anubandhasya tāsu eva avasthāsu darśanāt asya api pūrva abhyasta smṛti anubandha adharṣa bhaya śokāḥ jāyante iti anumīyate na ca pūrva abhyasta smṛti anubandhaḥ pūrva bhavam antareṇa bhavati iti pūrva anubhavaḥ kalpyate pūrva anubhavena pūrva śarīra yogaḥ tatas tatra api anena nyāyena tad prāktana śarīra yogaḥ tatas prāk api tathā iti evam anādi tvena akāraṇa tvāt ananta tvam api ākāśa ādi vat siddhyati iti nityaḥ ātmā iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.1.20	 pūrva abhyasta smṛti anubanvakāraṇa tvam harṣa ādīnām na asti iti ākṣipati padma ādiṣu prabodha saṃmīlana vikāra vat tad vikāraḥ yathā padma ādiṣu prabodhanam saṃmīlanam ca smṛti anubandha ādi adṛṣṭa kāraṇam na bhavati tathā harṣa ādayaḥ api smṛti anubandha ādi adṛṣṭa kāraṇam na bhavati vikāra tvāt padma ādi vikāra vat iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.1.21	 pariharati na uṣṇa śīta varṣā kāla nimitta tvāt pañca ātmaka vikārāṇām padma ādiṣu prabodha saṃmīlanena harṣa ādīnām smṛti anubandha ādi kāraṇa viśeṣa pūrvaka tvam pratiṣidhyate āhosvit kāraṇa mātra pūrvaka tvam na tāvat kāraṇa mātra pūrvakatva pratiṣedhaḥ uṣṇa śīta varṣā kāla nimitta tvāt pañca ātmaka vikārāṇām eka bhūta ārabdha tve api bhūta antarau= aṣṭaṃbhena vartamāna tvāt pañca ātmakāḥ ucyante padma ādayaḥ na punar pāñcabhautika tvena tad vikārāṇām prabodha ādīnām uṣṇa śīta varṣā kāla nimitta tvāt tena sa nimitta tvāt harṣa ādayaḥ api sa nimittāḥ iti na api smṛti anubandha ādi viśeṣa pūrvakatva pratiṣedhaḥ yasya anvaya vyatireka anuvidhāyi yat kāryam tat tasya kāraṇam iti pramāṇa pratītasya dṛṣṭāntena eva apahnotum a śakya tvāt anyathā bodha ādīnām api uṣṇa ādi kāraṇa tva abhāva prasaṅgāt tasmāt gharṣa ādīnām yauvana ādi avasthāsu pūrva abhyasta smṛti anubandha hetutva darśanāt bālya avasthāyām api tad hetuka tva siddheḥ na animitta tvam na aniyata nimitta tvam harṣa ādīnām iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.1.22	 sāmānyena uktam vispaṣṭam artham viśeṣataḥ sādhayati pretya āhāra abhyāsa kṛtāt stanya abhilāṣāt utpanna mātrasya vatsasya pravṛtti anumita stanya abhilāṣaḥ pretya āhāra abhyāsa kṛtaḥ janma antara anubhava janita saṃskāra udbodha kārita smaraṇa anubandha kṛtaḥ yauvana ādi avasthāsu tathābhūta smaraṇa anubandha hetu tvena abhilāṣa viśeṣasya darśanāditas api anādi tva siddhiḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.1.23–3.1.24	 tat etad nimitta tvena dūṣayati ayasaḥ ayat kānta abhigamana vat tad upasarpaṇam yathā ayasaḥ ayaskānta abhigama nam animittam tathā utpanna mātrasya vatsasya stana upasarpaṇam animittam iti sūtra arthaḥ dūṣayati na anyatra pravṛtti abhāvāt tad ukta m ayasaḥ ayaskānta abhigama nam animittam iti tat na anyatra pravṛtti abhāvāt ayaskāntaḥ eva pravṛtteḥ ayasā kāraṇam niyamaḥ kalpyate tam ca keṣāñcid adṛṣṭam iti na animittam tatas ca āyasaḥ ayaskānta abhigama nam animitta tvena dṛṣṭāntaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ
