NTD_3.1.25–3.1.26	 itas ca nityaḥ ātmā vīta rāga janma adarśanāt ca jāyamānaḥ khalu ayam kumārakaḥ sarvaḥ api sa rāgaḥ jāyate kasmāt vīta rāgāṇām janma adarśanāt rāgasya ca pūrva anubhūta viṣaya anucintanam yoniḥ pūrva anubhavaḥ ca pūrva śarīrāt iti anena nyāyena aneka śarīra yogāt anādi tvena atanta tvam api ātmanaḥ siddham iti sūtra arthaḥ asya ākṣepa sūtram sa guṇa dravya utpatti vat tad utpattiḥ tasya ātmanaḥ sa rāgasya utpattiḥ na pūrva anubhūta viṣaya anucintanāt kim tarhi saguṇasya ghaṭa ādeḥ dravyasya yathā utpatiḥ tathā iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.1.27	 pariharati na saṅkalpa nimitta tvāt rāga ādīnām ubhaya vādi saṃpratipannāsu yauvana ādi avasthāsu pūrva anubhūta viṣaya anucintana lakṣaṇasya rāgasya nimitta antara janya tve pramāṇa abhāvāt na rāga ādi adhikaraṇasya ātmanaḥ ghaṭa ādi dravya vat utpattiḥ saṃbhavati kāraṇa abhāvāt tasmāt pūrva anubhūta viṣaya anucintana lakṣaṇa saṅkalpa nimitta tvāt jāyamānasya rāga ādeḥ anekavidha śarīra yogaḥ anādiḥ apavarga ante iti siddham ātmanaḥ nitya tvam iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.1.28–3.1.29^1	 anantaram avasara prāptam śarīram parīkṣitum saṃśayam āha vipratipatteḥ saṃśayaḥ kecid eka prakṛti idam śarīram manyante kecid dvi bhūta ārabdham kecid tri bhūta ārabdham kecid pañcabhūta ārabdham iti tat evam vipratipatteḥ kim pramāṇa ādi vat eka prakṛti idam śarīram āhosvidh aneka prakṛti iti sūtra arthaḥ tatra eka prakṛti iti etat tattvam iti āha pārthivam guṇa antara utpatteḥ mānuṣam śarīram pārthivam kasmāt guṇa antara utpatteḥ yasmāt śarīre api gandha ādeḥ guṇa antarasya utpattiḥ upalabdhiḥ tasmāt pṛthivī paramāṇu dvaya ārabdhaiḥ dvi aṇukaiḥ tri aṇuka āditra sareṇu ādi krameṇa ārabdham śarīram pārthivam gandhavat tvāt pārthiva paramāṇu vat evam eva āpyam taijasam vāyavīyañca śarīram varuṇa loka ādiṣu vartate iti āgamāt abhyupetavyam yadi pārthiva pāthaḥ paramāṇubhyām dvi aṇukam ārabhyeta tadā kāraṇa guṇasya ekasya anārambhaka tvāt nirgandham syāt 
NTD_3.1.29^2	 na api pārthiva paramāṇubhyām pārthiva paramāṇunā ekena ca kārya ārambhaḥ paramāṇūnām bahūnām ārambhaka tvāt ghaṭopaśliṣṭa paramāṇu vat tatra api āraṃbhaka tve tatra aśeṣa kārya antara anupalabdhi prasaṅgaḥ na ca pārthivābhyām dvi aṇukābhyām ekena ca dvi aṇukena tri aṇuka utpattiḥ trasareṇat pattiḥ vijātīyānām anārambhaka tvasya dvi aṇuke api niścita tvāt evam anyatra api paramāṇu dvaya āraṃbhaka pakṣe samānaḥ doṣaḥ tathā tri catur pañcabhūta āraṃbha pakṣe yathā saṃbhavam guṇān utpattiḥ boddhavyā tasmāt gandha ādi guṇa antara utpatteḥ dvi aṇuka ādi prakrameṇa eka bhūta ārabdham śarīram iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.1.30–3.1.32	 tat evam eka prakṛti tvam pramāṇena viniścitya dvi tri catur pañca prakṛtiḥ eva upapādana artham paroktānām hetūnām pāṭha mātreṇa phalgu tvam darśayitum upanyasyati pārthiva apya taijasam tad guṇa upalabdheḥ niśvāsa ucchvāpa labdheḥ cāturbhautikam gandha kleda pāka vyūha avakāśā dānebhyaḥ pāñcabhautikam eka bhūta samavāyi kāraṇa tve api bhūta antara upaśleṣa vaśāt tad tad guṇa upalavdhiḥ pṛthivī ādiṣu iva saṃbhavati iti anyathā siddhāḥ te eva hetavaḥ iti sūtra tritaya pāṭha tātparya arthaḥ 
NTD_3.1.33	 imam artham śrutiḥ upodbalayati śruti prāmāṇyāt ca sūryam cakṣuḥ gamayatā dvāta prāṇam anvavasṛjatāt ityādi antyeṣṭi prayoga mantre pṛthivī śarīram iti śarīrasya pṛthivī eka prakṛti tvam śrūyate na veda vākyam apramāṇam mantra āyurveda vat iti sūtre parameśvara praṇīta tvena prāmāṇyasya sādhita tvāt tasmāt śruti prāmāṇyāt ca eka bhūta ārabdham śarīram iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.1.34	 atha idānīm avasara prāptāni indriyāṇi paricikṣiṣuḥ tad pūrvarūpam saṃśayam vipratipattyā darśayati kṛṣṇasāre sati upalambhāt vyatiricya upalambhāt ca saṃśayaḥ kṛṣṇasāre sati upalambhāt rūpasya diti tasmin= anupalambhāt kṛṣṇasāram eva cakṣuḥ iti kecid vyatiricya upalambhāt kṛṣṇa sāram aprāptasya vidūra deśa avasthitasya upalambhāt tad vyatirikta tejaḥ dravyam iti apere tathā tad vyatiricya upalambhaḥ na bhautika tve saṃbhavati iti āhaṅkārikam cakṣuḥ iti sāṃkhyāḥ bhautika tve api bahis vinismṛtasya taijasasya cakṣuṣaḥ gatvara tvāt viṣaya prāpteḥ vyatiricya upalambhaḥ sambhavati iti naiyāyikāḥ kim kṛṣṇasāram eva cakṣuḥ kiṃvā tat atiriktam tejaḥ kim āhaṅkārikam cakṣuḥ kim vā bhautikam iti ubhayavidhaḥ saṃśayaḥ bhavat = indriya antareṣu api evam saṃśayam āpādayati iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.1.35	 tatra abhautikam cakṣuḥ iti āha mahat aṇu grahaṇāt mahat ca aṇu ca mahat aṇunītayoḥ grahaṇam mahat aṇu grahaṇam tasmāt mahat aṇu grahaṇāt mahataḥ śailādeḥ aṇunaḥ sarṣapa ādeḥ grahaṇāt abhautikam cakṣuḥ tasya api bahu tvāt sarva vyāpaka tvena ubhaya grāhaka tva saṃbhavāt bhautikantu yāvat tāvat eva vyāpakam iti na ubhaya grahaṇam saṃbhavati iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.1.36	 tat etat dūṣayati raśmi artha sannikarṣa viśeṣāt tad grahaṇam tayoḥ mahadaṇvoḥ grahaṇam kṛṣṇasāra adhiṣṭhānasya bhautikasya tarasā bahis prasarataḥ raśmeḥ arthasya pṛthivī ādeḥ sannikarṣa viśeṣāt bhavati yatas tasmāt anyathā siddha tvāt na bhautika tve api kṛṣṇasāra mātram cakṣuḥ api tu tat atiriktaḥ tad adhiṣṭhānaḥ raśmi viśeṣaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.1.37–3.1.38	 codayati tad anupalabdheḥ ahetuḥ tasya kṛṣṇasāra adhiṣṭhānasya raśmeḥ mahattva aneka dravya tva viśeṣa viyukta tvena upalabdhum yogyasya anupalabdheḥ bāji viṣāṇa vat avidyamāna tvāt raśmi artha sannikarṣa viśeṣāt mahat aṇvoḥ grahaṇam saṃbhavati iti yaḥ ayam hetuḥ sa na hetuḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ na anumīyamānasya pratyakṣa tatas anupalabdhiḥ abhāve hetuḥ kuḍya ādi āvaraṇena anumīyamānasya raśmeḥ pratyakṣa anupalabdhiḥ na abhāve hetuḥ yogyasya api kvacid pratyakṣeṇa anupalabdhi darśanāt yathā candramasaḥ para bhāgasya pṛthivyāḥ ca adhas bhāgasya iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.1.39	 nanu candramasaḥ para bhāgasya pṛthivyāḥ ca adhas bhāgasya nityam arvāk bhāga vyavasthita tvena indriya sannikarṣa abhāvāt yogya tve api anupalabdhiḥ yuktā na ca nāyana raśmeḥ tathā indriya sannikarṣa abhāvaḥ iti atas āha dravya guṇa dharma bhedāt ca upalabdhi aniyamaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ khalu ayam dravya guṇa dharma bhedaḥ yathā hemanta śiśirayoḥ viṣakta avayavam āpya dravyam mahat tva anekam dravya tve sati api na upalabhyate sparśa mātram tasya upalabhyate śaityam tathā taijasasya tadṛśasya dravyasya rūpam grīṣme mahati aneka dravya samavāye sati api na upalabhyate sparśa mātram upalabhyate kim kāraṇam rūpa viśeṣa abhāvāt tathā na ayanasya raśmeḥ api rūpa viśeṣa abhāvanā upalabdhiḥ saṃbhavati dravya guṇa dharma bhedena upalabdhi aniyamasya dṛṣṭa tvāt iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.1.40	 nanu udbhūta rūpa sparśavat tvam kasmāt na ayanasya raśmeḥ na abhyupagatam iti atas āha karma kāritaḥ ca indriyāṇām vyūhaḥ puruṣa artha tantraḥ indriyāṇām vyūhaḥ racanā viśeṣaḥ puruṣa artha tantraḥ puruṣa artha adhīnaḥ adṛṣṭa kāritaḥ ca śabdaḥ hetu arthaḥ yasmāt karma vaśāt puruṣāṇām pravṛtti nivṛtti ādi vyavahāreṇa prayojana siddhi artham indriyāṇām vyūhaḥ karma kāritaḥ tasmāt anudbhūta rūpa sparśaḥ nāyanaḥ raśmiḥ iti niścīyate anyathā anupalabhyamānasya kāminī ādeḥ aneka raśmi sannipāte dāha prasaṅgena vyavahāra viyogāt iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.1.41–3.1.42	 nanu āvaraṇa anumeyaḥ cākṣuṣaḥ raśmiḥ iti uktam katham iti atas āha dravdha viśeṣe ca pratighātāt āvaraṇa upapattiḥ kuḍya ādi dravya viśeṣe cākṣuṣasya raśmeḥ pratighātāt pratihanyamāna tvāt āvaraṇa upapattiḥ kuḍya ādi antaritasya upalabdhi praṅgāt tasmāt asti āvaraṇam tat anumāpakam iti sūtra arthaḥ nanu bhautikasya raśmeḥ dravya viśeṣa pratighātāt āvaraṇa upapattiḥ uktāḥ tat ayuktam kāca abhra paṭala ādiṣu apratighātāt abhautika tvena āvaraṇa anupapattiḥ iti atas āha avyabhicārāt tu pratighātaḥ bhautika dharmaḥ bhautikānām api pradīpa raśmi prabhṛtīnām kāca abhra paṭala ādiṣu su accha dravyeṣu apratighāta darśanena vyabhicāra annābhautika dharmaḥ pratighātaḥ pratighātaḥ tu avyabhicārāt bhautika dharmaḥ tasmāt āvaraṇa upapattiḥ iti siddham āvaraṇa anumeya tvam cākṣuṣasya raśmeḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.1.43–3.1.44	 atha idānīm eka deśi matena uttaram āha madhyandina ulkā prakāśa anupalabdhi vat tad anupalabdhiḥ tasya cākṣuṣasya raśmeḥ anupalabdhiḥ madhyandina ulkā prakāśa anupalabdhi vat yathā madhyandina ulkā prakāśaḥ āditya prakāśena abhibhūta tvāt na upalabhyate tathā cākṣuṣaḥ api raśmiḥ prakāśa abhibhava at na upalabhyate iti sūtra arthaḥ tat etat dūṣayati na rātrau= api anupalabdheḥ cākṣuṣasya raśmeḥ abhibhavāt anupalabdhiḥ iti yat uktam tat na kasmāt rātrau= api anupalabdheḥ divā abhibhavāt anupalabdhaḥ ulkā prakāśaḥ yathā rātrau= upalabhyate na tathā na ayanam tejaḥ rātrau= api upalabhyate tasmāt rātrau= api anupalabdheḥ abhibhava anna upalabhyate iti etat na iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.1.45	 itas api abhibhavaḥ na asti iti āha bāhya prakāśa anugrahāt viṣaya upalabdheḥ anabhivyaktitaḥ anupalabdhiḥ yatra abhibhavaḥ tatra bāhya prakāśa anapekṣa tvam dṛṣṭam upalabdhau yathā ulkā prakāśe na ca tathā cākṣuṣasya raśmeḥ bāhya prakāśa anapekṣa tvam dṛṣṭam viṣaya upalabdhau tasmāt bāhya prakāśāt viṣaya upalabdheḥ anabhivyagra tayā anudbhūta rūpa anutpatteḥ eva anupalabdhiḥ na abhibhūtasya iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.1.46	 na kevalam bāhya prakāśa apekṣi tva abhāvāt eva abhibhava abhāvaḥ kim tarhi anudbhūta rūpa tvāt api iti āha abhivyaktau ca abhibhavāt abhivyaktiḥ udbhūtiḥ abhibhavāt ulkā prakāśāt vā yatra abhivyaktiḥ na asti tatra abhibhavaḥ na asti yathā viṣakta avayave pāthasi anudbhūta rūpaḥ ca nāyanaḥ raśmiḥ tasmāt na tasya abhibhavāt anupalabdhiḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.1.47	 na kevalam āvaraṇa anumeyaḥ cākṣuṣaḥ raśmiḥ kim tarhi cākṣuṣa ādi liṅga anumeyaḥ ca iti āha naktañcara nayana raśmi darśanāt ca naktañcarāṇām pṛṣadaṃśa prabhṛtīnām cakṣuṣi raśmi darśanāt tat dṛṣṭāntena mānuṣam api cakṣuḥ raśmi vat cakṣuṣṭvāt naktañcara cakṣuḥ vat iti anumātum śakyam eva na ca mārjāra manuṣya tva ādi jāti bheda vat indriyāṇām bhedaḥ iti vācyam ubhayatra āvaraṇa asadbhāvena raśmi sadbhāvasya apahnotum a śakyatvāt tasmāt asti cākṣuṣaḥ raśmiḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.1.48	 raśmi artha sannikarṣa viśeṣāt mahat aṇu grahaṇam iti uktam tad ayuktam indriyāṇām aprāpya kāri tvāt iti āha aprāpyagrahaṇam kāca abhra paṭala sphaṭika antarita upalabdheḥ aprāpya viṣayam indriyāṇi grahaṇam kurvanti tasmāt kāca abhra paṭala sphaṭika antaritānām vyavahitānām upalabdheḥ kāca ādi vyavahiteṣu artheṣu tṛṇa ādīnām iva saṃbandha abhāve api indriyāṇi upalabdhim utpādayanti yatas tasmāt aprāpya kārīṇi ataā iva abhautikāni iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.1.49–3.1.50	 tat etat na iti āha kuḍya antarita anupalabdheḥ apratiṣedhaḥ prāpteḥ yadi prāpya kāri tvam indriyāṇām na syāt tadā kuḍya ādi vyavahitānām anupalabdhiḥ na syāt dṛśyate ca anupalabdhiḥ atas manyāmahe na aprāpya kārīṇi iti sūtra arthaḥ yat punar kāca ādi vyavahiteṣu artheṣu tṛṇa ādīnām iva indriyāṇām api saṃbandha abhāvaḥ iti uktam tat ayuktam iti āha apratighātāt sannikarṣa upapattiḥ rindriyāṇām tad vyavahiteṣu artheṣu iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.1.51–3.1.52	 bhautikasya asti pratighātaḥ iti etat api na asti iti āha āditya raśmeḥ sphaṭika antarite api dāhye avighātāt āditya raśmeḥ kumbha ambhasi avighātāt pradīpa raśmeḥ sphaṭika antargata dṛśye avighātāt vibhāvasoḥ ca dāhye bharjana kapāla sthe avighātāt bhautika tve api indriyāṇām pratighātaḥ na iti sūtra arthaḥ codayati na itara itara dharma prasaṅgāt kuḍya ādiṣu pratighātaḥ kāca ādiṣu apratighātaḥ iti etat na kasmāt itaretara dharma prasaṅgāt kvacid prāptiḥ kvacid aprāptiḥ indriyāṇām iti etat ayuktam iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.1.53	 pariharati ādarśa udakayoḥ prasāda svābhāvyāt rūpa upalabdhi vat tad upalavdhiḥ yathā ādarśa udakayoḥ darpaṇa salilayoḥ prasāda svābhāvyāt prasāda svaccha tvāt rūpa upalabdhiḥ mukha ādi pratibimba upalabdhiḥ na kuḍya ghaṭayā uḥ asvaccha svabhāva tvāt samāne api vastu tve tathā tad upalabdhiḥ tasya kāca ādi vyavahitasya upalabdhiḥ na kuḍya ādi vyavahitasya samāne api vastu tve iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.1.54	 kvacid pratighātaḥ kvacid apratighātaḥ iti eva katham samāne api vastutvaḥ iti na aśaṅkanīyam vastu svabhāvasya aparyanuyojya tvāt iti āha dṛṣṭa anumitānām hi niyoga pratiṣedha anupapattiḥ pramāṇasya tattva viṣaya tvāt yena sva bhavena amī pramāṇena parijñātāḥ tena eva svabhāvena te avatiṣṭhante na punar amīṣām svabhāva antaram asti tatra pramāṇa abhāvāt tatas ca kāca ādiṣu avyavadhānam vyavadhānañca kuḍya ādiṣu indriyāṇām upalabhyate tarhi tathā abhyupagantavyam na itara itara dharma prasaṅgaḥ codanīyaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.1.55	 idānīm indriyāṇām eka aneka tvam vicārayitum saṃśayam āha sthāna anya tve nānā tvāt avayavi nānā sthāna tvāt ca saṃśayaḥ sthāna anyatva śabdena nānā sthāna tvam eva ucyate nānā sthāna tvena nānātvam dṛṣṭam bhinna bhājana gatānām tāla phalānām avayavinaḥ ca eka tvam dṛṣṭam nānā sthānasya tatas ca nānā sthāna tvāt avayavi vat indriyāṇām eka tvam āhosvit bhinna bhājana gata tāla phala vat aneka tvam iti saṃśayaḥ bhavati iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.1.56–3.1.57	 pūrva pakṣam parigṛhṇāti tvac avyatirekāt tvac ekam indriyam kasmāt avyatirekāt sarva indriya adhiṣṭhānānām tvacā vyāpta tvāt yasmāt satyām tvaci sarva indriya ādi adhiṣṭhāna vyāpinyām viṣaya grahaṇāni saṃbhavanti nāsatyām tasmāt sā tvac ekam indriyam iti sūtra arthaḥ dūṣayati na yugapad artha anupalabdheḥ yadi tvac ekam indriyam syāt tadā tasya karaṇa tvena prāpya kāri tvāt aprāptasya vidūra deśa avasthitasya rūpa ādeḥ grahaṇam na syāt iti karaṇa dharma atikrameṇa aprāpya kāri tvam abhyupagantavyam tathā satya prāptasya rūpa ādeḥ yugapad upalabdhyā bhavitavyam na ca etat asti tasmāt yugapad padārtha anupalabdheḥ na tvac ekam indriyam iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.1.58	 tat evam para pakṣa bhāvam dūṣayitvā sva pakṣa sādhanam āha indriya artha pañcatvāt indriyāṇām arthāḥ indriya arthāḥ prayojanāni teṣām pañcatvāt pañca bāhya indriyāṇi rūpa rasa gandha sparśa śabdeṣu madhye rūpa grahaṇa eka prayojanam cakṣuḥ evam itarāṇi api tad tad viṣaya eka prayojanāni iti prayojana pañcatvāt pañca indriyāṇi iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.1.59–3.1.60	 codayati na tad artha bahu tvāt yadi prayojana pañcatvāt indriya pañcatvam abhyupagamyate tarhi prayojana bahu tvāt bahūni indriyāṇi api prasajyeran= iti na prayojana pañcatvāt indriya pañcatvam siddhyati atiprasaṅga doṣam āpādayati iti sūtra arthaḥ pariharati gandha tva avyatirekāt gandha ādīnām apratiṣedhaḥ yadi api gandha ādīnām saurabha ādi dharma bhedāt prayojana bahu tvam tathā api gandha tva avyatirekāt gandha tva sāmānyena upaḍhaukitā gandha ādayaḥ pañcavidhāḥ eva iti prayojana pañcatvāt indriya pañcatvam siddhi anna atiprasaṅgam āpādayati iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.1.61	 punar codayati viṣaya tva avyatirekāt eka tvam yadi saurabhā saurabha ādi dharma bhedena aneka tve api gandha tva ādi sāmānya upaśleṣa balāt gandha ādayaḥ pañcavidhāḥ iti prayojana pañcatvam tarhi viṣaya tva avyatirekāt viṣaya tva sāmānya upaśleṣaṇāt sarveṣām viṣayāṇām ekatvam iti prayojanasya eka tvāt ekam indriyam prasajyeta iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.1.62^1	 pariharati na buddhi lakṣaṇa adhiṣṭhāna gati ākṛti jāti pañcatvebhyaḥ na viṣaya tva avyatirekāt eka tvam indriyāṇām kutas buddhi lakṣaṇa adhiṣṭhāna gati ākṛti jāti pañcatvebhyaḥ buddhi lakṣaṇa śabdena prayojanam ucyate adhiṣṭhāna śabdena āśrayaḥ gati śabdena indriya pravṛttiḥ ākṛti śabdena pramāṇam jāti śabdena bhūtātmaka tvam teṣām pañcatvāt indriya pañcatvam yadi api prayojana bahu tvam saurabhā saurabhāt yadi api ca eka tvam viṣaya rūpeṇa tathā api tat karaṇa antara prayojakam na bhavati 
NTD_3.1.62^2	 yathā gandha grahaṇam indriya antareṇa anupapadyamānam ghrāṇa indriyam upasthāpayati na tathā saurabhā saurabha ādi dharma bhedaḥ kāraṇa antaram upasthāpayati ghrāṇena eva tad ubhaya grahaṇasya siddha tvāt evam indriya antareṣu api tad tad viṣaya grahaṇa bhedānām prayojakā prayojaka mūla tvam siddhyati evam adhiṣṭhāna gati ākṛti jāti pañcatve tadvatām pañcatva darśanāt ūhanīyam na api viṣaya tva avyatirekeṇa prayojana aikyāt eka tvam yugapad upalabdhi prasaṅgasya ukta tvāt tatas ca buddhi lakṣaṇa pañcatvāt indriya pañcatvam siddhyati evam adhiṣṭhāna gati ākṛti jāti pañcatve tadvatām pañcatva darśanāt indriya pañcatvam siddhyati iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.1.63	 nanu jāti śabdena bhūtātmakasya ukta tvāt bhūta pañcatvāt indriya pañcatvam uktam tat eva bhūtātmakam kutastyam iti atas āha bhūta guṇa viśeṣasya upalabdheḥ tādātyam saḥ eva arthaḥ svabhāvaḥ yasya saḥ ayam tad arthaḥ tasya bhāvaḥ tādarthyam bhūta ātmaka tvam indriyāṇām iti yāvat tat kutas bhūta guṇa viśeṣa upalabdheḥ yasya bhūtasya yaḥ asau guṇa viśeṣaḥ tasya vyañjakaḥ tad ātmakaḥ yathā hi bhūtacandana gandha vyañjaka saraka ādi pārthivaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ tathā ghrāṇam tasmāt pārthivam iti evam tat tat bhūta guṇa viśeṣasya vyañja tvāt tad ātmaka tvam indriyāṇām iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.1.64–3.1.65	 idānīm artha lakṣaṇam parīkṣamāṇaḥ pṛthivī ādīnām dravyāṇām guṇa an āñca gandha ādīnām indriyaiḥ asmaryamāṇa tva lakṣaṇam artha lakṣaṇam teṣām ekakasya ekaika guṇa tve sarvasya vā sarva guṇa tve na saṃbhavatti kim tarhi kasyacid ekaguṇa tve kasyacid dviguṇa tve kasyacid triguṇa tve kasyacid caturguṇa tve ca saṃbhavati iti guṇa viniyogam vikalpa pakṣa avalambanena āha gandha rasa rūpa sparśa śabdānām sparśa paryantāḥ pṛthivyāḥ ap tejaḥ vāyūnām pūrva pūrvam apohya ākāśasya uttaraḥ gandha rasa rūpa sparśa śabdānām madhye sparśa paryantā guṇāḥ pṛthivyāḥ ap tejaḥ vāyūnām pūrvam pūrvam apohya ākṛṣya triguṇa dviguṇa eka guṇa tvam ākāśasya uttaraḥ sparśa paryantānām niyata indriya grāhya tvam saṃbhavati iti sūtra dvitaya arthaḥ 
NTD_3.1.66	 codayati na sarva guṇa anupalabdheḥ na catur tri dvi eka guṇa tvam pṛthivī ādīnām iti vikalpa pakṣaḥ saṃbhavati kasmāt sarva guṇa anupalabdheḥ yat bhūta ātmakam yat indriyam tena tad guṇasya sarvasya upalabdhyā bhavitavyam naca upalabhyate ghrāṇa ādīnām gandha ādiṣu evaka eka grahaṇe naipuṇyasya dṛṣṭāta tva tasmāt sarva guṇānām anupalabdheḥ na vikalpena saṃbhavati iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.1.67–3.1.68	 katham tarhi guṇa viniyogaḥ iti ced tatra āha ekaika śyena uttara uttara guṇa sadbhāvāt uttara uttarāṇām tad anupalabdhiḥ ekaikaśyena iti sautraḥ nirdeśaḥ pṛthivī ādiṣu ekaikam bhūtam prati gandhānām ekaika apakarṣeṇa uttarottara guṇa sadbhāvāt yathā krameṇa ekaika guṇa tvāt uttara uttarāṇām tad anupalabdhiḥ tasya ca na catur triguṇasya upalabdhiḥ tasmāt teṣām bhūtānām tad ātmakānām ca indriyāṇām ekaika guṇa tvena guṇa antarāṇām avidyamāna tvena grahaṇa anarha tvāt iti sūtra arthaḥ nanu guṇa antara asaṃbhave katham ekasmin= aneka guṇāḥ gṛhyante iti atas āha saṃsarga tva aneka guṇa tva grahaṇam pṛthivī ādīnām ekaika guṇa tve api bhūta antara saṃsargāt aneka guṇa grahaṇam na tad guṇa tvena eva iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.1.69	 yadi saṃsargāt aneka guṇa grahaṇam tarhi pṛthivī ādīnām trayāṇām catur triguṇa tva niyamaḥ na upapadyate saṃsargasya ubhayatra samāna tvena aniyata guṇa tva pralaṅgāt iti āha viṣṭam hi aparam pareṇa viṣṭa tvam saṃyogaḥ hi yasmāt aparam pṛthivī ādi pareṇa ābādinā viṣṭam na apareṇa param tasmāt samāne api saṃyoge viṣṭa tva lakṣaṇe vahni dhūmayoḥ saṃvṛttayoḥ dhūmasya vyāpya tvam iva aparāt parasya viśeṣaḥ vidyate iti catur tri dviguṇa tva niyama vyavahāraḥ saṃbhavati iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.1.70	 na parthiva āpyayoḥ pratyakṣa tvāt yadi ekaika guṇa tvam tadā tejasaḥ eva rūpa tvam iti nīrūpayoḥ pārthiva āpyayoḥ pratyakṣa tvam na syāt dṛśyate pārthiva āpyayoḥ pratyakṣa tvam rūpavat tvena tasmāt pārthiva apyayoḥ dravyayoḥ pratyakṣa tvāt pārthiva āpyayoḥ rūpa rasayoḥ pratyakṣa tvāt na pṛthivyā udīnām ekaika guṇa tvam na api viṣṭa tvasya samāna tve api dhūmasya vyāpya tvam iva saṃsargi guṇa grahaṇe viśeṣa lābhaḥ vyāpya tve api anya guṇānām anyatra anupalabdheḥ atas pṛthivī ādīnām ekaika guṇa tvam iti na niyoga pakṣaḥ sādhīyān iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.1.71	 nanu mā abhūt niyoga pakṣaḥ tathā api vikalpa pakṣe sarva guṇa anupalabdhiḥ doṣa tvena coditā iti atas āha pūrvam pūrvam guṇa utkarṣāt tad pradhānam tasmāt na sarva guṇa upalabdhiḥ ghrāṇa ādīnām pūrvam pūrvam indriya gandha ādi guṇa utkarṣāt tad pradhānam sva utkṛṣṭa guṇa samāna jātīya guṇa abhivyañjakam na sva guṇa samāna jātīya guṇa mātra vyañjakam tasmāt catur triguṇa tve api na sarva guṇa upalabdhiḥ kim tarhi utkṛṣṭa guṇa samājātīya guṇa upalabdhiḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.1.72	 nanu pārthiva tve samāne api kiñcid eva pārthivam ghrāṇam kiñcinnā iti evamādi vyavasthānam kutastyam iti atas āha tad vyavasthānantu bhūyaḥ tvāt puruṣa artha nivṛtti samarthasya saṃsargaḥ puruṣa adṛṣṭa kāritaḥ bhūyas tvam tasmāt bhūyas tvāt adṛṣṭa upaḍhaukita dṛṣṭi viśeṣāt kiñcid eva pārthiva ādi kasyacid arthasya nivṛttau samartham maṇi mantra ādi vat iti teṣām indriyāṇām vyavasthānam saṃbhavati iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.1.73–3.1.74	 yadi ghrāṇa ādīni indriyāṇi gandha ādīnām grāhakāṇi tarhi sva gata gandha ādīnām api grāhakāṇi prasajyeḥ anna viśeṣāt iti āśaṅkya tad sahacaritasya indriya abhāvāt na tad grahaṇam saṃbhavati iti pariharati sva guṇam na upalabhante indriyāṇi kasmāt iti ced sa guṇānām indriya abhāvāt sūtra arthaḥ nigadena vyākhyātaḥ na śabda guṇa upalabdheḥ sva guṇam na upalabhante indriyāṇi iti ayuktam kasmāt sva guṇa grahaṇasya śabda guṇe śrotre dṛṣṭa tvāt iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.1.75	 pariharati tad upalabdhiḥ itaretara dravya guṇa vaidharmyāt tasya guṇasya śabdasya śrotreṇa upalabdhiḥ itaretara dravya guṇa vaidharmyāditara dravya vaidharmyāt sa guṇasya indriya bhāva abhāvāt śrotrasya itara gaṇa vaidharmyāt sva samāna jātīya guṇa abhivyañjaka abhāvāt śabdasya na punar sa guṇasya indriya tvena sva guṇa abhivyañjaka tvāt iti sūtra arthaḥ iti śrī bhaṭṭavāgīśvara viracitāyām nyāya sūtra tātparyadīpikāyām tṛtīya adhyāyasya prathama āhnikam samāptam 
NTD_3.2.1	 atha idānīm avasara prāptam buddhi lakṣaṇam parīkṣitum tasyāḥ nitya tva anitya tve saṃśayam āha karma ākāśa sādharmyāt saṃśayaḥ karma ca ākāśam ca karma ākāśe tābhyām sādharmyam buddheḥ asparśa tvam tasmāt karma ākāśa sādharmyāt kim nityā vā syāt anityāḥ vā buddhiḥ iti saṃśayaḥ yadi nityāḥ tadā buddhi tattvasya antaḥkaraṇa bhūtasya sāṃkhya abhimatasya jñāna upalabdhi ādi vyatiriktasya siddheḥ buddhi ādi paryaya śabda abhidheya tvam buddhi lakṣaṇam anupapannam syāt anitya āyāntu tasyām jñāna upalabdhi ādi avyatiriktasya siddheḥ tad paryāya abhidheya tvam buddhi lakṣaṇam upapannam syāt iti sūtra tātparya arthaḥ 
NTD_3.2.2	 tatra nitya tva vādyāha viṣaya pratyabhijñānāt yam viṣayam pūrvam ajñāsiṣam tam imam jānāmi iti viṣaya pratyabhijñānam dṛṣṭam na ca cit rūpasya kūṭastha nityasya ātmanaḥ ubhaya vat aneka jñāna ādi vṛtti yogaḥ sambhavati vikāri tva prasaṅgāt buddheḥ tu pariṇāma nitya tvāt tādṛśa jñāna ādi vṛtti yogaḥ sambhavati iti sā eva pūrva apara jñānayoḥ anusandha atrī viṣaya pratyabhijñānāt avatiṣṭhamānā buddhiḥ nityā iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.2.3	 siddhānti āha sādhya sama tvāda hetuḥ yathā buddheḥ nitya tvam sādhyam tathā pratyabhijñāna tvam api sādhyam kasmāt vedana dharmasya karaṇe anupapatteḥ utpattau vā kāraṇa antarasya avaśyam bhāvi tvena saṃjñā mātra bheda prasaṅgāt na ca cit rūpasya jñātṛ tvam vikāri tvena kūṭastha nitya tā parityāgāt tasmāt viṣaya pratyabhijñānāt pratyabhijñātuḥ ātmanaḥ nitya tvam siddhyati na buddheḥ tasyāḥ tatra apratibhāsamāna tvena viṣaya pratyabhijñāna ādi hetoḥ asiddha tvāt iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.2.4–3.2.5	 nityāyāḥ buddheḥ anityāḥ jñāna ātmikā vṛttayaḥ iti sā eva pratyabhijñātrī iti pakṣe aniṣṭa prasaṅgam sūtra dvayena āha na yugapada grahaṇāt apratyabhijñāne ca vināśa prasaṅgāt nityāyāḥ buddheḥ anityāḥ vṛttayaḥ iti etat na kasmāt yugapada grahaṇāt vṛtti vṛttim atora bhedena vṛttīnām avyavasthānāt yugapad viṣayā gṛhyeran na gṛhyante tasmāt yugapada grahaṇāt nityā buddhiḥ tathā apratyabhijñāne pratyabhijñāna lakṣaṇe vṛtti viśeṣe api vinaṣṭe tad aikyāt vṛttimatyāḥ buddheḥ api vināśa prasaṅgāt na nityāyāḥ buddheḥ anitya jñāna ātmaka vṛtti viśeṣa asambhavena pratyabhijñātṛtvam iti sūtra dvitaya arthaḥ 
NTD_3.2.6–3.2.7	 nanu nityā vyāpinī buddhiḥ antaḥkaraṇa bhūtāḥ yugapad aneka grahaṇa prasaṅgāt na abhyupagamyate katham tarhi yugapad a grahaṇam iti āśaṅkya āha krama vṛtti tvāt ayugapad grahaṇam paramāṇu parimāṇam avibhu vā ekam antaḥkaraṇam paryāyeṇa indriyaiḥ saṃbadhyate iti krama vṛtti tvāt ayugapad grahaṇam vṛtti vṛttim atoḥ nānātve na sambhavati iti sūtra arthaḥ apratyabhijñānañca viṣaya antara vyāsaṅgāt viṣaya antara vyāsakte manasi vṛtti vṛttim atoḥ atyanta bhedena asmad pakṣe pratyabhijñāna abhāvaḥ ca sambhavati na bhavat pakṣaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.2.8	 antaḥkaraṇa rūpāyāḥ buddheḥ vyāpi tve api paryāyeṇa indriyaiḥ saṃyogaḥ kasmāt na iṣyate iti āśaṅkya āha na gati abhāvāt na paryāyeṇa indriyaiḥ vyāpinyā buddheḥ saṃyogaḥ sambhavati kasmāt gati abhāvāt vyāpi tvena vyoma vat buddheḥ api gamana kriyāyāḥ abhāvena paryāya yoga asambhavāt yugapad aneka viṣaya grahaṇasya tādavasthyāt na ca dīrgha śaṣkulī bhakṣaṇa nyāyena tad saṃbhavaḥ padma patra śata vyakti bheda pratyaya vada aśutara vināśi tve aneka viṣaya grahaṇa pratyayasya tatra api bhrānta tvāt tasmāt na yugapada grahaṇam buddhi nitya tva vādinaḥ sambhavati iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.2.9	 nanu buddhi nitya tve api paryāya grahaṇa abhāvaḥ doṣaḥ uktaḥ paryāya grahaṇasya apāramārthika tvāt iti āha sphaṭika anyat tva abhimāna vat tad anyatva abhimānaḥ yathā ekasya sphaṭika maṇeḥ japākarṇikāra ādi aneka upādhi saṃbandhāt rakta pīta ādi bhedaḥ na parama arthaḥ evam antaḥkaraṇa maṇeḥ api indriya praṇālikayā viṣaya ākāra pariṇatasya tad tad viṣaya uparāga vaśāt grahaṇa bhedaḥ upalakṣyate tad uparāgāt ca pratibimba udaya krameṇa cit rūpā bhede api jīve bhoga caitanya bheda iti na paryāya grahaṇa abhāvaḥ sāṃkhyasya doṣāya iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.2.10^1	 atra kvacid parama artha bheda pratyayam vinā upādhīnām api bheda asambhavena tad upādhi adhīna pārama arthika bhedasya tena eva sphaṭika dṛṣṭāntena anupapatteḥ bheda pratyayānām māna bādhita viṣaye paramārtha tvāt pratibimba nyāyena bhoga caitanya bhedasya jīve nirūpayitum aśakyatvāt ekasmin bodhe boddha dvittvā upapatteḥ ca tad tad viṣaya grahaṇāni paramārthataḥ bhinnāni iti paryāya grahaṇa abhāva doṣaḥ tad avastha eva iti parihāraḥ atispaṣṭaḥ iti manvānaḥ śākya mata avalambanena dūṣaṇam āha sphaṭike api apara apara utpatteḥ kṣaṇika tvāt vyaktīnām ahetuḥ 
NTD_3.2.10^2	 sphaṭika anyatva abhimāna vat buddheḥ api anyatva abhimānaḥ aparama arthaḥ iti ayam pūrva ukta parihāraḥ na hetuḥ kasmāt sphaṭike apara apara utpatteḥ aparasya apara sphaṭika bhedasya utpatteḥ śveta rakta pīta ādi sphaṭika bhedānām pṛthak pṛthak utpatteḥ etat ca kutas iti ced kṣaṇika tvāt vyaktīnām śarīra ādi vyaktīnām āhāra pariṇāma vaśāt upacaya apacaya prabandha darśanena pratikṣaṇam anya tvena kṣaṇika tvāt dṛṣṭāntena sphaṭika ādīnām api sattvena kṣaṇika tva siddheḥ yat sat tad kṣaṇikam yathā śarīram  tathā ca vivāda adhyāsitāḥ sphaṭika ādayaḥ iti tasmāt sphaṭika anyatva abhimāna vat tad anyatva abhimānaḥ iti ayam ahetuḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.2.11	 atra kṣaṇa sthiti kālāḥ kṣaṇikāḥ iti kṣaṇika śabdena ātma kāla saṃbandhi tvam vivakṣitam pūrva apara bhāga rahita kāla kalā mātra saṃbandhi tvam vā na tāvat pūrvaḥ kalpaḥ sambhavati iti āha niyama hetu abhāvāt yathādarśanam abhyanujñā upacaya apacaya prabandha darśanena yadi api kvacid śarīra āt au= alpa kāla saṃbandhi tvam dṛṣṭam tathā api pāṣāṇa prabhṛtiṣu upacaya apacaya prabandha darśana abhāvena tad vyāptam alpa kālaḥ saṃbandhi tvam vyāpaka nivṛttyā nivartate iti sattvasya api tatra api vartamāna tvena anaikāntika tvena sarvatra alpa kāla saṃbandhi tva sādhakasya niyama hetoḥ abhāvāt kvacid alpa kāla saṃbandhi tvam kvacid bahu kāla saṃbandhi tvam iti yathādarśanam yathāpramāṇam abhyanujñā nyāyena iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.2.12^1	 atha dvitīyaḥ kalpaḥ vivakṣitaḥ iti ced na utpatti vināśa kāraṇa anupalabdheḥ utpatti kāraṇam tāvat avayava upacayaḥ vināśa kāraṇam avayava apacayaḥ tat ubhayam avasthita vastu viṣaya tvāt pūrva apara bhāgarahitakālakṣaṇa mātram kṣaṇika tvam upalakṣyate na hetunā sarva bhāvānām kṣaṇika tvam eva sādhayati sattvam artha kriyā kāri tvam bhāvasya tat ca krama ākramābhyām vyāptam prakāra antarasya asamvāt tau ca kramākramau sthireṣu na sambhavataḥ samarthasya kṣepā saṃbhavena krama abhāvāt asamarthasya tena prayojana asambhavāt kṛta sakala kāryasya dvitīya ādi kṣaṇeṣu aprasaṅgāt ca na ca krama ākrama vat sahakāri samavadhāna vaśāt bhāvasya krama ākramābhyām vyāptam artha kriyā kāritvam vācyam sahakāriṇā bhāvasya atiśaya sādhanasya eva kāraṇa tvena bhāvasya akāraṇa tva prasaṅgāt anatiśaya ādhāne tu anupakāriṇī apekṣā virahaḥ iti sahakāri tvasya eva asambhavāt 
NTD_3.2.12^2	 tasmāt krama ākramābhyām vyāptam artha kriyā kāritva lakṣaṇam sattvam tayoḥ vyāpakayoḥ anupalabdhyā sthirebhyaḥ vyāvartamānaḥ kṣaṇikā ātmatayā avatiṣṭhate iti tasya āpi idam eva uttaram na utpatti vināśa kāraṇa anupalabdheḥ niranvayāt pūrva utpādane niranvaya vināśe ca yat kāraṇam pramāṇam artha kriyā kāritva lakṣaṇa tvam sattvam uktam tasya anupalabdheḥ sa apekṣa tva anapekṣa tvābhyām vyāptasya tasya tayoḥ vyāpakayoḥ anupalabdhyā kṣaṇikeṣu anupalabdheḥ tathā hi kṣaṇikaḥ hi bhāvaḥ sa apekṣaḥ vā artha kriyām karoti nirapekṣaḥ vā na tāvat sāpekṣaḥ apekṣāyā sthāyi dharma tvena kṣaṇikeṣu asambhavāt na api nirapekṣaḥ kṛṣi ādi parikarma nirapekṣāt kusūla nihitāt api bījāt aṃkura ādi kārya utpatti prasaṅgāt na ca parikarma sāpekṣasya bījasya aṅkura janana sāmarthyam na kusūla nihitasya iti vācyam nirapekṣa tva hā ni prasaṅgāt na ca nirapekṣa tve api sva kāraṇa paramparā labdha janmanām daivānām upanatānām avani pavana pāthaḥ prabhṛtīnām ajña tvena anyatara virati abhāvāt samartha bīja kṣaṇa utpattau sānnidhyam iti vācyam 
NTD_3.2.12^3	 kṛṣīvala ādeḥ jña tvena virati sambhavena sānnidhya prasaṅgāt na ca sva utpattāvantyasya bīja kṣaṇasya anya sāpekṣa tvam na punar sva kāryaḥ iti vācyam utpadyamānasya anyasya samartha bīja kṣaṇasya sva kāraṇa bīja kṣaṇa vyatiriktam tad samāna kāla salila ādi kṣaṇa apekṣa tve nānā kāraṇa janyasya kāryasya nānā tvena eka rūpya bīja kṣaṇasya abhāva prasaṅgāt tad kāraṇasya bīja kṣaṇasya sva samāna kāla vastu antara apekṣasya tad utpādaka tvena sa apekṣa tvāt kṣaṇika tva hā niprasaṅgaḥ na ca upādāna sahakāri tayā kṛtam kārya rūpa vaiṣamyam tad bhedasya eva śākyamate aśakya nirūpaṇa tvāt tat evam sa apekṣa tva anapekṣa tvayoḥ vyāpakayoḥ anupalabdhyā sattva hetoḥ vyāvṛtti rasādhāraṇa tvam kiñca kvacid akṣaṇikā anabhyupagame sattva hetoḥ tasmāt vyāvṛttiḥ aśakya nirūpaṇa iti tad sattva siddheḥ hetoḥ anaikāntika tvam 
NTD_3.2.12^4	 na ca kalpita sthairyasya rūpa ādeḥ vipakṣa tvam tad mūla anumānasya kālpanika tvena kṣaṇika tvasya api kālpa nikatva āpatteḥ na ca sahakāriṇā atiśaya ādhāne bhāvasya anya tvam dharma dharmiṇoḥ bheda abhyupagamena dharma utpāde api dharmiṇaḥ tādavasthyāt na api atiprasaṅgaḥ kalpya tva aviśeṣe api kaścid eva kasyacid dharmaḥ iti vyāpya vyāpaka bhāvaḥ iva pramāṇa siddha tvāt tasmāt sthirasya bhāvasya krama vat sahakāri samavadhāna vaśāt krameṇa tad tad kārya janaka tvam gati antara abhāvāt abhyupagantavyam sarvaiḥ iti na api kṛtaka bhāvasya vināśasya dhruva bhāvi tvena nirhetuka tvāt kṣaṇika tva siddhiḥ dhruva bhāvi tvasya sa hetukāyām kalāpa ādi saṃtatau= api sambhavena anaikāntika tvāt tasmāt niranvaya vināśāt pūrva utpāda lakṣaṇa kṣaṇika tva sādhanānām sattva ādi hetūnām pramāṇa tvena anupalabdheḥ na pūrva apara kāla rahita kāla mātra saṃbandhi tvam kṣaṇika tvam iti dvitīyaḥ kalpaḥ sambhavati iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.2.13	 sphaṭikasya utpatti vināśa kāraṇa anupalabdheḥ na utpatti vināśau= iti yat uktam pūrva sūtreṇa tat ayuktam iti āha kṣīra vināśa kāraṇa anupalabdhi vat dadhi utpatti vat ca tad utpattiḥ yathā kṣīrasya vināśānupalambhe api nāśaḥ dadhnaḥ ca utpatti kāraṇa anupalambhe api tat utpādaḥ abhyupagamyate tathā sphaṭikasya pratikṣaṇam utpāda vināśau tad kāraṇa anupalambhe api abhyupaganta vyau= iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.2.14	 atra kaścid parihāram āha na payasaḥ pariṇāmaḥ guṇa antara prādurbhāvāt vināśa utpatti kāraṇa anupalambhe api kṣīra dadhnoḥ vināśa utpādau bhavataḥ iti etat na kasmāt payasaḥ pariṇāmaḥ guṇa antara prādurbhāvāt payaḥ dadhi bhavati iti atra na payaḥ dravya vināśaḥ kim tarhi pariṇāmaḥ kaḥ punar pariṇāmaḥ pūrva dharma tirodhānena dharma antara prādurbhāvaḥ pūrva guṇa nivṛttau guṇa antara prādurbhāvaḥ vā ubhayatra api dravya vināśa utpatti asambhavāt kāraṇa anupalambhe api payaḥ dravyam vinaśyati dadhi utpadyate iti yat uktam tat na iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.2.15^1	 siddhānti āha kvacid vināśa kāraṇa anupalabdheḥ kvacid ca upalabdheḥ anekāntar vināśa kāraṇa anupalabdheḥ iti upalakṣaṇam kāraṇa anupalabdheḥ api draṣṭavyam tatas ca vināśa utpatti kāraṇa anupalabdheḥ hetoḥ kvacid kṣīra dadhnoḥ vināśa utpādakayoḥ upalabdheḥ kvacid tasmin= eva hetau sati api ghaṭa ādau pratikṣaṇa vināśa utpādakayoḥ anupalabdheḥ hetoḥ anaikāntika tvāt kim anupalabhyamāna kāraṇaka kṣīra dadhi vināśa utpāda vat sphaṭika ādi vyaktīnām vināśa utpādau syātām āhosvit anupalabhyamāna kāraṇaka kumabha ādi pratikṣaṇa vināśa utpāda abhāvavat vināśa utpādau na syātām iti ayam arthaḥ anekāntaḥ yadi saṃdigdhaḥ ayam arthaḥ tarhi bhavat abhilaṣita makṣaṇika tvam na sphaṭika ādīnām siddhi ati iti āśaṅkya āha yaḥ atra sādhakaḥ tasya abhyanujñānāt apratiṣedhaḥ atra kṣaṇike dadhi vat kumbha vat ca iti dṛṣṭānta dvaye yaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ sādhakaḥ pramāṇa aviruddha tvena niṣeddhum aśakyaḥ 
NTD_3.2.15^2–3.2.16^1	 tasya kumbha ādeḥ anujñānāt sphaṭika ādīnām akṣaṇika tvasya pratiṣedhaḥ avivāda siddheṣu ghaṭa śarāva ādiṣu vināśa utpādayoḥ niyamena sa kāraṇa tva darśanāt yatra tayoḥ kāraṇam na upalabhyate tatra tau na bhavataḥ iti pratikṣaṇa vināśa utpādayoḥ kāraṇam na upalabhyate tatra tau na bhavataḥ iti pratikṣaṇa vināśa utpādayoḥ kāraṇa abhāvena ghaṭa ādiṣu iva abhāvāt abādhita pratyabhijñayā sthira tva grahaṇāt ca tasya eva dṛṣṭāntasya sādhaka tvāt abhyanujñeya tvam na payaḥ dṛṣṭāntasya tayoḥ utpāda vināśa darśanena eva adya utpāda vināśa vat sa kāraṇaka tvasya anumāna prasiddha tvena tad kāraṇa anupalabdheḥ asiddha tvāt 
NTD_3.2.15^2–3.2.16^2	 satkārya vāda anabhyupagamena pariṇāma vāda pratiṣedhāt ca tasmāt akṣaṇikāḥ padārthāḥ na api nityāḥ buddhi kim tarhi anityāḥ upalabdhi ādi paryāya śabda vācyā iti sūtra arthaḥ anitya tve tasya cākṣuṣa pratyakṣa tvena buddheḥ guṇa tve siddhe kasya ayam guṇaḥ iti cintayitum saṃśayam āha sannikarṣa utpatteḥ saṃśayaḥ ātma indriya manaḥ arthānām sannikarṣāt utpadyamānā buddhiḥ kimātma guṇaḥ kim vā indriyāṇām āhosvid arthānām atha manasaḥ iti viśeṣa adarśanena saṃśayaḥ bhavati iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.2.17	 ātma ijñānam indriyāṇām arthānām vā guṇaḥ na bhavati iti āha na indriya arthayoḥ tad vināśe api jñāna avasthānāt indriya arthayoḥ na jñānam guṇaḥ kasmāt tad vināśe api jñāna avasthāt tayoḥ indriya arthayoḥ vināśe api adrākṣam iti smaraṇa jñānasya avasthānāt yadi tayoḥ jñātṛ tvam tadā jñātroḥ tayoḥ abhāve tad āśraya jñānasya vā avasthānam na syāt dṛśyate ca avasthānam tasmāt na tad guṇaḥ smṛti jñānam tat dṛṣṭāntena jñāna antaram api na tad guṇaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.2.18–3.2.19	 astu tarhi manaḥ guṇaḥ jñānam iti āśaṅkya āha yugapad jñeya anupalabdheḥ ca na manasaḥ yugapad jñeya anupalabdheḥ hetoḥ yat anumitam karaṇa tvena na tasya manasaḥ guṇaḥ jñānam tasya jñātṛ tvena karaṇa tva hāni prasaṅgāt iti sūtra arthaḥ kasya tarhi guṇaḥ iti atas āha jñasya vaśitvāt jānāti iti jñaḥ ātmā tasya guṇaḥ jñānam kutas vaśitvāt vaśī jñātāḥ avaśyam karaṇam tad guṇa tve tasya karaṇa bhāva nivṛttiḥ syāt iti vaśinaḥ svatantrasya ātmanaḥ guṇaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.2.20–3.2.21	 ātma guṇa tve hetu antaram āha yugapad jñeya upalabdheḥ ca yogī khalu ṛddhau prādurbhūtāyām vikaraṇa dharmā sa indriyāṇi deha antarāṇi nirmāya yugapad jñeyāni upalabhate iti dṛṣṭam tat ca etat vibhau jñātari upapadyate na aṇau manasi iti yoginaḥ yugapad jñeya upalabdheḥ ca hetoḥ vibhunaḥ jñānam guṇaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ nanu vibhu tve antaḥkaraṇasya yugapad upalabdhi doṣa prasaṅgāt aṇu tvam abhyupagantavyam sa ca ātmanaḥ vibhu tve api samānaḥ iti yugapad jñeya upalabdhiḥ yoginaḥ na syāt iti āha tad ātma guṇa tve api tulyam tasya vibhu tvasya ātma guṇa tve api yugapad indraya saṃbandhena paryāya saṃbandha abhāvāt yugapad upalabdhi lakṣaṇam tulyam iti ātmanaḥ api aṇu tva prasaṅgāt yugapad jñeya upalabdhiḥ yoginaḥ na syāt iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.2.22–3.2.23	 pariharati sannikarṣa abhāvāt tad anutpattiḥ tasyāḥ anutpattiḥ yugapad jñeya upalabdheḥ anutpattiḥ tatas ca ātmanaḥ aṇu tva prasaṅga abhāvāt vikaraṇa dharma tvamaṇaḥ vibhu tvena kadācid yugapad jñeya upalabdhiḥ ca sambhavati iti sūtra arthaḥ ātma indriya artha sannikarṣam eva jñāna utpattau kāraṇam na ātma manaḥ sannikarṣaḥ iti ced tatra āha na utpatti kāraṇa anapadeśāt yadi ātma manaḥ sannikarṣaḥ na kāraṇam tadātma indriya artha sannikarṣa mātrāt jñānam utpadyate om iti ced naḥ utpatti kāraṇa anapadeśāt tāvat mātrāt utpadyate iti atra kāraṇam pramāṇam na apadiśyate tasmāt kāraṇa anapadeśāt śarīrāt bahis api jñāna upeda prasaṅgāt ca ātma manaḥ sannikarṣaḥ api kāraṇam iti arthaḥ 
NTD_3.2.24–3.2.25	 buddheḥ ātma guṇa tve pūrva doṣam āha vināśa kāraṇa anupalabdheḥ ca avasthāne tad nitya tva prasaṅgaḥ kāraṇa vināśāt virodhi guṇa prādurbhāvāt ca guṇānām vināśaḥ bhavati tat ubhayam atra na asti iti vināśa kāraṇa anupalabdheḥ avasthāne tad nitya tva prasaṅgaḥ tasya doṣaḥ prasaṅga doṣaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ pariharati anitya tva grahaṇāt buddheḥ buddhi antara vināśaḥ śabda vat buddhi antara nitya tvasya sādhita tvāt savaiḥ gṛhyamāṇa tvāt ca buddhi antara virodhaḥ uttarottara buddhyā pūrva pūrva buddheḥ vināśaḥ śabda vat antyāya aḥ tu buddheḥ adṛṣṭa kṣayāt vināśaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.2.26	 manasaḥ sannikarṣasya kāraṇasya ayaugapadyāt yugapad jñeya anupalabdhiḥ ātmanaḥ tarhi yatra kāraṇasya saṃskārasya yaugapadyam asti tatra smṛti jñānāni yugapad utpadyeran= itya āśaṅkya eka deśi matena parihāram āha jñāna samaveta ātma pradeśa sannikarṣān sanasaḥ smṛti upapatteḥ na yugapad utpattiḥ jñāyate anena smaryamāṇaḥ arthaḥ iti jñānam saṃskāraḥ tena samavetaiḥ ātma deśaiḥ sannikarṣāt smṛti upapatteḥ na yugapad smṛtīnām utpattiḥ tad saṃskāra samavāyi ātma pradeśānām aneka tvena antaḥkaraṇasya ayaugapadyāt iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.2.27–3.2.28	 tat eka deśi matam dūṣayati na antar śarīra vṛtti tvāt manasaḥ manasaḥ antar śarīram vṛtti tvāt yāvat prāyaṇam śarīra manas sannikarṣāt tad tad smṛti ādi kārya utpatteḥ śarīrāt bahis jñāna saṃskṛtaiḥ ātma pradeśaiḥ sannikarṣa abhāvāt tad saṃyoga paryāyeṇa paryāya utpattiḥ smṛtīnām iti sūtra arthaḥ codayati sādhya tvāt ahetuḥ śarīra manas sannikarṣasya eva kārya utpādaka tvam na itarasya iti asya sādhya tvāt antar śarīra vṛttiḥ evam ahetuḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.2.29	 pariharati smarataḥ śarīra dhāraṇa upapatteḥ apratiṣedhaḥ yadi bahis viniḥsṛtya jñāna saṃskṛtaiḥ ātma pradeśaiḥ saṃyujya smṛtim utpādayati manaḥ tarhi smarataḥ puruṣasya dhāraka prayatna abhāvāt śarīra dhāraṇam na syāt dṛśyate ca śarīra dhāraṇam tasmāt śarīra dhāraṇa upapatteḥ manasaḥ antar śarīra tvasya apratiṣedhaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.2.30–3.2.31	 punar codayati na tad āśu gati tvāt tasya manasaḥ āśu gati tvāt bahis viniḥsṛtya kṛta kāryasya drutam āgamya dhāraka prayatna utpādaka tvam utpādya vā gamanam iti smarataḥ śarīra dhāraṇa upapattiḥ na iti sūtra arthaḥ pariharati na smaraṇa kāla aniyamāt kiñcid kṣipram smaryate kiñcid cireṇa yadā cireṇa tadā druta āgamanasya abhāvāt śarīra dhāraṇam na syāt śarīra saṃbandha nirapekṣa ātma manas sannikarṣasya jñāna utpādaka tve tad vaiyarthyañca syāt tasmāt kāraṇa kāla aniyamāt na tad āśu gati tvena śarīra dhāraṇam upapadyate iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.2.32	 tat evam sva matena śarīrāt bahis gamanam manasaḥ pratiṣiddhaya tasya eva eka deśi matena pratiṣedham āha ātma preraṇa yadṛcchā jña tābhiḥ ca na saṃyoga viśeṣaḥ na tāvat ātma preraṇena anya arthasya smṛti hetu saṃskāraḥ amuṣmin= ātma pradeśe samavetaḥ tena manaḥ saṃyujyatām iti ātma preraṇena tasya arthasya smṛta tvena smartavya tva abhāvāt na api yadṛcchayā su smūrṣayā manaḥ praṇidhānasya smṛti darśanena yādṛt chika tva asaṃbhavāt na jñatayā manasi jñātṛ tvasya pratiṣedhāt tasmāt ātma preraṇa yadṛcchā jña tānām ahetu tvāt gati antara abhāvāt ca na bahis saṃyogaḥ sambhavati iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.2.33	 tat eka deśi matam dūṣayati vyāsakta manasaḥ pāda vyathanena saṃyoga viśeṣeṇa samānam kvacid dṛśye vyāsakta manasaḥ puruṣasya adṛṣṭayā śarkarayā kaṇṭakena vā pāda vyathana hetuḥ saṃyoga viśeṣaḥ bhavati sukha duḥkha saṃvedanayoḥ dṛṣṭa tvāt na ca ātmā atra preraṇā ādi iti sambhavati atha ca asti saṃyoga viśeṣaḥ iti dehāt bahis api tadvat eva syāt adṛṣṭa vaśāt antar saṃbandhaḥ iti etat bahis api samānaḥ tasmāt vaya āsakta manasām pāda vyathanena saṃyoga viśeṣeṇa samāna tvāt na bahis gamanasya ayam parihāraḥ iti pūrvaḥ eva parihāraḥ nyāyyaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.2.34	 jñāna samaveta ātma pradeśa sannikarṣāt iti ayam smṛti yaugapadya pratiṣedhe na hetuḥ kaḥ tarhi hetuḥ iti āśaṅkya āha praṇidhāna liṅga ādi jñānānām ayugapad bhāvāt ayugapad smaraṇam na kevalāḥ saṃskārāḥ smṛti hetavaḥ kim tarhi praṇidhāna liṅga ādi jñānāni api atas teṣām ayugapad bhāvāt ayugapad bhāvaḥ smṛtīnām na ca praṇidhāna ādi nirapekṣam smārtam upapadyate iti vācyam tasya anabhyupagamāt na ca ātmanaḥ niṣpradeśa tvena sarva saṃskārāṇām eka deśa tvāt manaḥ sannikarṣa paryāya abhāvaḥ saṃskārāṇām śabda vat bāhya karaṇa sannidhāna apekṣayā vyāvṛtti tvena paryāya saṃbandha sambhavāt praṇidhāna ādi sa apekṣasya manassannikarṣasya ayaugapadyāt antaḥkaraṇasya yugapad aneka kriyā nivṛttau sāmarthya abhāvāt ca yugapada smaraṇam iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.2.35	 caitanyam ātmanaḥ icchā dveṣa ādayaḥ tu antaḥkaraṇasya iti buddhi samāna āśraya tvam icchā dveṣa prayatna ādīnām sāṃkhyāḥ na anumanyante tad nirākaraṇa artham āha jñasya icchā dveṣa nimitta tvāt ārambha nivṛttyoḥ sukha sādhanam jñātvā tad icchayā tad avāptaye pravṛttiḥ ārambhaḥ duḥkha sādhanam jñātvā tad dveṣāt tat parihārāya anyatra pravṛttiḥ nivṛttiḥ tayoḥ ārambha nivṛttyoḥ icchā dveṣa nimitta tvāt icchā dveṣayoḥ ca jñāna mūla tvāt jñāna ādīnām bhinna āśraya tve a tiprasaṅgāt buddhi samāna āśraya tvena jñasya puruṣasya eva icchā dveṣa ādayaḥ na anta karaṇasya iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.2.36	 yadi eka adhikaraṇa tvena puruṣasya eva ete iti iṣyate tarhi eka śarīra adhikaraṇa tvena api eka adhikaraṇa tvam siddhyati iti bhūta caitanyam prasaktam iti āha tad liṅga tvāt icchā dveṣayoḥ pārthiva ādyeṣu apratiṣedhaḥ te ārambha nivṛttī liṅge yayoḥ icchā dveṣayoḥ tau tad liṅgau tayoḥ bhāvaḥ tattvam tasmāt tad liṅga tvāt pravṛtti nivṛttyoḥ śarīre dṛṣṭa tvāt tad kāraṇayoḥ icchā dveṣayoḥ tad mūlāyāḥ buddheḥ api tad adhikaraṇa tvam bhinna adhikaraṇa tve ati prasaṅgāt iti pārthiva ādyeṣu caitanya ādīnām apratiṣedhaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.2.37	 pariharati niyama aniyamau tu tad viśeṣakau pravṛtti nivṛttyoḥ prayojya eka viṣaya tvam nimayaḥ aniyamaḥ tad abhāvaḥ tau niyata aniyatayoḥ bhṛta caitanyābhūta caitanyayoḥ viśeṣakau bhedakau= acetaneṣu para śu ādiṣu prayojya tvena ubhaya vādi siddheṣu pravṛtti nivṛttyoḥ niyamena darśanāt pravṛtti nivattimataḥ śarīrasya api tad dṛṣṭāntena prayojya tva niścayāt ajña tvam para śu ādi vat evam aṃśakti vat jña tve vā avayava caitanya prasaṅgāt kārya dravya viśeṣa guṇānām kāraṇa guṇa pūrvaka tvena śarīra ārambhakeṣu paramāṇuṣu caitanya abhyupagame pratyaya vyavasthā anumāna abhāvāt ca śarīrasya ajña tvena pravṛtti nivṛttyoḥ buddhiḥ avinā abhāvāt tad samāna āśraya tvena bhūta caitanya prasaṅgaḥ na iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.2.38	 manasaḥ tarhi caitanyam bhaviṣyati tad eka tvena eka adhikaraṇa tva sambhavāt avayava caitanya ādi doṣa prasaṅga abhāvāt ca iti atas āha yathā ukta hetu tvāt pāratantryāt sva kṛta abhyāgamāt ca na manasaḥ yathā ukta hetu tvāt darśanarspābhyām eka artha grahaṇāt iti evamādīnām ātma pratisandhātṛ tva sādhakānām hetu tvasya apratiṣedhāt manasaḥ tu kāraṇa tvena pāratantryāt sva karmaṇaḥ phalam svasmin= eva gamiṣyati iti sva kṛta abhyāgamāt ca ātmanaḥ eva kartṛ tva bhoktṛ tva siddheḥ na manasaḥ caitanyam sambhavati iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.2.39	 kasya tarhi caitanyam iti āha pariśeṣāt yathā ukta hetu upapatteḥ ca ātmanaḥ prasaktasya pratiṣedhe anyatra aprasaṅgāt śiṣyamāṇe saṃpratyayaḥ tasmāt pariśeṣāt pṛthivī ādi āśraya tvena prasaktasya caitanyasya pratiṣedhāt anyasya tad āśrayasya abhāvāt darśanarspanābhyām iti evamādibhiḥ yathā ukta hetubhiḥ ātmana upapatteḥ pramāṇa siddha tvāt ca ātmanaḥ eva caitanyam sambhavati iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.2.40–3.2.41^1	 smaraṇam tu ātmanaḥ jña svābhāvyāt praṇidhāna ādinā jñānānām yugapad bhāvāt yuga pada smaraṇam iti uktam tat idānīm darśayadi p r a ṇ i d h ā n a n i b a n d h a n ā b h y ā s a l i ṅ g a l a k ṣ a ṇ a s ā d ṛ ś y a p a r i g r a h ā ś r a y ā ś rita saṃbandha anantarya viyoga eka kārya virodha atiśaya prāpti vyavadhāna sukha duḥkha icchā dveṣa bhaya arthi tva kriyā rāga dhama adharma nimittebhyaḥ praṇidhānam avadhānam nibandhanam arthānām eka grantha upanibandhaḥ abhyāsaḥ jñāna āvṛttiḥ liṅgam avinābhūtam 
NTD_3.2.40–3.2.41^2	 lakṣaṇam cihnam sādṛśyam anyonya svarūpa tā parigrahaḥ sva svāmi saṃbandhaḥ āśrayaḥ rakṣakaḥ āśritaḥ rakṣyaḥ sambandhaḥ śiṣya upādhi ādi anurakta saṃbandha viśeṣaḥ ānantaryam krama nirdiṣṭeṣu paurvāparyam viyogaḥ virahaḥ eka kāryam bahūnām eka artha karaṇa tvam virodhaḥ vijigīṣamāṇayoḥ anyatara darśanena anyatara smaraṇam atiśayaḥ apūrva guṇa prāptiḥ prāptiḥ abhilaṣita artha saṃbhāvanā vyavadhānam niyata avadhāraṇam sukham anukūla vedanīyam duḥkham pratikūla vedanīyam icchā snehaḥ dveṣaḥ prajvalana ātmakaḥ bhayam duḥkha hetu sannipāta kṛtaḥ vikāraḥ arthi tvam ācchādana ādidravyākāṃkṣi tvam kriyā kāryam rāgaḥ kāminī āsaktiḥ dharmaḥ abhyudayasa adhamaḥ adharmaḥ tu viparīta sādhanaḥ tat etebhyaḥ nimittebhyaḥ smṛtiḥ bhavati iti teṣām ayugapad bhavitum arhati iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.2.42	 tat evam buddheḥ ātma guṇa tvam anitya tvañca prasādhya tatra viśeṣa cintā artham saṃśayam āha utpanna apavargi tvāt kāla antara avasthāyi tvāt ca anityānām saṃśayaḥ vidyut ādiṣu nityānām utpanna apavargi tvam dṛṣṭam kumbha ādiṣu kāla antara avasthāyi tvam tatas ca anitya tva sāmānya dharma darśanāt kim utpannā apavargiṇī buddhiḥ āhosvidh kāla antara avasthāyinī iti saṃśayaḥ bhavati iti sūtrāthaḥ 
NTD_3.2.43–3.2.44	 utpannā apavargiṇī iti āha karma anavasthāyi grahaṇāt karmaṇaḥ anavasthāyinaḥ grahaṇāt anavasthāyinī buddhiḥ siddhā iti kumbha ādiṣu api buddhiḥ anavasthāyinī buddhi tvāt karma buddhi vat vyavahite pratyakṣa tu a nivṛtti darśanāt iti satra arthaḥ codayati avyakta grahaṇam anavasthāyi tvāt vidyut saṃpāte rūpa avyakta grahaṇa vat anavasthāyinyā api vidyutā prakāśyamānānām ghaṭa ādīnām yathā rūpasya avyaktasya grahaṇam iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.2.45	 pariharati na pradīpa arciḥ santati abhivyakti grahaṇa vat tat grahaṇam anavasthāyi tve api yathā pradīpa arciṣām santatyā vartamānānām tad grāhiṇīnām ca buddhīnām anavasthāyi tve a pyabhivyakti grahaṇam dṛṣṭam tadvat buddheḥ anavasthāyi tve api ghaṭa ādīnām abhivyakti grahaṇam sambhavati tathā vidyut saṃpāta avyakta grahaṇa vacane buddheḥ anavasthāyitvā abhyupagamāt sarvasya api grahaṇasya viṣaye vyakta tvāt ca anavasthāyi tvena utpanna apavargiṇī buddhiḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.2.46	 bhūta indriya manasām caitanya pratiṣedhena arthāt śarīra caitanyam pratiṣiddham api tattva niścaya artha para tayā vipratiṣeddhum saṃśayam āha dravye sva guṇa para guṇa upalabdheḥ saṃśayaḥ dravye pāthasi sva guṇaḥ drava tvam upalabhyate para guṇaḥ ca uṣṇatā upalabhyate na ca śarīre caitanyam tat kim śarīra guṇaḥ kiṃvā anya guṇaḥ iti tatra upalabhyamāna tva aviśeṣa adarśana sannihitāt saṃśayaḥ bhavati iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.2.47	 śarīra guṇaḥ cetanaḥ iti āha yāvat śarīra bhāvi tvāt rūpa ādīnām ye śarīra viśeṣa guṇāḥ rūpa ādayaḥ te yāvat śarīra bhāvinaḥ dṛṣṭāḥ cetanā api ced śarīra viśeṣa guṇaḥ tayā api yāvat śarīra bhāvinyā bhavitavyam na tu etat asti tad rahitasya avasthāna darśanāt na api saṃyoga ādi vat sāmānya guṇaḥ tasyāḥ sva samaveta viśeṣaṇa viśiṣṭa tve sati sva āśraya eka jātīya avacchedaka tvena viśeṣa guṇa tvāt tasmāt śarīra guṇa vaidharmyāt na śarīra guṇaḥ cetanā iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.2.48	 nanu pārthive dravye śyāma ādeḥ viśeṣa guṇasya yāvat dravya bhāvi tvam dṛṣṭam tathā cetanāyāḥ api bhaviṣyati iti āśaṅkya āha na pāka ja guṇa antara utpatteḥ yadi api auṣṇya apekṣāt agni saṃyogāt ghaṭa ādyām a dravyasya śyāma ādeḥ guṇasya nivṛttiḥ tathā api tādṛśāt agni saṃyogāt pūrvarūpa ādi pradhvaṃsa apekṣāt pāka jasya rakta ādeḥ guṇa antarasya utpatteḥ na rūpa ādi hīnam kārya lakṣaṇam vā paramāṇu lakṣaṇam vā dravyam kadācid abhyupalabhyate śarīre tu na tathā cetanā aṃśe tad samāna jātīya guṇa antaram upalabhyate tat rahitasya eva śarīrasya dāha avasthānāt tasmāt pāka ja guṇa antara utpatteḥ na śyāma ādi guṇasya ayāvat dravya bhāvi tvam sambhavati iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.2.49	 itas api śyāma ādi vaiṣamyam iti āha pratidvandvi siddheḥ pāka jānām apratiṣedhaḥ pāka jānām rakta ādīnām guṇānām utpattau tad pratidvandvinām śyāma ādīnām nivartamānānām siddhe saha anavasthāna virodhena ayāvat dravya bhāvi tvam teṣu sambhavati na tu evam cetanāyāḥ pratidvandvi tvena nivartya tvam rakta ādi sthānīyasya nivartakasya abhāvāt acetana tvasya abhāva tvena aguṇa tvāt tasmāt pāka jānām apratidvandvi tvena eva śyāma ādeḥ ayāvat dravya bhāvi tve siddhe tad vidharmiṇi caitanye prasaktasya yāvat dravya bhāvi tvasya apratiṣedhaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.2.50–3.2.51	 itas api na śarīra guṇaḥ iti āha śarīra vyāpi tvāt aviśeṣāt śarīra avayavāḥ api cetanā iti caitanyasya śarīra vyāpi tvāt pratyavasthāna anumā na syāt aneka cetana saṃghāta tvāt śarīrasya iti sūtra arthaḥ codayati na keśa nakha ādiṣu anupalabdheḥ keśa nakha ādi śarīra avayaveṣu caitanya anupalabdheḥ tat dṛṣṭāntena avayava antareṣu api na caitanyam sambhavati iti pratyaya vyavasthāyāḥ na virodhaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.2.52	 pariharati tvac paryanta tvāt śarīrasya keśa nakha ādiṣu aprasaṅgaḥ indriya āśrayaḥ śarīram iti śarīra lakṣaṇena śarīrasya tvac paryanta tvāt keśa nakha ādīnām saṃyoga ādi dravya tvena śarīra avayava siddheḥ teṣu caitanyasya prasaṅgaḥ eva na asti tad dṛṣṭāntena avayava antarāṇām acaitanyasya sādhanam asaṅgatam iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.2.53–3.2.54	 itas ca na śarīra guṇaḥ iti āha śarīra guṇa vaidharmyāt ye hi śarīra guṇāḥ te bāhya karaṇa pratyakṣāḥ vā atīndriyāḥ vā vidha antaram tu cetanā tasyāḥ sva saṃvedya tvena antaḥkaraṇa pratyakṣa tvāt tasyāḥ śarīra guṇa tva vaidharmyāt na śarīra guṇaḥ cetanā iti sūtra arthaḥ codayati na rūpa ādīnām itaretara vaidharmyāt yathā rūpa ādīnām itaretara vaidharmye api cetanāyāḥ śarīra guṇa tva hāniḥ na iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.2.55	 pariharati aindriyaka tvāt rūpa ādīnām apratiṣedhaḥ rūpa rasa ādi bhedena itaretara vaidharmye api rūpa ādīnām aindriyaka tvāt bāhya indriya grāhya tvasya avyabhicāreṇa pratyakṣasya śarīra guṇa bāhya indriya grāhya tvasya avaśyaṃbhāvi tvāt cetanāyāḥ śarīra guṇa tva pratiṣedhakasya śarīra guṇa vaidharmyāt iti hetoḥ pratiṣedhaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.2.56–3.2.57	 idānīm avasara prāptam manaḥ parīkṣamāṇaḥ prathamam tāvat tasya prati śarīram eka tve hetum āha jñāna ayaugapadyāt ekam manaḥ yadi anekam ekasmin dehe manaḥ tadā manasaḥ tasya tena tena indriyeṇa saṃbandhāt indriya antara grāhyeṣu rūpa rasa ādiṣu pratyaya paryāyaḥ na syāt dṛśyate ca pratyaya paryāyaḥ tasmāt pratyaya paryāya lakṣaṇāt jñāna ayaugapadyāt pratiśarīram ekam manaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ codayati na yugapad aneka kriyā upalabdheḥ ekasya adhyetuḥ puruṣasya gamanam adhyayanam kamaṇḍalu dhāraṇam mārga nirīkṣaṇam vana gaja śabda grahaṇam ityādi aneka kriyāyāḥ yugapad upalabdheḥ pratyaya paryāyaḥ na iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.2.58–3.2.59	 pariharati alāta cakra darśana vat tad upalabdhiḥ āśu sañcārāt yathālātasya bhramataḥ vidyamānaḥ kramaḥ na upalabhyate iti aviccheda buddhyā ekatva darśanam tathā tasyāḥ kriyāyāḥ ayaugapadye api yugapad upalabdhiḥ bhrāntyā bhavati tasmāt āśu sañcārāt manasaḥ druta gati tvena krama grahaṇasya aśakya tvāt yugapad upalabdheḥ sarvatra vipratipanna tvena avivāda siddha dṛṣṭānta abhāvāt ayugapad upalahyedheḥ tu kvacid ubhaya va ādi siddha dṛṣṭānta tvena anyatra api śakya sādhana tvāt i ugat upalabdhiḥ asiddhā iti sūtra arthaḥ aṇu tvam ataā iva siddhi ati iti āha yathā ukta hetu tvāt ca aṇu yathā uktaḥ hetuḥ yasya tat yathā ukta hetuḥ tasya bhāvaḥ tattvam tasmāt yathā ukta hetu tvāt jñāna ayaugapadyāt aṇu ca manaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.2.60–3.2.61	 idānīm manaḥ saṃmbanadhi śarīra utpatti vicāra mukhena manaḥ vicārayaḥ tatra saṃśayam āha vipratipatteḥ saṃśayaḥ karma nirapekṣaiḥ bhūtaiḥ śarīram ārabhyate iti kecid tatas ca ācārya vipratipatteḥ samīpa sthasya karma sapekṣā vā akarma nimittā vā śarīra utpattiḥ iti saṃśayaḥ bhavati iti sūtra arthaḥ tatra karma sā apekṣā iti pakṣaḥ prekṣāvadbhiḥ pakṣīkartavyaḥ iti āha pūrva kṛta phala anubandhāt tad utpattiḥ pūrva śarīra upārjitā vāc buddhi śarīra ārambha lakṣaṇā pravṛttiḥ pūrva kṛtam tasya phalam dharma adharma lakṣaṇam karma tasya anubandhaḥ ātma samaveta tvena avasthānam tasmāt pūrva kṛta phala anubandhāt tad utpattiḥ tasya śarīrasya utpattiḥ puruṣa guṇa viśeṣa prerita bhūtaiḥ ārabdham puruṣa artha kriyā samartham ratha ādi dṛṣṭvā śarīram api puruṣa guṇa viśeṣa prerita bhūtaiḥ ārabdham puruṣa artha kriyā samartha tvāt ratha ādi vat iti pūrva kṛta phala anubandhāt prayojakāt tasya śarīra utpattiḥ iti anumātavyā iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.2.62–3.2.63	 codayati bhūtebhyaḥ mūrti upādāna vat tad upādānam mūrti śabdena mūrtam ucyate bhūtebhyaḥ pṛthivī ādibhyaḥ mūrtānām pāṣāṇa śarkarā prabhṛtīnām puruṣa artha kriyā samarthānām yathā upādānam tathā karma nirapekṣaiḥ bhūtaiḥ tasya śarīrasya upādānam bhaviṣyati iti pūrva sūtra ukta sādhanam anaikāntikam iti sūtra tātparya arthaḥ na anaikāntika tvam iti āha sādhya sama tvāt yatha aśarīra utpatteḥ karma sāpekṣa tvam sādhyam tathā pāṣāṇa ādīnām api karma nirapekṣa tvam sādhyam iti na taiḥ vyabhicāraḥ sambhavati teṣām api sādhya samāna dharma tvena sa pakṣa tvāt tad vipratipattau vā pakṣa tvāt iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.2.64	 karma nirapekṣa tve pāṣāṇa ādi sargasya na tat sādharmyam śarīra sargasya sambhavati iti āha na utpatti nimitta tvāt mātā pitroḥ mātā pitṛ śabdena śukra śoṇitayoḥ abhidhānam śukra śoṇitayoḥ bīja bhūtayoḥ śarīra utpatti nimitta tvāt karma sāpekṣā śarīra utpattiḥ śukra śoṇita kārya tvāt yat karma sāpekṣam na bhavati tad śukra śoṇita kāryam api na bhavati yathā pāṣāṇa ādi iti vaidharmyeṇa api karma sāpekṣa tvam siddhyati iti na atīva sādharmyam ārambhaṇīyam iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.2.65–3.2.66	 tathā āhārasya aśita pīta ādi āhārasya mātṛ śarīre niviśamānasya pranāḍyā garbha upacaya tvena śarīra utpatti nimitta tvāt pāṣāṇa ādiṣu tad abhāvāt karma sāpekṣa tvam vaidharmya anumānena pūrvavat siddhyati iti sūtra arthaḥ prāptau ca aniyamāt prāptiḥ dampatyoḥ saṃyogaḥ tasya aniyamaḥ prāpti mātrasya garbha śarīra anutpādaka tvam yadi karma nirapekṣā śarīra utpattiḥ tadā prāpti mātrasya tad utpādaka tvam syāt na tu etat asti tasmāt prāptau ca aniyam āda vinābhūta mātra kāryā śarīra utpattiḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.2.67	 yadi karma sāpekṣā śarīra utpattiḥ tasya karmaṇaḥ tasya ātmanaḥ saṃyoga ja tvāt sannikarṣasya sarva ātmanām sādhāraṇyāt tad utpādyasya karma sāpekṣasya śarīrasya api sādhāraṇyam prasajyate iti āśaṃkya āha śarīra utpatti nimitta vat saṃyoga utpatti nimittam karma śarīra utpattau yathā karma nimittam bhavati tathā saṃyoga utpattau= api nimittam na ca anayoḥ ita retara āśraya tvam pūrva pūrva karma apekṣāyām pūrva pūrva saṃyoga utpatteḥ anādi tvena tad abhāvāt na ca karmaṇaḥ api sādhāraṇa tvam tasya sukha duḥkha utpatti vyavasthayā vyavasthita puruṣa bhoga adhiṣṭhāna śarīra vyāpāra sāpekṣa kāraṇa janya tvena sādhāraṇa tvāt tasmāt na śarīra saṃyoga ādīnām sarva ātma sādha araṇyena atiprasaṅgaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.2.68–3.2.69	 etena aniyamaḥ pratyuktaḥ etena karmasā apekṣa utpatti pakṣa vyavasthā kathanena tad nirapekṣā utpatti pakṣe yaḥ a yama niyamaḥ prati puruṣam śarīra avyavasthā tayā pratyuktaḥ nirākṛtaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ na kevalam karma nimitte śarīra saṃsarge vyavasthāna abhāvaḥ eva doṣaḥ kim tarhi mokṣaḥ api tasmin pakṣe na syāt iti darśayitum sva pakṣe mokṣa upapattim āha upapannaḥ ca tad viyogaḥ karma kṣaya upapatteḥ tasya śarīrasya viyogaḥ ātyantikaḥ vināśaḥ upapannaḥ ca asmin pakṣe kasmāt karma kṣaya upapatteḥ karmaṇā ām āgatānām ca samādhi balāt ekīkṛtya upabhogena ca kṣayasya utpatti vināśa lakṣaṇasya yathāyogam upapatteḥ na ca īdṛśaḥ śarīra viyogaḥ karma nirapekṣa pakṣe sambhavati tad ārambhakasya pṛthivī ādeḥ bhūtamātrasya sārvaka ālīna tvāt iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.2.70	 idānīm sāṃkhya matam upanyasya nirasyati tat adṛṣṭa kāritam iti ced punar tad prasaṅgaḥ apavarge tat śarīram adṛṣṭa kāritam adṛṣṭam adarśanam prakṛti puruṣa vivekā darśana kāritam iti ced na etat yuktam punar tad prasaṅgaḥ apavarge yatas sarga ādau prakṛti puruṣa viveka prāgabhāvaḥ iva apavarga samaye api tad pradhvaṃsa abhāvaḥ asti na ca anayoḥ darśana tve kaścid viśeṣaḥ asti iti punar tasya śarīrasya prasaṅgaḥ apavarge syāt tatas ca saṃsāra anucchedaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.2.71	 ye tu jarantaḥ jaināḥ paramāṇu manaḥ guṇam adṛṣṭam varṇayitvā svakā deva adṛṣṭā atra paramāṇavaḥ parasparam saṃyujya śarīram ārabhante manaḥ ca svakā deva adṛṣṭāt tasya praviśya tasya jīva saṃyogam anubhavati iti menire teṣām api mokṣa avasthāyām śarīra manaḥ saṃyogasya api ucchedaḥ iti saṃsāra abhāvaḥ na iti āha manaḥ karma nimitta tvāt ca saṃyoga avyucchedaḥ manaḥ karma nimi tvāt manaḥ adṛṣṭa nimitta tvāt manasaḥ praveśasya cakārāt paramāṇu karma nimitta tvāt paramāṇūnām paraspara saṃyogasya śarīra ārambhakasya tasya ca paramāṇu gatasya tad gata rūpa ādi guṇa antara vat apavarga avasthāyām vyavasthānāt saṃyoga avyucchedaḥ ātmani śarīra saṃyogasya tad avacchinna jīva ākhya manaḥ saṃyogasya ca avyucchedaḥ viyoga abhāvaḥ tatas ca manaḥ saṃsāra anucchedaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.2.72–3.2.73	 nitya tva prasaṅgaḥ ca prāyaṇa anupapatteḥ api ca ātma gata adṛṣṭa nirapekṣa tve śarīra ārambhaka saṃyogasya tad avacchinna ātma manaḥ saṃyogasya ca tādavasthyena prāyaṇa abhāvāt nitya tva prasaṅgaḥ svabhāvataḥ tu prāyaṇe prāyaṇa bhedaḥ na syāt tasmāt prāyaṇa anupapatteḥ tad nitya tva prasaṅgaḥ śarīrasya anavasthāna prasaṅgaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ codayati aṇu śyāma tā anitya tva vat syāt yathā aṇau śyāma tā akāraṇikā api anityā dṛṣṭā tathā śarīra ārambhaka paramāṇu gatasya adṛṣṭasya akāraṇasya anitya tā syāt tatas ca śarīrasya api anitya tvam sva kāraṇa adṛṣṭa vaśāt siddhyati iti prāyaṇa upapattiḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_3.2.74	 pariharati na akṛta abhyāgama prasaṅgāt akṛtasya asamī cīna kṛtasya aprāmāṇikasya abhyupagamaḥ abhyāgamaḥ tasya prasaṅgaḥ tasmāt akṛta abhyāgama prasaṅgāt iti paramāṇu śyāma tāyāḥ pārthiva rūpa tvena lohita ādi rūpa vat pāka ja tvena sa kāraṇa tvāt akāraṇa vināśasya na asau dṛṣṭāntaḥ sādhya vikallapa tvāt iti paramāṇu gatasya adṛṣṭasya akāraṇa karasya vināśa abhyupagamaḥ prāmāṇika artha abhyupagamaḥ iti prasaktam athavā paramāṇu gata rūpa ādi vat tad gata adṛṣṭasya api nitya tvena kenacid akṛta tvāt akṛtasya karmaṇaḥ phalam puruṣeṇa upabhujyate iti akṛta abhyāgama prasaṅgaḥ tasmāt ubhayavidha akṛta abhyāgama prasaṅgāt pūrva sūtra arthaḥ na iti sūtra arthaḥ ātmā śarīram karaṇam tad arthaḥ buddhiḥ manaḥ ca iti padārtha ṣaṭkam prameya sūtrāt kramaśas amuṣya vicāritam sūtra kṛtā atra sūtraiḥ iti bhaṭṭa vāc īśvara viracitāyām nyāya sūtra tātparyadīpikāyām tṛtīya adhyāyaḥ samāptaḥ 
NTD_4.1.1–4.1.2	 atha manaḥ parīkṣā anantaram uddeśa krama anurodhena pravṛttiḥ parīkṣitum yuktāḥ sā kasmāt na parīkṣitā iti atas āha sūtrakāraḥ pravṛtiḥ yathā uktāḥ pravṛttiḥ yathālakṣitā tathā parīkṣitāḥ pravṛttiḥ dvividhā kāraṇa rūpā kārya rūpāḥ vā tatra kāraṇa rūpā vāc buddhi śarīra ārambha lakṣaṇā viṃśati prakāra bhinnā spaṣṭā eva kārya rūpā tu dharma adharma samākhyātā eva tasyāḥ punar saṃsāra hetu tvam pūrva kṛta ityādinā apavarga hetu tvam duḥkha ityādinā prāyaṇa ādi darśanāt anitya tvam kāryatve satya ātma samavāyāt tad guṇa tvam ityādi sarvam dharma dharma āśraya parīkṣayā eva amīṣām bahu parīkṣitam iti na pṛthak parīkṣati sūtra arthaḥ pravṛtti anantarāḥ tarhi doṣāḥ parīkṣyantām iti atas āha tathā doṣāḥ buddhi samāna āśraya tvena ātma guṇa tvāt vīta rāga janma adarśanena anādi tvāt mithyā jñāna nivṛttyā nivartanāt kārya pravṛtti tulya doṣāḥ atas tad parīkṣayā eva amīṣām bahu parīkṣitam iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_4.1.3	 nanu pravartanā lakṣaṇāḥ doṣāḥ iti doṣāṇām lakṣaṇam uktam tat ayuktam māna ādiṣu api sambhavena ati vyāpaka tvāt iti atas āha tat trairāśyam rāga dveṣa moha artha antara bhāvāt teṣām doṣāṇām trayaḥ rāśaya pakṣāḥ rāga pakṣaḥ dveṣapakṣaḥ moha pakṣaḥ iti tatra rāgapakṣaḥ kāmaḥ matsaraḥ spṛhā tṛṣṇā lobhaḥ iti dveṣapakṣaḥ krodhaḥ īrṣyā asūyā drohaḥ amarṣaḥ iti mohapakṣaḥ mithyājñānam vicikitsā mānam pramādaḥ iti kutas etat rāga dveṣa moha artha antara bhāvāt sakti lakṣaṇaḥ rāgaḥ jvalana ātmakaḥ dveṣaḥ mithyā pravṛtti lakṣaṇaḥ mohaḥ iti āntar gaṇika lakṣaṇa apekṣayā bheda upapatteḥ iti evañca māna ādīnām api lakṣya tvena saṃgrahāt na doṣa lakṣaṇasya ati vyāpaka tvena api tritva virodhaḥ na ca sāmānyam eka tve kāraṇam tathā ca sāmānyasya eva abhāvaḥ syāt tasmāt sāmānya lakṣaṇayā eka tve api avāntara bheda vivakṣayā tritvā upapatteḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_4.1.4–4.1.5	 ekena eka pratyanīka bhāvāt na artha antaram rāga ādayaḥ kasmāt eka pratyanīka bhāvāt ekena tattva jñānena viruddhi amāna tvāt eka saṃyogena viruddhi amāna vibhāga vat na aneka tvam iti sūtra arthaḥ pariharati vyabhicārāt ahetuḥ eka pratyanīkāḥ ca rūpa ādayaḥ eka agni saṃyoga virodhi tvāt na ca amīṣām eka tvam iti anaikāntika tvena vyabhicārāt ekam yat pratyanīkam tat rāga ādīnām ekatve na hetuḥ iti sūtra artham 
NTD_4.1.6	 eka pratyanīka bhāvaḥ anyathā asiddhaḥ iti āha teṣām mohaḥ pāpīya an na amūḍhasya itara utpatteḥ teṣām doṣāṇām madhye rāga mohayoḥ moha pāpīyān kutas na amūḍhasya itara utpatteḥ amūḍhasya itara utpattiḥ na bhavati iti yatas tatas ca moha nidāna tvāt rāga dveṣayoḥ tattva jñānāt tad nivṛttau tayoḥ api nivṛttiḥ iti ekā pratyanīka bhāva upapattiḥ na punar ekaṃtvāt iti eka pratyanīka tvam anyathā siddham iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_4.1.7	 mohasya doṣa antarbhovam asahamānaḥ pratyavatiṣṭhate nimitta naimittika nirdeśāt moha artha antara bhāvaḥ doṣebhyaḥ na amūḍhasya itara utpattiḥ iti atra mohasya nimitta tvam rāga dveṣayoḥ ca tad janya tvena naimittika tvam iti nimitta naimittika nirdeśāt mohasya doṣebhyaḥ artha antara bhāvaḥ pṛthaktvena adoṣa tvam tad nimitta tvāt rūpa ādi vat iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_4.1.8–4.1.9	 pariharati na doṣa lakṣaṇa avarodhāt mohasya na atra nimitta naimittika bhāvena padārthānām tad jātīya tvam atad jātīya tvam vā siddhyati kintu lakṣaṇasya abhedāt doṣa lakṣaṇam ca mohe asti iti mohasya doṣa tvena doṣa nimitta tvam sādhayati iti sūtra arthaḥ hetoḥ anaikantika tvam api āha nimitta naimittika upapatteḥ ca tulya jātīyānām apratiṣedhaḥ tulya jātīyānām api buddhi ādīnām nimitta naimittika bhāva upapatteḥ hetoḥ anaikāntika tvena mohāt artha antarasya apratiṣedhaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_4.1.10	 ātma nitya tve pretyabhāva siddhiḥ utpāda ucchedau pretyabhāvau na ca ātmanaḥ nityasya tau na staḥ tasmāt aspandanena yuktaḥ pretyabhāvaḥ vaināśikānāntu darśana sattva utpattiḥ pūrva abhyasta sūtreṇa ātma nitya tvasya vyavasthāpanāt sattva utpāda uccheda pakṣe ca kṛta nāśa akṛta abhyāgama doṣa prasaṅgāt deha indriya buddhi vedanā sambandha utpāda vināśau nityasya api ātmanaḥ janma prāyaṇe tathā ca tādṛśa pretya bhāvaḥ asmad darśanaḥ eva upapadyate na bhavat darśanaḥ iti siddhāntaḥ 
NTD_4.1.11	 pretyabhāvaḥ iti atra bhāvana prāyaṇayoḥ samāna kartṛ tva abhidhānena spaṣṭa eva iti manvānaḥ sūtrakāraḥ śarīra ādīnām utpatti prakāram vicārayati vyaktāt vyaktānām utpattiḥ pratyakṣa prāmāṇyāt kim dharmakāt kāraṇāt idam śarīra indriya mahābhūta ādi vyaktam utpadyate iti ced vyaktāt iti kim punar vyaktam upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptam rūpa ādi vat dravyam tad sāmānyā drūpa ādi guṇa yogāt paramāṇu lakṣaṇam pṛthivī ādi kāraṇam api vyaktam ucyate tasmāt paramāṇu lakṣaṇāt kāraṇāt idam śarīra indriya mahābhūta ādi vyaktam utpadyate kasmāt pratyakṣa prāmāṇyāt dṛṣṭāḥ hi rūpa ādi guṇa prayuktebhyaḥ mṛd prabhṛtibhyaḥ kāraṇebhyaḥ tathābhūtasya dravyasya utpattiḥ dṛṣṭena ca adṛṣṭasya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ anumīyate iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_4.1.12–4.1.13	 codayati na ghaṭāt ghaṭa aniṣpatteḥ ghaṭāt vyaktāt ghaṭasya vyaktasya aniṣpatteḥ niṣpatti abhāvāt vyaktāt vyaktasya utāttiḥ iti etat na iti sūtra arthaḥ vyaktāt ghaṭa niṣpatteḥ apratiṣedhaḥ yadi api sarvam vyaktam sarvasya vyaktasya na kāraṇam tathā api yat utpadyate vyaktam tat vyaktāt eva tatas ca vyaktasya vyakta hetu tva pratiṣedhaḥ na iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_4.1.14	 tat evam sva abhimatam tattvam nirūpya para abhimata darśanāni upanyasyati abhāvāt bhāva utpattiḥ na anupamṛdya prādurbhāvāt viśvam hi śūnyatāyāḥ eva jāyate kasmāt na anupamṛdya prādurbhāvāt kāraṇam anupamṛdya kāryam na bhavati yathā dṛṣṭā hi kāraṇa upamardena kāryasya utpattiḥ bīja aṅkura ādau tathā anyatra api iti asat upādānam api viśvam iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_4.1.15	 dūṣayati na vinaṣṭebhyaḥ aniṣpatteḥ bīja ādi kāraṇa vināśaḥ cat aṅkura ādi kārya utpatti hetuḥ tarhi vinaṣṭe bīja ādau kāraṇe tad avayaveṣu paraspara vicchinneṣu asati teṣām vyūha antare kasmāt aṅkura ādi kāryam na bhavati tasmāt vinaṣṭemyaḥ aṅkura ādi anutpatteḥ asati vyūha antare na bīja ādi vināśaḥ kāraṇam aṅkura ādi kāryasya na api upamardya upamardaka bhāvaḥ sambhavati vyāghātāt tasmāt dṛṣṭānta tvena asat upādānam viśvam iti uktam iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_4.1.16	 kāraṇa vināśasya kāryāt prāk kāla varti tvam ca anyathā siddham iti āha krama nirdeśāt na pratiṣedhaḥ pūrvam vināśaḥ paścāt aṅkura utpattiḥ iti kramasya vināśa utpattyoḥ paurvāparya niyamasya vidyamāna tva abhāvaḥ kāraṇam iṣyate tarhi tasmāt eva krama nirdeśāt asmad matasya apratiṣedhaḥ pūrvam vyūha antaram paścāt kārya antara utpattiḥ iti na ca āvṛtte pūrva vyūhe avayavānām śakyam vyūha antareṇa bhavitum iti vināśasya prāk kāla varti tvam tasmāt anyathā siddha paurvāparya niyamāt vyūha anterasya kārya janaka tvam na vināśasya tasya anyathā siddha tvāt tathā ca sat upādānam eva idam viśvam iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_4.1.17	 atha aparaḥ idānīm āha īśvaraḥ kāraṇam puruṣa karma aphalya darśanāt īśvaraḥ brahma īśanā śakti yogāt jñāna śakti kriyā śaktiḥ ca īśanā sā ca asti brahmaṇi iti brahyeśvaraḥ kāraṇam jagataḥ pariṇāmaḥ vā tad vivartaḥ vā prapañcaḥ iti nanu cetanā śakti yogāt tad karma nibandhanaḥ ayam prapañcaḥ bhaviṣyati iti kṛtam atra īśvareṇa iti atas uktam puruṣa karma aphalya darśanāt puruṣaḥ ced cetayate na eṣa cetayet na evam niṣphalam karma ārabheta niṣphalam tu vidvān pravartamānaḥ katham cetanaḥ nāma tasmāt puruṣa karma aphalya darśanena cetanā śakti abhāvāt na jīva karma nibandhanam jagat api tu brahmeśvara kāraṇam jagat iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_4.1.18	 dūṣayati na puruṣa karma abhāve phalāniṣpate yadi api brahmeśvarasya īśana ayogaḥ tathā api na tat pariṇāmaḥ ayam nāma rūpa prapañcaḥ sarva ātmanā pariṇāma pakṣe tattva vighātāt anitya tvam eka deśena pāraṇāme sa aṃśa tve anitya tva prasaṅgāt na api tad vivartaḥ vibhāgasya ekasya sva saṃvedana pratyakṣasya brahmaṇaḥ sattva rūpa agrahaṇa āsāmānyān nibandhana viparīta jñāna gocara tva asambhavena avidyā upadhāna bheda abhāvāt tasmāt na brahmeśvara upādānam jagat kim tarhi tad nimittam saṃvedana apekṣam kāraṇam iti ucyate na ca etat yuktam kasmāt puruṣa karma abhāve phala aniṣpatteḥ nirapekṣa īśvara adhīnā ced phala niṣpattiḥ puruṣasya samīhām antareṇa api phalam niṣpadyeta na ca etat dṛṣṭam iṣṭam vā tasmāt na nirasyate 
NTD_4.1.19	 sva abhimata īśvara nirākaraṇe ca na ayam hetuḥ iti āha tad kārita tvāt ahetuḥ paramāṇu upādānasya hi jagataḥ puruṣa karma tat api īśvara nimittam eva na ca yat apekṣate tasya animittattvam paryāya kartṛ tva abhyupagamāt na api paryāya kartṛ tve satya kartṛ tvam adarśanāt na ca anya kārya akartṛ tvam anādi tvāt nanu tathābhūta īśvara nimitta tve kim pramāṇam iti ced anumānam tathā hi vivāda avyāsitāḥ taru giri sāgara ādayaḥ sva upādāna ādi abhijña kartṛkā utpattimat tvāt yat utpattimat tat sarvam sva upādāna ādi abhijña kartṛkam yathā prāsāda ādi tathā ca vivāda adhyāsitāḥ taru giri sāgara ādayaḥ tasmāt tathā iti tat evam īśvarāt eva kārita tvāt puruṣakārasya tad sahāyaḥ īśvaraḥ nimitta kāraṇam paramāṇu upādānasya jagataḥ iti asya pakṣasya nirākaraṇe puruṣa karma abhāve phala aniṣpatteḥ iti ahetuḥ nirapekṣa īśvara nimitta tva nirākaraṇe hetuḥ eva iti sūtra arthaḥ paraḥ idānīm āha 
NTD_4.1.20–4.1.21	 animittataḥ bhāva utpattiḥ kaṇṭaka taikṣṇya ādi darśanāt yathā kaṇṭakasya taikṣṇyam parvata dhātūnām citra tā ityādi nirnimittam saṃsthāna bheda vat ca dṛṣṭam tathā śarīra ādeḥ bhāvasya utpattiḥ animittāḥ tasmāt saṃsthāna bhedasya tatra api vidyamāna tvāt iti sūtra arthaḥ atra adṛśyamāna nimittānām śarīra ādi kaṇṭaka ādīnām pakṣa nikṣepāt pakṣeṇa vyabhicāra anudbhāvane vā sarva anumāna uccheda prasaṅgāt sarvatra tasya sulabha tvāt ghaṭa ādi dṛṣṭāntena saṃsthānavat tvāt śarīra ādīnām nirnimitta anumānam iti rāddha antaḥ karma nimittaḥ śarīra sargaḥ iti asya pratiṣedhāt sūcitaḥ iti manvānaḥ sūtra kāraḥ mata antareṇa parihāram āha animitta nimitta tva at na animittataḥ animittataḥ bhāva utpattiḥ iti ucyate yatas ca utpattiḥ tad nimittam animittasya nimitta tva at na animittāḥ bhāva utpattiḥ kintu sa nimittā iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_4.1.22	 tat etat dūṣayati nimitta animittayoḥ artha antara bhāvāt apratiṣedhaḥ anyat nimittam anyat ca pratyākhyātam tathā hi nimittam iti artha antara abhyanujñā animittam iti tasya pratiṣedhaḥ na ca anujñā pratiṣedhayoḥ ekatvam yuktam yathā anudakaḥ kamaṇḍaluḥ iti na udaka pratiṣedhayoḥ ekatvam bhavati tasmāt nimitta animittayoḥ artha antara bhāvāt pūrva ukta pratiṣedhaḥ na iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_4.1.23–4.1.24	 anye tu manyante sarvam anityam utpatti vināśa dharmaka tvāt bhautikam abhautikam śarīra ādi buddhi ādi sakalam anityam tasmāt utpatti vināśa dharmaka tvāt pūrva apara kālayoḥ abhāvāt madhye ca bhāvāt iti sūtra arthaḥ tatra utpatti vināśa dharmaka tvasya hetoḥ anupasaṃhārya tvāt vyāpaka tve ati sphuṭa iti manvānaḥ sūtrakāraḥ prathamam tāvat parokta dūṣaṇam āha na anitya tā nitya tvāt sarvam anityam iti bruvāṇaḥ praṣṭavyaḥ kim sarvasya anitya tā nityāḥ āhosvit anityāḥ yadi tāvat nityāḥ na tarhi sarvam anityam atha anityāḥ anitya tāyāḥ abhāvāt sarvam anityam iti vyāhataḥ hetuḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_4.1.25–4.1.26	 tat etat dūṣayati tat anitya tvam agneḥ dāhyam vināśya anuvināśa vat yathā agniḥ dāhyam vināśya anuvinaśyati evam sarvasya anitya tā sarvam vināśya anuvinaśyati iti sūtra arthaḥ idānīm parama siddhāntam āha nityasya apratyākhyānam yathā upalabdhi vyavasthānāt ayam khalu vādaḥ nityam pratyācaṣṭe nityasya pratyākhyānam anupapannam kasmāt yathā upalabdhi vyavasthānāt yasya utpatti vināśa dharmaka tvam upapadyate pramāṇataḥ tat anityam yathā ghaṭa ādi yasya na upapadyate tat nityam yathā ākāśa paramāṇu ādi nahi utpatti vināśa dharmaka tvam ākāśa ādeḥ upalabhyate pramāṇataḥ tasmāt yathā upalabdhi vyavasthānāt kiñcid nityam kiñcid anityam iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_4.1.27–4.1.28	 ayam anyaḥ ekāntaḥ sarvam nityam pañcabhūta nitya tvāt pañca bhūtātmakam go ghaṭa ādi kārya jātam akhilam upalabhyate vyapadiśanti mṛd ghaṭaḥ mṛd śarīram iti laukikāḥ bhūtāni ca nityāni teṣām ucchedasya naiyāyikaiḥ anabhyupagamāt tena tad ātmakānām go ghaṭa ādīnām api nityatā iti sūtra arthaḥ pariharati na utpatti vinā kāraṇa upalabdheḥ bhūtebhyaḥ bhautikāni na hi parama sūkṣmāḥ paramāṇavaḥ eva go ghaṭa ādayaḥ paramāṇu vat teṣām api atīndriya tvena sarva agrahaṇa prasaṅgāt tasmāt grahaṇa agrahaṇa lakṣaṇa viruddha dharma yogāt anye bhautikāḥ bhūtebhyaḥ tathā ca teṣām utpatti vināśa kāraṇa upalabdheḥ nitya tvam bhūta nitya tvam iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_4.1.29–4.1.30	 punar api nitya tvam āśaṅkate tad lakṣaṇa avarodhāt apratiṣedhaḥ teṣām utpatti vināśa kāraṇam upalabhyate iti manyase na te api bhūta lakṣaṇa vilakṣaṇāḥ gṛhyante bhūta lakṣaṇa avarodhāt bhūtātmakāḥ iti amīṣām nitya tvasya apratiṣedhaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ pariharati na utpatti kāraṇa upalabdheḥ kāraṇa samāna guṇasya kāryasya upalabdhiḥ utpattiḥ utpattiḥ ca tad kāraṇaḥ ca utpatti kāraṇe tayoḥ upalabdheḥ utpatti kāraṇa upalabdheḥ yasmāt kāraṇena samāna guṇasya kāryasya utpadyamānasya tad kāraṇasya ca upalabdhiḥ asti prāmāṇikī kim tasmāt tayoḥ upalabdhyoḥ bhūtāt anyasya bhautikasya bhūta anumāpakasya vidyamāna tvena tad lakṣaṇa avarodhasya anyathā api upapattyā bhūta ātmaka tvasya asiddheḥ karma ādiṣu avyāpanāt ca hetoḥ na sarva nitya tvam siddhyati iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_4.1.31–4.1.33	 ayam api aparaḥ ekāntaḥ sarvam pṛthak bhāva lakṣaṇa pṛthaktvāt sarvam nānā na kaścid ekaḥ asti bhāvaḥ kasmāt bhāva lakṣaṇa pṛthaktvāt bhāvaḥ lakṣyate anena iti bhāva lakṣaṇasya samākhyā śabdasya pṛthaktvāt aneka artha abhidhāyi tvāt sarvam nānā artha abhidhāyaka śabda vācya tvāt senā vat iti sūtra arthaḥ dūṣayati na aneka lakṣaṇaiḥ eka bhāva niṣpatteḥ anekavidhaiḥ lakṣaṇaiḥ guṇa avayava ādibhiḥ sambandhasya ekasya ghaṭa ādeḥ bhāvasya utpatteḥ hetoḥ tat vācakasya ghaṭa ādi śabdasya tad artha abhidhāna mukhena tad anuṣaṅgī aneka artha abhidhāyaka tvam lakṣaṇayā na sākṣāt iti aneka artha abhidhāyaka śabda vācya tvam anyathā siddham iti sūtra arthaḥ asiddhaḥ ca ayam hetuḥ iti āha tad lakṣaṇa vyavasthānāt eva apratiṣedhaḥ tad lakṣaṇasya tad vācaka śabdasya vyavasthānāt yam kumbham adrākṣam tam spṛśāmi iti pratyabhijñā balena eka viṣaya tvasya vā aneka viṣaya tvasya asiddha tvāt ekasya apratiṣedhaḥ sādhya sādhana vikalaḥ ca senā ādi dṛṣṭāntaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_4.1.34	 ayam aparaḥ ekāntaḥ sarvam abhāvaḥ bhāveṣu itaretarābhāva siddheḥ yāvat bhāva jātam tat sarvam abhāvaḥ kasmāt bhāveṣu itaretarābhāva siddheḥ asan gauḥ aśva ātmanā iti anaśvaḥ gauḥ evam asannaśvaḥ gavā ātmanā iti āha gauḥ aśvaḥ iti itaretarābhāva siddheḥ asat pratyaya pratiṣedhābhyām bhāva śabdasya sāmānādhikaraṇyāt prayogaḥ ca bhāva śabdāḥ asat viṣayāḥ asat pratyaya bhāva pratiṣedha śabdābhyām sāmāna adhikaraṇyāt anutpanna pradhvasta ghaṭa vāca śabda vat iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_4.1.35	 dūṣayati na svabhāva siddheḥ bhāvānām sarvam abhāvaḥ iti etat na asti kasmāt svabhāva siddheḥ bhāvānām svabhāvaḥ svarūpam bhāvānām yena amī bhāvāḥ svabhāvāt vyāvartante tasya siddheḥ katham bhāveṣu itaretarābhāva siddheḥ iti abhāvaḥ bhavatā abhidhīyate na ca itaretarābhāva anabhyupagame itarasya itarasmin= abhāvaḥ śakyate pratipādayitum pratipādayati ca bhavān atas manyāmahe svabhāva siddhiḥ abhyupagatā bhavatā iti tatas ca viruddhaḥ hetuḥ asat pratyaya pratiṣedha śabdābhyām sāmānādhikaraṇyañca bhāva śabdānām asat viśeṣaṇam sat abhidhāyaka tve api upapattiḥ iti anyathā siddhiḥ ca iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_4.1.36	 codayati na svabhāva siddheḥ āpekṣika tvāt sarve eva hi bhāvāḥ bhinna svabhāvāḥ bhinna tvañca eṣām anya apekṣam tathā hi nīlam bhinnam pīta ādi apekṣayā na tu svabhāvāt evam hrasva tva dīrgha tva paratvāt ayopi paraspara apekṣāḥ draṣṭavyāḥ yat ca para apekṣam na tad svābhāvikam yathā japā kusuma apekṣa sphaṭikasya aruṇimā para apekṣāḥ ca bhinna svabhāvāḥ bhāvāḥ tasmāt na svābhāvikāḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_4.1.37	 pariharati vyāhata tvāt ahetuḥ atra bhinna tva ādayaḥ dharmāḥ na vastu svabhāvāḥ kiṃtu tad dharmāḥ teṣāñca na sva utpattau para apekṣa tvam api tu svarūpa nirūpaṇe yadi api apekṣā buddhi janyānām utpattau= api para apekṣa tvam api tu svar na syāt tadā apekṣāyāḥ api bheda abhāva adīrgha ādi pratyayānām avyavasthā syāt asti ca vyavasthā dīrghāt dīrghataram iti ādikāḥ tasmāt svabhāva siddhiḥ siddhāḥ bhāvānām iti para apekṣa tvam vyāhata tvena siddha tvāt ahetuḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_4.1.38–4.1.39	 atha ime saṃkhyā ekānta vādāḥ sarvam ekam sat aviśeṣāt sarvañca etat nityā aniti abhedāt ityādi tad pratiṣedha dvāraka sūtram saṃkhyā ekānta asiddhiḥ kāraṇa upapatti anupapattibhyām sarvam ekam sat aviśeṣāt ityādau yadi sādhya sādhanayoḥ nānātvam ekāntaḥ na siddhyati vyatirekāt atha sādhya sādhanayoḥ abhedaḥ evam api ekāntaḥ bhāvaḥ na siddhyati sādhana abhāvāt na hi sādhanam antareṇa sādhyam asti tasmāt kāraṇa upapatti anupapattibhyām sarvam ekam sat iti ekānta vādānām asiddhiḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ codayati na kāraṇa avayava bhāvāt na saṃkhyā ekāntānām asiddhiḥ kasmāt kāraṇasya sādhanasya sādhya avayava bhāvāt evañca na sādhya vyatiriktam sādhanam na ca asādhanā sādhya siddhiḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_4.1.40^1	 pariharati niravayava tvāt ahetuḥ sādhya avayavaḥ eva sādhanam iti ahetuḥ kasmāt niravayava tvāt pratijñāta arthasya sarvam ekam ityādi pratijñāta arthe na kaścid avaśiṣyate yaḥ hetuḥ syāt na ca sādhyam eva hetuḥ bhavati sva ātmani kriyāyāḥ virodhāt tasmāt tad avayavat tvena api saṃkhyā ekāntaḥ na yuktaḥ nanu mā bhūt saṃkhyā ekānta vādaḥ tu kutas ucyate atra tāvat ghaṭa paṭa ādi padārtha bheda pratibhāsaḥ na ca asati bādhake tasya apāramārthika tvam na ca advaita pratipādikā śrutiḥ bodhikā tasyāḥ parameśvara viṣaya tāyāḥ guṇavāda tvena ca upapatteḥ na api pratyakṣasya vidhātṛ tvena bheda pratipādaka tva ābhāsaḥ tad bhāsaka tvam antareṇa tasya avasthita ghaṭa ādi viṣaya vidhātṛ tvasya eva anupapatteḥ na ca vidhātṛ tve api pratyakṣasya padārtha abheda grāhi tvam svarūpa gra viṣaya tva abhyupagamāt bhedaḥ api na gṛhyate iti ced mā bhūt sau= adhikam bheda grahaṇa mayam asmāt bhinnaḥ iti tathā api svarūpa grahaṇe sati tad aparyavasānāt bhedaḥ api parisphurati eva nirvikalpaka jñāne pramāṇa antareṣu tathā adarśanāt 
NTD_4.1.40^2	 na api sā= adhika sa vikalpaka pratyaya antareṇa bheda grahaṇe anyonya āśraya tvam anavasthā vā bhaviṣyati iti vyāpyam apūrvam eva svetara vyāvṛtta tayā gṛhītasya arthasya avadhi tvena tasmāt asya bheda grahaṇe anyonya āśraya tā bhāvāt tat tat pūrva avadhi grahaṇam api saṃsārasya anādi tvena tad tad pūrva kāla bhāvaḥ siddhyati iti na anavasthā bhaya āvahā sarveṣām eka kāla grāhaka tva abhāvāt na ca māna antareṇa bādhaḥ tasya eva asambhavāt pratyuta ātma bheda grāhakam pramāṇam asti eka kāla varti asmad ādi aneka śarīrāṇi pratiniyata bhoktṛ bhoga adhiṣṭhitāni ayoni saṃbadhi eka kāla vividha viruddha bhoga adhiṣṭhāna tvāt 
NTD_4.1.40^3	 yat ukta sādhyam na bhavati tad ukta sādhanam api na bhavati yathā śarīram na ca tathā etāni tasmāt pratiniyata bhoktṛ bhoga adhiṣṭhānāni iti śrutiḥ api asti bheda grāhikā dve brahmaṇī veditavye iti paraḥ ca aparaḥ ca iti ādikā tasmāt pratyakṣa ādibhiḥ avadhāryamāṇasya bhedasya bādhakaḥ pramāṇam sūtritam yena dūṣayatā sūtrakāreṇa arthāt sva pakṣa sādhanam api uktam iti sūtra tātparya arthaḥ te khalu ete saṃkhyā ekānta vādāḥ pratyaya ābhāsa nirāsakāḥ iti tad siddhi artham tad parīkṣā= chalena nirākṛtāḥ 
NTD_4.1.41	 sadyas kāla antare ca phala niṣpatteḥ saṃśayaḥ laukikī pravṛttiḥ tātkālika phalā karṣati ādikāḥ iyañca pravṛttiḥ agnihotra ādikā vaidikī tatra sandehaḥ kim iyam tātkālika loka pakṣa pāta ādi phalā uta kāla antara upabhogya svarga ādi phalā iti evañca phala padātha lakṣaṇam tad svarūpa niścaya abhāvena saṃdigdha viṣaya tvāt asambaddham iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_4.1.42	 pariharati na sadyas kāla antara upabhogya tvāt na tāvat agnihotra ādi pravṛttīnām sadyas san jāyamānam laukika pakṣa pāta ādi phalam kasmāt śrūyamāṇasya svarga śabdasya artha vāda gata sukha atireka vācaka tve sambhavati upacarita loka pakṣa pāta ādi artha tva ayogāt na ca loka pakṣa pāta ādeḥ anuṣṭhāna phalam sambhavati pracchannam anutiṣṭhatām tad abhāvena tasya tad upalambha tvena niścayena aphala tvāt na ca kalpanā gauravam pramāṇa siddhasya anivārya tvāt na ca aphalam tat kriyā anuṣṭhāna vaidhuryāt tasmāt kāla antara upabhogya svarga ādeḥ phala niścayāt na saṃdigdha āśraya tvam phala lakṣaṇasya iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_4.1.43–4.1.44	 codayati kāla antareṇa aniṣpattiḥ hetu vināśāt kāla antareṇa agnihotra ādi kriyā phalasya svarga ādeḥ aniṣpattiḥ kasmāt hetoḥ agnihotra ādi karmaṇaḥ kṣaṇika tvena vinaṣṭasya kāla antare phala udaya samaye asattvena akāraṇa tvāt iti sūtra arthaḥ pariharati prāk niṣpatteḥ vṛkṣa phala vat tu tasya yathā vṛkṣa mūle kṛtam seka ādi parikarma pākaja utpatti nyāyena avāntara vyāpāra jananāt vinaṣṭam api kāla antare pallava kusuma ādikam phalam janayati evam agnihotra ādi karma phala niṣpatteḥ prāk svayam vinaṣṭam api puruṣa āśraya apūrva lakṣaṇa avāntara vyāpārā vaiyarthyāt phalam janayati eva iti na sat asat tasmāt sat asatoḥ jana nardvāreṇa kāla antara upabhogya svarga ādi phala hetuḥ bhavati iti yat uktam hetu vināśāt iti tad asaṃbaddham iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_4.1.45	 codayati na asat na sat na sat asat sat asatoḥ vaidharmyāt kim etat phalam utpatteḥ prāk sat vā asat vā sat asat vā anubhayam vā tatra na tāvat asat upādāna niyama darśanāt khura viṣāṇa ādi utpatti darśanāt ca na api sat kāraka vyāpāra vaiyarthyāt na sat asat kasmāt sat asatoḥ vaidharmyāt dharma svabhāva viruddhaḥ dharmaḥ api vidharmā tasya bhāvaḥ vaidharmyam tasmāt vaidharmyāt paraspara viruddha svabhāvayoḥ ekatra samāveśa abhāvāt iti na api anubhayam tad svarūpa anirdeśāt na prakāra antaram asti tasmāt phala abhāvaḥ iti
