NTD_4.1.46	 pariharati buddhi siddhantu tat asat tat kāryam utpatteḥ prāc asadbhāvi kasmāt kāraka vyāpāra darśanāt nanu asat kārya pakṣaḥ upādāna niyamaḥ na syāt iti uktam iti atas āha buddhi siddham tu iti yasmāt idam anena śakyam nirvartayitum idam anena iti anumāna buddhyā siddham kṛtavān kāryam tasmāt tad utpatteḥ yayā samartham tat upādatte na sarvam na hi sarvasmāt sarvam utpadyamānam anena dṛṣṭam iti yat ca khura viṣāṇa ādi utpatti sthānaḥ iti tat asat sa hi khura viṣāṇam asatvāt na utpadyate api tu kāraṇa abhāvāt na ca sattvam anutpattau hetuḥ kintu sataḥ anutpatteḥ asat utpadyate iti satkārya pakṣe ca sarvathā kāraka vyāpāra vaiyarthyam upādāna niyama abhāvaḥ ca eka tvāt sarva arthānām iti eka pakṣa svīkaraṇam itareṣām asādhu tvam sūcayati iti mantavyam tatas ca na asat na sat na sat asat na ubhayam na anubhayam utpadyamānam kāryam iti pakṣa trayam abhyupagamena eva parihṛtam iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_4.1.47	 punar codayati āśraya vyatirekāt vṛkṣa phala utpatti vat iti ahetuḥ vinaṣṭam api karma saṃskāra ādhāna dvāreṇa mūla seka ādi parikarma vat phalam janayiṣyati iti yat uktam nidarśanam tat na hetuḥ kasmāt āśraya vyatirekāt seka ādi parikarma parṇa ādi phalañca ubhayam eka vṛkṣa āśrayam dṛṣṭam na ca evam karma phalayoḥ āśraya aikyam atra sambhavati kṛta karmaṇaḥ dehasya vināśe deha antare phala niṣpatti darśanāt tasmāt āśraya vyatirekāt vṛkṣa phala utpatti vat iti ayuktam uktam iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_4.1.48	 pariharati prīteḥ ātma āśraya tvāt apratiṣedhaḥ yadi api kṛta karmaṇaḥ dehasya vināśaḥ tathā api tad adhiṣṭhātuḥ ātmanaḥ tādavasthyāt karma phalayoḥ eka āśraya tvam sambhavati deha vyatirikta ātmanaḥ satva nitya tvayoḥ sādhita tvāt tasmāt prīteḥ sukha atirekasya tad kāraṇa vyāpārasya ca ātmā āśraya tvena eka āśraya tvāt vṛkṣa phala utpatti vat iti asya apratiṣedhaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_4.1.49–4.1.50	 punar codayati na putra paśu strī pariccheda hiraṇya anna ādi phala nirdeśāt na prīti mātram eva karma phalam putra kāmaḥ yajeta paśu kāmaḥ yajeta iti evamādibhiḥ vākyaiḥ putra paśu strī pariccheda hiraṇya ādeḥ phala tvena nirdeśāt tasya ca ātmā āśraya tva asambhavena eka aśraya tva anupapatteḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ pariharati tad sambandhāt phala niṣpatteḥ teṣu phalavat upacāraḥ na putra ādeḥ svarūpeṇa karma phala tvam sambhavati apuruṣa artha tvāt tathā api sambandhāt phalasya prīti lakṣaṇasya ātmani utpatteḥ teṣu putra ādiṣu phalavat upacāraḥ na svarūpataḥ phala tvam teṣām tatas ca karma phalayoḥ eka āśraya tvam atra api sambhavati iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_4.1.51^1	 bādhanā lakṣaṇam duḥkham iti sūtreṇa bādhanayā duḥkhena lakṣyamāṇam anuṣajyamānam śarīra ādi sukha sahitam duḥkham iti uktam tat ayuktam anukūla vedanīyasya duḥkha tva anupapatteḥ yadi duḥkha anuṣaṅgāt sukham tad hetu tvāt śarīra ādi api duḥkham syāta tarhi sukha anuṣaṅgāt duḥkham sukha hetu tvāt śarīra ādi api sukham syāt tasmāt lokayātrā anurodhena sukham asti duḥkham api asti iti vaktavyam tatas ca sarvam śarīra ādi bādhanā lakṣaṇam duḥkham iti duḥkha lakṣaṇam anupapannam iti āśaṅkya āha vividha bādhana ayogāt duḥkham eva janma utpattiḥ 
NTD_4.1.51^2	 jāyate iti janma śarīra ādityasya svarga naraka ādi sthāneṣu āvirbhāvam utpattiḥ duḥkham eva iti duḥkha saṃjñā bhāvayitavyā asmāt vividha bādhana ayogāt anekavidha duḥkha yogena heya pakṣa nikṣepāt punar sukham eva na asti iti vaktavyam yat ca sukha anuṣaṅgāt duḥkham tad hetu tvāt śarīra ādi api sukham syāt iti uktam tat ayuktam upādeya anuṣaṅgāt heyasya upādeya tva adarśanāt yathā viṣa saṃpṛkta annasya na hi tasya viṣa anuṣaṅgāt heya tvam madhu anuṣaṅgāt upādeya tvam dṛṣṭam tasmāt sukhasya tad hetoḥ śarīra ādeḥ sadbhāve api duḥkha anuṣaṅgāt teṣu duḥkha saṃjñā bhāvayitavyā na sukha duḥkha saṃjñā mumukṣuṇā iti duḥkha lakṣaṇam upapannam syāt iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_4.1.52	 nanu kasmāt sukham svarūpataḥ duḥkham eva iti naiyāyikāḥ iti atas āha na sukhasya api antarāla niṣpatteḥ na sukhasya duḥkha abhāva ātmaka tvena svarūpataḥ nāstitvam vaktavyam kim tarhi duḥkha abhāvena eva upadeṣṭavyam kasmāt sukhasya api antarāla niṣpatteḥ duḥkha antarāleṣu pratyātmam anukūla vedanīyasya sukhasya api niṣpatteḥ tatas ca anubhava siddhasya sukhasya apahnotum a śakyatvāt vairāgya siddhi artham duḥkha abhāvena eva upadeṣṭavyam iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_4.1.53	 itas ca duḥkha saṃjñā bhāvanam na sukhasya pratiṣedhaḥ iti āha bādhanā anivṛtteḥ vedayataḥ paryeṣaṇā doṣāt apratiṣedhaḥ prakāra paryeṣaṇa doṣa antara ādi iti evaṃvedayataḥ puruṣasya bādhanāyāḥ duḥkhasya anivṛtteḥ sukhe duḥkha bhāvanā upadeśaḥ kriyate lakṣaṇa sūtreṇa tena sukhasya svarūpataḥ na pratiṣedhaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_4.1.54	 nanu antarā sukham anubhavan= api kasmāt bahu duḥkham anubhavan svayam eva nirvetsyati kim duḥkha bhāvena upadeśena iti atas āha duḥkha vikalpe sukha abhimānāt ca yadi api vivekinaḥ bahu duḥkha sambhinnam sukham iti manyamānasya svayam eva vairāgyam tathā api avivekinām sukhāya yatamānānām tad anukte duḥkha vikalpe duḥkha viśeṣe duḥkha abhimāna sukha buddhiḥ ca asti tad aṅga bhāvena tatas ca tad buddhyā tad artham punar punar yatamānasya asya saṃsāra nivṛttiḥ syāt tasmāt duḥkha vikalpe sukha abhimānāt hetoḥ saṃsāra nivṛttiḥ mābhūt iti sukha ādiṣu duḥkha bhāvanā upadeśaḥ arthavān iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_4.1.55	 atha apavarga lakṣaṇam parīkṣamāṇaḥ tad sādhana anuṣṭhānasya avasara abhāvena tat asambhavam āha ṛṇa kleśa pravṛtti anubandhāt apavarga abhāvaḥ ṛṇam yajña brahmacarya ādi kleśaḥ sukha duḥkha ādi pravṛttiḥ vāc buddhi śarīra ārambhaḥ tad anubandhaḥ sarva kāla sambandhaḥ tasmāt ṛṇa kleśa pravṛtti anubandhāt jarayā vai eṣaḥ etasmāt vipramucyate ityādi vacanāt yāvat prāyaṇam agnihotra karma anuṣṭhānasya aparityāgena ṛṇa anubandhaḥ tathā sukha daḥkha moha rāga dveṣa ādi viṣaktasya na kadācid api avasthānam sambhavati kleśa anubandhāt apravartamānasya anavasthānena pravṛtti asambandhāt ca brāhmaṇasya turīyāṃśa prāpteḥ avasara abhāvena mokṣa upāya anuṣṭhāna abhāvāt apavargaḥ na sambhavati iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_4.1.56	 tatra ṛṇa anubandha ādityasya parihāram āha samāropaṇāt ātmani apratiṣedhaḥ prājāpatyām iṣṭim nirūpya tasyāḥ ca sarva vedasam hutvā ātmani agnīn samāropya brāhmaṇaḥ pravrajet iti vacanena prayāṇāt prāk eva ātmani agni samāropa sambhavāt jarayā ha vā iti ādeḥ ca mukhya artha asaṃbhavena guṇavāda tvāt phala gāminaḥ jīrṇa paratvena vyākhyānāt anyathā mṛtyunā eva iti anena siddha tvena tasya vaiyarthya prasaṅgāt asaktasya antevāsya ādi bāhya śakti vidhānāt ca turīya āśrama prāpteḥ avasara tvena mokṣa upāya anuṣṭhāna sambhavāt apavargasya pratiṣedhaḥ na iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_4.1.57	 itas ca ṛṇa anubandhaḥ na iti āha pātra caya anta anupapatteḥ ca phala abhāvaḥ āhitāgnim agniḥ dahantiti yajñāpātraiḥ ca iti vacanena āhitāgni ādīnām antya iṣṭi vidhau pratyavayavam yajña pātra nidhānena pātra caya anta tā dṛṣṭāḥ sa agni hotrāde jarā āmarye karmaṇi aviśeṣeṇa phala kāminam puruṣam prati yāvat āyuṣam pravartamāne vīta rāgāṇām eṣaṇā traya vyutthānena pravṛtti jātānām na antya karmaṇi api pravartete teṣām vahana ādi prakāreṇa antya karma śravaṇāt tasmāt sarva pātra caya anta tā anupapatteḥ phalasya sarvatra prayojaka tva abhāvaḥ tatas ca phala kalpanā rahitasya turīya āśrama prāptyā mokṣa upāya īśvara dhyāna ādi anuṣṭhāna sambhavāt apavarga abhāvaḥ na iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_4.1.58	 kleśa anubandha ādityasya parihāram āha suṣuptasya svapna darśane kleśa abhāvāt apavargaḥ yathā suptasya svapna darśinaḥ tad avasthāyām sukha duḥkha moha anubandhaḥ na asti cittasya nirindriya ātma pradeśa avasthānena karaṇe vyāpāra abhāvāt tathā apavarga avasthāyām api kleśa anubandhaḥ na asti niṣkāraṇa tvāt aśarīram vāvasantam iti ādi śrutau tad ātmā kadācid nirasta samasta viśeṣa guṇa anitya viśeṣa guṇa tve sati nitya tvāt pārthiva paramāṇu vat tat evam kleśa anubandhasya kādācitka tvāt apavargaḥ a sti iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_4.1.59	 pravṛtti anubandha āditi asya parihāram āha na pravṛttiḥ pratisandhānāya hīna kleśasya hīna kleśasya mithyā kleśa rāga dveṣa ādi viyuktasya puruṣasya pravṛttiḥ vidyamānā api mithyā saṅkalpita ādi lakṣaṇa sahakāri kāraṇa abhāvāt pratisandhānāya punar śarīra utpādaka adṛṣṭa utpādanāya na bhavati iti pravṛti anubanvaḥ api mokṣa abhāve na hetuḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_4.1.60–4.1.62	 kleśa anubandhaḥ na asti iti etat amṛṣyamāṇaḥ āha na kleśa santateḥ svābhāvika tvāt na asti kleśa anubandha vicchedaḥ kasmāt kleśa santateḥ svābhāvika tvāt iti sūtra arthaḥ idānīm anyaḥ eka deśī pariharati prāk utpatteḥ abhāvāt nitya tva vat svābhāvika tve api anitya tvam yathā prāk utpatteḥ prāc abhāva nitya tvam svābhāvika tve api bhāva utpattyā tathā svābhāvikyāḥ api kleśa santateḥ anitya tvam sambhavati iti sūtra arthaḥ idānīm anyaḥ eka deśī bhāvam eva dṛṣṭāntayati iti āha aṇu śyāma tā anitya tva vat vā yathā pārthivasya aṇoḥ śyāma tā anādi tvena āgama siddhā tathā anyasya api agni saṃyogāt vināśena anitya tā tathā kleśa santatiḥ anādiḥ api anityā bhavitum arhati iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_4.1.63^1	 tatra anitya tvasya kāraṇa sattā sambandha rūpa tvena asat rūpasya prāgabhāvasya tad asambhavāt vyapadeśasya bhākta tvāt aṇu śyāma tāyāḥ ca pārthiva rūpa tvena rakta ādi rūpa vat anitya tvena anāditva abhāvena asmad ādi praśna pūrvaka tva abhāva mātreṇa anādi vyapadeśasya āgamasya upapatteḥ na etat dṛṣṭa dvayam kleśa santateḥ svābhāvikyāḥ anitya tve sambhavati iti sva matena parihāram āha na saṅkalpa nimitta tvāt ca rāga ādīnām saṅkalpyate anena iti saṅkalpaḥ mithyājñānam cakāraḥ anukta samuccaya arthaḥ rāga ādīnām kleśānām prabandhena vartamānānām saṅkalpa nimitta tvāt 
NTD_4.1.63^2	 karma nimitta tva ādi rahita nimitta tvāt ca tasya api kūṭastha tayā anādi tva abhāvāt tattva jñānena apūrveṇa guru upadeśa ādinā labdhena abhyāsa ādinā sarisatvena virodhinā sa vāsanasya mithyājñāna lakṣaṇasya saṅkalpasya nivṛttau tad kārya rāga dveṣa ādi doṣa nivṛtti krameṇa dvitīya sūtra uktena kleśa santateḥ bhāvinyau= udbheda upāttāyāḥ ca samādhi balāt ekīkṛtya upabhogena prakṣayāt akhila kleśa santati viyuktasya ātmanaḥ avasthānam sambhavati iti na kleśa anubandha avicchedena apavarga abhāvaḥ sarveṣām rāga ādīnām saṅkalpa nimitta tve nānā vitta bhāvāt iti sūtra tātparya arthaḥ 
NTD_4.2.1^1	 tat evam chala saṃśaya pramāṇa prameyāṇi parīkṣitāni prayojana ādayaḥ api pramāṇa prameya antargata tvena yatra saṃśayaḥ tatra evam uttarottara prasaṅgaḥ iti tad padārtha parīkṣā aṅga bhūta saṃśaya nirākaraṇa samādhāna hetu prakāra atideśataḥ ca kathañcid parīkṣitāḥ vāda jalpa vitaṇḍānām ca agre kācid parīkṣā vartiṣyate tatra itareṣām tattva jñānam prameya tva jñāna aṅga tayā prameya tva jñānantu sākṣāt niḥśreyasa hetuḥ iti ca uktam atha idānīm cintyate kim sarva prāṇabhṛt saṃbandhya ātmā prameya viṣayam tattva jñānam mithyājñāna nivṛtti krameṇa niḥśreyasa hetuḥ āhosvit sva saṃbandhya ātma ādi viṣayam iti tatra prāṇa tanmātra saṃbandhya ātma ādi prameyāṇām ānantyena tad viṣaya tattva jñānasya aśakya karaṇīya tvāt tad viṣaya mithyā jñānasya anivṛtteḥ anya viṣaya tva jñānena anya viṣaya mithyā jñāna nivṛttau= atiprasaṅgāt ca anirmokṣa tā syāt iti saṃbandhya ātma ādi viṣaya tattva jñānam eva tad viṣaya mithyā jñāna ādi nivṛtti krameṇa mokṣa hetuḥ iti āha 
NTD_4.2.1^2	 doṣa nimittānām tattva jñānāt ahaṅkāra nivṛttiḥ doṣa nimittānām śarīra ādīnām duḥkha ādīnām prameyāṇām tatu a jñānāt ahaṅkāra nivṛttiḥ tat viṣaya aham iti mithyājñāna nivṛttiḥ tad vyatirikta ātmanām tattva adhyāropanivṛttiḥ ca sva saṃbandhi śarīra ādi duḥkha anta prameyam ahabhiti buddhvā tad upacārāya ghaṭamānaḥ pravṛtti ādi janana dvāreṇa saṃsāram anudhāvati na para śarīra ādi tatra mā nivartiṣṭa tad viṣaya mithyā jñānam nivartatām vā sva śarīra ādi dṛṣṭāntena na tena asya saṃsāra nivṛttim prati kaścid upayogaḥ tasmāt sva saṃbandhinām śarīra ādīnām doṣa nimittānām tattva jñānānām tad viṣaya mithyā jñāna ādi nivṛtti krameṇa dvitīya sūtra uktena niḥśreyasa prāptiḥ bhavati iti sarvam avadātam iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_4.2.2	 nanu saṃbandhiṣu śarīra ādiṣu savāsana viparyaya jñāna śamanāya utpadyamānam tattva jñānam kasmin viṣaye prathamam utpadyate iti atra āha doṣa nimittam rūpa ādayaḥ viṣayāḥ saṅkalpa kṛtāḥ rūpa ādayaḥ viṣayāḥ indriya arthāḥ saṅkalpa kṛtāḥ mithyājñānena viṣayīkṛtāḥ kāma rāgam pravartayanti iti te eva prathamam doṣa nimittam atas teṣu prathamam prasaṃkhyānam kṛtvā tad viṣayam mithyājñānam nivartya paścāt adhyātma śarīra ādiṣu prasaṃkhyāna abhyāsena tad viṣaya mithyā jñāna nivṛttiḥ kartavyā iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_4.2.3	 tat idam artha ādiṣu prameyeṣu nivartamāna mithyā jñāna avayavi ādi artham nirāsa mukhena nivartanīyam kinnu tad viṣaya aśubha saṃjñā bhāvanā mukhena iti āha tad nimittam tu avayavi abhimānaḥ teṣām doṣāṇām nimittam tad nimittam avayavi abhimāna avayavini kāminyadau= ittham avayavī iva na kevalena upamānam ittham dantā dāḍima bīja prakhyāpanam ittham oṣṭhaḥ bimba upamānaḥ ityādi abhimānaḥ kasmāt tasya śubha saṃjñā tve tathā abhimanyamānasya kāminī ādi viṣaya rāga anativṛtteḥ na punar kāminī ādi avayavi sattvam tad nimittam tad sattve api keśa loma māṃsa śoṇita asthi snāyu kapha pitta uccāra ādya āśraya tvena aśubha saṃjñām tatra bhāvayataḥ tad viṣaya rāga ādi anutpatteḥ tasmāt aśubha saṃjñā bhāvanā mukhena tad viṣaya mithyā jñānam nivartanīyam na tad asattva pratipādanena itara asya vraṇa siddha tvena nivartayitum aśakya tvāt iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_4.2.4–4.2.5	 idānīm artha nirāsa mukhena prasaṃkhyānam upadiśya tām upadarśayiṣyan prathamam avayavi nirāsāya saṃśayam āha vidyā avidyā dvaividhyāt saṃśayaḥ vidyā vedanam upalabdhiḥ avidyā avedanam anupalabdhiḥ tayoḥ dvaividhyāt upalabhyamānasya ca anupalabhyamānasya ca sat asat tvena dvaividhya darśanāt avayavini upalabhyamāne a nupalabhyamāne ca sattva asattvaḥ iti ubhayathā api saṃśayaḥ bhavati iti sūtra arthaḥ pramāṇa siddhe avayavini saṃśaya uktim asahamānaḥ siddhānti āha tad asaṃśayaḥ pūrva hetu prasiddha tvāt tasmin= avayavini saṃśayaḥ na yuktaḥ kasmāt pūrva hetu prasiddha tvāt pūrva uktaiḥ hetubhiḥ prasiddha tvāt avayavina prasiddhe ca tasmin saṃśaya anupapattiḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_4.2.6	 ukta sādhaka pramāṇāt ucyamānam vṛtti anupapatti lakṣaṇam bādhaka pramāṇam bala vat iti manasi nidhāya tena avayavinam nirākṛtya tat asiddha tvena tad viṣaya saṃśayam nirācikīrṣuḥ prathamam avayavānām avayavi nivṛtti pratiṣedhena avayavi abhāvam āha kṛtsna eka deśa avṛtti tvāt avayavānām avayavi abhāvaḥ avayavāḥ avayavini vartamānāḥ kṛtsne avayavini vartteḥ anna kedeśe vā na tāvat kṛtsne mahā parimāṇasya avayavinaḥ alpa parimāṇena avayavena avyāpteḥ eka dravya tva abhāvāt ca na api eka deśe prakṛta avayava vyatirekeṇa avayavinaḥ eka deśa antara abhāvāt bhāve api tadvat eva āvṛtteḥ tasmāt kṛtsna eka deśa avṛtti tvāt avayavānām na asti avayavī iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_4.2.7	 atha avayaveṣu avayavī vartate iti pakṣaḥ saḥ api na yuktaḥ iti āha teṣu ca āvṛtteḥ avayavi abhāvaḥ avayaveṣu avayavī vartamānaḥ eka deśena vā kārtsnyena vā vartate na tāvat eka deśena avayava vyatirekeṇa eka deśa antara abhāvāt bhāve ca anavasthāpātāt na api kārtsnyena ekasmin= avayave parisamāptasya anyatra vṛtti abhāvāt vṛttau ca aneka tva prasaṅgāt eka dravyasya kāraṇa vibhāga asambhavena nitya tva prasaṅgāt ca tasmannāvayaveṣu avayavī vartate iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_4.2.8–4.2.9	 mā bhūt avayaveṣu avayavinaḥ vṛttiḥ tathā api anyatra vartatām iti āśaṅkya āha pṛthak ca avayavebhyaḥ avṛtteḥ pṛthak anyatra avayavinaḥ avṛtteḥ asaṃbhavena anādhāra tvena vṛtti abhāvaḥ nitya tva prasaṅgaḥ ca iti sūtra arthaḥ avayavāḥ eva kenacid avasthā viśeṣeṇa anugṛhītaḥ avayavī iti vṛtti kalpaḥ na yuktaḥ iti ced tatra āha na avaya vi avayavāḥ avayavāḥ eva na avayavī bhavitum arhanti abhede dharmi bhāva anupapatteḥ matuppratyaya yoga asambhavāt bheda abheda pakṣasya anabhyupagamāt ca iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_4.2.10	 nanu avayavya grahaṇe sarva agrahaṇam prasajyate iti āśaṅkya āha keśa samūhe taimirika upalabdhi vat tad upalabdhiḥ pratyekam anupalabhamānānām keśānām samūhe yathā taimirikasya upalabdhiḥ tadvat eṣām pratyekam anupalabhyamānānām samūhaḥ upalabhyate tatas ca upalabdheḥ aṇu sañcayasi atra viṣaya tvena avayavi anabhyupagame api sarvathā grahaṇam na prasajyate iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_4.2.11	 tam enam vṛtti vikalpam sva āśraya vyāghātena dūṣayati avayava avayavi prasaṅgaḥ ca evam ālayāt tatra avayavāḥ avayavini vartante iti pakṣaḥ anabhyupagamena pratikṣiptaḥ avayavī avayaveṣu vartamānaḥ kim eka deśena sarva ātmanā vā iti vikalpaḥ samāna nyāya tayā tad tad avayava ādiṣu avayava avayavi tvena prasajyamānaḥ pralayāt vā nivartate uta paramāṇutaḥ vā na nivarteta vā na tāvat pralayāt tasya sarva upākhyā rahitasya darśana viṣaya tva anupapattyā vikalpasya anāśraya tvena ātma lābha abhāvāt tathā paramāṇoḥ api atīndriya tvena darśana viṣaya tva anupapatteḥ vikalpasya anāśraya tvena asambhavaḥ eva tathā nivṛtti pakṣe api ādyasya aniścayāt nānā āśraya tvam eva tasmāt vṛtti vikalpam abhyupagacchatā avayava avayavi prasaṅga bhītyā pralayāda aparamāṇoḥ ānivṛtteḥ vā vikalpa viṣayaḥ avayavi abhyupetavyaḥ tathā sati vṛtti vikalpaḥ eva sva āśraya siddhi artham avayavinam sādhayati iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_4.2.12	 nanu ca apralayāt iti sūtra eka deśena pralayaḥ tvayā abhyupetaḥ iti arthasya asattvam prasajyate iti āśaṅkya āha na pralayaḥ aṇu sadbhāvāt na asti pralayaḥ kasmāt aṇu sadbhāvāt vibhāge tvalpatara prasaṅgasya yatas na alpīyaḥ te trāvasthānāt paramāṇuḥ asti yadi tatra api avayava vibhāge na alpatara prasaṅgaḥ syāt tadā anantā avayava tvena trasareṇuḥ api meruṇā tulyaḥ syāt na ca etat dṛṣṭam iṣṭam vā na api pralaya anta tā vibhāgasya vibhajyamānasya abhāvena vibhāgasya api abhāva prasaṅgāt tasmāt asti niravayavaḥ paramāṇuḥ iti na anarthasya asattvam prasajyate iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_4.2.13–4.2.14	 niravayavasya paramāṇoḥ sattvena pralaya anta tā nirākaraṇam asahamānaḥ yoga ācāraḥ pratyavatiṣṭhate ākāśa vyatibhedāt tad anupapattiḥ ākāśa asarva gata tvam vā tad anupapattiḥ tasya paramāṇoḥ niravayavatu asya anupapattiḥ kasmāt akāśa vyatibhedāt ākāśena atyanta vyatibhinnaḥ yadi paramāṇuḥ tadā sa avayavaḥ syāt atha na vyatibhinnaḥ ākāśasya asarva gata tvam prasajyate na ca anyā gatiḥ asti tasmāt sāvayavaḥ paramāṇuḥ iti sūtra dvitaya arthaḥ 
NTD_4.2.15	 itas ca sāvayavaḥ paramāṇuḥ iti āha mūrtimatāñca saṃsthāna upapatteḥ ayava vyabhāvaḥ yadi api mūrtimatām api ṣaṣṭhyāḥ nirdeśaḥ tathā api hetu paratvena vyākhyeyam paramāṇuḥ sa avayavaḥ mūtimat tvāt saṃsthāna vat tvāt ca yat mūrtimat saṃsthāna vat ca tat sāvayavam dṛṣṭam yathā ghaṭaḥ tathā ca paramāṇuḥ tasmāt sāvayavaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_4.2.16	 itas api sāvayavaḥ iti āha saṃyoga upapatteḥ ca pūrva sūtra stha saṃsthāna śabdena yadi api pralaya ākhyaḥ saṃyoga viśeṣaḥ vivakṣitaḥ tathā api saṃyoga mātra sya anena sūtreṇa hetu tvena upādānam na paunaruktyam madhye san= aṇuḥ pūrva aparābhyām dakṣiṇa uttarābhyām upari adhovṛttimyām ca paramāṇubhyām yugapad saṃyujya parasparam ṣaṇṇām api vyavadhānam karoti tena anumīyate tad bhāgena tena aṇunā saṃyujyate iti sāvayavat tvam itarathā sarveṣām samāna deśa tvena piṇḍasya aṇu mātra tva prasaṅgaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_4.2.17	 tat evam paramāṇūnām sāvayavat tvam prasādhya sāvayavasya sarvasya api buddhyā vivecane kriyamāṇe ghaṭa ādi vat yāthātmyam na upalabhyate iti prameya mātrasya asattvāt nirālambana prameya mātram eva avaśiṣyate iti āha buddhyā vivecanāt tu bhāvānām yāthātmyānupalabdheḥ tantu apakarṣaṇesadbhāva anupalabdhi vat tad anupalabdhiḥ yathā ayam tantuḥ ayam tantuḥ iti tantuṣu buddhyā apakṛṣyamāṇeṣu tantu vyatirekeṇa na kaścid upalabhyate paṭa buddheḥ viṣayaḥ evam aśva ādiṣu sarva padārtheṣu buddhyā vivicyamāneṣu na kaścid buddheḥ viṣayaḥ syāt tattva ādi padārthāḥ tāvat yāvat pralayaḥ iti sarva bhāvānām buddhyā vivecanāt ya athātmya anupapatteḥ su a ākāra bāhya viṣayam vijñāna mātram eva vidyate na atra arthaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_4.2.18	 nanu bāhyam vastu sarvam na asti iti bruvāṇaḥ bhavān yadi tatra na pramāṇam bravīti tarhi pramāṇa abhāvāt bāhyasya sarvasya āsan= iti na siddhyati athavā sarvasya bāhyasya asattvam pramāṇa bhāvasya apakṣapita tvāt atha pramāṇam bravīti tarhi tasya pramāṇasya sa viṣaya tvena bāhya viṣaya tva abhyupagamāt bāhyam vastu sanna asti iti vyāhanyete tyāśaṅkya āha svapna viṣaya abhimāna vat ayam pramāṇa prameya abhimānaḥ yathā svapne viṣayāḥ na santi atha ca pratibhānti iti abhimānaḥ kalpanā mātraṇa tathā pramāṇa prameya bhāvaḥ api na vāstavaḥ kaścid asti kintu ana ādi va āsanā nibandhanaḥ kālpanikaḥ tathā ca sāṃvṛtena aparamārtha satā pramāṇa prameya bhāvena bāhya artha śūnyatā sidhyati parama artha satī pratyayānām dṛṣṭā ca mithyā jñānānām tattva pratipatti hetu tā vanaspati viṣaya mithyā hasti jñānasya iva vanaspati tattva buddhau tathā ca pada ādi pratyayaḥ mithyā pratyaya tvāt svapna pratyaya vat iti nirālambana tvam vijñānānām siddham iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_4.2.19^1	 tat etat yoga ācāra matam dūṣayati mithyā upalabdhi vināśaḥ tattva jñānāt viṣaya abhimāna praṇāśa vat pratibodhe yathā pratibodhe svapna viṣaya anupalabdhi lakṣaṇāt tattva jñānāt bādhāt svapna viṣaya abhimānasya smaryamāṇasya anubhūyamāna tva adhyāropasya praṇāśana smṛti vat smaraṇa viṣayasya vā tathā jāgrat pratyayānām api tattva jñānāt bādhakā dadhi āropita mithyā upalabdhi vināśaḥ bhavane viṣayasya paṭa ādeḥ iti svapna ādi dṛṣṭānta vikalpa tvam na ca yāsahāḥ mātra nibandhana tvena kālpanika tvam pramāṇa prameya bhāvasya pratyāyya bhedam antareṇa pratyaya bhedānupapattyā tad bhedāyāḥ vāsanāyāḥ bheda abhāvena vaicitrya anupapatteḥ tad adhīna kālpanika pramāṇa prameya bheda vyavahāra anupapatteḥ 
NTD_4.2.19^2	 tatas ca parārtha satā pramāṇena nirālambana tvam pratyayānām sādhanīyam yathā ca tena eva sūtra avayavena ākāśa vyatibhedāt iti evamādīnām api para pakṣa sādhana ābhāsānām mithyā upalabdhi tvāt tad tad ajñānāt bādhakāt vināśaḥ sūcitaḥ bhavati iti api mantavyam tatra yat tāvat ākāśa vyati bhedāt paramāṇoḥ sāvayava tvam ākāśā sarva gata tvam vā iti tat ayuktam antarita kāryasya kāraṇa viśeṣa vacana tvena akāryasya paramāṇoḥ antar deśa abhāvena ākāśasya tad viṣaya saṃyoga abhāvena vyatibheda abhāvāt na ca tāvatā ākāśasya asarva gata tvam sarva mūrta saṃyogasya sarva gata tve vidyamāna saṃyoga abhāve api sarva gata tva siddheḥ na api mūrtimatvāt sāvayava tvam tad abhyuyagataḥ 
NTD_4.2.19^3	 sāvayava paramāṇu avayavena anavasthā abhītyā tu kācana samāna parimāṇa prasaṅga bhītyā ca niravayava tvena vikalpate na vyabhicārāt na api saṃsthāna pakṣe tvata sāvayava tvam avayava racanā viśeṣasya eva saṃsthāna tvena sādhya sama tvāt na api ṣaṭka yogena vyavadhāyaka tvāt sāvayava tvam niravayava tve api mūrta tvena vyavadhāyaka tva siddhyā ṣaṭka yogasya anyathā siddha tvāt na ca niravayava tve samāna deśa tvena ṣaṣ paramāṇukasya piṇḍasya aṇu mātra tvam vikalpa anupapatteḥ kim ca paramāṇu apekṣayā samāna deśa tve api ekatra nihita ṣaṣ ghaṭika dīrgha vat sthaulyasya avirodhāt na ca saṃyogānām api samāna deśa tvam tad tad paramāṇu apekṣayā dviṣṭhasya saṃyogasya samāna deśa tva abhāvāt 
NTD_4.2.19^4	 na api buddhyā api ca anādya ātmā anupalabdhiḥ iti nyāyena nirālambanatva tad vivecanasya eva avadhi bhūta bāhya vastu abhāve a nupapatteḥ yat vyatirekeṇa idam na asti iti tantu ādiṣu vivicyamāneṣu kaścid avadhi bhūtaḥ arthaḥ na gṛhyate tathā anavasthāyāḥ bāhya arthasya asattvam na siddhyet anantara avayava tvena tu raparimeya tat eva para pakṣa sādhanānām asatvāt sva pakṣe ca madīyāḥ cittāt artha anantaram viṣayā madīya ahaṅkārān āspada tve sati sāmānya viśeṣavat tvāt sattā anantara citta vat iti ādi anumānena pratyakṣeṇa pratyayānām sa ālambana tva siddheḥ na yoga ācāra pakṣaḥ pākṣikaiḥ pakṣīkartum yuktaḥ iti tātparya arthaḥ 
NTD_4.2.20	 yaḥ tu mādhyamikaḥ mithyā buddhi dṛṣṭāntena bāhya artha apahnavam kṛtvā tena eva dṛṣṭāntena jñāna apahnavam kṛtvā vicāra asaha tvam bhāvānām vyavasthāpayāṃbabhūva tam pratyāha buddheḥ ca evam nimitta sadbhāva upalambhāt mithyā buddheḥ ca arthavat pratiṣedhaḥ arthe hi niṣiddhe bhavet api etat tad vyavasthāpane tadvat eva apratyūham buddhi sadbhāvaḥ api siddhyati na ca evam vādinaḥ pramāṇam asti asatā ca pramāṇena vicāra saha tvam bhāvānām saṃsthāpayan na para pakṣam pratiṣeddhum arhanti aprāmāṇikāyāḥ siddheḥ tatra api samāna tvāt tasmāt asti buddhiḥ tathā ca buddheḥ api evam arthavat nimittena satta asadbhāva upalambhāt athavā bhavat mate buddheḥ mithyā rūpāyāḥ sāmānya ādi darśanena nimittena satta asadbhāva upalambhān aparama artha sat tad kalpanā mūla tve tu mithyājñānasya anutpatteḥ sarvam abhāvaḥ bhāveṣu itaretarābhāva siddheḥ iti atra śūnya vādi matasya dūṣita tvāt ca anarthasya asattvam asattbabuddheḥ api asattvam siddhyati iti tad nirāsa mukhena prasaṃkhyānam kartavyam iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_4.2.21	 nanu āgamāt yuktitaḥ ca upapanna tattva jñānasya api doṣa nimitteṣu padārtheṣu ahaṅkāra ādi mithyā anuvṛtti darśanāt sākṣātkāraṇasya tattva jñānasya utpattau= upāya abhāvāt katham sa vāsana mithyā jñāna nivṛttiḥ śarīra ādiṣu saṃbhavati iti āśaṅkya asti eva upāyaḥ sākṣātkārasya iti āha samādhi viśeṣa abhyāsāt indriyebhyaḥ pratyāhṛtasya manasaḥ dhārakeṇa prayatnena dhāryamāṇasya ātmanā kvacid ātma pradeśe saṃyogaḥ samādhiḥ tasya viśeṣaḥ tattva bubhutsā tad viśiṣṭa tvam tena hi suṣṭhu vyavasthātaḥ samādhiḥ viśiṣyate tasya abhyāsaḥ dhāraka prayatna āvṛttiḥ tasmāt samādhi viśeṣa abhyāsāt sākṣītkāra kāraṇam tattva jñānam upapadyate tena ca utpannena tattva jñānena sa vāsanasya śarīra ādi viṣayasya nivṛttiḥ sambhavati iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_4.2.22–4.2.25	 codayati na artha viśeṣa prābalyāt anicchataḥ api buddhi utpatteḥ kṣudhā ādibhiḥ pravartanāt ca na samādhi viśeṣa abhyāsaḥ yuktaḥ kasmāt artha viśeṣa prābalyāt anicchataḥ abubhutsamānasya api stanayitnu śabda prabhṛtiṣu buddhi utpatteḥ buddhi utpāda darśanāt tathā kṣudh pipāsā ādibhiḥ upahatasya anicchataḥ api pravartanāt buddhi pravṛtti darśanāt ca iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_4.2.26	 pariharati pūrva kṛta phala anubandhāt tad utpattiḥ pūrva kṛtaḥ pūrva śarīra abhyasta samādhi viśeṣaḥ tad phalam saṃskāraḥ tasya anubandhaḥ sthemā tasmāt pūrva kṛta phala anubandhasya sākṣātkāraṇasya tattva jñānasya utpattiḥ janma antara abhyāsa āhita saṃskāra sahāyāt aihika janma kṛtāt samādhi viśeṣāt aspṛṣṭa viṣaya antaram saṃvartatayā ekāgreṇa utpadyamānaḥ sākṣātkāraḥ na artha antareṇa prabalena api niroddhum śakyate iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_4.2.27–4.2.28	 codayati apavarge api evam prasaṅgaḥ yadi artha viśeṣa prābalyāt anicchataḥ api buddhi utpattiḥ tahi artha viśeṣa prābalyasyāḥ nivṛtteḥ apavarge api evam vidhānām buddhīnām prasaṅgaḥ syāt indriya ādi nirapekṣasi a iva arthasya tathā sāmarthya abhyanujñānāt iti sūtra arthaḥ pariharati na niṣpanna avaśyaṃbhāvi tvāt karma vaśāt niṣpannasya śarīra ādeḥ avaśyam bhāvi tvāt prabalaḥ api arthaḥ tad rahitaḥ na apavarge jñānam utpādayitum samarthaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_4.2.29–4.2.30	 nanu tarhi tad abhyupagamya tām apavargaḥ iti āśaṅkya āha tad abhāvaḥ ca apavarge tasya śarīra ādeḥ abhāvaḥ eva apavarge tad mūlasya dharma adharma saṃskāra ādeḥ atyanta abhāvāt ati sūtra arthaḥ prakṛtam upasaṃharati tasmāt sarva duḥkha vimokṣaḥ apavargaḥ yasmāt sarva duḥkha bījam duḥkham ca apavargeṇa vicchidyate tasmāt sarveṇa duḥkhena vimuktiḥ apavargaḥ iti etat sugamam iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_4.2.31	 kim samādhi viśeṣaḥ eva sākṣātkārasya kāraṇam iti āśaṅkya āha tad artham yama niyamābhyām ātma saṃskāraḥ yogāt vā adhyātma vidhi upāyaiḥ tad artham tattva jñāna artham yama niyamābhyām yamaḥ sādhāraṇa dharma sādhanam āśramiṇām niyamaḥ tu asādhāraṇaḥ tābhyām ātma śodhanam ātma saṃskāraḥ kartavyaḥ iti tathā yogāt yoga śāstrāt hiraṇyagarbha ādeḥ vihitaiḥ adhyātma vidhi upāyaiḥ tathā prāṇāyāma ādibhiḥ ca ātma saṃskāraḥ kartavyaḥ iti te api sākṣātkāra utpādana dvāreṇa mokṣa upāyāḥ iti sūtra tātparya arthaḥ 
NTD_4.2.32	 nanu yadi ete tattva jñāna utpāda krameṇa apavarga upāyāḥ kṛtam tarhi ānvīkṣikya iti atas āha jñāna grahaṇa abhyāsaḥ tad vidyaiḥ ca saha saṃvādāt jñāyate anena iti jñānam nyāya śāstram tasya grahaṇam adhyayanam tasya abhyāsaḥ dhāraṇa artham satata kriyā tad vidyaiḥ ca saha saṃvādaḥ sā vidyā yeṣām te tad vidyāḥ taiḥ saha saṃvādaḥ saha adhyāya adhyāpanam tad vidyāyām sama tva āpādanam apavādaḥ tat ubhayam kartavyam sākṣātkāra jñāna utpāda janana dvāreṇa apavarga artham iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_4.2.33	 tad vidyaiḥ ca saha saṃvādaḥ iti etat vivektum āha tam śiṣya guru sabrahmacāri śiṣṭa śreyaḥ arthibhiḥ anasūyubhiḥ abhyupeyāt tam vādam śiṣyaiḥ gurubhiḥ saha adhyāyibhiḥ śiṣṭaiḥ guru ādi vyatiriktaiḥ śāstreṇa anuśiṣṭaiḥ śreyaḥ a rthibhiḥ niḥśreyasam prati śraddhāvadbhiḥ anasūyubhiḥ asūyā rahitaiḥ abhyupeyāt prāpnuyāt tatas ca tattva avabodhaḥ pariśuddhaḥ bhavati iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_4.2.34	 yaḥ tu manyate pakṣa pratipakṣa parigrahaḥ pratikūlaḥ parasya guru ādeḥ tatas ca tena saha vādaḥ api na kartum yuktaḥ iti tam pratyāha tam pratipakṣa hīnam api vā prayojana artham arthi tve tam vādam pratipakṣa hīnam api vā abhyupeyāt kim artham prayojana artham arthi tve sati paratas guru ādeḥ prajñām upāditsamānaḥ tattva bubhutsā prakāśanena ātmanaḥ śarīra ādibhyaḥ bhedam aham bhavataḥ bubhūtsam iti abhidadhānaḥ sva pakṣam anavasthāpayan sva darśanam guru ādi kṛtāt vicārāt pūrva pakṣa ucchedena sva pakṣa vyavasthā lakṣaṇāt sva darśanam pariśodhayet itim sūtra tātparya arthaḥ 
NTD_4.2.35	 nanu yatra vādasya eva īdṛśī daśā tatra tattva nirṇaye jalpa vitaṇḍe dattāñjalī iti tad āśaṅkya āha tattva adhyavasāya saṃrakṣaṇa artham jalpa vitaṇḍe bīja praroha saṃrakṣaṇa artham kaṇṭaka śākhā āvaraṇa vat yathā bīja praroha saṃrakṣaṇa artham kaṇṭaka śākhābhiḥ āvaraṇam āvṛtiḥ kriyate tathā tattva adhyavasāya saṃrakṣaṇa artham anutpanna sākṣātkāra tattva jñānaiḥ tad artham ghaṭamānam kartavye jalpa vitaṇḍe iti te api sa prayojane grati sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_4.2.36	 na kevalam tad artham ghaṭamānānām jalpa vitaṇḍe kim tarhi vidyābhiḥ veda ādibhiḥ ca pareṇa avajñāyamānasya tābhyām jalpa vitaṇḍābhyām vigṛhya kathanam yuktam iti āha tābhyām vigṛhya kathanam yaḥ tu kudarśana abhyāsa āhita mithyā jñāna avalepa durvidagdha tayā kuhetubhiḥ īśvarāṇām jñānāḥ dhārāṇām puratas veda brāhmaṇa para loka ādi dūṣaṇena tad mata vibhrama āpādane pravṛttaḥ tam prati vādī samācīna dūṣaṇam apratibhayā a paśyan jalpa vitaṇḍe avatārya vijigīṣayā tām nigṛhya tattva kathanam karoti mā bhūt īśvarāṇām mati vibhrameṇa tad carita anuvartinīnām prajānām api dharma viplavaḥ iti anena api prayojanena jalpa vitaṇḍe iti sūtra arthaḥ dvidhā pravṛttim trividhān= ca doṣān saṃprati abhāvā phala duḥkha mokṣāḥ mārgaḥ ca mokṣasya yathāpramāṇam parīkṣitam sarvam idam caturthe iti bhaṭṭa vāc īśvara viracitāyām nyāya sūtra tātparyadīpikāyām caturthaḥ adhyāyaḥ 
NTD_5.1.1	 atha idānīm jalpa vitaṇḍā parīkṣā anantaram tad aṅga tvena avasara prāptāni jāti nigraha sthānāni vivicya kathyante tatra jātiḥ nāma sādharmya vaidharmyābhyām pratīpam avasthānam jātiḥ iti sāmānya lakṣaṇam uktam pūrvam eva saṃprati tad viśeṣa lakṣaṇa artham vibhāga uddeśa sūtram s ā d h a r m y a v a i d h a r m y o t k a r ṣ ā p a k a r ṣ a v a r ṇ y ā v a r ṇ y a v i k a l p a s ā d hi aprāpti aprāpti prasaṅga pratidṛṣṭānta an utpatti saṃśaya prakaraṇa hetu artha apatti aviśeṣa upapati upalabdhi anupalabdhi nitya anitya kārya samāḥ sādharmyam eva samaḥ yasmin prayoge sa sādharmya samaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ evam vaidharmya sama prabhṛtayaḥ api nirvaktavyāḥ te ete caturviṃśati hetavaḥ sthāpana ahetau prayukte sambhavati iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_5.1.2	 sādharmya vaidharmyābhyām upasaṃhāre tad dharma viparyaya upapatteḥ sādharmya vaidharmya samau sādharmyeṇa upasaṃhāre tat sādharmyeṇa pratyavasthānam sādharmya samaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ yathā nityaḥ śabdaḥ utpatti dharmaka tvāt ghaṭa vat iti ukte jāti vādya āha yadi anitya ghaṭa sādharmyāt anityaḥ tarhi nityena api ākāśena sādharmyam amūrta tvam asti iti nityaḥ prāptaḥ ekasmin= eva hetau ākāśa vaidharmyāt iti ukte yaḥ nitya ākāśa vaidharmyāt utpatti vaidharmaka tvāt anityaḥ sādharmyam api ākāśe na asti amūrta tvam atas nityaḥ śabdaḥ prāptaḥ atha manyase sati api etasmin sādharmyeṇa nityaḥ iti na tarhi vaktavyam anitya ghaṭa sādharmyāt nitya ākāśa vaidharmyāt anityaḥ iti anityena api asya ghaṭena vaidharmyam amūrta tvam asti atas nityaḥ prāptaḥ tasmin= eva hetau ghaṭa sādharmyāt iti kṛte yadi anitya ghaṭa sādharmyāt anityaḥ vaidharmyam api asya anena asti amūrta tvam atas nityaḥ prāptaḥ iti 
NTD_5.1.3	 anayoḥ uttaram go tvāt go siddhi vat tad siddhiḥ gavā aśvasā dharmye sattva ādau samāne vaidharmye ca eka śapha ādau na sādharmya mātrāt sattvāt gauḥ aśvaḥ bhavati na vaidharmya mātrāt eka śapha ādeḥ aśvaḥ gauḥ bhavati iti kim kāraṇam go tve sādhye sattvasya aśvādau go tvena vyabhicāreṇa gavāḥ cabādhāt ago tve sādhye vā eka śapha ādeḥ vaidharmyasya mahiṣa ādeḥ api vyāvatteḥ yat anvayavi atireki sādharmyam tasmāt tad dharma vyavasthā bhavati go tvañca tathā tasmāt go tvāt eva gauḥ siddhyati tathā iha api amūrta tvam ubhaya vyatireki ubhaya anvayi na tasmāt nityam anityam vā śakyam pratipattum api tu anvayavyatireki saṃpannāt utpatti dharma tvāt pratyavasthānam sādharmyeṇa ukte hetau tad vaidharmyeṇa pratyavasthānam vaidharmya samaḥ yathā tasmin= eva hetau= ākāśa vaidharmyāt iti ukte yadi nitya ākāśa vaidharmyāt anityaḥ atas yat bravīṣi viśeṣa hetu abhāvāt iti tat na ayam aviśeṣaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_5.1.4^1	 sādhya dṛṣṭāntayoḥ dharma vikalpāt ubhaya sādhya tvāt ca utkarṣa apakarṣa varṇyāvarṇya vikalpa sādhya samāḥ sādhya dṛṣṭāntayoḥ dharma vikalpāt vaicitryāt sādhye avidyamāna dharma adhyāropaḥ utkarṣaḥ vidyamāna dharma apanayaḥ apakarṣaḥ varṇyaḥ sādhyaḥ avarṇyaḥ asādhyaḥ vikalpaḥ viśeṣaḥ eteṣām dharmāṇām udbhāvanā arthāḥ prayogāḥ utkarṣa sama ādyāḥ jātayaḥ iti sādhya sādhana dharmayoḥ tulya tayā pratyavasthānam sādhyasameti ucyate iti udāharaṇantu anityaḥ śabdaḥ utpatti dharmaka tvāt ghaṭa vat iti ukte yadi yathā ghaṭaḥ tathā śabdaḥ ghaṭaḥ rūpa ādimān śabdaḥ api evam prasaktaḥ iti utkarṣaḥ 
NTD_5.1.4^2	 ghaṭaḥ śrāvaṇaḥ na bhavati iti śabdaḥ api evam prasaktaḥ iti apakarṣa samaḥ śabdaḥ nitya varṇaḥ ghaṭaḥ api evam aghaṭaḥ vā nitya varṇaḥ śabdaḥ api evam iti varṇyāvarṇya samau yathā sati ekasmin= utpatti dharmaka tve vibhāga jaḥ śabdaḥ na vibhāga jaḥ ghaṭaḥ vibhāga jā vibhāga ja vikalpaḥ nitya anitya vikalpaḥ iti vikalpa samaḥ sati api vikalpa vaicitrye sarvatra utkarṣa ādīnām samākhyā nirukti vaśāt vikalpa samatas mithas ca bhedaḥ draṣṭavyaḥ ghaṭaḥ vā nityaḥ iti atra kaḥ hetuḥ ayam api sādhya vat pañca avayava yogi tvena prajñāpayitavyaḥ iti sādhya samaḥ 
NTD_5.1.5–5.1.6	 eteṣām uttaram kiñcid sādharmyāt upasaṃhāra asiddheḥ vaidharmyāt apratiṣedhaḥ na brūmaḥ yāvantaḥ ghaṭa dharmāḥ te sarve eva śabde bhavanti iti api tu yaḥ dharmaḥ sādharmyeṇa svabhāva pratibandha yuktaḥ bhavati sa tatra upasaṃhriyate tathā ca śabdaḥ iti upanaya padena evañca sati yathoktam na saṃbandham yathā gauḥ tathā gavayaḥ iti ukte na go dharmāḥ sarve eva gavaye na gavaya dharmāḥ sarve eva gavi api tu yaḥ ca itareṇa saṃvadhyate tāvat mātre eva upasaṃhriyate aśeṣa dharma upasaṃhāre tu yathā iti eva na syāt saḥ eva asau= iti yathā iha api iti adoṣaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ sādhya atideśāt ca dṛṣṭānta upapatteḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ sādhyaḥ iti bruvatā na dṛṣṭānta lakṣaṇam hi nāma api iha tayoḥ daśanayoḥ viṣayaḥ tathā ca sādhya tvam anupapannam atha darśanam vihanyate na asau dṛṣṭānte lakṣaṇa abhāvāt iti varṇya avarṇya vikalpa sādhya asādhya samānām anutthānam iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_5.1.7–5.1.8	 prāpi asādhyam aprāpya vā hetoḥ prāptyā viśiṣṭa tvāt aprāptyā asādhaka tvāt ca prāpti aprāpti samau hetuḥ prāpya vā artham sādhayet aprāpya vā yadi prāpya tarhi prāpti viṣaya tvena vidyamāna tvāt sādhyasya kasya idam sādhanam na hi siddham sādhyate atha aprāpya na tarhi sādhaka tvam na hi agniḥ aprāptaḥ dahatti iti prāptyā pratyavasthānam prāpti samaḥ anayoḥ uttaram ghaṭa ādi niṣpatti darśanāt pīḍane ca abhicārāt apratiṣedhaḥ kartṛ karaṇam mṛdam prāpya sādhya karma asādhāraṇam ghaṭa ādikam phalam niṣpādayati tathā pīḍane ca abhicārāt aprāpya sādhaka tvam dṛṣṭam iti prāpti aprāpti samayoḥ anutthānam pratiṣedhe api tulya tvāt iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_5.1.9	 dṛṣṭāntasya kāraṇa anapadeśāt pratyavasthānāt ca pratidṛṣṭāntena prasaṅga pratidṛṣṭānta samau dṛṣṭāntasya dṛṣṭānta gata anitya tvasya kāraṇa anapadeśāt pramāṇa anapadeśāt iti dṛṣṭānta gata nitya tvasya pramāṇam vācyam iti prasaṅgena pratyavasthānam prasaṅga samaḥ pramāṇa mātra pratyavasthānam sādhya samānaḥ viśeṣaḥ prasaṅgam asya iti pratidṛṣṭāntena pratyavasthānam pratidṛṣṭānta samaḥ yathā anityaḥ prameya tvāt ghaṭa vat iti ukte jāti vādya āha prameyam ākāśam nityam dṛṣṭam ayam api tathā astu iti anaikāntika tvam udbhāvayitum aśaknuvan na pratidṛṣṭāntaḥ dṛṣṭānta mātreṇa pratyavatiṣṭhate iti jāti tvam anyathā sat uttaram eva syāt iti mantavyam iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_5.1.10–5.1.11	 tatra prasaṅga samasya uttaram pradīpa upādāna prasaṅga nivṛtti vat tad vinivṛttiḥ pratyakṣa darśana artham pradīpam upādadānaiḥ na pradīpa antaram upādīyate pradīpa pradarśana artham tadvat aprajñātasya prajñāpana artham dṛṣṭāntam upādadānaiḥ na dṛṣṭāntasya kāraṇam apadeṣṭavyam apadiṣṭa kāraṇa tvāt tasya iti sūtra arthaḥ atha pratidṛṣṭānta samasya uttaram pratidṛṣṭānta hetu tve ca na ahetuḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ pratidṛṣṭāntam bruvatā na viśeṣa hetuḥ ucyate yena kāraṇena pratidṛṣṭāntar sādhakaḥ na dṛṣṭāntaḥ iti pratidṛṣṭānta hetu tve ahetuḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ iti na upapadyate hetu tve ca dṛṣṭāntasya pratidṛṣṭāntasya anutthānam iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_5.1.12–5.1.13	 prāk utpatteḥ kāraṇa abhāvāt anutpatti samaḥ anityaḥ śabdaḥ utpatti dharmaka tvāt kumbha vat iti ukte brūyāt prāk utpatteḥ utpattiḥ na asti iti anitya tvasya akāraṇam tad abhāvāt anutpatti dharmaka tvam anutpatti dharmaka tvāt ca nityaḥ iti anupapattyā pratyavasthānam anutpatti samaḥ asya idam uttaram tathā abhāvāt utpannasya kāraṇa upapatteḥ na kāraṇa pratiṣedhaḥ utpannaḥ khalu ayam śabdaḥ iti bhavati utpatti dharmakaḥ iti ca prāk utpatteḥ śabdaḥ eva na asti utpannasya tathā abhāvāt śabdasya sataḥ utpatti dharmaka tvam anitya tva kāraṇam upapadyate kāraṇa upapatteḥ ca prāk utātteḥ kāraṇa abhāvāt iti kāraṇa pratiṣedhaḥ na yuktaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_5.1.14	 sāmānya dṛṣṭāntayoḥ aindrayaka tve samāne nitya anitya sādharmyāt saṃśaya samaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ prayatnanā antarīyaka tvasya hetoḥ dhaṭaḥ yathā hi viśeṣa dharmasya prayatna anantarīyaka tvasya darśanam niścaya kāraṇam asti iti niścaya utpattiḥ eva sāmānya dharmasya aindriyaka tvasya darśana saṃśaya kāraṇam asti saṃśayena pratyavasthānam saṃśaya samaḥ iti saṃśaya samā sādharmya samātaḥ na bhidyate iti ced naḥ ubhaya eka sādharmya bhedāt ubhaya sādharmyāt saṃśaya samaḥ eka sādharmyāt sādharmya samaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_5.1.15	 asya uttaram sādharmyāt saṃśaye na saṃśayaḥ vaidharmyāt ubhayathāḥ vā saṃśaye a tyanta saṃśaya prasaṅgaḥ nitya tva anabhyupagamāt ca sāmānyasya apratiṣedhaḥ sādharmyāt sāmānya dharma darśanāt saṃśaye na saṃśayaḥ vaidharmyāt viśeṣa darśanāt ubhayathā vā sāmānya viśeṣa darśanābhyām saṃśaye atyantam nitya saṃśaya prasaṅgaḥ nitya tvāna bhyupagamāt ca sāmānyasya sādhāraṇa dharmasya nityam saṃśaya hetu tvena anabhyupagamāt ca pratiṣedhaḥ saṃśaya sama lakṣaṇa pratiṣedhaḥ na asti iti na sādharmyasya aindriyaka tvasya darśana mātram saṃśaya kāraṇam api tu viśeṣa darśana sahitam viśeṣasya prayatnanā antarīyaka tvasya darśane tu na tat rahitam sāmānya darśanam asti iti saṃśaya samasya anutthānam iti sūtra tātparya arthaḥ 
NTD_5.1.16	 ubhaya sādharmyāt prakriyā siddheḥ prakaraṇa samaḥ ubhayena nityena ca sādharmyāt prakriyā siddheḥ pakṣa pratipakṣayoḥ pravṛtti siddheḥ prakaraṇa anativṛttyā pratyavasthānam karaṇa samaḥ upalakṣaṇañca etat ubhaya vaidharmyāt iti api draṣṭavyam yathā anityaḥ śabdaḥ prayatnanā antarīyaka tvāt ghaṭa vat iti ekaḥ pakṣam pravartayati dvitīyaḥ ca nityaḥ śabdaḥ śrāvaṇa tvāt śabda tva vat iti ubhaya dharmasya udāharaṇam yathā nityaḥ śabdaḥ kṛtaka tvāt ākāśa vat iti ekaḥ nityaḥ śabdaḥ asparśa tvāt ghaṭa vat iti aparaḥ evañca satya nitya nitya sādharmyāt nitya vaidharmyāt vādinaḥ sādhanāt prakaraṇam anativartamānāt nirṇayāt niṣpattiḥ iti nanu saṃśaya samātaḥ prakaraṇa samā na bhidyate tatra api ubhaya sādharmyam iha api iti na ubhaya pakṣa siddhi asiddhi bhedāt bheda upapatteḥ prakaraṇa samāyā tu vādī sva pakṣa viniścayena para pakṣam dūṣaṇīyam iti buddhyā pratyavatiṣṭhate saṃśaya samāyām tu vādī sādhanena sādharmya mātra āpādanena prativādī tu sva pakṣa niścayena iti sāmya apādanañca sa dūṣaṇaiḥ na sādhanena iti 
NTD_5.1.17	 asya uttaram pratipakṣāt prakaraṇa siddheḥ pratiṣedha anupapattiḥ pratipakṣa upapatteḥ pratipakṣāt pratipakṣa sādhanāt prakaraṇasya pratīyamānasya sādhyasya siddheḥ pratiṣedhasya prativādi sādhanasya sva pakṣa siddhi dvāreṇa para pakṣa sādhana pratiṣedhanasya anupapattiḥ tasmāt pratipakṣa upapatteḥ iti ayam arthaḥ dvayoḥ sādhanayoḥ tat ānīma gṛhyamāṇa viṣayayoḥ samāna balayoḥ ca ayam ātmīyāt sādhanāt sva pakṣa siddhim icchati prativādī tatas ca anicchan= api vādinā api sādhanāt balāt pakṣa siddhim abhyupagamayitavyaḥ anyathā rāja kula sthiti prasaṅgāt evam ca tayoḥ api phalataḥ vyabhicāraḥ siddhaḥ bhavati na ca viruddha avyabhicārī sa bhavati vastunaḥ dvairūpya prasaṅgāt iti prakaraṇa samasya pratiṣedhasya anupapattiḥ iti nanu prakaraṇa samāt dhetvābhāsāt asya kaḥ viśeṣaḥ ayam viśeṣaḥ sva sādhya nirṇayena para sādhana vighna buddhyā prativādinā sādhanam prayujyamānam prakaraṇa sama jāti uttaram bhavati sat pratipakṣatayā vādinaḥ sādhanam aniścāyakam karomi iti buddhyā pratipakṣa sādhanam prayujyamānam sat uttaram bhavati iti 
NTD_5.1.18–5.1.19	 traikālya asiddheḥ hetoḥ ahetu samaḥ hetoḥ triṣu api kāleṣu asiddheḥ hetuḥ ahetunā na viśiṣyate ahetu sāmyāt pratyavasthānam ahetu samaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ asya uttaram na hetutaḥ sādhya siddheḥ traikālya asiddhiḥ na utpadyamānam ahetutaḥ utpadyate jñāpyamānam ahetutaḥ vā jñāpyate tatas ca na hetoḥ traikālya asiddhiḥ loka pramāṇa virodhāt iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_5.1.20–5.1.21	 arthāpattitaḥ pratipakṣa siddheḥ arthāpatti samaḥ anityaḥ śabdaḥ iti artha āpattyā pratipakṣam sādhayataḥ arthāpatti samaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ bhavati sādharmya samādau vādī abhiprāya varṇanam iti etāvatā bhedaḥ draṣṭavyaḥ asya uttaram anuktasya arthāpatteḥ pakṣa hāneḥ upapattiḥ anukta tvāt anaikāntika tvāt ca arthāpatteḥ tat etat khalu anuktam vacanāt labhyate yat kalpanām antareṇa vacana arthaḥ na ghaṭate pīnaḥ devadattaḥ divā na bhuṅkte iti ukte rātrau bhuṅkte iti vākya artha upapādane tasya sāmarthyāt na tu avyabhicāriṇaḥ sādharmyāt sādhye sādhyamāne arthāt uktam bhavati vyabhicāriṇā api sādharmyeṇa sādhyam sādhayitavyam iti tasya vākya artha upapādane asāmarthyāt tad antareṇa api vākya artha upapatteḥ yadi punar anukta mātrasya arthāt āpattiḥ tatas tvayā nitya tva āpādane śabdasya ucyamāne anucyamānam anitya tvam pratyetavyam anitya tva pakṣasya hetoḥ upapattiḥ tasyāḥ api anitya tvāt iti sūtra arthaḥ na hi ghanasya grābṇaḥ patanam iti ukte dravasya udakasya āpatanam arthāt labhyate iti vyabhicāraḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_5.1.22–5.1.23	 eka dharma upapatteḥ aviśeṣe sarva aviśeṣa prasaṅgāt sadbhāva upapatteḥ aviśeṣa samaḥ ekasya prayatna anantarīyaka tvasya ghaṭa sādharmyāt upapatteḥ ghaṭa śabdayoḥ aviśeṣaḥ anitya tve sati sarveṣām aviśeṣa prasaṅgaḥ kasmāt sadbhāva upapatteḥ iti atha sādharmya sama viśeṣa samayoḥ bhedaḥ abhidheyaḥ iti asya uttaram kvacid dharma upapatteḥ kvacid ca anupapatteḥ pratiṣedha abhāvaḥ kvacid sādharmye prayatna anantarīyaka tva ādau sati śabda ādeḥ ghaṭa ādinā samāna dharmasya ghaṭa dharmasya anitya tvasya upapatteḥ kvacid ca sādharmye śabdasya bhāva mātreṇa saha sattva ādau sati bhāva mātra dharmasya anupapatteḥ pratiṣedha abhāvaḥ kasmāt avinā abhā= a saṃpannasya sādharmyasya gamaka tvāt anyasya sattva ādeḥ agamaka tvāt iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_5.1.24–5.1.25	 ubhaya kāraṇa upapatteḥ upapatti samaḥ ubhayasya nitya anitya tvasya kāraṇa upapattyā pratyavasthānam upapatti samaḥ yadi anitya tvasya kāraṇam upapadyate śabdasya iti anityaḥ evam nitya tvasya api kāraṇam upapadyate asparśa tvam iti nityaḥ syāt iti prakaraṇa samāyām jātau pakṣa pratipakṣa sādhanayoḥ samāna bala tve api prativādī sva sādhanāt sva pakṣa siddhyā vādinaḥ sādhana dūṣaṇe pravartate upapatti samāyāntu sva sādhanena eva iti viśeṣaḥ boddhavyaḥ iti asya uttaram upapatti kāraṇa abhyanujñānāt apratiṣedhaḥ nitya tva kāraṇam api asya upapadyate iti bruvatā abhyanujñātam anitya tva kāraṇam tathā ca virodhāt uttara pakṣa utthānam ayuktam iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_5.1.26–5.1.27	 nirdiṣṭa kāraṇa abhāve api upalambhāt upalabdhi samaḥ nirdiṣṭasya sādhya dharma kāraṇasya abhāve api sādhya dharma upalabdhyā pratyavasthānam upalabdhi samaḥ yathā anityaḥ śabdaḥ sāmānya viśeṣavat tve sati asmad ādi bāhya indriya grāhya tvāt iti ukte sarvam anityam iti adhyāropya dūṣayati na hi ayam hetuḥ sarvasmin= anitye vartate dvi aṇuka ādau vyabhicārāt iti sūtra arthaḥ kāraṇa antarāt api tad dharma upapatteḥ apratiṣedhaḥ kāraṇa antarāt jñāpaka antarāt api tad dharma upapatteḥ apakṣīkṛtānām na pūrva uktaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ pakṣīkṛteṣu prakṛtasya api jñāpaka tva sya anapāyāt anukta adhyāra upasya ayukta tvāt ca iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_5.1.28	 tad anupalabdheḥ anupalambhāt abhāva siddhau tad viparīta upapatteḥ anupalabdhi samaḥ na prāc uccāraṇāt śabdasya sataḥ anupalabdhiḥ āvaraṇa ādeḥ anupalabdheḥ iti ukte jāti vādya āha teṣām āvaraṇa ādīnām anupalabdhiḥ na upalabhyate upalabhyamāna tve tu upalabdhi rūpa tayā anupalabdhi tva anupapatteḥ tathā ca anupalabdheḥ anupalambhāt anupalabdhiḥ na asti iti āvaraṇa ādi upalabdhi siddheḥ āvaraṇa ādi siddhiḥ iti āvaraṇa anupalabdhau ca samaya anupalabdhyā pratyavasthānam anupalabdhi samaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_5.1.29–5.1.30	 asya uttaram anupalambha ātmaka tvāt anupalabdheḥ ahetuḥ āvaraṇa ādi anupalabdhiḥ na asti anupalambhāt iti ayamahetuḥ kasmāt anupalambha ātmaka tvāt anupalabdheḥ upalambha abhāva mātra tvāt anupalabdheḥ upalambha abhāvaḥ anupalabdhyā niścīyate natu ātmanaḥ yadi ātmanaḥ api abhāvaḥ niścīyate tad āvaraṇa anupalabdheḥ anupalabdhyā api svabhāvaḥ niścīyate tatas ca āvaraṇa anupalabdhi siddheḥ āvaraṇa abhāva siddhiḥ iti pratiṣedha an utthānam iti sūtra arthaḥ jñāna vikalpānāñca bhāva abhāva saṃvedanāt adhyātmam āvaraṇa anupalabdheḥ anupalambha āditya siddhaḥ hetuḥ tasyāḥ prati puruṣam saṃvedya tvāt na api upalabdhi rūpa tayā anupalabdhi tva hāniḥ upalambha abhāva tad upalabdhyoḥ atyanta vilakṣaṇa tvāt iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_5.1.31	 sādharmyāt tulya dharma upapatteḥ sarva anitya tva prasaṅgaḥ anitya samaḥ anityena ghaṭena sādharmyāt anityaḥ śabdaḥ tatas anityena ghaṭena sarva bhāvānām sādharmyam iti sarvasya anitya tvam prasajyate iti anitya tvena pratyavasthānam anitya samaḥ aviśeṣa samātaḥ anitya samā na bhidyate iti ced sarva aviśeṣa sarva anitya tva prasaṅga bhedāt bheda upapattiḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_5.1.32	 asya uttaram sādharmyāt asiddheḥ pratiṣedha asiddhiḥ pratiṣedhya sādharmyāt yadi ghaṭa sādharmyāt pratiṣedhyasya anitya tvasya asiddhiḥ tarhi pratiṣedhyasya api asiddhiḥ kasmāt pratiṣedhyasādhyarmyāt pratiṣedhyena pakṣeṇa sādharmyasya pratijña ādi yogasya pratiṣedhasya vidyamāna tvāt sādharmyasya viśeṣasya gamaka tvāt ca anitya samasya anutthānam iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_5.1.33–5.1.34	 nityam anitya bhāvāt anitye nitya tva upapatteḥ nitya samaḥ anityaḥ śabdaḥ iti pratijñāyate tad anitya tvam kim śabde nityam atha anityam tad dharmasya nitya tvāt tat dharmiṇaḥ api nitya tvam atha anityaḥ tarhi anitya tvasya abhāvāt nityaḥ śabdaḥ iti nitya tvena pratyavasthānam nitya samaḥ asya uttaram pratiṣedhye nityam anitya bhāvāt anitye nitya tva upapatteḥ pratiṣedha abhāvaḥ pratiṣedhye śabde nityam anitya bhāvāt iti ucyamāne anujñāta śabdasya anitya tvam anitya tva upapatteḥ na anityaḥ śabdaḥ iti pratiṣedhaḥ na upapadyate atha tu na anujñāyate nitya tvam anitya tvasya abhāvāt iti hetuḥ na bhavati iti hetu abhāvāt pratiṣedha anupapattiḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_5.1.35	 prayatna kārya aneka tvāt kārya samaḥ anityaḥ śabdaḥ prayatna anantarīyaka tvāt iti ukte yadā jāti vādī prayatna antaram upalabdheḥ iti hetu artha adhyāropeṇa pratiṣedhati prayatna anantaram upalabhyamānam anityañca dṛṣṭam śabdaḥ api kim nityaḥ uta anityaḥ iti tadā kārya viśeṣeṇa pratyavasthānāt kārya samaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ viśeṣa upalabdhi vivakṣaya upalabdhi sādharmyāt saṃśaya samaḥ tad avivakṣayā hetu artha adhyāropeṇa kārya samaḥ sādharmya mātreṇa sādharmya samaḥ iti trayāṇām parasparam bhedaḥ draṣṭavyaḥ 
NTD_5.1.36	 asya uttaram kārya anya tve prayatna ahetu tvam anupalabdhi kāraṇa anupapatteḥ anupalabdhi kāraṇa āvaraṇa ādeḥ artha sattvena bhavat adhi āropitasya prayatna anantara upalambhasya hetu tvena vivakṣita tvāt iti uttara vādinam prati sādhana vādinā samyak sādhanam sva sādhyasya vaktavyam tattva nirṇaya avasāna tvāt kathāyāḥ iti darśitam 
NTD_5.1.37–5.1.38	 saṃprati samādhāna abhāva vādinam prati ṣaṣ pakṣam darśayati sūtrakāraḥ pratiṣedhe api samānaḥ doṣaḥ prayatna kārya aneka tvāt iti yaḥ ayam pratiṣedhaḥ jāti vādinaḥ tasya api anaikāntikaḥ kasyacid pratiṣedhāt kasyacid apratiṣedhāt iti sūtra arthaḥ sarvatra evam na kevalasya ajñātāḥ vayam samādhāna ābhāsa vādinaḥ api sarvā jātiṣu eṣā yuktiḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_5.1.39–5.1.40	 pratiṣedha vipratiṣedhe pratiṣedha doṣa vat doṣaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ jāti vādinaḥ tasya pratiṣedhaḥ mūla sādhana vādinaḥ tasmin= tulyaḥ doṣaḥ iti jāti vādinaḥ pratyavasthānam iti sūtra arthaḥ pratiṣedham sa doṣam abhyupetya pratiṣedha vipratiṣedhe samāna doṣa prasaṅgaḥ mata anujñā caturtha pakṣa vādinam prati pañcama pakṣe sthitaḥ sādhana vādī mata anujñā pādanam karoti iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_5.1.41^1	 sva pakṣa lakṣaṇa apekṣā upapatti upasaṃhāre hetu nirdeśe para pakṣa doṣa abhyupagamāt samānaḥ doṣaḥ sva pakṣe lakṣyate iti sva pakṣa lakṣaṇam anaikāntika tvacodanā apekṣa anujñā upapattiḥ saṃbhāvanā tat ayam arthaḥ sthāpanā hetu vādī sva pakṣa uktam anaikāntika tvam anuddhṛtya sva pakṣe saṃbhāvyamānam anaikāntika tva doṣam jāti vāda pakṣe pratiṣedhe api samānaḥ doṣaḥ iti upasaṃhṛtya tatra hetum nirdiśati tatas ca pareṇa sva pakṣaḥ uktasya anaikāntika tva doṣasya sādhana vādinā abhyupagamāt anyasya api mata anujñā lakṣaṇaḥ doṣaḥ samānaḥ iti ṣaṣṭhe pakṣe sthitasya jāti vādinaḥ vacanam iti caturtha ṣaṣṭhyoḥ pakṣayoḥ artha aviśeṣāt punar ukta doṣa prasaṅgaḥ samānaḥ tṛtīya pañcamayoḥ caturtha pakṣeṇa api dvitīya pakṣa ukta doṣaḥ abhyanujñāyate ṣaṣṭha pakṣeṇa api pañcama pakṣa ukta doṣaḥ 
NTD_5.1.41^2	 evam tṛtīya pakṣeṇa api dvitīya pakṣa ukta doṣaḥ abhyanujñāyate pañcama pakṣeṇa api caturtha pakṣa ukta doṣaḥ evam tṛtīya caturthayoḥ mata anujñā pañcama ṣaṣṭhayoḥ vādi prativādinoḥ sva pakṣa apekṣayā punar uktā iti sūtra dvitaya arthaḥ ṣaṣ pakṣyām ubhayoḥ asiddhiḥ prathama dvitīya pakṣayoḥ viśeṣa hetu abhāvāt anyeṣām caturṇām pakṣāṇām mata anujñā pauna rukta doṣāt ubhayoḥ pakṣayoḥ asiddhiḥ iti tat evam anyatara nirṇaya avasāna tvāt kathāyāḥ iti samīcīnam eva sādhana vādī jāti vādinam prati vaktavyam prāyaśas tathā ca ṣaṣ pakṣī na vartate anyathā tu ṣaṣ pakṣī pravartate iti sūtra tātparyarthaḥ iti iha yatnena vipañcitam mayā samasta jāti uttaram uttara anvitam kvacid prayogaḥ phalam asya varṇanam kvacid prayuktau= anuyogaḥ iti api iti bhaṭṭa vāc īśvara viracitāyām nyāya sūtra tātparyadīpikāyām pañcama adhyāyasya ādyam āhnikam 
NTD_5.2.1	 atha idānīm avasara prāptānām nigraha sthānānām viśeṣa lakṣaṇa artham vibhāga uddeśa sūtram pratijñāhāniḥ pratijñāntaram pratijñā virodhaḥ pratijñāsannyāsaḥ hetu antaram artha antaram nirarthakam avijñāta artham apārthakam aprāpta kālam nyūnam adhikam punaruktam ananubhāṣaṇam ajñānam apratibhā vikṣepaḥ mata anujñā paryanuyojya upekṣaṇam niranuyojya anuyogaḥ apasiddhāntaḥ hetvābhāsāḥ ca iti nigraha sthānāni tāni idānīm dvāviṃśatidhā vibhajya lakṣyante iti sūtra arthaḥ nanu kartṛ karaṇa karmaṇām kasya nigrahaḥ kartuḥ kasmāt svātantryāt karma karaṇayoḥ pāratantryāt yathā ākāśe asim vyāpārayataḥ puruṣasya aparādhaḥ na ākāśasya na api aseḥ tasmāt asamarthayoḥ karma karaṇayoḥ upādānāt vipratipattyoḥ tad ādhāra tvāt ca kartuḥ eva nigrahaḥ vacana dvāreṇa tu udbhāvyante iti nyūna tā ādayaḥ vacana doṣāḥ na sākṣāt iti 
NTD_5.2.2	 pratidṛṣṭānta dharma abhyanujñā sva dṛṣṭānte pratijñā hāniḥ dṛṣṭaḥ ca asau= ante nigamane vyavasthitaḥ ca iti dṛṣṭāntaḥ svaḥ ca asau dṛṣṭāntaḥ ca iti sva dṛṣṭānta śabdena sva pakṣaḥ ucyate evam pratidṛṣṭānta śabdena api pratipakṣaḥ pratipakṣasya yaḥ dharmaḥ tasya sva pakṣe abhyanujñānam pratijñā hāniḥ yathā anityaḥ śabdaḥ aindriyaka tvāt ghaṭa vat iti ukte sāmānyam aindriyakam nityam dṛṣṭam iti anaikāntika tvena prativādinā pratyavasthitaḥ vādī yathā sarvam nityam iti sāṃkhya siddhānta avalambanena anaikāntika tvam ujjahīrṣuḥ śabda nitya tvam abhyupaiti tadā vipakṣa abhāva at na anaikāntika tvam na api viruddha tā kim tarhi pratijñāta artha hāniḥ iti tayā gṛhyate iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_5.2.3	 pratijñāta artha vipratiṣedhe dharma vikalpāt tad artha nirdeśaḥ pratijñāntaram anityaḥ śabdaḥ aindriyaka tvāt iti yaḥ asya pratiṣedhaḥ pratidṛṣṭāntena hetu vyabhicāraḥ sāmānyam aindriyakam nityam dṛṣṭam iti atha aindriyaka tvena pratiṣedhe kṛte dharma vikalpāt ghaṭa sāmānyayoḥ sarva gata tvāt sarva gata tva dharma bhedāt tad artham pratijñāta artha siddhi artham śabdasya asarva gata tvam pratipādayitum asarva gataḥ śabdaḥ iti yaḥ asau nirdeśaḥ sa pratijñāntaram iti sūtra arthaḥ nanu anaikāntika tvāt eva asya nigrahaḥ bhaviṣyati kim artham pratijñā antara kalpanaḥ paryavasita padaḥ evam madhye prativādinā hetoḥ anaka antikaḥ śabdasya asarva gata tvam sādhayitvā tena aindriyaka tvam viśiṣya sarva gataḥ śabdaḥ iti pratijñā antaram kṛtvā saha adarśana bhītyā vā na tatra hetum bravīti tena yathā joya vādī pratijñā mātrasyā sā sādhaka tva buddhyā upādānāt iti mantavyam 
NTD_5.2.4	 pratijñā hetvoḥ virodhaḥ pratijñā virodhaḥ pratijñā hetvoḥ iti pratiyogi dvaya mātra upalakṣaṇa param tena dṛṣṭānta ādayaḥ api pratiyoginaḥ upalakṣayitavyāḥ lakṣya sthitasya api pratijñā grahaṇasya upalakṣaṇa paratvam veditavyam tena etat uktam bhavati yeṣām vākya gatānām padārthānām mithas vyāghātaḥ saṃbandha smṛti anapekṣayā eva apātataḥ pratīyate pramāṇa antaram ca virodhakam sa virodhaḥ nāma nigraha sthānam iti yathā guṇa vyatiriktam dravyam tat api atirikta tvāt yadi atas bhinnam tat sarvam tatas vyatiriktam dṛṣṭam yathā ghaṭāt paṭaḥ vyatiriktam ca dravyam guṇāt tatas vyatiriktam iti evamādi na ca viruddha ādi hetu ābhāsānām virodha nigraha sthāna tva prasaṅgaḥ teṣām saṃbandha smṛti anapekṣa tvāt virodha pratīteḥ tad apekṣa tvāt asya iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_5.2.5	 pakṣa pratiṣedhe pratijñāta artha apanayaḥ pratijñāsannyāsaḥ anityaḥ śabdaḥ aindriyaka tvāt ghaṭa vat iti ukte samā anyam aindriyakam dṛṣṭam nityam iti anaikāntika tvena pratiṣedhe kṛte prativādinā vādi pratilā artha apahnava ena anaikāntika tvam ujjihīrṣuḥ pratijñā artha apanayam karoti saḥ evam āhānityaḥ śabdaḥ iti tadā pratijñā āsannyāsaḥ eva vādinaḥ nigrahaḥ na tu anaikāntika tvam apahnave satya naikāntika tva anupapattiḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_5.2.6	 aviśeṣa ukte hetau pratiṣiddhe viśeṣam icchataḥ hetu antaram nityāḥ vedāḥ asmaryamāṇa kartṛka tva āditya viśeṣeṇa ukte hetau jīrṇa kayā ādi nā anaikāntika tvena pratiṣedhe asmaryamāṇa kartṛka tve sati iti viśeṣam icchataḥ vādinaḥ hetu antaram nigraha sthānam bhavati punar tasya hetoḥ asāmarthya ākhyānāt sāmarthye vā hetu antara upādāna vaiyarthyāt iti nanu anaikāntika tvāt eva asya nigrahaḥ bhaviṣyati iti kim artham hetu antara kalpanā iti aneka antika tvasya tu viśeṣaṇena eva samāhita tvāt iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_5.2.7	 prakṛtāt arthāt apratisaṃbaddha artham artha antaram hetu sādhya siddhau prakṛtāyām vādī sādhanam brūyāt nityaḥ śabdaḥ asparśa tvāt iti atra antaraiḥ sukha ādibhiḥ vyabhicārāt sva heta uḥ asāmarthyam paśyan tad pracchādanāya prasakta anuprasaktyā hetuḥ nāma hinoteḥ dhātostuni pratyaye kṛte kṛdantam padam iti ādi abhidhāyi tvāt iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_5.2.8–5.2.9	 varṇa krama nirdeśa vat nirarthakam anityaḥ śabdaḥ kacaṭatapānām jabagaḍada tvāt jhabha gha ḍhadha vat iti yathā varṇa krama nirdeśaḥ nirarthakaḥ nirabhidheyaḥ evam yad artha bheda vivakṣa utthāpitam vacanam tat sarvam nirarthakam nigraha sthānam tasya samayena sa abhidheya tve api āryam pratyanabhidhāyaka tvena tad pratipādaka śabda apratipatteḥ tad ārambha vaiyarthyāt iti sūtra arthaḥ pariṣad prativādibhyaḥ tris abhihitam api avijñātam avijñāta artham yat vākyam vādinā tris abhihitam api pariṣadā prativādinā vā na jñāyate kliṣṭa śabdam apratīta prayogam atidruta uccāritam ityādinā kāraṇena tat avijñāta artham nāma nigraha sthānam bhavati vādinaḥ prayogeṣu asāmarthya khyāpanāt iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_5.2.10	 paurvāparya ayogāt apratisaṃbaddha artham apārthakam yatra anekasya padasya vākyasya vā paurvāparyeṇa artha saṃbandhaḥ na asti iti asaṃbaddha artha tā gṛhyate tat apārthakam nāma nigraha sthānam samudāya artha asaṃbhavena vākya artha pratyāyana prayojana śūnya tvāt yathā daśa dāḍimāni ṣaṣ apūpāḥ kuṇḍam palam piṇḍam ityādinā nirarthaka apārthakayoḥ abhedaḥ nirabhidheya tva niṣprayojana tvayoḥ atyanta vilakṣaṇa tvāt iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_5.2.11	 avayava viparyāsa vacanam aprāpta kālam avayavānām yathālakṣaṇam prayogaḥ arthavat siddhaḥ tad viparyāse tu ākāṅkṣa abhāvena tad pūrvakasya padārtha saṃbandhasya abhāvāt aprāpta kālam saṃbandha nigraha sthānam bhavati yatra avayava viparyāse avayava artha saṃbandhaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ tatra api prayoga apeta śabda vat mūla ānupūrvīsmṛtyā eva artha pratyayaḥ boddhavyaḥ iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_5.2.12–5.2.13	 hīnam anyatamena api avayavena nyūnam pratijña ādīnām militānām sādhana tvam upapāditam nyūna tve sādhana tvam na asti tad abhāve na sādhya siddhiḥ na hi sāmagrī niṣpādyam kāryam sāmagrya eka deśāt bhavati tasmāt nyūnam tad vādinaḥ nigraha sthānam iti sūtra arthaḥ hetu udāharaṇa adhikam adhikam yasmin vākye dvau hetū dvau dṛṣṭāntau tat vākyam adhikam nigraha sthānam iti niṣpādita kriye karmaṇi aviśeṣa abhidhāyinaḥ sādhanasya sādhana nyāya atipātāt tivādanāt iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_5.1.14–5.1.15	 śabda arthayoḥ punarvacanam punaruktam anyatra anuvādāt arthāt āpannasya sva śabdena punarvacanam punaruktam tat anena sūtra dvayena punaruktam ekam eva nigraha sthānam kvacid śabda abhyāsāt kvacid paryāya antarāt kvacid arthāt iti kathañcid ava antara bheda vivakṣayā trividham iti punarukta prayoge tad prayojana anusaraṇa samākula cittaḥ prathama abhidhānāt āpātatas pratītam api artham apratītam iva manyamānaḥ na viśvasitum arhati tatas ca pratipādanāya pravṛttaḥ api na pratipādayet iti viruddha prayojana tvena punaruktasya nigraha sthāna tvam veditavyam iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_5.2.16	 vijñātasya pariṣadā tris abhihitasya apratyuccāraṇam ananubhāṣaṇam prativādinā na tāvat sarvam dūṣaṇīyam anyatama avayava dūṣaṇena eva sādhanasya dūṣita tvena doṣa antara abhidhāna vaiyarthyāt na khalu mṛtaḥ mṛtyunā punar śakyaḥ mārayitum evam dūṣitam api na śakyam dūṣayitum tasmāt anyatamasya dūṣaṇasya pariṣadā vijñātasya vādinā tris abhihitasya tad śabdena śabda antareṇa vā yat apratyuccāraṇam na tad ananubhāṣaṇam nigraha sthānam anyathā dūṣaṇa āśrayasya anirdeśena tasya avayavasya idam dūṣaṇam iti saṃśaya prasaṅgāt na ca sarva anuvādaḥ abhimataḥ tathā satya dūṣya anuvādat viranuvāda ādi doṣa prasaṅgāt iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_5.2.17–5.2.19	 avijñātam ca ajñānam pariṣadā vijñātasya dūṣyasya yat aparijñānam tat ajñānam nāma nigraha sthānam tad viṣaya apratyuccāraṇāt bhinnam iti sūtra arthaḥ uttarasya apratipattiḥ apratibhā para pakṣa pratiṣedhaḥ uttaram tat yadā na pratipadyate śloka pāṭhā ādibhiḥ avajñām karoti tadā nigṛhītaḥ veditavyaḥ iyañcā pratibhā tad sādhana upanyāse draṣṭavyā sādhana abhāve tu paryanuyojya upekṣaṇam iti sūtra arthaḥ kārya vyāsaṅgrāt kathā vicchedaḥ vikṣepaḥ yatra kartavyam vyāsa jya abhyupagatām kathām vicchinnatti idam me karaṇīyam parihīyate tasmin paryavasite paścāt kathayiṣyāmi iti sa vikṣepaḥ nāma nigraha sthānam ekatara nigraha antāyām kathāyām svayam eva kathā antam pratipadyate iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_5.2.20–5.2.21	 sva pakṣe doṣa abhyupagamāt para pakṣa doṣa prasaṅgaḥ mata anujñā pareṇa codita doṣam sva pakṣe abhyupagamyān uddhṛtya para pakṣe doṣam prasajati bhavat pakṣe api samānaḥ doṣaḥ iti para matam anujānāti iti para anujñayā nigṛhyate para udita doṣa antara aparijñānāt iti sūtra arthaḥ udāharaṇam tu bhavān= cauraḥ iti ukte tvam api coraḥ ityādi nigraha prāptasya anigrahaḥ paryanuyojya upekṣaṇam yaḥ nigraha prāptam puruṣam na nigṛhṇāti sa nigṛhītaḥ veditavyaḥ kutas paryanuyojyasya upekṣaṇāt tad viṣaya nigraha sthāna aparijñānāt iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_5.2.22	 anigraha sthāne nigraha sthāna abhiyogaḥ niranuyojya anuyogaḥ nigraha sthāna lakṣaṇasya mithyā adhyavasāyāt anigraha sthāne nigṛhītaḥ asi iti param bruvan niranuyojya anuyogāt nigṛhītaḥ veditavyaḥ iti anena ca sarvāḥ eva jātaya chalāni ca nigraha sthāna tvena saṃgṛhītāni iti mantavyam niranuyojya anuyogāt teṣām hetvābhāsānāntu hetu huddhyā upa vādibhiḥ anutthāna tva vivakṣayā asmin niranuyojya anuyogāt prativādi nigraha sthānāt bhedena upanyāsaḥ iti sūtra tātparya arthaḥ 
NTD_5.2.23	 siddhāntam abhyupetya aniyamāt kathā prasaṅgaḥ apasiddhāntaḥ kañcid siddhāntam abhyupetya aniyamāt siddhānta viparyayāt yaḥ kathā prasaṅgaḥ saḥ apasiddhāntaḥ nāma nigraha sthānam yathā anityaḥ śabdaḥ jātimat tve satyasmad ādi bāhya indriya grāhya tvāt iti ukte vaiśeṣikeṇa mīmāṃsakaḥ pratyavatiṣṭhate asti tarhi go tva sāmānyasya api jātimattve satyasmad ādi bāhya indriya grāhya tvam sattā yogi tvāt iti sa punar vaiśeṣikaḥ tat uktim abhyupetya yadā dūṣaṇa antaram mṛgayate tadā niḥsāmānyāni pasiddhāntān nigṛhyate pūrva apara viruddha artha abhidhāyi tvāt iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NTD_5.2.24	 hetvābhāsāḥ ca yathā uktāḥ yathā eva vibhaktā lakṣaṇena tathā eva teṣām nigraha sthāna bhāvaḥ na lakṣaṇa antareṇa cakārāt yat kiñcid anuktam api nigra sthānam asti ced tat api nigraha sthānam iti sūtra arthaḥ evam nigraha vastu tattvam akhilam nirṇītam etat punar jñātam jalpa vitaṇḍayoḥ bahu phalam sūte svayam vādinām mukharāḥ jetum katham vādinaḥ śakyante katham evam ātma viṣayam jñānam katham vā ucyate iti jagati janānām īśa sāyujya bhājām anupajanita bhāṣaṇeṣu paśupatiḥ api yasmai sa smitaḥ sādhu sādhu iti avadat avatu saḥ asmān akṣapādaḥ muni indraḥ iti
